Waitha hadara alqismata oloo alqurba walyatama walmasakeenu farzuqoohum minhu waqooloo lahum qawlan ma'roofa

# 502

Walyakhsha allatheena law tarakoo min khalfihim thurriyyatan di'afan khafoo 'alayhim falyattaqoo Allaha walyaqooloo qawlan sadeeda

# 503

Inna allatheena yakuloona amwala alyatama thulman innama yakuloona fee butoonihim naran wasayaslawna sa'eera

# 504

Yooseekumu Allahu fee awladikum liththakari mithlu haththi alonthayayni fain kunna nisaan fawqa ithnatayni falahunna thulutha ma taraka wain kanat wahidatan falaha annisfu waliabawayhi likulli wahidin minhuma assudusu mimma taraka in kana lahu waladun fain lam yakun lahu waladun wawarithahu abawahu faliommihi aththuluthu fain kana lahu ikhwatun faliommihi assudusu min ba'di wasiyyatin yoosee biha aw daynin abaokum waabnaokum la tadroona ayyuhum aqrabu lakum naf'an fareedatan mina Allahi inna Allaha kana 'aleeman hakeema

# 505

Walakum nisfu ma taraka azwajukum in lam yakun lahunna waladun fain kana lahunna waladun falakumu arrubu'u mimma tarakna min ba'di wasiyyatin yooseena biha aw daynin walahunna arrubu'u mimma taraktum in lam yakun lakum waladun fain kana lakum waladun falahunna aththumunu mimma taraktum min ba'di wasiyyatin toosoona biha aw daynin wain kana rajulun yoorathu kalalatan awi imraatun walahu akhun aw okhtun falikulli wahidin minhuma assudusu fain kanoo akthara min thalika fahum shurakao fee aththuluthi min ba'di wasiyyatin yoosa biha aw daynin ghayra mudarrin wasiyyatan mina Allahi wallahu 'aleemun haleem

# 506

Tilka hudoodu Allahi waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wathalika alfawzu al'atheem

# 507

Waman ya'si Allaha warasoolahu wayata'adda hudoodahu yudkhilhu naran khalidan feeha walahu 'athabun muheen

# 508

Wallatee yateena alfahishata min nisaikum fastashhidoo 'alayhinna arba'atan minkum fain shahidoo faamsikoohunna fee albuyooti hatta yatawaffahunna almawtu aw yaj'ala Allahu lahunna sabeela

# 509

Wallathani yatiyaniha minkum faathoohuma fain taba waaslaha faa'ridoo 'anhuma inna Allaha kana tawwaban raheema

# 510

Innama attawbatu 'ala Allahi lillatheena ya'maloona assooa bijahalatin thumma yatooboona min qareebin faolaika yatoobu Allahu 'alayhim wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 511

Walaysati attawbatu lillatheena ya'maloona assayyiati hatta itha hadara ahadahumu almawtu qala innee tubtu alana wala allatheena yamootoona wahum kuffarun olaika a'tadna lahum 'athaban aleema

# 512

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yahillu lakum an tarithoo annisaa karhan wala ta'duloohunna litathhaboo biba'di ma ataytumoohunna illa an yateena bifahishatin mubayyinatin wa'ashiroohunna bilma'roofi fain karihtumoohunna fa'asa an takrahoo shayan wayaj'ala Allahu feehi khayran katheera

# 513

Wain aradtumu istibdala zawjin makana zawjin waataytum ihdahunna qintaran fala takhuthoo minhu shayan atakhuthoonahu buhtanan waithman mubeena

# 514

Wakayfa takhuthoonahu waqad afda ba'dukum ila ba'din waakhathna minkum meethaqan ghaleetha

# 515

Wala tankihoo ma nakaha abaokum mina annisai illa ma qad salafa innahu kana fahishatan wamaqtan wasaa sabeela

# 516

Hurrimat 'alaykum ommahatukum wabanatukum waakhawatukum wa'ammatukum wakhalatukum wabanatu alakhi wabanatu alokhti waommahatukumu allatee arda'nakum waakhawatukum mina arrada'ati waommahatu nisaikum warabaibukumu allatee fee hujoorikum min nisaikumu allatee dakhaltum bihinna fain lam takoonoo dakhaltum bihinna fala junaha 'alaykum wahalailu abnaikumu allatheena min aslabikum waan tajma'oo bayna alokhtayni illa ma qad salafa inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheema

# 517

Walmuhsanatu mina annisai illa ma malakat aymanukum kitaba Allahi 'alaykum waohilla lakum ma waraa thalikum an tabtaghoo biamwalikum muhsineena ghayra musafiheena fama istamta'tum bihi minhunna faatoohunna ojoorahunna fareedatan wala junaha 'alaykum feema taradaytum bihi min ba'di alfareedati inna Allaha kana 'aleeman hakeema

# 518

Waman lam yastati' minkum tawlan an yankiha almuhsanati almuminati famin ma malakat aymanukum min fatayatikumu almuminati wallahu a'lamu bieemanikum ba'dukum min ba'din fankihoohunna biithni ahlihinna waatoohunna ojoorahunna bilma'roofi muhsanatin ghayra masafihatin wala muttakhithati akhdanin faitha ohsinna fain atayna bifahishatin fa'alayhinna nisfu ma 'ala almuhsanati mina al'athabi thalika liman khashiya al'anata minkum waan tasbiroo khayrun lakum wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 519

Yureedu Allahu liyubayyina lakum wayahdiyakum sunana allatheena min qablikum wayatooba 'alaykum wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 520

Wallahu yureedu an yatooba 'alaykum wayureedu allatheena yattabi'oona ashshahawati an tameeloo maylan 'atheem

# 521

Yureedu Allahu an yukhaffifa 'ankum wakhuliqa alinsanu da'eefa

# 522

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takuloo amwalakum baynakum bilbatili illa an takoona tijaratan 'an taradin minkum wala taqtuloo anfusakum inna Allaha kana bikum raheema

# 523

Waman yaf'al thalika 'udwanan wathulman fasawfa nusleehi naran wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera

# 524

In tajtaniboo kabaira ma tunhawna 'anhu nukaffir 'ankum sayyiatikum wanudkhilkum mudkhalan kareema

# 525

Wala tatamannaw ma faddala Allahu bihi ba'dakum 'ala ba'din lirrijali naseebun mimma iktasaboo walinnisai naseebun mimma iktasabna wasaloo Allaha min fadlihi inna Allaha kana bikulli shayin 'aleema

# 526

Walikullin ja'alna mawaliya mimma taraka alwalidani walaqraboona wallatheena 'aqadat aymanukum faatoohum naseebahum inna Allaha kana 'ala kulli shayin shaheeda

# 527

Arrijalu qawwamoona 'ala annisai bima faddala Allahu ba'dahum 'ala ba'din wabima anfaqoo min amwalihim fassalihatu qanitatun hafithatun lilghaybi bima hafitha Allahu wallatee takhafoona nushoozahunna fa'ithoohunna wahjuroohunna fee almadaji'i wadriboohunna fain ata'nakum fala tabghoo 'alayhinna sabeelan inna Allaha kana 'aliyyan kabeera

# 528

Wain khiftum shiqaqa baynihima fab'athoo hakaman min ahlihi wahakaman min ahliha in yureeda islahan yuwaffiqi Allahu baynahuma inna Allaha kana 'aleeman khabeera

# 529

Wa'budoo Allaha wala tushrikoo bihi shayan wabilwalidayni ihsanan wabithee alqurba walyatama walmasakeeni waljari thee alqurba waljari aljunubi wassahibi biljanbi wabni assabeeli wama malakat aymanukum inna Allaha la yuhibbu man kana mukhtalan fakhoora

# 530

Allatheena yabkhaloona wayamuroona annasa bilbukhli wayaktumoona ma atahumu Allahu min fadlihi waa'tadna lilkafireena 'athaban muheena

# 531

Wallatheena yunfiqoona amwalahum riaa annasi wala yuminoona billahi wala bilyawmi alakhiri waman yakuni ashshaytanu lahu qareenan fasaa qareena

# 532

Wamatha 'alayhim law amanoo billahi walyawmi alakhiri waanfaqoo mimma razaqahumu Allahu wakana Allahu bihim 'aleema

# 533

Inna Allaha la yathlimu mithqala tharratin wain taku hasanatan yuda'ifha wayuti min ladunhu ajran 'atheema

# 534

Fakayfa itha jina min kulli ommatin bishaheedin wajina bika 'ala haolai shaheeda

# 535

Yawmaithin yawaddu allatheena kafaroo wa'asawoo arrasoola law tusawwa bihimu alardu wala yaktumoona Allaha hadeetha

# 536

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la taqraboo assalata waantum sukara hatta ta'lamoo ma taqooloona wala junuban illa 'abiree sabeelin hatta taghtasiloo wain kuntum marda aw 'ala safarin aw jaa ahadun minkum mina alghaiti aw lamastumu annisaa falam tajidoo maan fatayammamoo sa'eedan tayyiban famsahoo biwujoohikum waaydeekum inna Allaha kana 'afuwwan ghafoora

# 537

Alam tara ila allatheena ootoo naseeban mina alkitabi yashtaroona addalalata wayureedoona an tadilloo assabeel

# 538

Wallahu a'lamu bia'daikum wakafa billahi waliyyan wakafa billahi naseera

# 539

Mina allatheena hadoo yuharrifoona alkalima 'an mawadi'ihi wayaqooloona sami'na wa'asayna wasma' ghayra musma'in wara'ina layyan bialsinatihim wata'nan fee addeeni walaw annahum qaloo sami'na waata'na wasma' wanthurna lakana khayran lahum waaqwama walakin la'anahumu Allahu bikufrihim fala yuminoona illa qaleela

# 540

Ya ayyuha allatheena ootoo alkitaba aminoo bima nazzalna musaddiqan lima ma'akum min qabli an natmisa wujoohan fanaruddaha 'ala adbariha aw nal'anahum kama la'anna ashaba assabti wakana amru Allahi maf'oola

# 541

Inna Allaha la yaghfiru an yushraka bihi wayaghfiru ma doona thalika liman yashao waman yushrik billahi faqadi iftara ithman 'atheema

# 542

Alam tara ila allatheena yuzakkoona anfusahum bali Allahu yuzakkee man yashao wala yuthlamoona fateela

# 543

Onthur kayfa yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba wakafa bihi ithman mubeena

# 544

Alam tara ila allatheena ootoo naseeban mina alkitabi yuminoona biljibti wattaghooti wayaqooloona lillatheena kafaroo haolai ahda mina allatheena amanoo sabeela

# 545

Olaika allatheena la'anahumu Allahu waman yal'ani Allahu falan tajida lahu naseera

# 546

Am lahum naseebun mina almulki faithan la yutoona annasa naqeera

# 547

Am yahsudoona annasa 'ala ma atahumu Allahu min fadlihi faqad atayna ala ibraheema alkitaba walhikmata waataynahum mulkan 'atheema

# 548

Faminhum man amana bihi waminhum man sadda 'anhu wakafa bijahannama sa'eera

# 549

Inna allatheena kafaroo biayatina sawfa nusleehim naran kullama nadijat julooduhum baddalnahum juloodan ghayraha liyathooqoo al'athaba inna Allaha kana 'azeezan hakeema

# 550

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati sanudkhiluhum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan lahum feeha azwajun mutahharatun wanudkhiluhum thillan thaleela

# 551

Inna Allaha yamurukum an tuaddoo alamanati ila ahliha waitha hakamtum bayna annasi an tahkumoo bil'adli inna Allaha ni'imma ya'ithukum bihi inna Allaha kana samee'an baseera

# 552

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola waolee alamri minkum fain tanaza'tum fee shayin faruddoohu ila Allahi warrasooli in kuntum tuminoona billahi walyawmi alakhiri thalika khayrun waahsanu taweela

# 553

Alam tara ila allatheena yaz'umoona annahum amanoo bima onzila ilayka wama onzila min qablika yureedoona an yatahakamoo ila attaghooti waqad omiroo an yakfuroo bihi wayureedu ashshaytanu an yudillahum dalalan ba'eeda

# 554

Waitha qeela lahum ta'alaw ila ma anzala Allahu waila arrasooli raayta almunafiqeena yasuddoona 'anka sudooda

# 555

Fakayfa itha asabathum museebatun bima qaddamat aydeehim thumma jaooka yahlifoona billahi in aradna illa ihsanan watawfeeqa

# 556

Olaika allatheena ya'lamu Allahu ma fee quloobihim faa'rid 'anhum wa'ithhum waqul lahum fee anfusihim qawlan baleegha

# 557

Wama arsalna min rasoolin illa liyuta'a biithni Allahi walaw annahum ith thalamoo anfusahum jaooka fastaghfaroo Allaha wastaghfara lahumu arrasoolu lawajadoo Allaha tawwaban raheema

# 558

Fala warabbika la yuminoona hatta yuhakkimooka feema shajara baynahum thumma la yajidoo fee anfusihim harajan mimma qadayta wayusallimoo tasleema

# 559

Walaw anna katabna 'alayhim ani oqtuloo anfusakum awi okhrujoo min diyarikum ma fa'aloohu illa qaleelun minhum walaw annahum fa'aloo ma yoo'athoona bihi lakana khayran lahum waashadda tathbeeta

# 560

Waithan laataynahum min ladunna ajran 'atheema

# 561

Walahadaynahum siratan mustaqeema

# 562

Waman yuti'i Allaha warrasoola faolaika ma'a allatheena an'ama Allahu 'alayhim mina annabiyyeena wassiddeeqeena washshuhadai wassaliheena wahasuna olaika rafeeqa

# 563

Thalika alfadlu mina Allahi wakafa billahi 'aleema

# 564

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo khuthoo hithrakum fanfiroo thubatin awi infiroo jamee'a

# 565

Wainna minkum laman layubattianna fain asabatkum museebatun qala qad an'ama Allahu 'alayya ith lam akun ma'ahum shaheeda

# 566

Walain asabakum fadlun mina Allahi layaqoolanna kaan lam takun baynakum wabaynahu mawaddatun ya laytanee kuntu ma'ahum faafooza fawzan 'atheema

# 567

Falyuqatil fee sabeeli Allahi allatheena yashroona alhayata addunya bilakhirati waman yuqatil fee sabeeli Allahi fayuqtal aw yaghlib fasawfa nuteehi ajran 'atheema

# 568

Wama lakum la tuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi walmustad'afeena mina arrijali wannisai walwildani allatheena yaqooloona rabbana akhrijna min hathihi alqaryati aththalimi ahluha waj'al lana min ladunka waliyyan waj'al lana min ladunka naseera

# 569

Allatheena amanoo yuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi wallatheena kafaroo yuqatiloona fee sabeeli attaghooti faqatiloo awliyaa ashshaytani inna kayda ashshaytani kana da'eefa

# 570

Alam tara ila allatheena qeela lahum kuffoo aydiyakum waaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata falamma kutiba 'alayhimu alqitalu itha fareequn minhum yakhshawna annasa kakhashyati Allahi aw ashadda khashyatan waqaloo rabbana lima katabta 'alayna alqitala lawla akhkhartana ila ajalin qareebin qul mata'u addunya qaleelun walakhiratu khayrun limani ittaqa wala tuthlamoona fateela

# 571

Aynama takoonoo yudrikkumu almawtu walaw kuntum fee buroojin mushayyadatin wain tusibhum hasanatun yaqooloo hathihi min 'indi Allahi wain tusibhum sayyiatun yaqooloo hathihi min 'indika qul kullun min 'indi Allahi famali haolai alqawmi la yakadoona yafqahoona hadeetha

# 572

Ma asabaka min hasanatin famina Allahi wama asabaka min sayyiatin famin nafsika waarsalnaka linnasi rasoolan wakafa billahi shaheedan

# 573

Man yuti'i arrasoola faqad ata'a Allaha waman tawalla fama arsalnaka 'alayhim hafeetha

# 574

Wayaqooloona ta'atun faitha barazoo min 'indika bayyata taifatun minhum ghayra allathee taqoolu wallahu yaktubu ma yubayyitoona faa'rid 'anhum watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa billahi wakeela

# 575

Afala yatadabbaroona alqurana walaw kana min 'indi ghayri Allahi lawajadoo feehi ikhtilafan katheera

# 576

Waitha jaahum amrun mina alamni awi alkhawfi atha'oo bihi walaw raddoohu ila arrasooli waila olee alamri minhum la'alimahu allatheena yastanbitoonahu minhum walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu lattaba'tumu ashshaytana illa qaleela

# 577

Faqatil fee sabeeli Allahi la tukallafu illa nafsaka waharridi almumineena 'asa Allahu an yakuffa basa allatheena kafaroo wallahu ashaddu basan waashaddu tankeela

# 578

Man yashfa' shafa'atan hasanatan yakun lahu naseebun minha waman yashfa' shafa'atan sayyiatan yakun lahu kiflun minha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin muqeeta

# 579

Waitha huyyeetum bitahiyyatin fahayyoo biahsana minha aw ruddooha inna Allaha kana 'ala kulli shayin haseeba

# 580

Allahu la ilaha illa huwa layajma'annakum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi waman asdaqu mina Allahi hadeetha

# 581

Fama lakum fee almunafiqeena fiatayni wallahu arkasahum bima kasaboo atureedoona an tahdoo man adalla Allahu waman yudlili Allahu falan tajida lahu sabeela

# 582

Waddoo law takfuroona kama kafaroo fatakoonoona sawaan fala tattakhithoo minhum awliyaa hatta yuhajiroo fee sabeeli Allahi fain tawallaw fakhuthoohum waqtuloohum haythu wajadtumoohum wala tattakhithoo minhum waliyyan wala naseera

# 583

Illa allatheena yasiloona ila qawmin baynakum wabaynahum meethaqun aw jaookum hasirat sudooruhum an yuqatilookum aw yuqatiloo qawmahum walaw shaa Allahu lasallatahum 'alaykum falaqatalookum faini i'tazalookum falam yuqatilookum waalqaw ilaykumu assalama fama ja'ala Allahu lakum 'alayhim sabeela

# 584

Satajidoona akhareena yureedoona an yamanookum wayamanoo qawmahum kulla ma ruddoo ila alfitnati orkisoo feeha fain lam ya'tazilookum wayulqoo ilaykumu assalama wayakuffoo aydiyahum fakhuthoohum waqtuloohum haythu thaqiftumoohum waolaikum ja'alna lakum 'alayhim sultanan mubeena

# 585

Wama kana limuminin an yaqtula muminan illa khataan waman qatala muminan khataan fatahreeru raqabatin muminatin wadiyatun musallamatun ila ahlihi illa an yassaddaqoo fain kana min qawmin 'aduwwin lakum wahuwa muminun fatahreeru raqabatin muminatin wain kana min qawmin baynakum wabaynahum meethaqun fadiyatun musallamatun ila ahlihi watahreeru raqabatin muminatin faman lam yajid fasiyamu shahrayni mutatabi'ayni tawbatan mina Allahi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 586

Waman yaqtul muminan muta'ammidan fajazaohu jahannamu khalidan feeha waghadiba Allahu 'alayhi wala'anahu waa'adda lahu 'athaban 'atheema

# 587

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha darabtum fee sabeeli Allahi fatabayyanoo wala taqooloo liman alqa ilaykumu assalama lasta muminan tabtaghoona 'arada alhayati addunya fa'inda Allahi maghanimu katheeratun kathalika kuntum min qablu famanna Allahu 'alaykum fatabayyanoo inna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeera

# 588

La yastawee alqa'idoona mina almumineena ghayru olee addarari walmujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalihim waanfusihim faddala Allahu almujahideena biamwalihim waanfusihim 'ala alqa'ideena darajatan wakullan wa'ada Allahu alhusna wafaddala Allahu almujahideena 'ala alqa'ideena ajran 'atheema

# 589

Darajatin minhu wamaghfiratan warahmatan wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 590

Inna allatheena tawaffahumu almalaikatu thalimee anfusihim qaloo feema kuntum qaloo kunna mustad'afeena fee alardi qaloo alam takun ardu Allahi wasi'atan fatuhajiroo feeha faolaika mawahum jahannamu wasaat maseera

# 591

Illa almustad'afeena mina arrijali wannisai walwildani la yastatee'oona heelatan wala yahtadoona sabeela

# 592

Faolaika 'asa Allahu an ya'fuwa 'anhum wakana Allahu 'afuwwan ghafoora

# 593

Waman yuhajir fee sabeeli Allahi yajid fee alardi muraghaman katheeran wasa'atan waman yakhruj min baytihi muhajiran ila Allahi warasoolihi thumma yudrikhu almawtu faqad waqa'a ajruhu 'ala Allahi wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 594

Waitha darabtum fee alardi falaysa 'alaykum junahun an taqsuroo mina assalati in khiftum an yaftinakumu allatheena kafaroo inna alkafireena kanoo lakum 'aduwwan mubeena

# 595

Waitha kunta feehim faaqamta lahumu assalata faltaqum taifatun minhum ma'aka walyakhuthoo aslihatahum faitha sajadoo falyakoonoo min waraikum waltati taifatun okhra lam yusalloo falyusalloo ma'aka walyakhuthoo hithrahum waaslihatahum wadda allatheena kafaroo law taghfuloona 'an aslihatikum waamti'atikum fayameeloona 'alaykum maylatan wahidatan wala junaha 'alaykum in kana bikum athan min matarin aw kuntum marda an tada'oo aslihatakum wakhuthoo hithrakum inna Allaha a'adda lilkafireena 'athaban muheena

# 596

Faitha qadaytumu assalata fathkuroo Allaha qiyaman waqu'oodan wa'ala junoobikum faitha itmanantum faaqeemoo assalata inna assalata kanat 'ala almumineena kitaban mawqoota

# 597

Wala tahinoo fee ibtighai alqawmi in takoonoo talamoona fainnahum yalamoona kama talamoona watarjoona mina Allahi ma la yarjoona wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 598

Inna anzalna ilayka alkitaba bilhaqqi litahkuma bayna annasi bima araka Allahu wala takun lilkhaineena khaseema

# 599

Wastaghfiri Allaha inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheema

# 600

Wala tujadil 'ani allatheena yakhtanoona anfusahum inna Allaha la yuhibbu man kana khawwanan atheema

# 601

Yastakhfoona mina annasi wala yastakhfoona mina Allahi wahuwa ma'ahum ith yubayyitoona ma la yarda mina alqawli wakana Allahu bima ya'maloona muheeta

# 602

Haantum haolai jadaltum 'anhum fee alhayati addunya faman yujadilu Allaha 'anhum yawma alqiyamati am man yakoonu 'alayhim wakeela

# 603

Waman ya'mal sooan aw yathlim nafsahu thumma yastaghfiri Allaha yajidi Allaha ghafooran raheema

# 604

Waman yaksib ithman fainnama yaksibuhu 'ala nafsihi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 605

Waman yaksib khateeatan aw ithman thumma yarmi bihi bareean faqadi ihtamala buhtanan waithman mubeena

# 606

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alayka warahmatuhu lahammat taifatun minhum an yudillooka wama yudilloona illa anfusahum wama yadurroonaka min shayin waanzala Allahu 'alayka alkitaba walhikmata wa'allamaka ma lam takun ta'lamu wakana fadlu Allahi 'alayka 'atheema

# 607

La khayra fee katheerin min najwahum illa man amara bisadaqatin aw ma'roofin aw islahin bayna annasi waman yaf'al thalika ibtighaa mardati Allahi fasawfa nuteehi ajran 'atheema

# 608

Waman yushaqiqi arrasoola min ba'di ma tabayyana lahu alhuda wayattabi' ghayra sabeeli almumineena nuwallihi ma tawalla wanuslihi jahannama wasaat maseera

# 609

Inna Allaha la yaghfiru an yushraka bihi wayaghfiru ma doona thalika liman yashao waman yushrik billahi faqad dalla dalalan ba'eeda

# 610

In yad'oona min doonihi illa inathan wain yad'oona illa shaytanan mareeda

# 611

La'anahu Allahu waqala laattakhithanna min 'ibadika naseeban mafrooda

# 612

Walaodillannahum walaomanniyannahum walaamurannahum falayubattikunna athana alan'ami walaamurannahum falayughayyirunna khalqa Allahi waman yattakhithi ashshaytana waliyyan min dooni Allahi faqad khasira khusranan mubeena

# 613

Ya'iduhum wayumanneehim wama ya'iduhumu ashshaytanu illa ghuroora

# 614

Olaika mawahum jahannamu wala yajidoona 'anha maheesa

# 615

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati sanudkhiluhum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan wa'da Allahi haqqan waman asdaqu mina Allahi qeela

# 616

Laysa biamaniyyikum wala amaniyyi ahli alkitabi man ya'mal sooan yujza bihi wala yajid lahu min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseera

# 617

Waman ya'mal mina assalihati min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata wala yuthlamoona naqeera

# 618

Waman ahsanu deenan mimman aslama wajhahu lillahi wahuwa muhsinun wattaba'a millata ibraheema haneefan wattakhatha Allahu ibraheema khaleela

# 619

Walillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wakana Allahu bikulli shayin muheeta

# 620

Wayastaftoonaka fee annisai quli Allahu yufteekum feehinna wama yutla 'alaykum fee alkitabi fee yatama annisai allatee la tutoonahunna ma kutiba lahunna watarghaboona an tankihoohunna walmustad'afeena mina alwildani waan taqoomoo lilyatama bilqisti wama taf'aloo min khayrin fainna Allaha kana bihi 'aleema

# 621

Waini imraatun khafat min ba'liha nushoozan aw i'radan fala junaha 'alayhima an yusliha baynahuma sulhan wassulhu khayrun waohdirati alanfusu ashshuhha wain tuhsinoo watattaqoo fainna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeera

# 622

Walan tastatee'oo an ta'diloo bayna annisai walaw harastum fala tameeloo kulla almayli fatatharooha kalmu'allaqati wain tuslihoo watattaqoo fainna Allaha kana ghafooran raheema

# 623

Wain yatafarraqa yughni Allahu kullan min sa'atihi wakana Allahu wasi'an hakeema

# 624

Walillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi walaqad wassayna allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum waiyyakum ani ittaqoo Allaha wain takfuroo fainna lillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wakana Allahu ghaniyyan hameeda

# 625

Walillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wakafa billahi wakeela

# 626

In yasha yuthhibkum ayyuha annasu wayati biakhareena wakana Allahu 'ala thalika qadeera

# 627

Man kana yureedu thawaba addunya fa'inda Allahi thawabu addunya walakhirati wakana Allahu samee'an baseera

# 628

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo qawwameena bilqisti shuhadaa lillahi walaw 'ala anfusikum awi alwalidayni walaqrabeena in yakun ghaniyyan aw faqeeran fallahu awla bihima fala tattabi'oo alhawa an ta'diloo wain talwoo aw tu'ridoo fainna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeera

# 629

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo aminoo billahi warasoolihi walkitabi allathee nazzala 'ala rasoolihi walkitabi allathee anzala min qablu waman yakfur billahi wamalaikatihi wakutubihi warusulihi walyawmi alakhiri faqad dalla dalalan ba'eeda

# 630

Inna allatheena amanoo thumma kafaroo thumma amanoo thumma kafaroo thumma izdadoo kufran lam yakuni Allahu liyaghfira lahum wala liyahdiyahum sabeela

# 631

Bashshiri almunafiqeena bianna lahum 'athaban aleema

# 632

Allatheena yattakhithoona alkafireena awliyaa min dooni almumineena ayabtaghoona 'indahumu al'izzata fainna al'izzata lillahi jamee'a

# 633

Waqad nazzala 'alaykum fee alkitabi an itha sami'tum ayati Allahi yukfaru biha wayustahzao biha fala taq'udoo ma'ahum hatta yakhoodoo fee hadeethin ghayrihi innakum ithan mithluhum inna Allaha jami'u almunafiqeena walkafireena fee jahannama jamee'a

# 634

Allatheena yatarabbasoona bikum fain kana lakum fathun mina Allahi qaloo alam nakun ma'akum wain kana lilkafireena naseebun qaloo alam nastahwith 'alaykum wanamna'kum mina almumineena fallahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati walan yaj'ala Allahu lilkafireena 'ala almumineena sabeela

# 635

Inna almunafiqeena yukhadi'oona Allaha wahuwa khadi'uhum waitha qamoo ila assalati qamoo kusala yuraoona annasa wala yathkuroona Allaha illa qaleela

# 636

Muthabthabeena bayna thalika la ila haolai wala ila haolai waman yudlili Allahu falan tajida lahu sabeela

# 637

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo alkafireena awliyaa min dooni almumineena atureedoona an taj'aloo lillahi 'alaykum sultanan mubeena

# 638

Inna almunafiqeena fee addarki alasfali mina annari walan tajida lahum naseera

# 639

Illa allatheena taboo waaslahoo wa'tasamoo billahi waakhlasoo deenahum lillahi faolaika ma'a almumineena wasawfa yuti Allahu almumineena ajran 'atheema

# 640

Ma yaf'alu Allahu bi'athabikum in shakartum waamantum wakana Allahu shakiran 'aleema

# 641

La yuhibbu Allahu aljahra bissooi mina alqawli illa man thulima wakana Allahu samee'an 'aleema

# 642

In tubdoo khayran aw tukhfoohu aw ta'foo 'an sooin fainna Allaha kana 'afuwwan qadeera

# 643

Inna allatheena yakfuroona billahi warusulihi wayureedoona an yufarriqoo bayna Allahi warusulihi wayaqooloona numinu biba'din wanakfuru biba'din wayureedoona an yattakhithoo bayna thalika sabeela

# 644

Olaika humu alkafiroona haqqan waa'tadna lilkafireena 'athaban muheena

# 645

Wallatheena amanoo billahi warusulihi walam yufarriqoo bayna ahadin minhum olaika sawfa yuteehim ojoorahum wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 646

Yasaluka ahlu alkitabi an tunazzila 'alayhim kitaban mina assamai faqad saaloo moosa akbara min thalika faqaloo arina Allaha jahratan faakhathathumu assa'iqatu bithulmihim thumma ittakhathoo al'ijla min ba'di ma jaathumu albayyinatu fa'afawna 'an thalika waatayna moosa sultanan mubeena

# 647

Warafa'na fawqahumu attoora bimeethaqihim waqulna lahumu odkhuloo albaba sujjadan waqulna lahum la ta'doo fee assabti waakhathna minhum meethaqan ghaleetha

# 648

Fabima naqdihim meethaqahum wakufrihim biayati Allahi waqatlihimu alanbiyaa bighayri haqqin waqawlihim quloobuna ghulfun bal taba'a Allahu 'alayha bikufrihim fala yuminoona illa qaleela

# 649

Wabikufrihim waqawlihim 'ala maryama buhtanan 'atheema

# 650

Waqawlihim inna qatalna almaseeha 'eesa ibna maryama rasoola Allahi wama qataloohu wama salaboohu walakin shubbiha lahum wainna allatheena ikhtalafoo feehi lafee shakkin minhu ma lahum bihi min 'ilmin illa ittiba'a aththanni wama qataloohu yaqeena

# 651

Bal rafa'ahu Allahu ilayhi wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema

# 652

Wain min ahli alkitabi illa layuminanna bihi qabla mawtihi wayawma alqiyamati yakoonu 'alayhim shaheeda

# 653

Fabithulmin mina allatheena hadoo harramna 'alayhim tayyibatin ohillat lahum wabisaddihim 'an sabeeli Allahi katheera

# 654

Waakhthihimu arriba waqad nuhoo 'anhu waaklihim amwala annasi bilbatili waa'tadna lilkafireena minhum 'athaban aleema

# 655

Lakini arrasikhoona fee al'ilmi minhum walmuminoona yuminoona bima onzila ilayka wama onzila min qablika walmuqeemeena assalata walmutoona azzakata walmuminoona billahi walyawmi alakhiri olaika sanuteehim ajran 'atheema

# 656

Inna awhayna ilayka kama awhayna ila noohin wannabiyyeena min ba'dihi waawhayna ila ibraheema waisma'eela waishaqa waya'qooba walasbati wa'eesa waayyooba wayoonusa waharoona wasulaymana waatayna dawooda zaboora

# 657

Warusulan qad qasasnahum 'alayka min qablu warusulan lam naqsushum 'alayka wakallama Allahu moosa takleema

# 658

Rusulan mubashshireena wamunthireena lialla yakoona linnasi 'ala Allahi hujjatun ba'da arrusuli wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema

# 659

Lakini Allahu yashhadu bima anzala ilayka anzalahu bi'ilmihi walmalaikatu yashhadoona wakafa billahi shaheeda

# 660

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi qad dalloo dalalan ba'eeda

# 661

Inna allatheena kafaroo wathalamoo lam yakuni Allahu liyaghfira lahum wala liyahdiyahum tareeqa

# 662

Illa tareeqa jahannama khalideena feeha abadan wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera

# 663

Ya ayyuha annasu qad jaakumu arrasoolu bilhaqqi min rabbikum faaminoo khayran lakum wain takfuroo fainna lillahi ma fee assamawati walardi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 664

Ya ahla alkitabi la taghloo fee deenikum wala taqooloo 'ala Allahi illa alhaqqa innama almaseehu 'eesa ibnu maryama rasoolu Allahi wakalimatuhu alqaha ila maryama waroohun minhu faaminoo billahi warusulihi wala taqooloo thalathatun intahoo khayran lakum innama Allahu ilahun wahidun subhanahu an yakoona lahu waladun lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wakafa billahi wakeela

# 665

Lan yastankifa almaseehu an yakoona 'abdan lillahi wala almalaikatu almuqarraboona waman yastankif 'an 'ibadatihi wayastakbir fasayahshuruhum ilayhi jamee'a

# 666

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fayuwaffeehim ojoorahum wayazeeduhum min fadlihi waamma allatheena istankafoo wastakbaroo fayu'aththibuhum 'athaban aleeman wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseera

# 667

Ya ayyuha annasu qad jaakum burhanun min rabbikum waanzalna ilaykum nooran mubeena

# 668

Faamma allatheena amanoo billahi wa'tasamoo bihi fasayudkhiluhum fee rahmatin minhu wafadlin wayahdeehim ilayhi siratan mustaqeema

# 669

Yastaftoonaka quli Allahu yufteekum fee alkalalati ini imruon halaka laysa lahu waladun walahu okhtun falaha nisfu ma taraka wahuwa yarithuha in lam yakun laha waladun fain kanata ithnatayni falahuma aththuluthani mimma taraka wain kanoo ikhwatan rijalan wanisaan faliththakari mithlu haththi alonthayayni yubayyinu Allahu lakum an tadilloo wallahu bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 670

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo awfoo bil'uqoodi ohillat lakum baheematu alan'ami illa ma yutla 'alaykum ghayra muhillee assaydi waantum hurumun inna Allaha yahkumu ma yureed

# 671

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuhilloo sha'aira Allahi wala ashshahra alharama wala alhadya wala alqalaida wala ammeena albayta alharama yabtaghoona fadlan min rabbihim waridwanan waitha halaltum fastadoo wala yajrimannakum shanaanu qawmin an saddookum 'ani almasjidi alharami an ta'tadoo wata'awanoo 'ala albirri wattaqwa wala ta'awanoo 'ala alithmi wal'udwani wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha shadeedu al'iqab

# 672

Hurrimat 'alaykumu almaytatu waddamu walahmu alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi walmunkhaniqatu walmawqoothatu walmutaraddiyatu wannateehatu wama akala assabu'u illa ma thakkaytum wama thubiha 'ala annusubi waan tastaqsimoo bilazlami thalikum fisqun alyawma yaisa allatheena kafaroo min deenikum fala takhshawhum wakhshawni alyawma akmaltu lakum deenakum waatmamtu 'alaykum ni'matee waradeetu lakumu alislama deenan famani idturra fee makhmasatin ghayra mutajanifin liithmin fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 673

Yasaloonaka matha ohilla lahum qul ohilla lakumu attayyibatu wama 'allamtum mina aljawarihi mukallibeena tu'allimoonahunna mimma 'allamakumu Allahu fakuloo mimma amsakna 'alaykum wathkuroo isma Allahi 'alayhi wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha saree'u alhisab

# 674

Alyawma ohilla lakumu attayyibatu wata'amu allatheena ootoo alkitaba hillun lakum wata'amukum hillun lahum walmuhsanatu mina almuminati walmuhsanatu mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum itha ataytumoohunna ojoorahunna muhsineena ghayra musafiheena wala muttakhithee akhdanin waman yakfur bileemani faqad habita 'amaluhu wahuwa fee alakhirati mina alkhasireen

# 675

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha qumtum ila assalati faghsiloo wujoohakum waaydiyakum ila almarafiqi wamsahoo biruoosikum waarjulakum ila alka'bayni wain kuntum junuban fattahharoo wain kuntum marda aw 'ala safarin aw jaa ahadun minkum mina alghaiti aw lamastumu annisaa falam tajidoo maan fatayammamoo sa'eedan tayyiban famsahoo biwujoohikum waaydeekum minhu ma yureedu Allahu liyaj'ala 'alaykum min harajin walakin yureedu liyutahhirakum waliyutimma ni'matahu 'alaykum la'allakum tashkuroon

# 676

Wathkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum wameethaqahu allathee wathaqakum bihi ith qultum sami'na waata'na wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 677

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo qawwameena lillahi shuhadaa bilqisti wala yajrimannakum shanaanu qawmin 'ala alla ta'diloo i'diloo huwa aqrabu littaqwa wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloon

# 678

Wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun 'atheem

# 679

Wallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheem

# 680

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith hamma qawmun an yabsutoo ilaykum aydiyahum fakaffa aydiyahum 'ankum wattaqoo Allaha wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon

# 681

Walaqad akhatha Allahu meethaqa banee israeela waba'athna minhumu ithnay 'ashara naqeeban waqala Allahu innee ma'akum lain aqamtumu assalata waataytumu azzakata waamantum birusulee wa'azzartumoohum waaqradtumu Allaha qardan hasanan laokaffiranna 'ankum sayyiatikum walaodkhilannakum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu faman kafara ba'da thalika minkum faqad dalla sawaa assabeel

# 682

Fabima naqdihim meethaqahum la'annahum waja'alna quloobahum qasiyatan yuharrifoona alkalima 'an mawadi'ihi wanasoo haththan mimma thukkiroo bihi wala tazalu tattali'u 'ala khainatin minhum illa qaleelan minhum fa'fu 'anhum wasfah inna Allaha yuhibbu almuhsineen

# 683

Wamina allatheena qaloo inna nasara akhathna meethaqahum fanasoo haththan mimma thukkiroo bihi faaghrayna baynahumu al'adawata walbaghdaa ila yawmi alqiyamati wasawfa yunabbiohumu Allahu bima kanoo yasna'oon

# 684

Ya ahla alkitabi qad jaakum rasooluna yubayyinu lakum katheeran mimma kuntum tukhfoona mina alkitabi waya'foo 'an katheerin qad jaakum mina Allahi noorun wakitabun mubeen

# 685

Yahdee bihi Allahu mani ittaba'a ridwanahu subula assalami wayukhrijuhum mina aththulumati ila annoori biithnihi wayahdeehim ila siratin mustaqeem

# 686

Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha huwa almaseehu ibnu maryama qul faman yamliku mina Allahi shayan in arada an yuhlika almaseeha ibna maryama waommahu waman fee alardi jamee'an walillahi mulku assamawati walardi wama baynahuma yakhluqu ma yashao wallahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 687

Waqalati alyahoodu wannasara nahnu abnao Allahi waahibbaohu qul falima yu'aththibukum bithunoobikum bal antum basharun mimman khalaqa yaghfiru liman yashao wayu'aththibu man yashao walillahi mulku assamawati walardi wama baynahuma wailayhi almaseer

# 688

Ya ahla alkitabi qad jaakum rasooluna yubayyinu lakum 'ala fatratin mina arrusuli an taqooloo ma jaana min basheerin wala natheerin faqad jaakum basheerun wanatheerun wallahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 689

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith ja'ala feekum anbiyaa waja'alakum mulookan waatakum ma lam yuti ahadan mina al'alameen

# 690

Ya qawmi odkhuloo alarda almuqaddasata allatee kataba Allahu lakum wala tartaddoo 'ala adbarikum fatanqaliboo khasireen

# 691

Qaloo ya moosa inna feeha qawman jabbareena wainna lan nadkhulaha hatta yakhrujoo minha fain yakhrujoo minha fainna dakhiloon

# 692

Qala rajulani mina allatheena yakhafoona an'ama Allahu 'alayhima odkhuloo 'alayhimu albaba faitha dakhaltumoohu fainnakum ghaliboona wa'ala Allahi fatawakkaloo in kuntum mumineen

# 693

Qaloo ya moosa inna lan nadkhulaha abadan ma damoo feeha faithhab anta warabbuka faqatila inna hahuna qa'idoon

# 694

Qala rabbi innee la amliku illa nafsee waakhee fafruq baynana wabayna alqawmi alfasiqeen

# 695

Qala fainnaha muharramatun 'alayhim arba'eena sanatan yateehoona fee alardi fala tasa 'ala alqawmi alfasiqeen

# 696

Watlu 'alayhim nabaa ibnay adama bilhaqqi ith qarraba qurbanan fatuqubbila min ahadihima walam yutaqabbal mina alakhari qala laaqtulannaka qala innama yataqabbalu Allahu mina almuttaqeen

# 697

Lain basatta ilayya yadaka litaqtulanee ma ana bibasitin yadiya ilayka liaqtulaka innee akhafu Allaha rabba al'alameen

# 698

Innee oreedu an tabooa biithmee waithmika fatakoona min ashabi annari wathalika jazao aththalimeen

# 699

Fatawwa'at lahu nafsuhu qatla akheehi faqatalahu faasbaha mina alkhasireen

# 700

Faba'atha Allahu ghuraban yabhathu fee alardi liyuriyahu kayfa yuwaree sawata akheehi qala ya waylata a'ajaztu an akoona mithla hatha alghurabi faowariya sawata akhee faasbaha mina annadimeen

# 701

Min ajli thalika katabna 'ala banee israeela annahu man qatala nafsan bighayri nafsin aw fasadin fee alardi fakaannama qatala annasa jamee'an waman ahyaha fakaannama ahya annasa jamee'an walaqad jaa thum rusuluna bilbayyinati thumma inna katheeran minhum ba'da thalika fee alardi lamusrifoon

# 702

Innama jazao allatheena yuhariboona Allaha warasoolahu wayas'awna fee alardi fasadan an yuqattaloo aw yusallaboo aw tuqatta'a aydeehim waarjuluhum min khilafin aw yunfaw mina alardi thalika lahum khizyun fee addunya walahum fee alakhirati 'athabun 'atheem

# 703

Illa allatheena taboo min qabli an taqdiroo 'alayhim fa'lamoo anna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 704

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha wabtaghoo ilayhi alwaseelata wajahidoo fee sabeelihi la'allakum tuflihoon

# 705

Inna allatheena kafaroo law anna lahum ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu liyaftadoo bihi min 'athabi yawmi alqiyamati ma tuqubbila minhum walahum 'athabun aleem

# 706

Yureedoona an yakhrujoo mina annari wama hum bikharijeena minha walahum 'athabun muqeem

# 707

Wassariqu wassariqatu faqta'oo aydiyahuma jazaan bima kasaba nakalan mina Allahi wallahu 'azeezun hakeem

# 708

Faman taba min ba'di thulmihi waaslaha fainna Allaha yatoobu 'alayhi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 709

Alam ta'lam anna Allaha lahu mulku assamawati walardi yu'aththibu man yashao wayaghfiru liman yashao wallahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 710

Ya ayyuha arrasoolu la yahzunka allatheena yusari'oona fee alkufri mina allatheena qaloo amanna biafwahihim walam tumin quloobuhum wamina allatheena hadoo samma'oona lilkathibi samma'oona liqawmin akhareena lam yatooka yuharrifoona alkalima min ba'di mawadi'ihi yaqooloona in ooteetum hatha fakhuthoohu wain lam tutawhu fahtharoo waman yuridi Allahu fitnatahu falan tamlika lahu mina Allahi shayan olaika allatheena lam yuridi Allahu an yutahhira quloobahum lahum fee addunya khizyun walahum fee alakhirati 'athabun 'atheem

# 711

Samma'oona lilkathibi akkaloona lissuhti fain jaooka fahkum baynahum aw a'rid 'anhum wain tu'rid 'anhum falan yadurrooka shayan wain hakamta fahkum baynahum bilqisti inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteen

# 712

Wakayfa yuhakkimoonaka wa'indahumu attawratu feeha hukmu Allahi thumma yatawallawna min ba'di thalika wama olaika bilmumineen

# 713

Inna anzalna attawrata feeha hudan wanoorun yahkumu biha annabiyyoona allatheena aslamoo lillatheena hadoo warrabbaniyyoona walahbaru bima istuhfithoo min kitabi Allahi wakanoo 'alayhi shuhadaa fala takhshawoo annasa wakhshawni wala tashtaroo biayatee thamanan qaleelan waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu alkafiroon

# 714

Wakatabna 'alayhim feeha anna annafsa binnafsi wal'ayna bil'ayni walanfa bilanfi walothuna bilothuni wassinna bissinni waljurooha qisasun faman tasaddaqa bihi fahuwa kaffaratun lahu waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu aththalimoon

# 715

Waqaffayna 'ala atharihim bi'eesa ibni maryama musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina attawrati waataynahu alinjeela feehi hudan wanoorun wamusaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina attawrati wahudan wamaw'ithatan lilmuttaqeen

# 716

Walyahkum ahlu alinjeeli bima anzala Allahu feehi waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu alfasiqoon

# 717

Waanzalna ilayka alkitaba bilhaqqi musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina alkitabi wamuhayminan 'alayhi fahkum baynahum bima anzala Allahu wala tattabi' ahwaahum 'amma jaaka mina alhaqqi likullin ja'alna minkum shir'atan waminhajan walaw shaa Allahu laja'alakum ommatan wahidatan walakin liyabluwakum fee ma atakum fastabiqoo alkhayrati ila Allahi marji'ukum jamee'an fayunabbiokum bima kuntum feehi takhtalifoon

# 718

Waani ohkum baynahum bima anzala Allahu wala tattabi' ahwaahum wahtharhum an yaftinooka 'an ba'di ma anzala Allahu ilayka fain tawallaw fa'lam annama yureedu Allahu an yuseebahum biba'di thunoobihim wainna katheeran mina annasi lafasiqoon

# 719

Afahukma aljahiliyyati yabghoona waman ahsanu mina Allahu hukman liqawmin yooqinoon

# 720

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo alyahooda wannasara awliyaa ba'duhum awliyao ba'din waman yatawallahum minkum fainnahu minhum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 721

Fatara allatheena fee quloobihim maradun yusari'oona feehim yaqooloona nakhsha an tuseebana dairatun fa'asa Allahu an yatiya bilfathi aw amrin min 'indihi fayusbihoo 'ala ma asarroo fee anfusihim nadimeen

# 722

Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo ahaolai allatheena aqsamoo billahi jahda aymanihim innahum lama'akum habitat a'maluhum faasbahoo khasireen

# 723

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo man yartadda minkum 'an deenihi fasawfa yatee Allahu biqawmin yuhibbuhum wayuhibboonahu athillatin 'ala almumineena a'izzatin 'ala alkafireena yujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi wala yakhafoona lawmata laimin thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao wallahu wasi'un 'aleem

# 724

Innama waliyyukumu Allahu warasooluhu wallatheena amanoo allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wahum raki'oon

# 725

Waman yatawalla Allaha warasoolahu wallatheena amanoo fainna hizba Allahi humu alghaliboon

# 726

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo allatheena ittakhathoo deenakum huzuwan wala'iban mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum walkuffara awliyaa wattaqoo Allaha in kuntum mumineen

# 727

Waitha nadaytum ila assalati ittakhathooha huzuwan wala'iban thalika biannahum qawmun la ya'qiloon

# 728

Qul ya ahla alkitabi hal tanqimoona minna illa an amanna billahi wama onzila ilayna wama onzila min qablu waanna aktharakum fasiqoon

# 729

Qul hal onabbiokum bisharrin min thalika mathoobatan 'inda Allahi man la'anahu Allahu waghadiba 'alayhi waja'ala minhumu alqiradata walkhanazeera wa'abada attaghooti olaika sharrun makanan waadallu 'an sawai assabeel

# 730

Waitha jaookum qaloo amanna waqad dakhaloo bilkufri wahum qad kharajoo bihi wallahu a'lamu bima kanoo yaktumoon

# 731

Watara katheeran minhum yusari'oona fee alithmi wal'udwani waaklihimu assuhta labisa ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 732

Lawla yanhahumu arrabbaniyyoona walahbaru 'an qawlihimu alithma waaklihimu assuhta labisa ma kanoo yasna'oon

# 733

Waqalati alyahoodu yadu Allahi maghloolatun ghullat aydeehim walu'inoo bima qaloo bal yadahu mabsootatani yunfiqu kayfa yashao walayazeedanna katheeran minhum ma onzila ilayka min rabbika tughyanan wakufran waalqayna baynahumu al'adawata walbaghdaa ila yawmi alqiyamati kullama awqadoo naran lilharbi atfaaha Allahu wayas'awna fee alardi fasadan wallahu la yuhibbu almufsideen

# 734

Walaw anna ahla alkitabi amanoo wattaqaw lakaffarna 'anhum sayyiatihim walaadkhalnahum jannati anna'eem

# 735

Walaw annahum aqamoo attawrata walinjeela wama onzila ilayhim min rabbihim laakaloo min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim minhum ommatun muqtasidatun wakatheerun minhum saa ma ya'maloon

# 736

Ya ayyuha arrasoolu balligh ma onzila ilayka min rabbika wain lam taf'al fama ballaghta risalatahu wallahu ya'simuka mina annasi inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireen

# 737

Qul ya ahla alkitabi lastum 'ala shayin hatta tuqeemoo attawrata walinjeela wama onzila ilaykum min rabbikum walayazeedanna katheeran minhum ma onzila ilayka min rabbika tughyanan wakufran fala tasa 'ala alqawmi alkafireen

# 738

Inna allatheena amanoo wallatheena hadoo wassabioona wannasara man amana billahi walyawmi alakhiri wa'amila salihan fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon

# 739

Laqad akhathna meethaqa banee israeela waarsalna ilayhim rusulan kullama jaahum rasoolun bima la tahwa anfusuhum fareeqan kaththaboo wafareeqan yaqtuloon

# 740

Wahasiboo alla takoona fitnatun fa'amoo wasammoo thumma taba Allahu 'alayhim thumma 'amoo wasammoo katheerun minhum wallahu baseerun bima ya'maloon

# 741

Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha huwa almaseehu ibnu maryama waqala almaseehu ya banee israeela o'budoo Allaha rabbee warabbakum innahu man yushrik billahi faqad harrama Allahu 'alayhi aljannata wamawahu annaru wama liththalimeena min ansar

# 742

Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha thalithu thalathatin wama min ilahin illa ilahun wahidun wain lam yantahoo 'amma yaqooloona layamassanna allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athabun aleem

# 743

Afala yatooboona ila Allahi wayastaghfiroonahu wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 744

Ma almaseehu ibnu maryama illa rasoolun qad khalat min qablihi arrusulu waommuhu siddeeqatun kana yakulani atta'ama onthur kayfa nubayyinu lahumu alayati thumma onthur anna yufakoon

# 745

Qul ata'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lakum darran wala naf'an wallahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 746

Qul ya ahla alkitabi la taghloo fee deenikum ghayra alhaqqi wala tattabi'oo ahwaa qawmin qad dalloo min qablu waadalloo katheeran wadalloo 'an sawai assabeel

# 747

Lu'ina allatheena kafaroo min banee israeela 'ala lisani dawooda wa'eesa ibni maryama thalika bima 'asaw wakanoo ya'tadoon

# 748

Kanoo la yatanahawna 'an munkarin fa'aloohu labisa ma kanoo yaf'aloon

# 749

Tara katheeran minhum yatawallawna allatheena kafaroo labisa ma qaddamat lahum anfusuhum an sakhita Allahu 'alayhim wafee al'athabi hum khalidoon

# 750

Walaw kanoo yuminoona billahi wannabiyyi wama onzila ilayhi ma ittakhathoohum awliyaa walakinna katheeran minhum fasiqoon

# 751

Latajidanna ashadda annasi 'adawatan lillatheena amanoo alyahooda wallatheena ashrakoo walatajidanna aqrabahum mawaddatan lillatheena amanoo allatheena qaloo inna nasara thalika bianna minhum qisseeseena waruhbanan waannahum la yastakbiroon

# 752

Waitha sami'oo ma onzila ila arrasooli tara a'yunahum tafeedu mina addam'i mimma 'arafoo mina alhaqqi yaqooloona rabbana amanna faktubna ma'a ashshahideen

# 753

Wama lana la numinu billahi wama jaana mina alhaqqi wanatma'u an yudkhilana rabbuna ma'a alqawmi assaliheen

# 754

Faathabahumu Allahu bima qaloo jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wathalika jazao almuhsineen

# 755

Wallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheem

# 756

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuharrimoo tayyibati ma ahalla Allahu lakum wala ta'tadoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu almu'tadeen

# 757

Wakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban wattaqoo Allaha allathee antum bihi muminoon

# 758

La yuakhithukumu Allahu billaghwi fee aymanikum walakin yuakhithukum bima 'aqqadtumu alaymana fakaffaratuhu it'amu 'asharati masakeena min awsati ma tut'imoona ahleekum aw kiswatuhum aw tahreeru raqabatin faman lam yajid fasiyamu thalathati ayyamin thalika kaffaratu aymanikum itha halaftum wahfathoo aymanakum kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi la'allakum tashkuroon

# 759

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo innama alkhamru walmaysiru walansabu walazlamu rijsun min 'amali ashshaytani fajtaniboohu la'allakum tuflihoon

# 760

Innama yureedu ashshaytanu an yooqi'a baynakumu al'adawata walbaghdaa fee alkhamri walmaysiri wayasuddakum 'an thikri Allahi wa'ani assalati fahal antum muntahoon

# 761

Waatee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola wahtharoo fain tawallaytum fa'lamoo annama 'ala rasoolina albalaghu almubeen

# 762

Laysa 'ala allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati junahun feema ta'imoo itha ma ittaqaw waamanoo wa'amiloo assalihati thumma ittaqaw waamanoo thumma ittaqaw waahsanoo wallahu yuhibbu almuhsineen

# 763

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo layabluwannakumu Allahu bishayin mina assaydi tanaluhu aydeekum warimahukum liya'lama Allahu man yakhafuhu bilghaybi famani i'tada ba'da thalika falahu 'athabun aleem

# 764

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la taqtuloo assayda waantum hurumun waman qatalahu minkum muta'ammidan fajazaon mithlu ma qatala mina anna'ami yahkumu bihi thawa 'adlin minkum hadyan baligha alka'bati aw kaffaratun ta'amu masakeena aw 'adlu thalika siyaman liyathooqa wabala amrihi 'afa Allahu 'amma salafa waman 'ada fayantaqimu Allahu minhu wallahu 'azeezun thoo intiqam

# 765

Ohilla lakum saydu albahri wata'amuhu mata'an lakum walissayyarati wahurrima 'alaykum saydu albarri ma dumtum huruman wattaqoo Allaha allathee ilayhi tuhsharoon

# 766

Ja'ala Allahu alka'bata albayta alharama qiyaman linnasi washshahra alharama walhadya walqalaida thalika lita'lamoo anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi waanna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 767

I'lamoo anna Allaha shadeedu al'iqabi waanna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 768

Ma 'ala arrasooli illa albalaghu wallahu ya'lamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoon

# 769

Qul la yastawee alkhabeethu wattayyibu walaw a'jabaka kathratu alkhabeethi fattaqoo Allaha ya olee alalbabi la'allakum tuflihoon

# 770

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tasaloo 'an ashyaa in tubda lakum tasukum wain tasaloo 'anha heena yunazzalu alquranu tubda lakum 'afa Allahu 'anha wallahu ghafoorun haleem

# 771

Qad saalaha qawmun min qablikum thumma asbahoo biha kafireen

# 772

Ma ja'ala Allahu min baheeratin wala saibatin wala waseelatin wala hamin walakinna allatheena kafaroo yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba waaktharuhum la ya'qiloon

# 773

Waitha qeela lahum ta'alaw ila ma anzala Allahu waila arrasooli qaloo hasbuna ma wajadna 'alayhi abaana awalaw kana abaohum la ya'lamoona shayan wala yahtadoon

# 774

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo 'alaykum anfusakum la yadurrukum man dalla itha ihtadaytum ila Allahi marji'ukum jamee'an fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 775

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo shahadatu baynikum itha hadara ahadakumu almawtu heena alwasiyyati ithnani thawa 'adlin minkum aw akharani min ghayrikum in antum darabtum fee alardi faasabatkum museebatu almawti tahbisoonahuma min ba'di assalati fayuqsimani billahi ini irtabtum la nashtaree bihi thamanan walaw kana tha qurba wala naktumu shahadata Allahi inna ithan lamina alathimeen

# 776

Fain 'uthira 'ala annahuma istahaqqa ithman faakharani yaqoomani maqamahuma mina allatheena istahaqqa 'alayhimu alawlayani fayuqsimani billahi lashahadatuna ahaqqu min shahadatihima wama i'tadayna inna ithan lamina aththalimeen

# 777

Thalika adna an yatoo bishshahadati 'ala wajhiha aw yakhafoo an turadda aymanun ba'da aymanihim wattaqoo Allaha wasma'oo wallahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeen

# 778

Yawma yajma'u Allahu arrusula fayaqoolu matha ojibtum qaloo la 'ilma lana innaka anta 'allamu alghuyoob

# 779

Ith qala Allahu ya 'eesa ibna maryama othkur ni'matee 'alayka wa'ala walidatika ith ayyadtuka biroohi alqudusi tukallimu annasa fee almahdi wakahlan waith 'allamtuka alkitaba walhikmata wattawrata walinjeela waith takhluqu mina atteeni kahayati attayri biithnee fatanfukhu feeha fatakoonu tayran biithnee watubrio alakmaha walabrasa biithnee waith tukhriju almawta biithnee waith kafaftu banee israeela 'anka ith jitahum bilbayyinati faqala allatheena kafaroo minhum in hatha illa sihrun mubeen

# 780

Waith awhaytu ila alhawariyyeena an aminoo bee wabirasoolee qaloo amanna washhad biannana muslimoon

# 781

Ith qala alhawariyyoona ya 'eesa ibna maryama hal yastatee'u rabbuka an yunazzila 'alayna maidatan mina assamai qala ittaqoo Allaha in kuntum mumineen

# 782

Qaloo nureedu an nakula minha watatmainna quloobuna wana'lama an qad sadaqtana wanakoona 'alayha mina ashshahideen

# 783

Qala 'eesa ibnu maryama allahumma rabbana anzil 'alayna maidatan mina assamai takoonu lana 'eedan liawwalina waakhirina waayatan minka warzuqna waanta khayru arraziqeen

# 784

Qala Allahu innee munazziluha 'alaykum faman yakfur ba'du minkum fainnee o'aththibuhu 'athaban la o'aththibuhu ahadan mina al'alameen

# 785

Waith qala Allahu ya 'eesa ibna maryama aanta qulta linnasi ittakhithoonee waommiya ilahayni min dooni Allahi qala subhanaka ma yakoonu lee an aqoola ma laysa lee bihaqqin in kuntu qultuhu faqad 'alimtahu ta'lamu ma fee nafsee wala a'lamu ma fee nafsika innaka anta 'allamu alghuyoob

# 786

Ma qultu lahum illa ma amartanee bihi ani o'budoo Allaha rabbee warabbakum wakuntu 'alayhim shaheedan ma dumtu feehim falamma tawaffaytanee kunta anta arraqeeba 'alayhim waanta 'ala kulli shayin shaheed

# 787

In tu'aththibhum fainnahum 'ibaduka wain taghfir lahum fainnaka anta al'azeezu alhakeem

# 788

Qala Allahu hatha yawmu yanfa'u assadiqeena sidquhum lahum jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan radiya Allahu 'anhum waradoo 'anhu thalika alfawzu al'atheem

# 789

Lillahi mulku assamawati walardi wama feehinna wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 790

Alhamdu lillahi allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda waja'ala aththulumati wannoora thumma allatheena kafaroo birabbihim ya'diloon

# 791

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min teenin thumma qada ajalan waajalun musamman 'indahu thumma antum tamtaroon

# 792

Wahuwa Allahu fee assamawati wafee alardi ya'lamu sirrakum wajahrakum waya'lamu ma taksiboon

# 793

Wama tateehim min ayatin min ayati rabbihim illa kanoo 'anha mu'rideen

# 794

Faqad kaththaboo bilhaqqi lamma jaahum fasawfa yateehim anbao ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 795

Alam yaraw kam ahlakna min qablihim min qarnin makkannahum fee alardi ma lam numakkin lakum waarsalna assamaa 'alayhim midraran waja'alna alanhara tajree min tahtihim faahlaknahum bithunoobihim waanshana min ba'dihim qarnan akhareen

# 796

Walaw nazzalna 'alayka kitaban fee qirtasin falamasoohu biaydeehim laqala allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeen

# 797

Waqaloo lawla onzila 'alayhi malakun walaw anzalna malakan laqudiya alamru thumma la yuntharoon

# 798

Walaw ja'alnahu malakan laja'alnahu rajulan walalabasna 'alayhim ma yalbisoon

# 799

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa billatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 800

Qul seeroo fee alardi thumma onthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeen

# 801

Qul liman ma fee assamawati walardi qul lillahi kataba 'ala nafsihi arrahmata layajma'annakum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi allatheena khasiroo anfusahum fahum la yuminoon

# 802

Walahu ma sakana fee allayli wannahari wahuwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 803

Qul aghayra Allahi attakhithu waliyyan fatiri assamawati walardi wahuwa yut'imu wala yut'amu qul innee omirtu an akoona awwala man aslama wala takoonanna mina almushrikeen

# 804

Qul innee akhafu in 'asaytu rabbee 'athaba yawmin 'atheem

# 805

Man yusraf 'anhu yawmaithin faqad rahimahu wathalika alfawzu almubeen

# 806

Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yamsaska bikhayrin fahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 807

Wahuwa alqahiru fawqa 'ibadihi wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeer

# 808

Qul ayyu shayin akbaru shahadatan quli Allahu shaheedun baynee wabaynakum waoohiya ilayya hatha alquranu lionthirakum bihi waman balagha ainnakum latashhadoona anna ma'a Allahi alihatan okhra qul la ashhadu qul innama huwa ilahun wahidun wainnanee bareeon mimma tushrikoon

# 809

Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba ya'rifoonahu kama ya'rifoona abnaahum allatheena khasiroo anfusahum fahum la yuminoon

# 810

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu aththalimoon

# 811

Wayawma nahshuruhum jamee'an thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo ayna shurakaokumu allatheena kuntum taz'umoon

# 812

Thumma lam takun fitnatuhum illa an qaloo wallahi rabbina ma kunna mushrikeen

# 813

Onthur kayfa kathaboo 'ala anfusihim wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 814

Waminhum man yastami'u ilayka waja'alna 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain yaraw kulla ayatin la yuminoo biha hatta itha jaooka yujadiloonaka yaqoolu allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen

# 815

Wahum yanhawna 'anhu wayanawna 'anhu wain yuhlikoona illa anfusahum wama yash'uroon

# 816

Walaw tara ith wuqifoo 'ala annari faqaloo ya laytana nuraddu wala nukaththiba biayati rabbina wanakoona mina almumineen

# 817

Bal bada lahum ma kanoo yukhfoona min qablu walaw ruddoo la'adoo lima nuhoo 'anhu wainnahum lakathiboon

# 818

Waqaloo in hiya illa hayatuna addunya wama nahnu bimab'ootheen

# 819

Walaw tara ith wuqifoo 'ala rabbihim qala alaysa hatha bilhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroon

# 820

Qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai Allahi hatta itha jaathumu assa'atu baghtatan qaloo ya hasratana 'ala ma farratna feeha wahum yahmiloona awzarahum 'ala thuhoorihim ala saa ma yaziroon

# 821

Wama alhayatu addunya illa la'ibun walahwun waladdaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena yattaqoona afala ta'qiloon

# 822

Qad na'lamu innahu layahzunuka allathee yaqooloona fainnahum la yukaththiboonaka walakinna aththalimeena biayati Allahi yajhadoon

# 823

Walaqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika fasabaroo 'ala ma kuththiboo waoothoo hatta atahum nasruna wala mubaddila likalimati Allahi walaqad jaaka min nabai almursaleen

# 824

Wain kana kabura 'alayka i'raduhum faini istata'ta an tabtaghiya nafaqan fee alardi aw sullaman fee assamai fatatiyahum biayatin walaw shaa Allahu lajama'ahum 'ala alhuda fala takoonanna mina aljahileen

# 825

Innama yastajeebu allatheena yasma'oona walmawta yab'athuhumu Allahu thumma ilayhi yurja'oon

# 826

Waqaloo lawla nuzzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha qadirun 'ala an yunazzila ayatan walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 827

Wama min dabbatin fee alardi wala tairin yateeru bijanahayhi illa omamun amthalukum ma farratna fee alkitabi min shayin thumma ila rabbihim yuhsharoon

# 828

Wallatheena kaththaboo biayatina summun wabukmun fee aththulumati man yashai Allahu yudlilhu waman yasha yaj'alhu 'ala siratin mustaqeem

# 829

Qul araaytakum in atakum 'athabu Allahi aw atatkumu assa'atu aghayra Allahi tad'oona in kuntum sadiqeen

# 830

Bal iyyahu tad'oona fayakshifu ma tad'oona ilayhi in shaa watansawna ma tushrikoon

# 831

Walaqad arsalna ila omamin min qablika faakhathnahum bilbasai waddarrai la'allahum yatadarra'oon

# 832

Falawla ith jaahum basuna tadarra'oo walakin qasat quloobuhum wazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 833

Falamma nasoo ma thukkiroo bihi fatahna 'alayhim abwaba kulli shayin hatta itha farihoo bima ootoo akhathnahum baghtatan faitha hum mublisoon

# 834

Faquti'a dabiru alqawmi allatheena thalamoo walhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 835

Qul araaytum in akhatha Allahu sam'akum waabsarakum wakhatama 'ala quloobikum man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bihi onthur kayfa nusarrifu alayati thumma hum yasdifoon

# 836

Qul araaytakum in atakum 'athabu Allahi baghtatan aw jahratan hal yuhlaku illa alqawmu aththalimoon

# 837

Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena faman amana waaslaha fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon

# 838

Wallatheena kaththaboo biayatina yamassuhumu al'athabu bima kanoo yafsuqoon

# 839

Qul la aqoolu lakum 'indee khazainu Allahi wala a'lamu alghayba wala aqoolu lakum innee malakun in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya qul hal yastawee ala'ma walbaseeru afala tatafakkaroon

# 840

Waanthir bihi allatheena yakhafoona an yuhsharoo ila rabbihim laysa lahum min doonihi waliyyun wala shafee'un la'allahum yattaqoon

# 841

Wala tatrudi allatheena yad'oona rabbahum bilghadati wal'ashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu ma 'alayka min hisabihim min shayin wama min hisabika 'alayhim min shayin fatatrudahum fatakoona mina aththalimeen

# 842

Wakathalika fatanna ba'dahum biba'din liyaqooloo ahaolai manna Allahu 'alayhim min baynina alaysa Allahu bia'lama bishshakireen

# 843

Waitha jaaka allatheena yuminoona biayatina faqul salamun 'alaykum kataba rabbukum 'ala nafsihi arrahmata annahu man 'amila minkum sooan bijahalatin thumma taba min ba'dihi waaslaha faannahu ghafoorun raheem

# 844

Wakathalika nufassilu alayati walitastabeena sabeelu almujrimeen

# 845

Qul innee nuheetu an a'buda allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi qul la attabi'u ahwaakum qad dalaltu ithan wama ana mina almuhtadeen

# 846

Qul innee 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee wakaththabtum bihi ma 'indee ma tasta'jiloona bihi ini alhukmu illa lillahi yaqussu alhaqqa wahuwa khayru alfasileen

# 847

Qul law anna 'indee ma tasta'jiloona bihi laqudiya alamru baynee wabaynakum wallahu a'lamu biththalimeen

# 848

Wa'indahu mafatihu alghaybi la ya'lamuha illa huwa waya'lamu ma fee albarri walbahri wama tasqutu min waraqatin illa ya'lamuha wala habbatin fee thulumati alardi wala ratbin wala yabisin illa fee kitabin mubeen

# 849

Wahuwa allathee yatawaffakum billayli waya'lamu ma jarahtum binnahari thumma yab'athukum feehi liyuqda ajalun musamman thumma ilayhi marji'ukum thumma yunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 850

Wahuwa alqahiru fawqa 'ibadihi wayursilu 'alaykum hafathatan hatta itha jaa ahadakumu almawtu tawaffathu rusuluna wahum la yufarritoon

# 851

Thumma ruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi ala lahu alhukmu wahuwa asra'u alhasibeen

# 852

Qul man yunajjeekum min thulumati albarri walbahri tad'oonahu tadarru'an wakhufyatan lain anjana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina ashshakireen

# 853

Quli Allahu yunajjeekum minha wamin kulli karbin thumma antum tushrikoon

# 854

Qul huwa alqadiru 'ala an yab'atha 'alaykum 'athaban min fawqikum aw min tahti arjulikum aw yalbisakum shiya'an wayutheeqa ba'dakum basa ba'din onthur kayfa nusarrifu alayati la'allahum yafqahoon

# 855

Wakaththaba bihi qawmuka wahuwa alhaqqu qul lastu 'alaykum biwakeel

# 856

Likulli nabain mustaqarrun wasawfa ta'lamoon

# 857

Waitha raayta allatheena yakhoodoona fee ayatina faa'rid 'anhum hatta yakhoodoo fee hadeethin ghayrihi waimma yunsiyannaka ashshaytanu fala taq'ud ba'da aththikra ma'a alqawmi aththalimeen

# 858

Wama 'ala allatheena yattaqoona min hisabihim min shayin walakin thikra la'allahum yattaqoon

# 859

Wathari allatheena ittakhathoo deenahum la'iban walahwan wagharrathumu alhayatu addunya wathakkir bihi an tubsala nafsun bima kasabat laysa laha min dooni Allahi waliyyun wala shafee'un wain ta'dil kulla 'adlin la yukhath minha olaika allatheena obsiloo bima kasaboo lahum sharabun min hameemin wa'athabun aleemun bima kanoo yakfuroon

# 860

Qul anad'oo min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'una wala yadurruna wanuraddu 'ala a'qabina ba'da ith hadana Allahu kallathee istahwathu ashshayateenu fee alardi hayrana lahu ashabun yad'oonahu ila alhuda itina qul inna huda Allahi huwa alhuda waomirna linuslima lirabbi al'alameen

# 861

Waan aqeemoo assalata wattaqoohu wahuwa allathee ilayhi tuhsharoon

# 862

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda bilhaqqi wayawma yaqoolu kun fayakoonu qawluhu alhaqqu walahu almulku yawma yunfakhu fee assoori 'alimu alghaybi washshahadati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeer

# 863

Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi azara atattakhithu asnaman alihatan innee araka waqawmaka fee dalalin mubeen

# 864

Wakathalika nuree ibraheema malakoota assamawati walardi waliyakoona mina almooqineen

# 865

Falamma janna 'alayhi allaylu raa kawkaban qala hatha rabbee falamma afala qala la ohibbu alafileen

# 866

Falamma raa alqamara bazighan qala hatha rabbee falamma afala qala lain lam yahdinee rabbee laakoonanna mina alqawmi addalleen

# 867

Falamma raa ashshamsa bazighatan qala hatha rabbee hatha akbaru falamma afalat qala ya qawmi innee bareeon mimma tushrikoon

# 868

Innee wajjahtu wajhiya lillathee fatara assamawati walarda haneefan wama ana mina almushrikeen

# 869

Wahajjahu qawmuhu qala atuhajjoonnee fee Allahi waqad hadani wala akhafu ma tushrikoona bihi illa an yashaa rabbee shayan wasi'a rabbee kulla shayin 'ilman afala tatathakkaroon

# 870

Wakayfa akhafu ma ashraktum wala takhafoona annakum ashraktum billahi ma lam yunazzil bihi 'alaykum sultanan faayyu alfareeqayni ahaqqu bilamni in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 871

Allatheena amanoo walam yalbisoo eemanahum bithulmin olaika lahumu alamnu wahum muhtadoon

# 872

Watilka hujjatuna ataynaha ibraheema 'ala qawmihi narfa'u darajatin man nashao inna rabbaka hakeemun 'aleem

# 873

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba kullan hadayna wanoohan hadayna min qablu wamin thurriyyatihi dawooda wasulaymana waayyooba wayoosufa wamoosa waharoona wakathalika najzee almuhsineen

# 874

Wazakariyya wayahya wa'eesa walyasa kullun mina assaliheen

# 875

Waisma'eela walyasa'a wayoonusa walootan wakullan faddalna 'ala al'alameen

# 876

Wamin abaihim wathurriyyatihim waikhwanihim wajtabaynahum wahadaynahum ila siratin mustaqeem

# 877

Thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi walaw ashrakoo lahabita 'anhum ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 878

Olaika allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba walhukma wannubuwwata fain yakfur biha haolai faqad wakkalna biha qawman laysoo biha bikafireen

# 879

Olaika allatheena hada Allahu fabihudahumu iqtadih qul la asalukum 'alayhi ajran in huwa illa thikra lil'alameen

# 880

Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi ith qaloo ma anzala Allahu 'ala basharin min shayin qul man anzala alkitaba allathee jaa bihi moosa nooran wahudan linnasi taj'aloonahu qarateesa tubdoonaha watukhfoona katheeran wa'ullimtum ma lam ta'lamoo antum wala abaokum quli Allahu thumma tharhum fee khawdihim yal'aboon

# 881

Wahatha kitabun anzalnahu mubarakun musaddiqu allathee bayna yadayhi walitunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha wallatheena yuminoona bilakhirati yuminoona bihi wahum 'ala salatihim yuhafithoon

# 882

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw qala oohiya ilayya walam yooha ilayhi shayon waman qala saonzilu mithla ma anzala Allahu walaw tara ithi aththalimoona fee ghamarati almawti walmalaikatu basitoo aydeehim akhrijoo anfusakumu alyawma tujzawna 'athaba alhooni bima kuntum taqooloona 'ala Allahi ghayra alhaqqi wakuntum 'an ayatihi tastakbiroon

# 883

Walaqad jitumoona furada kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin wataraktum ma khawwalnakum waraa thuhoorikum wama nara ma'akum shufa'aakumu allatheena za'amtum annahum feekum shurakao laqad taqatta'a baynakum wadalla 'ankum ma kuntum taz'umoon

# 884

Inna Allaha faliqu alhabbi wannawa yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wamukhriju almayyiti mina alhayyi thalikumu Allahu faanna tufakoon

# 885

Faliqu alisbahi waja'ala allayla sakanan washshamsa walqamara husbanan thalika taqdeeru al'azeezi al'aleem

# 886

Wahuwa allathee ja'ala lakumu annujooma litahtadoo biha fee thulumati albarri walbahri qad fassalna alayati liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 887

Wahuwa allathee anshaakum min nafsin wahidatin famustaqarrun wamustawda'un qad fassalna alayati liqawmin yafqahoon

# 888

Wahuwa allathee anzala mina assamai maan faakhrajna bihi nabata kulli shayin faakhrajna minhu khadiran nukhriju minhu habban mutarakiban wamina annakhli min tal'iha qinwanun daniyatun wajannatin min a'nabin wazzaytoona warrummana mushtabihan waghayra mutashabihin onthuroo ila thamarihi itha athmara wayan'ihi inna fee thalikum laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 889

Waja'aloo lillahi shurakaa aljinna wakhalaqahum wakharaqoo lahu baneena wabanatin bighayri 'ilmin subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yasifoon

# 890

Badee'u assamawati walardi anna yakoonu lahu waladun walam takun lahu sahibatun wakhalaqa kulla shayin wahuwa bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 891

Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum la ilaha illa huwa khaliqu kulli shayin fa'budoohu wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin wakeel

# 892

La tudrikuhu alabsaru wahuwa yudriku alabsara wahuwa allateefu alkhabeer

# 893

Qad jaakum basairu min rabbikum faman absara falinafsihi waman 'amiya fa'alayha wama ana 'alaykum bihafeeth

# 894

Wakathalika nusarrifu alayati waliyaqooloo darasta walinubayyinahu liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 895

Ittabi' ma oohiya ilayka min rabbika la ilaha illa huwa waa'rid 'ani almushrikeen

# 896

Walaw shaa Allahu ma ashrakoo wama ja'alnaka 'alayhim hafeethan wama anta 'alayhim biwakeel

# 897

Wala tasubboo allatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi fayasubboo Allaha 'adwan bighayri 'ilmin kathalika zayyanna likulli ommatin 'amalahum thumma ila rabbihim marji'uhum fayunabbiohum bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 898

Waaqsamoo billahi jahda aymanihim lain jaathum ayatun layuminunna biha qul innama alayatu 'inda Allahi wama yush'irukum annaha itha jaat la yuminoon

# 899

Wanuqallibu afidatahum waabsarahum kama lam yuminoo bihi awwala marratin wanatharuhum fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon

# 900

Walaw annana nazzalna ilayhimu almalaikata wakallamahumu almawta wahasharna 'alayhim kulla shayin qubulan ma kanoo liyuminoo illa an yashaa Allahu walakinna aktharahum yajhaloon

# 901

Wakathalika ja'alna likulli nabiyyin 'aduwwan shayateena alinsi waljinni yoohee ba'duhum ila ba'din zukhrufa alqawli ghurooran walaw shaa rabbuka ma fa'aloohu fatharhum wama yaftaroon

# 902

Walitasgha ilayhi afidatu allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati waliyardawhu waliyaqtarifoo ma hum muqtarifoon

# 903

Afaghayra Allahi abtaghee hakaman wahuwa allathee anzala ilaykumu alkitaba mufassalan wallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba ya'lamoona annahu munazzalun min rabbika bilhaqqi fala takoonanna mina almumtareen

# 904

Watammat kalimatu rabbika sidqan wa'adlan la mubaddila likalimatihi wahuwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 905

Wain tuti' akthara man fee alardi yudillooka 'an sabeeli Allahi in yattabi'oona illa aththanna wain hum illa yakhrusoon

# 906

Inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu man yadillu 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bilmuhtadeen

# 907

Fakuloo mimma thukira ismu Allahi 'alayhi in kuntum biayatihi mumineen

# 908

Wama lakum alla takuloo mimma thukira ismu Allahi 'alayhi waqad fassala lakum ma harrama 'alaykum illa ma idturirtum ilayhi wainna katheeran layudilloona biahwaihim bighayri 'ilmin inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu bilmu'tadeen

# 909

Watharoo thahira alithmi wabatinahu inna allatheena yaksiboona alithma sayujzawna bima kanoo yaqtarifoon

# 910

Wala takuloo mimma lam yuthkari ismu Allahi 'alayhi wainnahu lafisqun wainna ashshayateena layoohoona ila awliyaihim liyujadilookum wain ata'tumoohum innakum lamushrikoon

# 911

Awa man kana maytan faahyaynahu waja'alna lahu nooran yamshee bihi fee annasi kaman mathaluhu fee aththulumati laysa bikharijin minha kathalika zuyyina lilkafireena ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 912

Wakathalika ja'alna fee kulli qaryatin akabira mujrimeeha liyamkuroo feeha wama yamkuroona illa bianfusihim wama yash'uroon

# 913

Waitha jaathum ayatun qaloo lan numina hatta nuta mithla ma ootiya rusulu Allahi Allahu a'lamu haythu yaj'alu risalatahu sayuseebu allatheena ajramoo sagharun 'inda Allahi wa'athabun shadeedun bima kanoo yamkuroon

# 914

Faman yuridi Allahu an yahdiyahu yashrah sadrahu lilislami waman yurid an yudillahu yaj'al sadrahu dayyiqan harajan kaannama yassa''adu fee assamai kathalika yaj'alu Allahu arrijsa 'ala allatheena la yuminoon

# 915

Wahatha siratu rabbika mustaqeeman qad fassalna alayati liqawmin yaththakkaroon

# 916

Lahum daru assalami 'inda rabbihim wahuwa waliyyuhum bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 917

Wayawma yahshuruhum jamee'an ya ma'shara aljinni qadi istakthartum mina alinsi waqala awliyaohum mina alinsi rabbana istamta'a ba'duna biba'din wabalaghna ajalana allathee ajjalta lana qala annaru mathwakum khalideena feeha illa ma shaa Allahu inna rabbaka hakeemun 'aleem

# 918

Wakathalika nuwallee ba'da aththalimeena ba'dan bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 919

Ya ma'shara aljinni walinsi alam yatikum rusulun minkum yaqussoona 'alaykum ayatee wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo shahidna 'ala anfusina wagharrathumu alhayatu addunya washahidoo 'ala anfusihim annahum kanoo kafireen

# 920

Thalika an lam yakun rabbuka muhlika alqura bithulmin waahluha ghafiloon

# 921

Walikullin darajatun mimma 'amiloo wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ya'maloon

# 922

Warabbuka alghaniyyu thoo arrahmati in yasha yuthhibkum wayastakhlif min ba'dikum ma yashao kama anshaakum min thurriyyati qawmin akhareen

# 923

Inna ma too'adoona laatin wama antum bimu'jizeen

# 924

Qul ya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun fasawfa ta'lamoona man takoonu lahu 'aqibatu addari innahu la yuflihu aththalimoon

# 925

Waja'aloo lillahi mimma tharaa mina alharthi walan'ami naseeban faqaloo hatha lillahi biza'mihim wahatha lishurakaina fama kana lishurakaihim fala yasilu ila Allahi wama kana lillahi fahuwa yasilu ila shurakaihim saa ma yahkumoon

# 926

Wakathalika zayyana likatheerin mina almushrikeena qatla awladihim shurakaohum liyurdoohum waliyalbisoo 'alayhim deenahum walaw shaa Allahu ma fa'aloohu fatharhum wama yaftaroon

# 927

Waqaloo hathihi an'amun waharthun hijrun la yat'amuha illa man nashao biza'mihim waan'amun hurrimat thuhooruha waan'amun la yathkuroona isma Allahi 'alayha iftiraan 'alayhi sayajzeehim bima kanoo yaftaroon

# 928

Waqaloo ma fee butooni hathihi alan'ami khalisatun lithukoorina wamuharramun 'ala azwajina wain yakun maytatan fahum feehi shurakao sayajzeehim wasfahum innahu hakeemun 'aleem

# 929

Qad khasira allatheena qataloo awladahum safahan bighayri 'ilmin waharramoo ma razaqahumu Allahu iftiraan 'ala Allahi qad dalloo wama kanoo muhtadeen

# 930

Wahuwa allathee anshaa jannatin ma'rooshatin waghayra ma'rooshatin wannakhla wazzar'a mukhtalifan okuluhu wazzaytoona warrummana mutashabihan waghayra mutashabihin kuloo min thamarihi itha athmara waatoo haqqahu yawma hasadihi wala tusrifoo innahu la yuhibbu almusrifeen

# 931

Wamina alan'ami hamoolatan wafarshan kuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu wala tattabi'oo khutuwati ashshaytani innahu lakum 'aduwwun mubeen

# 932

Thamaniyata azwajin mina addani ithnayni wamina alma'zi ithnayni qul aththakarayni harrama ami alonthayayni amma ishtamalat 'alayhi arhamu alonthayayni nabbioonee bi'ilmin in kuntum sadiqeen

# 933

Wamina alibili ithnayni wamina albaqari ithnayni qul aththakarayni harrama ami alonthayayni amma ishtamalat 'alayhi arhamu alonthayayni am kuntum shuhadaa ith wassakumu Allahu bihatha faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban liyudilla annasa bighayri 'ilmin inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 934

Qul la ajidu fee ma oohiya ilayya muharraman 'ala ta'imin yat'amuhu illa an yakoona maytatan aw daman masfoohan aw lahma khinzeerin fainnahu rijsun aw fisqan ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala 'adin fainna rabbaka ghafoorun raheem

# 935

Wa'ala allatheena hadoo harramna kulla thee thufurin wamina albaqari walghanami harramna 'alayhim shuhoomahuma illa ma hamalat thuhooruhuma awi alhawaya aw ma ikhtalata bi'athmin thalika jazaynahum bibaghyihim wainna lasadiqoon

# 936

Fain kaththabooka faqul rabbukum thoo rahmatin wasi'atin wala yuraddu basuhu 'ani alqawmi almujrimeen

# 937

Sayaqoolu allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma ashrakna wala abaona wala harramna min shayin kathalika kaththaba allatheena min qablihim hatta thaqoo basana qul hal 'indakum min 'ilmin fatukhrijoohu lana in tattabi'oona illa aththanna wain antum illa takhrusoon

# 938

Qul falillahi alhujjatu albalighatu falaw shaa lahadakum ajma'een

# 939

Qul halumma shuhadaakumu allatheena yashhadoona anna Allaha harrama hatha fain shahidoo fala tashhad ma'ahum wala tattabi' ahwaa allatheena kaththaboo biayatina wallatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati wahum birabbihim ya'diloon

# 940

Qul ta'alaw atlu ma harrama rabbukum 'alaykum alla tushrikoo bihi shayan wabilwalidayni ihsanan wala taqtuloo awladakum min imlaqin nahnu narzuqukum waiyyahum wala taqraboo alfawahisha ma thahara minha wama batana wala taqtuloo annafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bilhaqqi thalikum wassakum bihi la'allakum ta'qiloon

# 941

Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa billatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo alkayla walmeezana bilqisti la nukallifu nafsan illa wus'aha waitha qultum fa'diloo walaw kana tha qurba wabi'ahdi Allahi awfoo thalikum wassakum bihi la'allakum tathakkaroon

# 942

Waanna hatha siratee mustaqeeman fattabi'oohu wala tattabi'oo assubula fatafarraqa bikum 'an sabeelihi thalikum wassakum bihi la'allakum tattaqoon

# 943

Thumma atayna moosa alkitaba tamaman 'ala allathee ahsana watafseelan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan la'allahum biliqai rabbihim yuminoon

# 944

Wahatha kitabun anzalnahu mubarakun fattabi'oohu wattaqoo la'allakum turhamoon

# 945

An taqooloo innama onzila alkitabu 'ala taifatayni min qablina wain kunna 'an dirasatihim laghafileen

# 946

Aw taqooloo law anna onzila 'alayna alkitabu lakunna ahda minhum faqad jaakum bayyinatun min rabbikum wahudan warahmatun faman athlamu mimman kaththaba biayati Allahi wasadafa 'anha sanajzee allatheena yasdifoona 'an ayatina sooa al'athabi bima kanoo yasdifoon

# 947

Hal yanthuroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya rabbuka aw yatiya ba'du ayati rabbika yawma yatee ba'du ayati rabbika la yanfa'u nafsan eemanuha lam takun amanat min qablu aw kasabat fee eemaniha khayran quli intathiroo inna muntathiroon

# 948

Inna allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiya'an lasta minhum fee shayin innama amruhum ila Allahi thumma yunabbiohum bima kanoo yaf'aloon

# 949

Man jaa bilhasanati falahu 'ashru amthaliha waman jaa bissayyiati fala yujza illa mithlaha wahum la yuthlamoon

# 950

Qul innanee hadanee rabbee ila siratin mustaqeemin deenan qiyaman millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeen

# 951

Qul inna salatee wanusukee wamahyaya wamamatee lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 952

La shareeka lahu wabithalika omirtu waana awwalu almuslimeen

# 953

Qul aghayra Allahi abghee rabban wahuwa rabbu kulli shayin wala taksibu kullu nafsin illa 'alayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra thumma ila rabbikum marji'ukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum feehi takhtalifoon

# 954

Wahuwa allathee ja'alakum khalaifa alardi warafa'a ba'dakum fawqa ba'din darajatin liyabluwakum fee ma atakum inna rabbaka saree'u al'iqabi wainnahu laghafoorun raheem

# 955

Aliflammeemsad

# 956

Kitabun onzila ilayka fala yakun fee sadrika harajun minhu litunthira bihi wathikra lilmumineen

# 957

Ittabi'oo ma onzila ilaykum min rabbikum wala tattabi'oo min doonihi awliyaa qaleelan ma tathakkaroon

# 958

Wakam min qaryatin ahlaknaha fajaaha basuna bayatan aw hum qailoon

# 959

Fama kana da'wahum ith jaahum basuna illa an qaloo inna kunna thalimeen

# 960

Falanasalanna allatheena orsila ilayhim walanasalanna almursaleen

# 961

Falanaqussanna 'alayhim bi'ilmin wama kunna ghaibeen

# 962

Walwaznu yawmaithini alhaqqu faman thaqulat mawazeenuhu faolaika humu almuflihoon

# 963

Waman khaffat mawazeenuhu faolaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum bima kanoo biayatina yathlimoon

# 964

Walaqad makkannakum fee alardi waja'alna lakum feeha ma'ayisha qaleelan ma tashkuroon

# 965

Walaqad khalaqnakum thumma sawwarnakum thumma qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa lam yakun mina assajideen

# 966

Qala ma mana'aka alla tasjuda ith amartuka qala ana khayrun minhu khalaqtanee min narin wakhalaqtahu min teen

# 967

Qala fahbit minha fama yakoonu laka an tatakabbara feeha fakhruj innaka mina assaghireen

# 968

Qala anthirnee ila yawmi yub'athoon

# 969

Qala innaka mina almunthareen

# 970

Qala fabima aghwaytanee laaq'udanna lahum sirataka almustaqeem

# 971

Thumma laatiyannahum min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim wa'an aymanihim wa'an shamailihim wala tajidu aktharahum shakireen

# 972

Qala okhruj minha mathooman madhooran laman tabi'aka minhum laamlaanna jahannama minkum ajma'een

# 973

Waya adamu oskun anta wazawjuka aljannata fakula min haythu shituma wala taqraba hathihi ashshajarata fatakoona mina aththalimeen

# 974

Fawaswasa lahuma ashshaytanu liyubdiya lahuma ma wooriya 'anhuma min sawatihima waqala ma nahakuma rabbukuma 'an hathihi ashshajarati illa an takoona malakayni aw takoona mina alkhalideen

# 975

Waqasamahuma innee lakuma lamina annasiheen

# 976

Fadallahuma bighuroorin falamma thaqa ashshajarata badat lahuma sawatuhuma watafiqa yakhsifani 'alayhima min waraqi aljannati wanadahuma rabbuhuma alam anhakuma 'an tilkuma ashshajarati waaqul lakuma inna ashshaytana lakuma 'aduwwun mubeen

# 977

Qala rabbana thalamna anfusana wain lam taghfir lana watarhamna lanakoonanna mina alkhasireen

# 978

Qala ihbitoo ba'dukum liba'din 'aduwwun walakum fee alardi mustaqarrun wamata'un ila heen

# 979

Qala feeha tahyawna wafeeha tamootoona waminha tukhrajoon

# 980

Ya banee adama qad anzalna 'alaykum libasan yuwaree sawatikum wareeshan walibasu attaqwa thalika khayrun thalika min ayati Allahi la'allahum yaththakkaroon

# 981

Ya banee adama la yaftinannakumu ashshaytanu kama akhraja abawaykum mina aljannati yanzi'u 'anhuma libasahuma liyuriyahuma sawatihima innahu yarakum huwa waqabeeluhu min haythu la tarawnahum inna ja'alna ashshayateena awliyaa lillatheena la yuminoon

# 982

Waitha fa'aloo fahishatan qaloo wajadna 'alayha abaana wallahu amarana biha qul inna Allaha la yamuru bilfahshai ataqooloona 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 983
