Qul amara rabbee bilqisti waaqeemoo wujoohakum 'inda kulli masjidin wad'oohu mukhliseena lahu addeena kama badaakum ta'oodoon

# 984

Fareeqan hada wafareeqan haqqa 'alayhimu addalalatu innahumu ittakhathoo ashshayateena awliyaa min dooni Allahi wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoon

# 985

Ya banee adama khuthoo zeenatakum 'inda kulli masjidin wakuloo washraboo wala tusrifoo innahu la yuhibbu almusrifeen

# 986

Qul man harrama zeenata Allahi allatee akhraja li'ibadihi wattayyibati mina arrizqi qul hiya lillatheena amanoo fee alhayati addunya khalisatan yawma alqiyamati kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 987

Qul innama harrama rabbiya alfawahisha ma thahara minha wama batana walithma walbaghya bighayri alhaqqi waan tushrikoo billahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan waan taqooloo 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 988

Walikulli ommatin ajalun faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoon

# 989

Ya banee adama imma yatiyannakum rusulun minkum yaqussoona 'alaykum ayatee famani ittaqa waaslaha fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon

# 990

Wallatheena kaththaboo biayatina wastakbaroo 'anha olaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoon

# 991

Faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi olaika yanaluhum naseebuhum mina alkitabi hatta itha jaathum rusuluna yatawaffawnahum qaloo ayna ma kuntum tad'oona min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo 'anna washahidoo 'ala anfusihim annahum kanoo kafireen

# 992

Qala odkhuloo fee omamin qad khalat min qablikum mina aljinni walinsi fee annari kullama dakhalat ommatun la'anat okhtaha hatta itha iddarakoo feeha jamee'an qalat okhrahum lioolahum rabbana haolai adalloona faatihim 'athaban di'fan mina annari qala likullin di'fun walakin la ta'lamoon

# 993

Waqalat oolahum liokhrahum fama kana lakum 'alayna min fadlin fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum taksiboon

# 994

Inna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina wastakbaroo 'anha la tufattahu lahum abwabu assamai wala yadkhuloona aljannata hatta yalija aljamalu fee sammi alkhiyati wakathalika najzee almujrimeen

# 995

Lahum min jahannama mihadun wamin fawqihim ghawashin wakathalika najzee aththalimeen

# 996

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati la nukallifu nafsan illa wus'aha olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoon

# 997

Wanaza'na ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee hadana lihatha wama kunna linahtadiya lawla an hadana Allahu laqad jaat rusulu rabbina bilhaqqi wanoodoo an tilkumu aljannatu oorithtumooha bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 998

Wanada ashabu aljannati ashaba annari an qad wajadna ma wa'adana rabbuna haqqan fahal wajadtum ma wa'ada rabbukum haqqan qaloo na'am faaththana muaththinun baynahum an la'natu Allahi 'ala aththalimeen

# 999

Allatheena yasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan wahum bilakhirati kafiroon

# 1000

Wabaynahuma hijabun wa'ala ala'rafi rijalun ya'rifoona kullan biseemahum wanadaw ashaba aljannati an salamun 'alaykum lam yadkhulooha wahum yatma'oon

# 1001

Waitha surifat absaruhum tilqaa ashabi annari qaloo rabbana la taj'alna ma'a alqawmi aththalimeen

# 1002

Wanada ashabu ala'rafi rijalan ya'rifoonahum biseemahum qaloo ma aghna 'ankum jam'ukum wama kuntum tastakbiroon

# 1003

Ahaolai allatheena aqsamtum la yanaluhumu Allahu birahmatin odkhuloo aljannata la khawfun 'alaykum wala antum tahzanoon

# 1004

Wanada ashabu anari ashaba aljannati an afeedoo 'alayna mina almai aw mimma razaqakumu Allahu qaloo inna Allaha harramahuma 'ala alkafireen

# 1005

Allatheena ittakhathoo deenahum lahwan wala'iban wagharrathumu alhayatu addunya falyawma nansahum kama nasoo liqaa yawmihim hatha wama kanoo biayatina yajhadoon

# 1006

Walaqad jinahum bikitabin fassalnahu 'ala 'ilmin hudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoon

# 1007

Hal yanthuroona illa taweelahu yawma yatee taweeluhu yaqoolu allatheena nasoohu min qablu qad jaat rusulu rabbina bilhaqqi fahal lana min shufa'aa fayashfa'oo lana aw nuraddu fana'mala ghayra allathee kunna na'malu qad khasiroo anfusahum wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 1008

Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi yughshee allayla annahara yatlubuhu hatheethan washshamsa walqamara wannujooma musakhkharatin biamrihi ala lahu alkhalqu walamru tabaraka Allahu rabbu al'alameen

# 1009

Od'oo rabbakum tadarru'an wakhufyatan innahu la yuhibbu almu'tadeen

# 1010

Wala tufsidoo fee alardi ba'da islahiha wad'oohu khawfan watama'an inna rahmata Allahi qareebun mina almuhsineen

# 1011

Wahuwa allathee yursilu arriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi hatta itha aqallat sahaban thiqalan suqnahu libaladin mayyitin faanzalna bihi almaa faakhrajna bihi min kulli aththamarati kathalika nukhriju almawta la'allakum tathakkaroon

# 1012

Walbaladu attayyibu yakhruju nabatuhu biithni rabbihi wallathee khabutha la yakhruju illa nakidan kathalika nusarrifu alayati liqawmin yashkuroon

# 1013

Laqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin 'atheem

# 1014

Qala almalao min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee dalalin mubeen

# 1015

Qala ya qawmi laysa bee dalalatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameen

# 1016

Oballighukum risalati rabbee waansahu lakum waa'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 1017

Awa'ajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum 'ala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum walitattaqoo wala'allakum turhamoon

# 1018

Fakaththaboohu faanjaynahu wallatheena ma'ahu fee alfulki waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawman 'ameen

# 1019

Waila 'adin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoon

# 1020

Qala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee safahatin wainna lanathunnuka mina alkathibeen

# 1021

Qala ya qawmi laysa bee safahatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameen

# 1022

Oballighukum risalati rabbee waana lakum nasihun ameen

# 1023

Awa'ajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum 'ala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum wathkuroo ith ja'alakum khulafaa min ba'di qawmi noohin wazadakum fee alkhalqi bastatan fathkuroo alaa Allahi la'allakum tuflihoon

# 1024

Qaloo ajitana lina'buda Allaha wahdahu wanathara ma kana ya'budu abaona fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 1025

Qala qad waqa'a 'alaykum min rabbikum rijsun waghadabun atujadiloonanee fee asmain sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma nazzala Allahu biha min sultanin fantathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireen

# 1026

Faanjaynahu wallatheena ma'ahu birahmatin minna waqata'na dabira allatheena kaththaboo biayatina wama kanoo mumineen

# 1027

Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum 'athabun aleem

# 1028

Wathkuroo ith ja'alakum khulafaa min ba'di 'adin wabawwaakum fee alardi tattakhithoona min suhooliha qusooran watanhitoona aljibala buyootan fathkuroo alaa Allahi wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideen

# 1029

Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lillatheena istud'ifoo liman amana minhum ata'lamoona anna salihan mursalun min rabbihi qaloo inna bima orsila bihi muminoon

# 1030

Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna billathee amantum bihi kafiroon

# 1031

Fa'aqaroo annaqata wa'ataw 'an amri rabbihim waqaloo ya salihu itina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina almursaleen

# 1032

Faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeen

# 1033

Fatawalla 'anhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalata rabbee wanasahtu lakum walakin la tuhibboona annasiheen

# 1034

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina al'alameen

# 1035

Innakum latatoona arrijala shahwatan min dooni annisai bal antum qawmun musrifoon

# 1036

Wama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoohum min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoon

# 1037

Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireen

# 1038

Waamtarna 'alayhim mataran fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almujrimeen

# 1039

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum faawfoo alkayla walmeezana wala tabkhasoo annasa ashyaahum wala tufsidoo fee alardi ba'da islahiha thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineen

# 1040

Wala taq'udoo bikulli siratin too'idoona watasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi man amana bihi watabghoonaha 'iwajan wathkuroo ith kuntum qaleelan fakaththarakum wanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideen

# 1041

Wain kana taifatun minkum amanoo billathee orsiltu bihi wataifatun lam yuminoo fasbiroo hatta yahkuma Allahu baynana wahuwa khayru alhakimeen

# 1042

Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lanukhrijannaka ya shu'aybu wallatheena amanoo ma'aka min qaryatina aw lata'oodunna fee millatina qala awalaw kunna kariheen

# 1043

Qadi iftarayna 'ala Allahi kathiban in 'udna fee millatikum ba'da ith najjana Allahu minha wama yakoonu lana an na'ooda feeha illa an yashaa Allahu rabbuna wasi'a rabbuna kulla shayin 'ilman 'ala Allahi tawakkalna rabbana iftah baynana wabayna qawmina bilhaqqi waanta khayru alfatiheen

# 1044

Waqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi laini ittaba'tum shu'ayban innakum ithan lakhasiroon

# 1045

Faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeen

# 1046

Allatheena kaththaboo shu'ayban kaan lam yaghnaw feeha allatheena kaththaboo shu'ayban kanoo humu alkhasireen

# 1047

Fatawalla 'anhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalati rabbee wanasahtu lakum fakayfa asa 'ala qawmin kafireen

# 1048

Wama arsalna fee qaryatin min nabiyyin illa akhathna ahlaha bilbasai waddarrai la'allahum yaddarra'oon

# 1049

Thumma baddalna makana assayyiati alhasanata hatta 'afaw waqaloo qad massa abaana addarrao wassarrao faakhathnahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon

# 1050

Walaw anna ahla alqura amanoo wattaqaw lafatahna 'alayhim barakatin mina assamai walardi walakin kaththaboo faakhathnahum bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 1051

Afaamina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna bayatan wahum naimoon

# 1052

Awa amina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna duhan wahum yal'aboon

# 1053

Afaaminoo makra Allahi fala yamanu makra Allahi illa alqawmu alkhasiroon

# 1054

Awalam yahdi lillatheena yarithoona alarda min ba'di ahliha an law nashao asabnahum bithunoobihim wanatba'u 'ala quloobihim fahum la yasma'oon

# 1055

Tilka alqura naqussu 'alayka min anbaiha walaqad jaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo min qablu kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala quloobi alkafireen

# 1056

Wama wajadna liaktharihim min 'ahdin wain wajadna aktharahum lafasiqeen

# 1057

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihim moosa biayatina ila fir'awna wamalaihi fathalamoo biha fanuthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideen

# 1058

Waqala moosa ya fir'awnu innee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameen

# 1059

Haqeequn 'ala an la aqoola 'ala Allahi illa alhaqqa qad jitukum bibayyinatin min rabbikum faarsil ma'iya banee israeel

# 1060

Qala in kunta jita biayatin fati biha in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 1061

Faalqa 'asahu faitha hiya thu'banun mubeen

# 1062

Wanaza'a yadahu faitha hiya baydao linnathireen

# 1063

Qala almalao min qawmi fir'awna inna hatha lasahirun 'aleem

# 1064

Yureedu an yukhrijakum min ardikum famatha tamuroon

# 1065

Qaloo arjih waakhahu waarsil fee almadaini hashireen

# 1066

Yatooka bikulli sahirin 'aleem

# 1067

Wajaa assaharatu fir'awna qaloo inna lana laajran in kunna nahnu alghalibeen

# 1068

Qala na'am wainnakum lamina almuqarrabeen

# 1069

Qaloo ya moosa imma an tulqiya waimma an nakoona nahnu almulqeen

# 1070

Qala alqoo falamma alqaw saharoo a'yuna annasi wastarhaboohum wajaoo bisihrin 'atheem

# 1071

Waawhayna ila moosa an alqi 'asaka faitha hiya talqafu ma yafikoon

# 1072

Fawaqa'a alhaqqu wabatala ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1073

Faghuliboo hunalika wanqalaboo saghireen

# 1074

Waolqiya assaharatu sajideen

# 1075

Qaloo amanna birabbi al'alameen

# 1076

Rabbi moosa waharoon

# 1077

Qala fir'awnu amantum bihi qabla an athana lakum inna hatha lamakrun makartumoohu fee almadeenati litukhrijoo minha ahlaha fasawfa ta'lamoon

# 1078

Laoqati'anna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khilafin thumma laosallibannakum ajma'een

# 1079

Qaloo inna ila rabbina munqaliboon

# 1080

Wama tanqimu minna illa an amanna biayati rabbina lamma jaatna rabbana afrigh 'alayna sabran watawaffana muslimeen

# 1081

Waqala almalao min qawmi fir'awna atatharu moosa waqawmahu liyufsidoo fee alardi wayatharaka waalihataka qala sanuqattilu abnaahum wanastahyee nisaahum wainna fawqahum qahiroon

# 1082

Qala moosa liqawmihi ista'eenoo billahi wasbiroo inna alarda lillahi yoorithuha man yashao min 'ibadihi wal'aqibatu lilmuttaqeen

# 1083

Qaloo ootheena min qabli an tatiyana wamin ba'di ma jitana qala 'asa rabbukum an yuhlika 'aduwwakum wayastakhlifakum fee alardi fayanthura kayfa ta'maloon

# 1084

Walaqad akhathna ala fir'awna bissineena wanaqsin mina aththamarati la'allahum yaththakkaroon

# 1085

Faitha jaathumu alhasanatu qaloo lana hathihi wain tusibhum sayyiatun yattayyaroo bimoosa waman ma'ahu ala innama tairuhum 'inda Allahi walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 1086

Waqaloo mahma tatina bihi min ayatin litasharana biha fama nahnu laka bimumineen

# 1087

Faarsalna 'alayhimu attoofana waljarada walqummala waddafadi'a waddama ayatin mufassalatin fastakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeen

# 1088

Walamma waqa'a 'alayhimu arrijzu qaloo ya moosa od'u lana rabbaka bima 'ahida 'indaka lain kashafta 'anna arrijza lanuminanna laka walanursilanna ma'aka banee israeel

# 1089

Falamma kashafna 'anhumu arrijza ila ajalin hum balighoohu itha hum yankuthoon

# 1090

Fantaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum fee alyammi biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo 'anha ghafileen

# 1091

Waawrathna alqawma allatheena kanoo yustad'afoona mashariqa alardi wamagharibaha allatee barakna feeha watammat kalimatu rabbika alhusna 'ala banee israeela bima sabaroo wadammarna ma kana yasna'u fir'awnu waqawmuhu wama kanoo ya'rishoon

# 1092

Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faataw 'ala qawmin ya'kufoona 'ala asnamin lahum qaloo ya moosa ij'al lana ilahan kama lahum alihatun qala innakum qawmun tajhaloon

# 1093

Inna haolai mutabbarun ma hum feehi wabatilun ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1094

Qala aghayra Allahi abgheekum ilahan wahuwa faddalakum 'ala al'alameen

# 1095

Waith anjaynakum min ali fir'awna yasoomoonakum sooa al'athabi yuqattiloona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum 'atheem

# 1096

Wawa'adna moosa thalatheena laylatan waatmamnaha bi'ashrin fatamma meeqatu rabbihi arba'eena laylatan waqala moosa liakheehi haroona okhlufnee fee qawmee waaslih wala tattabi' sabeela almufsideen

# 1097

Walamma jaa moosa limeeqatina wakallamahu rabbuhu qala rabbi arinee anthur ilayka qala lan taranee walakini onthur ila aljabali faini istaqarra makanahu fasawfa taranee falamma tajalla rabbuhu liljabali ja'alahu dakkan wakharra moosa sa'iqan falamma afaqa qala subhanaka tubtu ilayka waana awwalu almumineen

# 1098

Qala ya moosa innee istafaytuka 'ala annasi birisalatee wabikalamee fakhuth ma ataytuka wakun mina ashshakireen

# 1099

Wakatabna lahu fee alalwahi min kulli shayin maw'ithatan watafseelan likulli shayin fakhuthha biquwwatin wamur qawmaka yakhuthoo biahsaniha saoreekum dara alfasiqeen

# 1100

Saasrifu 'an ayatiya allatheena yatakabbaroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wain yaraw kulla ayatin la yuminoo biha wain yaraw sabeela arrushdi la yattakhithoohu sabeelan wain yaraw sabeela alghayyi yattakhithoohu sabeelan thalika biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo 'anha ghafileen

# 1101

Wallatheena kaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati habitat a'maluhum hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1102

Wattakhatha qawmu moosa min ba'dihi min huliyyihim 'ijlan jasadan lahu khuwarun alam yaraw annahu la yukallimuhum wala yahdeehim sabeelan ittakhathoohu wakanoo thalimeen

# 1103

Walamma suqita fee aydeehim waraaw annahum qad dalloo qaloo lain lam yarhamna rabbuna wayaghfir lana lanakoonanna mina alkhasireen

# 1104

Walamma raja'a moosa ila qawmihi ghadbana asifan qala bisama khalaftumoonee min ba'dee a'ajiltum amra rabbikum waalqa alalwaha waakhatha birasi akheehi yajurruhu ilayhi qala ibna omma inna alqawma istad'afoonee wakadoo yaqtuloonanee fala tushmit biya ala'daa wala taj'alnee ma'a alqawmi aththalimeen

# 1105

Qala rabbi ighfir lee waliakhee waadkhilna fee rahmatika waanta arhamu arrahimeen

# 1106

Inna allatheena ittakhathoo al'ijla sayanaluhum ghadabun min rabbihim wathillatun fee alhayati addunya wakathalika najzee almuftareen

# 1107

Wallatheena 'amiloo assayyiati thumma taboo min ba'diha waamanoo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheem

# 1108

Walamma sakata 'an moosa alghadabu akhatha alalwaha wafee nuskhatiha hudan warahmatun lillatheena hum lirabbihim yarhaboon

# 1109

Wakhtara moosa qawmahu sab'eena rajulan limeeqatina falamma akhathathumu arrajfatu qala rabbi law shita ahlaktahum min qablu waiyyaya atuhlikuna bima fa'ala assufahao minna in hiya illa fitnatuka tudillu biha man tashao watahdee man tashao anta waliyyuna faghfir lana warhamna waanta khayru alghafireen

# 1110

Waktub lana fee hathihi addunya hasanatan wafee alakhirati inna hudna ilayka qala 'athabee oseebu bihi man ashao warahmatee wasi'at kulla shayin fasaaktubuha lillatheena yattaqoona wayutoona azzakata wallatheena hum biayatina yuminoon

# 1111

Allatheena yattabi'oona arrasoola annabiyya alommiyya allathee yajidoonahu maktooban 'indahum fee attawrati walinjeeli yamuruhum bilma'roofi wayanhahum 'ani almunkari wayuhillu lahumu attayyibati wayuharrimu 'alayhimu alkhabaitha wayada'u 'anhum israhum walaghlala allatee kanat 'alayhim fallatheena amanoo bihi wa'azzaroohu wanasaroohu wattaba'oo annoora allathee onzila ma'ahu olaika humu almuflihoon

# 1112

Qul ya ayyuha annasu innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum jamee'an allathee lahu mulku assamawati walardi la ilaha illa huwa yuhyee wayumeetu faaminoo billahi warasoolihi annabiyyi alommiyyi allathee yuminu billahi wakalimatihi wattabi'oohu la'allakum tahtadoon

# 1113

Wamin qawmi moosa ommatun yahdoona bilhaqqi wabihi ya'diloon

# 1114

Waqatta'nahumu ithnatay 'ashrata asbatan omaman waawhayna ila moosa ithi istasqahu qawmuhu ani idrib bi'asaka alhajara fanbajasat minhu ithnata 'ashrata 'aynan qad 'alima kullu onasin mashrabahum wathallalna 'alayhimu alghamama waanzalna 'alayhimu almanna wassalwa kuloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wama thalamoona walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 1115

Waith qeela lahumu oskunoo hathihi alqaryata wakuloo minha haythu shitum waqooloo hittatun wadkhuloo albaba sujjadan naghfir lakum khateeatikum sanazeedu almuhsineen

# 1116

Fabaddala allatheena thalamoo minhum qawlan ghayra allathee qeela lahum faarsalna 'alayhim rijzan mina assamai bima kanoo yathlimoon

# 1117

Wasalhum 'ani alqaryati allatee kanat hadirata albahri ith ya'doona fee assabti ith tateehim heetanuhum yawma sabtihim shurra'an wayawma la yasbitoona la tateehim kathalika nabloohum bima kanoo yafsuqoon

# 1118

Waith qalat ommatun minhum lima ta'ithoona qawman Allahu muhlikuhum aw mu'aththibuhum 'athaban shadeedan qaloo ma'thiratan ila rabbikum wala'allahum yattaqoon

# 1119

Falamma nasoo ma thukkiroo bihi anjayna allatheena yanhawna 'ani assooi waakhathna allatheena thalamoo bi'athabin baeesin bima kanoo yafsuqoon

# 1120

Falamma 'ataw 'an ma nuhoo 'anhu qulna lahum koonoo qiradatan khasieen

# 1121

Waith taaththana rabbuka layab'athanna 'alayhim ila yawmi alqiyamati man yasoomuhum sooa al'athabi inna rabbaka lasaree'u al'iqabi wainnahu laghafoorun raheem

# 1122

Waqatta'nahum fee alardi omaman minhumu assalihoona waminhum doona thalika wabalawnahum bilhasanati wassayyiati la'allahum yarji'oon

# 1123

Fakhalafa min ba'dihim khalfun warithoo alkitaba yakhuthoona 'arada hatha aladna wayaqooloona sayughfaru lana wain yatihim 'aradun mithluhu yakhuthoohu alam yukhath 'alayhim meethaqu alkitabi an la yaqooloo 'ala Allahi illa alhaqqa wadarasoo ma feehi waddaru alakhiratu khayrun lillatheena yattaqoona afala ta'qiloon

# 1124

Wallatheena yumassikoona bilkitabi waaqamoo assalata inna la nudee'u ajra almusliheen

# 1125

Waith nataqna aljabala fawqahum kaannahu thullatun wathannoo annahu waqi'un bihim khuthoo ma ataynakum biquwwatin wathkuroo ma feehi la'allakum tattaqoon

# 1126

Waith akhatha rabbuka min banee adama min thuhoorihim thurriyyatahum waashhadahum 'ala anfusihim alastu birabbikum qaloo bala shahidna an taqooloo yawma alqiyamati inna kunna 'an hatha ghafileen

# 1127

Aw taqooloo innama ashraka abaona min qablu wakunna thurriyyatan min ba'dihim afatuhlikuna bima fa'ala almubtiloon

# 1128

Wakathalika nufassilu alayati wala'allahum yarji'oon

# 1129

Watlu 'alayhim nabaa allathee ataynahu ayatina fansalakha minha faatba'ahu ashshaytanu fakana mina alghaween

# 1130

Walaw shina larafa'nahu biha walakinnahu akhlada ila alardi wattaba'a hawahu famathaluhu kamathali alkalbi in tahmil 'alayhi yalhath aw tatrukhu yalhath thalika mathalu alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina faqsusi alqasasa la'allahum yatafakkaroon

# 1131

Saa mathalan alqawmu allatheena kaththaboo biayatina waanfusahum kanoo yathlimoon

# 1132

Man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadee waman yudlil faolaika humu alkhasiroon

# 1133

Walaqad tharana lijahannama katheeran mina aljinni walinsi lahum quloobun la yafqahoona biha walahum a'yunun la yubsiroona biha walahum athanun la yasma'oona biha olaika kalan'ami bal hum adallu olaika humu alghafiloon

# 1134

Walillahi alasmao alhusna fad'oohu biha watharoo allatheena yulhidoona fee asmaihi sayujzawna ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1135

Wamimman khalaqna ommatun yahdoona bilhaqqi wabihi ya'diloon

# 1136

Wallatheena kaththaboo biayatina sanastadrijuhum min haythu la ya'lamoon

# 1137

Waomlee lahum inna kaydee mateen

# 1138

Awalam yatafakkaroo ma bisahibihim min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun mubeen

# 1139

Awalam yanthuroo fee malakooti assamawati walardi wama khalaqa Allahu min shayin waan 'asa an yakoona qadi iqtaraba ajaluhum fabiayyi hadeethin ba'dahu yuminoon

# 1140

Man yudlili Allahu fala hadiya lahu wayatharuhum fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon

# 1141

Yasaloonaka 'ani assa'ati ayyana mursaha qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda rabbee la yujalleeha liwaqtiha illa huwa thaqulat fee assamawati walardi la tateekum illa baghtatan yasaloonaka kaannaka hafiyyun 'anha qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda Allahi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 1142

Qul la amliku linafsee naf'an wala darran illa ma shaa Allahu walaw kuntu a'lamu alghayba lastakthartu mina alkhayri wama massaniya assooo in ana illa natheerun wabasheerun liqawmin yuminoon

# 1143

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin waja'ala minha zawjaha liyaskuna ilayha falamma taghashshaha hamalat hamlan khafeefan famarrat bihi falamma athqalat da'awa Allaha rabbahuma lain ataytana salihan lanakoonanna mina ashshakireen

# 1144

Falamma atahuma salihan ja'ala lahu shurakaa feema atahuma fata'ala Allahu 'amma yushrikoon

# 1145

Ayushrikoona ma la yakhluqu shayan wahum yukhlaqoon

# 1146

Wala yastatee'oona lahum nasran wala anfusahum yansuroon

# 1147

Wain tad'oohum ila alhuda la yattabi'ookum sawaon 'alaykum ada'awtumoohum am antum samitoon

# 1148

Inna allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi 'ibadun amthalukum fad'oohum falyastajeeboo lakum in kuntum sadiqeen

# 1149

Alahum arjulun yamshoona biha am lahum aydin yabtishoona biha am lahum a'yunun yubsiroona biha am lahum athanun yasma'oona biha quli od'oo shurakaakum thumma keedooni fala tunthiroon

# 1150

Inna waliyyiya Allahu allathee nazzala alkitaba wahuwa yatawalla assaliheen

# 1151

Wallatheena tad'oona min doonihi la yastatee'oona nasrakum wala anfusahum yansuroon

# 1152

Wain tad'oohum ila alhuda la yasma'oo watarahum yanthuroona ilayka wahum la yubsiroon

# 1153

Khuthi al'afwa wamur bil'urfi waa'rid 'ani aljahileen

# 1154

Waimma yanzaghannaka mina ashshaytani nazghun fasta'ith billahi innahu samee'un 'aleem

# 1155

Inna allatheena ittaqaw itha massahum taifun mina ashshaytani tathakkaroo faitha hum mubsiroon

# 1156

Waikhwanuhum yamuddoonahum fee alghayyi thumma la yuqsiroon

# 1157

Waitha lam tatihim biayatin qaloo lawla ijtabaytaha qul innama attabi'u ma yooha ilayya min rabbee hatha basairu min rabbikum wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yuminoon

# 1158

Waitha quria alquranu fastami'oo lahu waansitoo la'allakum turhamoon

# 1159

Wathkur rabbaka fee nafsika tadarru'an wakheefatan wadoona aljahri mina alqawli bilghuduwwi walasali wala takun mina alghafileen

# 1160

Inna allatheena 'inda rabbika la yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatihi wayusabbihoonahu walahu yasjudoon

# 1161

Yasaloonaka 'ani alanfali quli alanfalu lillahi warrasooli fattaqoo Allaha waaslihoo thata baynikum waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu in kuntum mumineen

# 1162

Innama almuminoona allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum waitha tuliyat 'alayhim ayatuhu zadathum eemanan wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon

# 1163

Allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon

# 1164

Olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum darajatun 'inda rabbihim wamaghfiratun warizqun kareem

# 1165

Kama akhrajaka rabbuka min baytika bilhaqqi wainna fareeqan mina almumineena lakarihoon

# 1166

Yujadiloonaka fee alhaqqi ba'dama tabayyana kaannama yusaqoona ila almawti wahum yanthuroon

# 1167

Waith ya'idukumu Allahu ihda attaifatayni annaha lakum watawaddoona anna ghayra thati ashshawkati takoonu lakum wayureedu Allahu an yuhiqqa alhaqqa bikalimatihi wayaqta'a dabira alkafireen

# 1168

Liyuhiqqa alhaqqa wayubtila albatila walaw kariha almujrimoon

# 1169

Ith tastagheethoona rabbakum fastajaba lakum annee mumiddukum bialfin mina almalaikati murdifeen

# 1170

Wama ja'alahu Allahu illa bushra walitatmainna bihi quloobukum wama annasru illa min 'indi Allahi inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeem

# 1171

Ith yughashsheekumu annu'asa amanatan minhu wayunazzilu 'alaykum mina assamai maan liyutahhirakum bihi wayuthhiba 'ankum rijza ashshaytani waliyarbita 'ala quloobikum wayuthabbita bihi alaqdam

# 1172

Ith yoohee rabbuka ila almalaikati annee ma'akum fathabbitoo allatheena amanoo saolqee fee quloobi allatheena kafaroo arru'ba fadriboo fawqa ala'naqi wadriboo minhum kulla banan

# 1173

Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqiqi Allaha warasoolahu fainna Allaha shadeedu al'iqab

# 1174

Thalikum fathooqoohu waanna lilkafireena 'athaba annar

# 1175

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo zahfan fala tuwalloohumu aladbar

# 1176

Waman yuwallihim yawmaithin duburahu illa mutaharrifan liqitalin aw mutahayyizan ila fiatin faqad baa bighadabin mina Allahi wamawahu jahannamu wabisa almaseer

# 1177

Falam taqtuloohum walakinna Allaha qatalahum wama ramayta ith ramayta walakinna Allaha rama waliyubliya almumineena minhu balaan hasanan inna Allaha samee'un 'aleem

# 1178

Thalikum waanna Allaha moohinu kaydi alkafireen

# 1179

In tastaftihoo faqad jaakumu alfathu wain tantahoo fahuwa khayrun lakum wain ta'oodoo na'ud walan tughniya 'ankum fiatukum shayan walaw kathurat waanna Allaha ma'a almumineen

# 1180

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha warasoolahu wala tawallaw 'anhu waantum tasma'oon

# 1181

Wala takoonoo kallatheena qaloo sami'na wahum la yasma'oon

# 1182

Inna sharra addawabbi 'inda Allahi assummu albukmu allatheena la ya'qiloon

# 1183

Walaw 'alima Allahu feehim khayran laasma'ahum walaw asma'ahum latawallaw wahum mu'ridoon

# 1184

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo istajeeboo lillahi walirrasooli itha da'akum lima yuhyeekum wa'lamoo anna Allaha yahoolu bayna almari waqalbihi waannahu ilayhi tuhsharoon

# 1185

Wattaqoo fitnatan la tuseebanna allatheena thalamoo minkum khassatan wa'lamoo anna Allaha shadeedu al'iqab

# 1186

Wathkuroo ith antum qaleelun mustad'afoona fee alardi takhafoona an yatakhattafakumu annasu faawakum waayyadakum binasrihi warazaqakum mina attayyibati la'allakum tashkuroon

# 1187

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takhoonoo Allaha warrasoola watakhoonoo amanatikum waantum ta'lamoon

# 1188

Wa'lamoo annama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun waanna Allaha 'indahu ajrun 'atheem

# 1189

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tattaqoo Allaha yaj'al lakum furqanan wayukaffir 'ankum sayyiatikum wayaghfir lakum wallahu thoo alfadli al'atheem

# 1190

Waith yamkuru bika allatheena kafaroo liyuthbitooka aw yaqtulooka aw yukhrijooka wayamkuroona wayamkuru Allahu wallahu khayru almakireen

# 1191

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna qaloo qad sami'na law nashao laqulna mithla hatha in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen

# 1192

Waith qaloo allahumma in kana hatha huwa alhaqqa min 'indika faamtir 'alayna hijaratan mina assamai awi itina bi'athabin aleem

# 1193

Wama kana Allahu liyu'aththibahum waanta feehim wama kana Allahu mu'aththibahum wahum yastaghfiroon

# 1194

Wama lahum alla yu'aththibahumu Allahu wahum yasuddoona 'ani almasjidi alharami wama kanoo awliyaahu in awliyaohu illa almuttaqoona walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 1195

Wama kana salatuhum 'inda albayti illa mukaan watasdiyatan fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroon

# 1196

Inna allatheena kafaroo yunfiqoona amwalahum liyasuddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi fasayunfiqoonaha thumma takoonu 'alayhim hasratan thumma yughlaboona wallatheena kafaroo ila jahannama yuhsharoon

# 1197

Liyameeza Allahu alkhabeetha mina attayyibi wayaj'ala alkhabeetha ba'dahu 'ala ba'din fayarkumahu jamee'an fayaj'alahu fee jahannama olaika humu alkhasiroon

# 1198

Qul lillatheena kafaroo in yantahoo yughfar lahum ma qad salafa wain ya'oodoo faqad madat sunnatu alawwaleen

# 1199

Waqatiloohum hatta la takoona fitnatun wayakoona addeenu kulluhu lillahi faini intahaw fainna Allaha bima ya'maloona baseer

# 1200

Wain tawallaw fa'lamoo anna Allaha mawlakum ni'ma almawla wani'ma annaseer

# 1201

Wa'lamoo annama ghanimtum min shayin faanna lillahi khumusahu walirrasooli walithee alqurba walyatama walmasakeeni wabni assabeeli in kuntum amantum billahi wama anzalna 'ala 'abdina yawma alfurqani yawma iltaqa aljam'ani wallahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 1202

Ith antum bil'udwati addunya wahum bil'udwati alquswa warrakbu asfala minkum walaw tawa'adtum lakhtalaftum fee almee'adi walakin liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana maf'oolan liyahlika man halaka 'an bayyinatin wayahya man hayya 'an bayyinatin wainna Allaha lasamee'un 'aleem

# 1203

Ith yureekahumu Allahu fee manamika qaleelan walaw arakahum katheeran lafashiltum walatanaza'tum fee alamri walakinna Allaha sallama innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 1204

Waith yureekumoohum ithi iltaqaytum fee a'yunikum qaleelan wayuqallilukum fee a'yunihim liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana maf'oolan waila Allahi turja'u alomoor

# 1205

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetum fiatan fathbutoo wathkuroo Allaha katheeran la'allakum tuflihoon

# 1206

Waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu wala tanaza'oo fatafshaloo watathhaba reehukum wasbiroo inna Allaha ma'a assabireen

# 1207

Wala takoonoo kallatheena kharajoo min diyarihim bataran wariaa annasi wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wallahu bima ya'maloona muheet

# 1208

Waith zayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum waqala la ghaliba lakumu alyawma mina annasi wainnee jarun lakum falamma taraati alfiatani nakasa 'ala 'aqibayhi waqala innee bareeon minkum innee ara ma la tarawna innee akhafu Allaha wallahu shadeedu al'iqab

# 1209

Ith yaqoolu almunafiqoona wallatheena fee quloobihim maradun gharra haolai deenuhum waman yatawakkal 'ala Allahi fainna Allaha 'azeezun hakeem

# 1210

Walaw tara ith yatawaffa allatheena kafaroo almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum wathooqoo 'athaba alhareeq

# 1211

Thalika bima qaddamat aydeekum waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lil'abeed

# 1212

Kadabi ali fir'awna wallatheena min qablihim kafaroo biayati Allahi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim inna Allaha qawiyyun shadeedu al'iqab

# 1213

Thalika bianna Allaha lam yaku mughayyiran ni'matan an'amaha 'ala qawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waanna Allaha samee'un 'aleem

# 1214

Kadabi ali fir'awna wallatheena min qablihim kaththaboo biayati rabbihim faahlaknahum bithunoobihim waaghraqna ala fir'awna wakullun kanoo thalimeen

# 1215

Inna sharra addawabbi 'inda Allahi allatheena kafaroo fahum la yuminoon

# 1216

Allatheena 'ahadta minhum thumma yanqudoona 'ahdahum fee kulli marratin wahum la yattaqoon

# 1217

Faimma tathqafannahum fee alharbi fasharrid bihim man khalfahum la'allahum yaththakkaroon

# 1218

Waimma takhafanna min qawmin khiyanatan fanbith ilayhim 'ala sawain inna Allaha la yuhibbu alkhaineen

# 1219

Wala yahsabanna allatheena kafaroo sabaqoo innahum la yu'jizoon

# 1220

Waa'iddoo lahum ma istata'tum min quwwatin wamin ribati alkhayli turhiboona bihi 'aduwwa Allahi wa'aduwwakum waakhareena min doonihim la ta'lamoonahumu Allahu ya'lamuhum wama tunfiqoo min shayin fee sabeeli Allahi yuwaffa ilaykum waantum la tuthlamoon

# 1221

Wain janahoo lissalmi fajnah laha watawakkal 'ala Allahi innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 1222

Wain yureedoo an yakhda'ooka fainna hasbaka Allahu huwa allathee ayyadaka binasrihi wabilmumineen

# 1223

Waallafa bayna quloobihim law anfaqta ma fee alardi jamee'an ma allafta bayna quloobihim walakinna Allaha allafa baynahum innahu 'azeezun hakeem

# 1224

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu hasbuka Allahu wamani ittaba'aka mina almumineen

# 1225

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu harridi almumineena 'ala alqitali in yakun minkum 'ishroona sabiroona yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum miatun yaghliboo alfan mina allatheena kafaroo biannahum qawmun la yafqahoon

# 1226

Alana khaffafa Allahu 'ankum wa'alima anna feekum da'fan fain yakun minkum miatun sabiratun yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum alfun yaghliboo alfayni biithni Allahi wallahu ma'a assabireen

# 1227

Ma kana linabiyyin an yakoona lahu asra hatta yuthkhina fee alardi tureedoona 'arada addunya wallahu yureedu alakhirata wallahu 'azeezun hakeem

# 1228

Lawla kitabun mina Allahi sabaqa lamassakum feema akhathtum 'athabun 'atheem

# 1229

Fakuloo mimma ghanimtum halalan tayyiban wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 1230

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liman fee aydeekum mina alasra in ya'lami Allahu fee quloobikum khayran yutikum khayran mimma okhitha minkum wayaghfir lakum wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 1231

Wain yureedoo khiyanataka faqad khanoo Allaha min qablu faamkana minhum wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 1232

Inna allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi wallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika ba'duhum awliyao ba'din wallatheena amanoo walam yuhajiroo ma lakum min walayatihim min shayin hatta yuhajiroo waini istansarookum fee addeeni fa'alaykumu annasru illa 'ala qawmin baynakum wabaynahum meethaqun wallahu bima ta'maloona baseer

# 1233

Wallatheena kafaroo ba'duhum awliyao ba'din illa taf'aloohu takun fitnatun fee alardi wafasadun kabeer

# 1234

Wallatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi wallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem

# 1235

Wallatheena amanoo min ba'du wahajaroo wajahadoo ma'akum faolaika minkum waoloo alarhami ba'duhum awla biba'din fee kitabi Allahi inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 1236

Baraatun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila allatheena 'ahadtum mina almushrikeen

# 1237

Faseehoo fee alardi arba'ata ashhurin wa'lamoo annakum ghayru mu'jizee Allahi waanna Allaha mukhzee alkafireen

# 1238

Waathanun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila annasi yawma alhajji alakbari anna Allaha bareeon mina almushrikeena warasooluhu fain tubtum fahuwa khayrun lakum wain tawallaytum fa'lamoo annakum ghayru mu'jizee Allahi wabashshiri allatheena kafaroo bi'athabin aleem

# 1239

Illa allatheena 'ahadtum mina almushrikeena thumma lam yanqusookum shayan walam yuthahiroo 'alaykum ahadan faatimmoo ilayhim 'ahdahum ila muddatihim inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeen

# 1240

Faitha insalakha alashhuru alhurumu faqtuloo almushrikeena haythu wajadtumoohum wakhuthoohum wahsuroohum waq'udoo lahum kulla marsadin fain taboo waaqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata fakhalloo sabeelahum inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 1241

Wain ahadun mina almushrikeena istajaraka faajirhu hatta yasma'a kalama Allahi thumma ablighhu mamanahu thalika biannahum qawmun la ya'lamoon

# 1242

Kayfa yakoonu lilmushrikeena 'ahdun 'inda Allahi wa'inda rasoolihi illa allatheena 'ahadtum 'inda almasjidi alharami fama istaqamoo lakum fastaqeemoo lahum inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeen

# 1243

Kayfa wain yathharoo 'alaykum la yarquboo feekum illan wala thimmatan yurdoonakum biafwahihim wataba quloobuhum waaktharuhum fasiqoon

# 1244

Ishtaraw biayati Allahi thamanan qaleelan fasaddoo 'an sabeelihi innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1245

La yarquboona fee muminin illan wala thimmatan waolaika humu almu'tadoon

# 1246

Fain taboo waaqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata faikhwanukum fee addeeni wanufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 1247

Wain nakathoo aymanahum min ba'di 'ahdihim wata'anoo fee deenikum faqatiloo aimmata alkufri innahum la aymana lahum la'allahum yantahoon

# 1248

Ala tuqatiloona qawman nakathoo aymanahum wahammoo biikhraji arrasooli wahum badaookum awwala marratin atakhshawnahum fallahu ahaqqu an takhshawhu in kuntum mumineen

# 1249

Qatiloohum yu'aththibhumu Allahu biaydeekum wayukhzihim wayansurkum 'alayhim wayashfi sudoora qawmin mumineen

# 1250

Wayuthhib ghaytha quloobihim wayatoobu Allahu 'ala man yashao wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 1251

Am hasibtum an tutrakoo walamma ya'lami Allahu allatheena jahadoo minkum walam yattakhithoo min dooni Allahi wala rasoolihi wala almumineena waleejatan wallahu khabeerun bima ta'maloon

# 1252

Ma kana lilmushrikeena an ya'muroo masajida Allahi shahideena 'ala anfusihim bilkufri olaika habitat a'maluhum wafee annari hum khalidoon

# 1253

Innama ya'muru masajida Allahi man amana billahi walyawmi alakhiri waaqama assalata waata azzakata walam yakhsha illa Allaha fa'asa olaika an yakoonoo mina almuhtadeen

# 1254

Aja'altum siqayata alhajji wa'imarata almasjidi alharami kaman amana billahi walyawmi alakhiri wajahada fee sabeeli Allahi la yastawoona 'inda Allahi wallahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 1255

Allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalihim waanfusihim a'thamu darajatan 'inda Allahi waolaika humu alfaizoon

# 1256

Yubashshiruhum rabbuhum birahmatin minhu waridwanin wajannatin lahum feeha na'eemun muqeem

# 1257

Khalideena feeha abadan inna Allaha 'indahu ajrun 'atheem

# 1258

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo abaakum waikhwanakum awliyaa ini istahabboo alkufra 'ala aleemani waman yatawallahum minkum faolaika humu aththalimoon

# 1259

Qul in kana abaokum waabnaokum waikhwanukum waazwajukum wa'asheeratukum waamwalun iqtaraftumooha watijaratun takhshawna kasadaha wamasakinu tardawnaha ahabba ilaykum mina Allahi warasoolihi wajihadin fee sabeelihi fatarabbasoo hatta yatiya Allahu biamrihi wallahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeen

# 1260

Laqad nasarakumu Allahu fee mawatina katheeratin wayawma hunaynin ith a'jabatkum kathratukum falam tughni 'ankum shayan wadaqat 'alaykumu alardu bima rahubat thumma wallaytum mudbireen

# 1261

Thumma anzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'ala rasoolihi wa'ala almumineena waanzala junoodan lam tarawha wa'aththaba allatheena kafaroo wathalika jazao alkafireen

# 1262

Thumma yatoobu Allahu min ba'di thalika 'ala man yashao wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 1263

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo innama almushrikoona najasun fala yaqraboo almasjida alharama ba'da 'amihim hatha wain khiftum 'aylatan fasawfa yughneekumu Allahu min fadlihi in shaa inna Allaha 'aleemun hakeem

# 1264

Qatiloo allatheena la yuminoona billahi wala bilyawmi alakhiri wala yuharrimoona ma harrama Allahu warasooluhu wala yadeenoona deena alhaqqi mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba hatta yu'too aljizyata 'an yadin wahum saghiroon

# 1265

Waqalati alyahoodu 'uzayrun ibnu Allahi waqalati annasara almaseehu ibnu Allahi thalika qawluhum biafwahihim yudahioona qawla allatheena kafaroo min qablu qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoon

# 1266

Ittakhathoo ahbarahum waruhbanahum arbaban min dooni Allahi walmaseeha ibna maryama wama omiroo illa liya'budoo ilahan wahidan la ilaha illa huwa subhanahu 'amma yushrikoon

# 1267

Yureedoona an yutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim wayaba Allahu illa an yutimma noorahu walaw kariha alkafiroon

# 1268

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bilhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu 'ala addeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoon

# 1269

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna katheeran mina alahbari warruhbani layakuloona amwala annasi bilbatili wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wallatheena yaknizoona aththahaba walfiddata wala yunfiqoonaha fee sabeeli Allahi fabashshirhum bi'athabin aleem

# 1270

Yawma yuhma 'alayha fee nari jahannama fatukwa biha jibahuhum wajunoobuhum wathuhooruhum hatha ma kanaztum lianfusikum fathooqoo ma kuntum taknizoon

# 1271

Inna 'iddata ashshuhoori 'inda Allahi ithna 'ashara shahran fee kitabi Allahi yawma khalaqa assamawati walarda minha arba'atun hurumun thalika addeenu alqayyimu fala tathlimoo feehinna anfusakum waqatiloo almushrikeena kaffatan kama yuqatiloonakum kaffatan wa'lamoo anna Allaha ma'a almuttaqeen

# 1272

Innama annaseeo ziyadatun fee alkufri yudallu bihi allatheena kafaroo yuhilloonahu 'aman wayuharrimoonahu 'aman liyuwatioo 'iddata ma harrama Allahu fayuhilloo ma harrama Allahu zuyyina lahum sooo a'malihim wallahu la yahdee alqawma alkafireen

# 1273

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ma lakum itha qeela lakumu infiroo fee sabeeli Allahi iththaqaltum ila alardi aradeetum bilhayati addunya mina alakhirati fama mata'u alhayati addunya fee alakhirati illa qaleel

# 1274

Illa tanfiroo yu'aththibkum 'athaban aleeman wayastabdil qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroohu shayan wallahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 1275

Illa tansuroohu faqad nasarahu Allahu ith akhrajahu allatheena kafaroo thaniya ithnayni ith huma fee alghari ith yaqoolu lisahibihi la tahzan inna Allaha ma'ana faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'alayhi waayyadahu bijunoodin lam tarawha waja'ala kalimata allatheena kafaroo assufla wakalimatu Allahi hiya al'ulya wallahu 'azeezun hakeem

# 1276

Infiroo khifafan wathiqalan wajahidoo biamwalikum waanfusikum fee sabeeli Allahi thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 1277

Law kana 'aradan qareeban wasafaran qasidan lattaba'ooka walakin ba'udat 'alayhimu ashshuqqatu wasayahlifoona billahi lawi istata'na lakharajna ma'akum yuhlikoona anfusahum wallahu ya'lamu innahum lakathiboon

# 1278

'afa Allahu 'anka lima athinta lahum hatta yatabayyana laka allatheena sadaqoo wata'lama alkathibeen

# 1279

La yastathinuka allatheena yuminoona billahi walyawmi alakhiri an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim wallahu 'aleemun bilmuttaqeen

# 1280

Innama yastathinuka allatheena la yuminoona billahi walyawmi alakhiri wartabat quloobuhum fahum fee raybihim yataraddadoon

# 1281

Walaw aradoo alkhurooja laa'addoo lahu 'uddatan walakin kariha Allahu inbi'athahum fathabbatahum waqeela oq'udoo ma'a alqa'ideen

# 1282

Law kharajoo feekum ma zadookum illa khabalan walaawda'oo khilalakum yabghoonakumu alfitnata wafeekum samma'oona lahum wallahu 'aleemun biththalimeen

# 1283

Laqadi ibtaghawoo alfitnata min qablu waqallaboo laka alomoora hatta jaa alhaqqu wathahara amru Allahi wahum karihoon

# 1284

Waminhum man yaqoolu ithan lee wala taftinnee ala fee alfitnati saqatoo wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bilkafireen

# 1285

In tusibka hasanatun tasuhum wain tusibka museebatun yaqooloo qad akhathna amrana min qablu wayatawallaw wahum farihoon

# 1286

Qul lan yuseebana illa ma kataba Allahu lana huwa mawlana wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon

# 1287

Qul hal tarabbasoona bina illa ihda alhusnayayni wanahnu natarabbasu bikum an yuseebakumu Allahu bi'athabin min 'indihi aw biaydeena fatarabbasoo inna ma'akum mutarabbisoon

# 1288

Qul anfiqoo taw'an aw karhan lan yutaqabbala minkum innakum kuntum qawman fasiqeen

# 1289

Wama mana'ahum an tuqbala minhum nafaqatuhum illa annahum kafaroo billahi wabirasoolihi wala yatoona assalata illa wahum kusala wala yunfiqoona illa wahum karihoon

# 1290

Fala tu'jibka amwaluhum wala awladuhum innama yureedu Allahu liyu'aththibahum biha fee alhayati addunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum kafiroon

# 1291

Wayahlifoona billahi innahum laminkum wama hum minkum walakinnahum qawmun yafraqoon

# 1292

Law yajidoona maljaan aw magharatin aw muddakhalan lawallaw ilayhi wahum yajmahoon

# 1293

Waminhum man yalmizuka fee assadaqati fain o'too minha radoo wain lam yu'taw minha itha hum yaskhatoon

# 1294

Walaw annahum radoo ma atahumu Allahu warasooluhu waqaloo hasbuna Allahu sayuteena Allahu min fadlihi warasooluhu inna ila Allahi raghiboon

# 1295

Innama assadaqatu lilfuqarai walmasakeeni wal'amileena 'alayha walmuallafati quloobuhum wafee arriqabi walgharimeena wafee sabeeli Allahi wabni assabeeli fareedatan mina Allahi wallahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1296

Waminhumu allatheena yuthoona annabiyya wayaqooloona huwa othunun qul othunu khayrin lakum yuminu billahi wayuminu lilmumineena warahmatun lillatheena amanoo minkum wallatheena yuthoona rasoola Allahi lahum 'athabun aleem

# 1297

Yahlifoona billahi lakum liyurdookum wallahu warasooluhu ahaqqu an yurdoohu in kanoo mumineen

# 1298

Alam ya'lamoo annahu man yuhadidi Allaha warasoolahu faanna lahu nara jahannama khalidan feeha thalika alkhizyu al'atheem

# 1299

Yahtharu almunafiqoona an tunazzala 'alayhim sooratun tunabbiohum bima fee quloobihim quli istahzioo inna Allaha mukhrijun ma tahtharoon

# 1300

Walain saaltahum layaqoolunna innama kunna nakhoodu wanal'abu qul abillahi waayatihi warasoolihi kuntum tastahzioon

# 1301

La ta'tathiroo qad kafartum ba'da eemanikum in na'fu 'an taifatin minkum nu'aththib taifatan biannahum kanoo mujrimeen

# 1302

Almunafiqoona walmunafiqatu ba'duhum min ba'din yamuroona bilmunkari wayanhawna 'ani alma'roofi wayaqbidoona aydiyahum nasoo Allaha fanasiyahum inna almunafiqeena humu alfasiqoon

# 1303

Wa'ada Allahu almunafiqeena walmunafiqati walkuffara nara jahannama khalideena feeha hiya hasbuhum wala'anahumu Allahu walahum 'athabun muqeem

# 1304

Kallatheena min qablikum kanoo ashadda minkum quwwatan waakthara amwalan waawladan fastamta'oo bikhalaqihim fastamta'tum bikhalaqikum kama istamta'a allatheena min qablikum bikhalaqihim wakhudtum kallathee khadoo olaika habitat a'maluhum fee addunya walakhirati waolaika humu alkhasiroon

# 1305

Alam yatihim nabao allatheena min qablihim qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda waqawmi ibraheema waashabi madyana walmutafikati atathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 1306

Walmuminoona walmuminatu ba'duhum awliyao ba'din yamuroona bilma'roofi wayanhawna 'ani almunkari wayuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wayutee'oona Allaha warasoolahu olaika sayarhamuhumu Allahu inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeem

# 1307

Wa'ada Allahu almumineena walmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati 'adnin waridwanun mina Allahi akbaru thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheem

# 1308

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu jahidi alkuffara walmunafiqeena waghluth 'alayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseer

# 1309

Yahlifoona billahi ma qaloo walaqad qaloo kalimata alkufri wakafaroo ba'da islamihim wahammoo bima lam yanaloo wama naqamoo illa an aghnahumu Allahu warasooluhu min fadlihi fain yatooboo yaku khayran lahum wain yatawallaw yu'aththibhumu Allahu 'athaban aleeman fee addunya walakhirati wama lahum fee alardi min waliyyin wala naseer

# 1310

Waminhum man 'ahada Allaha lain atana min fadlihi lanassaddaqanna walanakoonanna mina assaliheen

# 1311

Falamma atahum min fadlihi bakhiloo bihi watawallaw wahum mu'ridoon

# 1312

Faa'qabahum nifaqan fee quloobihim ila yawmi yalqawnahu bima akhlafoo Allaha ma wa'adoohu wabima kanoo yakthiboon

# 1313

Alam ya'lamoo anna Allaha ya'lamu sirrahum wanajwahum waanna Allaha 'allamu alghuyoob

# 1314

Allatheena yalmizoona almuttawwi'eena mina almumineena fee assadaqati wallatheena la yajidoona illa juhdahum fayaskharoona minhum sakhira Allahu minhum walahum 'athabun aleem

# 1315

Istaghfir lahum aw la tastaghfir lahum in tastaghfir lahum sab'eena marratan falan yaghfira Allahu lahum thalika biannahum kafaroo billahi warasoolihi wallahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeen

# 1316

Fariha almukhallafoona bimaq'adihim khilafa rasooli Allahi wakarihoo an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi waqaloo la tanfiroo fee alharri qul naru jahannama ashaddu harran law kanoo yafqahoon

# 1317

Falyadhakoo qaleelan walyabkoo katheeran jazaan bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 1318

Fain raja'aka Allahu ila taifatin minhum fastathanooka lilkhurooji faqul lan takhrujoo ma'iya abadan walan tuqatiloo ma'iya 'aduwwan innakum radeetum bilqu'oodi awwala marratin faq'udoo ma'a alkhalifeen

# 1319

Wala tusalli 'ala ahadin minhum mata abadan wala taqum 'ala qabrihi innahum kafaroo billahi warasoolihi wamatoo wahum fasiqoon

# 1320

Wala tu'jibka amwaluhum waawladuhum innama yureedu Allahu an yu'aththibahum biha fee addunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum kafiroon

# 1321

Waitha onzilat sooratun an aminoo billahi wajahidoo ma'a rasoolihi istathanaka oloo attawli minhum waqaloo tharna nakun ma'a alqa'ideen

# 1322

Radoo bian yakoonoo ma'a alkhawalifi watubi'a 'ala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoon

# 1323

Lakini arrasoolu wallatheena amanoo ma'ahu jahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim waolaika lahumu alkhayratu waolaika humu almuflihoon

# 1324

a'adda Allahu lahum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha thalika alfawzu al'atheem

# 1325

Wajaa almu'aththiroona mina ala'rabi liyuthana lahum waqa'ada allatheena kathaboo Allaha warasoolahu sayuseebu allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athabun aleem

# 1326

Laysa 'ala addu'afai wala 'ala almarda wala 'ala allatheena la yajidoona ma yunfiqoona harajun itha nasahoo lillahi warasoolihi ma 'ala almuhsineena min sabeelin wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 1327

Wala 'ala allatheena itha ma atawka litahmilahum qulta la ajidu ma ahmilukum 'alayhi tawallaw waa'yunuhum tafeedu mina addam'i hazanan alla yajidoo ma yunfiqoon

# 1328

Innama assabeelu 'ala allatheena yastathinoonaka wahum aghniyao radoo bian yakoonoo ma'a alkhawalifi wataba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim fahum la ya'lamoon

# 1329

Ya'tathiroona ilaykum itha raja'tum ilayhim qul la ta'tathiroo lan numina lakum qad nabbaana Allahu min akhbarikum wasayara Allahu 'amalakum warasooluhu thumma turaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi washshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 1330

Sayahlifoona billahi lakum itha inqalabtum ilayhim litu'ridoo 'anhum faa'ridoo 'anhum innahum rijsun wamawahum jahannamu jazaan bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 1331

Yahlifoona lakum litardaw 'anhum fain tardaw 'anhum fainna Allaha la yarda 'ani alqawmi alfasiqeen

# 1332

Ala'rabu ashaddu kufran wanifaqan waajdaru alla ya'lamoo hudooda ma anzala Allahu 'ala rasoolihi wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 1333

Wamina ala'rabi man yattakhithu ma yunfiqu maghraman wayatarabbasu bikumu addawaira 'alayhim dairatu assawi wallahu samee'un 'aleem

# 1334

Wamina ala'rabi man yuminu billahi walyawmi alakhiri wayattakhithu ma yunfiqu qurubatin 'inda Allahi wasalawati arrasooli ala innaha qurbatun lahum sayudkhiluhumu Allahu fee rahmatihi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 1335

Wassabiqoona alawwaloona mina almuhajireena walansari wallatheena ittaba'oohum biihsanin radiya Allahu 'anhum waradoo 'anhu waa'adda lahum jannatin tajree tahtaha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu al'atheem

# 1336

Wamimman hawlakum mina ala'rabi munafiqoona wamin ahli almadeenati maradoo 'ala annifaqi la ta'lamuhum nahnu na'lamuhum sanu'aththibuhum marratayni thumma yuraddoona ila 'athabin 'atheem

# 1337

Waakharoona i'tarafoo bithunoobihim khalatoo 'amalan salihan waakhara sayyian 'asa Allahu an yatooba 'alayhim inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 1338

Khuth min amwalihim sadaqatan tutahhiruhum watuzakkeehim biha wasalli 'alayhim inna salataka sakanun lahum wallahu samee'un 'aleem

# 1339

Alam ya'lamoo anna Allaha huwa yaqbalu attawbata 'an 'ibadihi wayakhuthu assadaqati waanna Allaha huwa attawwabu arraheem

# 1340

Waquli i'maloo fasayara Allahu 'amalakum warasooluhu walmuminoona wasaturaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi washshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 1341

Waakharoona murjawna liamri Allahi imma yu'aththibuhum waimma yatoobu 'alayhim wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 1342

Wallatheena ittakhathoo masjidan diraran wakufran watafreeqan bayna almumineena wairsadan liman haraba Allaha warasoolahu min qablu walayahlifunna in aradna illa alhusna wallahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboon

# 1343

La taqum feehi abadan lamasjidun ossisa 'ala attaqwa min awwali yawmin ahaqqu an taqooma feehi feehi rijalun yuhibboona an yatatahharoo wallahu yuhibbu almuttahhireen

# 1344

Afaman assasa bunyanahu 'ala taqwa mina Allahi waridwanin khayrun am man assasa bunyanahu 'ala shafa jurufin harin fanhara bihi fee nari jahannama wallahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 1345

La yazalu bunyanuhumu allathee banaw reebatan fee quloobihim illa an taqatta'a quloobuhum wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 1346

Inna Allaha ishtara mina almumineena anfusahum waamwalahum bianna lahumu aljannata yuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi fayaqtuloona wayuqtaloona wa'dan 'alayhi haqqan fee attawrati walinjeeli walqurani waman awfa bi'ahdihi mina Allahi fastabshiroo bibay'ikumu allathee baya'tum bihi wathalika huwa alfawzu al'atheem

# 1347

Attaiboona al'abidoona alhamidoona assaihoona arraki'oona assajidoona alamiroona bilma'roofi wannahoona 'ani almunkari walhafithoona lihudoodi Allahi wabashshiri almumineen

# 1348

Ma kana linnabiyyi wallatheena amanoo an yastaghfiroo lilmushrikeena walaw kanoo olee qurba min ba'di ma tabayyana lahum annahum ashabu aljaheem

# 1349

Wama kana istighfaru ibraheema liabeehi illa 'an maw'idatin wa'adaha iyyahu falamma tabayyana lahu annahu 'aduwwun lillahi tabarraa minhu inna ibraheema laawwahun haleem

# 1350

Wama kana Allahu liyudilla qawman ba'da ith hadahum hatta yubayyina lahum ma yattaqoona inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 1351

Inna Allaha lahu mulku assamawati walardi yuhyee wayumeetu wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseer

# 1352

Laqad taba Allahu 'ala annabiyyi walmuhajireena walansari allatheena ittaba'oohu fee sa'ati al'usrati min ba'di ma kada yazeeghu quloobu fareeqin minhum thumma taba 'alayhim innahu bihim raoofun raheem

# 1353

Wa'ala aththalathati allatheena khullifoo hatta itha daqat 'alayhimu alardu bima rahubat wadaqat 'alayhim anfusuhum wathannoo an la maljaa mina Allahi illa ilayhi thumma taba 'alayhim liyatooboo inna Allaha huwa attawwabu arraheem

# 1354

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha wakoonoo ma'a assadiqeen

# 1355

Ma kana liahli almadeenati waman hawlahum mina ala'rabi an yatakhallafoo 'an rasooli Allahi wala yarghaboo bianfusihim 'an nafsihi thalika biannahum la yuseebuhum thamaon wala nasabun wala makhmasatun fee sabeeli Allahi wala yataoona mawtian yagheethu alkuffara wala yanaloona min 'aduwwin naylan illa kutiba lahum bihi 'amalun salihun inna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineen

# 1356

Wala yunfiqoona nafaqatan sagheeratan wala kabeeratan wala yaqta'oona wadiyan illa kutiba lahum liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1357

Wama kana almuminoona liyanfiroo kaffatan falawla nafara min kulli firqatin minhum taifatun liyatafaqqahoo fee addeeni waliyunthiroo qawmahum itha raja'oo ilayhim la'allahum yahtharoon

# 1358

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qatiloo allatheena yaloonakum mina alkuffari walyajidoo feekum ghilthatan wa'lamoo anna Allaha ma'a almuttaqeen

# 1359

Waitha ma onzilat sooratun faminhum man yaqoolu ayyukum zadathu hathihi eemanan faamma allatheena amanoo fazadathum eemanan wahum yastabshiroon

# 1360

Waamma allatheena fee quloobihim maradun fazadathum rijsan ila rijsihim wamatoo wahum kafiroon

# 1361

Awala yarawna annahum yuftanoona fee kulli 'amin marratan aw marratayni thumma la yatooboona wala hum yaththakkaroon

# 1362

Waitha ma onzilat sooratun nathara ba'duhum ila ba'din hal yarakum min ahadin thumma insarafoo sarafa Allahu quloobahum biannahum qawmun la yafqahoon

# 1363

Laqad jaakum rasoolun min anfusikum 'azeezun 'alayhi ma 'anittum hareesun 'alaykum bilmumineena raoofun raheem

# 1364

Fain tawallaw faqul hasbiya Allahu la ilaha illa huwa 'alayhi tawakkaltu wahuwa rabbu al'arshi al'atheem

# 1365

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeem

# 1366

Akana linnasi 'ajaban an awhayna ila rajulin minhum an anthiri annasa wabashshiri allatheena amanoo anna lahum qadama sidqin 'inda rabbihim qala alkafiroona inna hatha lasahirun mubeen

# 1367

Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi yudabbiru alamra ma min shafee'in illa min ba'di ithnihi thalikumu Allahu rabbukum fa'budoohu afala tathakkaroon

# 1368

Ilayhi marji'ukum jamee'an wa'da Allahi haqqan innahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati bilqisti wallatheena kafaroo lahum sharabun min hameemin wa'athabun aleemun bima kanoo yakfuroon

# 1369

Huwa allathee ja'ala ashshamsa diyaan walqamara nooran waqaddarahu manazila lita'lamoo 'adada assineena walhisaba ma khalaqa Allahu thalika illa bilhaqqi yufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 1370

Inna fee ikhtilafi allayli wannahari wama khalaqa Allahu fee assamawati walardi laayatin liqawmin yattaqoon

# 1371

Inna allatheena la yarjoona liqaana waradoo bilhayati addunya watmaannoo biha wallatheena hum 'an ayatina ghafiloon

# 1372

Olaika mawahumu annaru bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 1373

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati yahdeehim rabbuhum bieemanihim tajree min tahtihimu alanharu fee jannati anna'eem

# 1374

Da'wahum feeha subhanaka allahumma watahiyyatuhum feeha salamun waakhiru da'wahum ani alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 1375

Walaw yu'ajjilu Allahu linnasi ashsharra isti'jalahum bilkhayri laqudiya ilayhim ajaluhum fanatharu allatheena la yarjoona liqaana fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon

# 1376

Waitha massa alinsana addurru da'ana lijanbihi aw qa'idan aw qaiman falamma kashafna 'anhu durrahu marra kaan lam yad'una ila durrin massahu kathalika zuyyina lilmusrifeena ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1377

Walaqad ahlakna alquroona min qablikum lamma thalamoo wajaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati wama kanoo liyuminoo kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeen

# 1378

Thumma ja'alnakum khalaifa fee alardi min ba'dihim linanthura kayfa ta'maloon

# 1379

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana iti biquranin ghayri hatha aw baddilhu qul ma yakoonu lee an obaddilahu min tilqai nafsee in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya innee akhafu in 'asaytu rabbee 'athaba yawmin 'atheem

# 1380

Qul law shaa Allahu ma talawtuhu 'alaykum wala adrakum bihi faqad labithtu feekum 'umuran min qablihi afala ta'qiloon

# 1381

Faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu almujrimoon

# 1382

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhum wala yanfa'uhum wayaqooloona haolai shufa'aona 'inda Allahi qul atunabbioona Allaha bima la ya'lamu fee assamawati wala fee alardi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 1383

Wama kana annasu illa ommatan wahidatan fakhtalafoo walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum feema feehi yakhtalifoon

# 1384

Wayaqooloona lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi faqul innama alghaybu lillahi fantathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireen

# 1385

Waitha athaqna annasa rahmatan min ba'di darraa massathum itha lahum makrun fee ayatina quli Allahu asra'u makran inna rusulana yaktuboona ma tamkuroon

# 1386

Huwa allathee yusayyirukum fee albarri walbahri hatta itha kuntum fee alfulki wajarayna bihim bireehin tayyibatin wafarihoo biha jaatha reehun 'asifun wajaahumu almawju min kulli makanin wathannoo annahum oheeta bihim da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena lain anjaytana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina ashshakireen

# 1387

Falamma anjahum itha hum yabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi ya ayyuha annasu innama baghyukum 'ala anfusikum mata'a alhayati addunya thumma ilayna marji'ukum fanunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 1388

Innama mathalu alhayati addunya kamain anzalnahu mina assamai fakhtalata bihi nabatu alardi mimma yakulu annasu walan'amu hatta itha akhathati alardu zukhrufaha wazzayyanat wathanna ahluha annahum qadiroona 'alayha ataha amruna laylan aw naharan faja'alnaha haseedan kaan lam taghna bilamsi kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 1389

Wallahu yad'oo ila dari assalami wayahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeem

# 1390

Lillatheena ahsanoo alhusna waziyadatun wala yarhaqu wujoohahum qatarun wala thillatun olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoon

# 1391

Wallatheena kasaboo assayyiati jazao sayyiatin bimithliha watarhaquhum thillatun ma lahum mina Allahi min 'asimin kaannama oghshiyat wujoohuhum qita'an mina allayli muthliman olaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoon

# 1392

Wayawma nahshuruhum jamee'an thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo makanakum antum washurakaokum fazayyalna baynahum waqala shurakaohum ma kuntum iyyana ta'budoon

# 1393

Fakafa billahi shaheedan baynana wabaynakum in kunna 'an 'ibadatikum laghafileen

# 1394

Hunalika tabloo kullu nafsin ma aslafat waruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 1395

Qul man yarzuqukum mina assamai walardi amman yamliku assam'a walabsara waman yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi waman yudabbiru alamra fasayaqooloona Allahu faqul afala tattaqoon

# 1396

Fathalikumu Allahu rabbukumu alhaqqu famatha ba'da alhaqqi illa addalalu faanna tusrafoon

# 1397

Kathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena fasaqoo annahum la yuminoon

# 1398

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu quli Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu faanna tufakoon

# 1399

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yahdee ila alhaqqi quli Allahu yahdee lilhaqqi afaman yahdee ila alhaqqi ahaqqu an yuttaba'a amman la yahiddee illa an yuhda fama lakum kayfa tahkumoon

# 1400

Wama yattabi'u aktharuhum illa thannan inna aththanna la yughnee mina alhaqqi shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yaf'aloon

# 1401

Wama kana hatha alquranu an yuftara min dooni Allahi walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameen

# 1402

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bisooratin mithlihi wad'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeen

# 1403

Bal kaththaboo bima lam yuheetoo bi'ilmihi walamma yatihim taweeluhu kathalika kaththaba allatheena min qablihim fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu aththalimeen

# 1404

Waminhum man yuminu bihi waminhum man la yuminu bihi warabbuka a'lamu bilmufsideen

# 1405

Wain kaththabooka faqul lee 'amalee walakum 'amalukum antum bareeoona mimma a'malu waana bareeon mimma ta'maloon

# 1406

Waminhum man yastami'oona ilayka afaanta tusmi'u assumma walaw kanoo la ya'qiloon

# 1407

Waminhum man yanthuru ilayka afaanta tahdee al'umya walaw kanoo la yubsiroon

# 1408

Inna Allaha la yathlimu annasa shayan walakinna annasa anfusahum yathlimoon

# 1409

Wayawma yahshuruhum kaan lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan mina annahari yata'arafoona baynahum qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai Allahi wama kanoo muhtadeen

# 1410

Waimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna marji'uhum thumma Allahu shaheedun 'ala ma yaf'aloon

# 1411

Walikulli ommatin rasoolun faitha jaa rasooluhum qudiya baynahum bilqisti wahum la yuthlamoon

# 1412

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen

# 1413

Qul la amliku linafsee darran wala naf'an illa ma shaa Allahu likulli ommatin ajalun itha jaa ajaluhum fala yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoon

# 1414

Qul araaytum in atakum 'athabuhu bayatan aw naharan matha yasta'jilu minhu almujrimoon

# 1415

Athumma itha ma waqa'a amantum bihi alana waqad kuntum bihi tasta'jiloon

# 1416

Thumma qeela lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi hal tujzawna illa bima kuntum taksiboon

# 1417

Wayastanbioonaka ahaqqun huwa qul ee warabbee innahu lahaqqun wama antum bimu'jizeen

# 1418

Walaw anna likulli nafsin thalamat ma fee alardi laftadat bihi waasarroo annadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waqudiya baynahum bilqisti wahum la yuthlamoon

# 1419

Ala inna lillahi ma fee assamawati walardi ala inna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 1420

Huwa yuhyee wayumeetu wailayhi turja'oon

# 1421

Ya ayyuha annasu qad jaatkum maw'ithatun min rabbikum washifaon lima fee assudoori wahudan warahmatun lilmumineen

# 1422

Qul bifadli Allahi wabirahmatihi fabithalika falyafrahoo huwa khayrun mimma yajma'oon

# 1423

Qul araaytum ma anzala Allahu lakum min rizqin faja'altum minhu haraman wahalalan qul allahu athina lakum am 'ala Allahi taftaroon

# 1424

Wama thannu allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala annasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroon

# 1425

Wama takoonu fee shanin wama tatloo minhu min quranin wala ta'maloona min 'amalin illa kunna 'alaykum shuhoodan ith tufeedoona feehi wama ya'zubu 'an rabbika min mithqali tharratin fee alardi wala fee assamai wala asghara min thalika wala akbara illa fee kitabin mubeen

# 1426

Ala inna awliyaa Allahi la khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon

# 1427

Allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon

# 1428

Lahumu albushra fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati la tabdeela likalimati Allahi thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheem

# 1429

Wala yahzunka qawluhum inna al'izzata lillahi jamee'an huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 1430

Ala inna lillahi man fee assamawati waman fee alardi wama yattabi'u allatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi shurakaa in yattabi'oona illa aththanna wain hum illa yakhrusoon

# 1431

Huwa allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi wannahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oon

# 1432

Qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan subhanahu huwa alghaniyyu lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi in 'indakum min sultanin bihatha ataqooloona 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 1433

Qul inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoon

# 1434

Mata'un fee addunya thumma ilayna marji'uhum thumma nutheequhumu al'athaba ashshadeeda bima kanoo yakfuroon

# 1435

Watlu 'alayhim nabaa noohin ith qala liqawmihi ya qawmi in kana kabura 'alaykum maqamee watathkeeree biayati Allahi fa'ala Allahi tawakkaltu faajmi'oo amrakum washurakaakum thumma la yakun amrukum 'alaykum ghummatan thumma iqdoo ilayya wala tunthiroon

# 1436

Fain tawallaytum fama saaltukum min ajrin in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeen

# 1437

Fakaththaboohu fanajjaynahu waman ma'ahu fee alfulki waja'alnahum khalaifa waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almunthareen

# 1438

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihi rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bilbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo bihi min qablu kathalika natba'u 'ala quloobi almu'tadeen

# 1439

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihim moosa waharoona ila fir'awna wamalaihi biayatina fastakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeen

# 1440

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo inna hatha lasihrun mubeen

# 1441

Qala moosa ataqooloona lilhaqqi lamma jaakum asihrun hatha wala yuflihu assahiroon

# 1442

Qaloo ajitana litalfitana 'amma wajadna 'alayhi abaana watakoona lakuma alkibriyao fee alardi wama nahnu lakuma bimumineen

# 1443

Waqala fir'awnu itoonee bikulli sahirin 'aleem

# 1444

Falamma jaa assaharatu qala lahum moosa alqoo ma antum mulqoon

# 1445

Falamma alqaw qala moosa ma jitum bihi assihru inna Allaha sayubtiluhu inna Allaha la yuslihu 'amala almufsideen

# 1446

Wayuhiqqu Allahu alhaqqa bikalimatihi walaw kariha almujrimoon

# 1447

Fama amana limoosa illa thurriyyatun min qawmihi 'ala khawfin min fir'awna wamalaihim an yaftinahum wainna fir'awna la'alin fee alardi wainnahu lamina almusrifeen

# 1448

Waqala moosa ya qawmi in kuntum amantum billahi fa'alayhi tawakkaloo in kuntum muslimeen

# 1449

Faqaloo 'ala Allahi tawakkalna rabbana la taj'alna fitnatan lilqawmi aththalimeen

# 1450

Wanajjina birahmatika mina alqawmi alkafireen

# 1451

Waawhayna ila moosa waakheehi an tabawwaa liqawmikuma bimisra buyootan waj'aloo buyootakum qiblatan waaqeemoo assalata wabashshiri almumineen

# 1452

Waqala moosa rabbana innaka atayta fir'awna wamalaahu zeenatan waamwalan fee alhayati addunya rabbana liyudilloo 'an sabeelika rabbana itmis 'ala amwalihim washdud 'ala quloobihim fala yuminoo hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleem

# 1453

Qala qad ojeebat da'watukuma fastaqeema wala tattabi'anni sabeela allatheena la ya'lamoon

# 1454

Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faatba'ahum fir'awnu wajunooduhu baghyan wa'adwan hatta itha adrakahu algharaqu qala amantu annahu la ilaha illa allathee amanat bihi banoo israeela waana mina almuslimeen

# 1455

Alana waqad 'asayta qablu wakunta mina almufsideen

# 1456

Falyawma nunajjeeka bibadanika litakoona liman khalfaka ayatan wainna katheeran mina annasi 'an ayatina laghafiloon

# 1457

Walaqad bawwana banee israeela mubawwaa sidqin warazaqnahum mina attayyibati fama ikhtalafoo hatta jaahumu al'ilmu inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon

# 1458

Fain kunta fee shakkin mimma anzalnna ilayka fasali allatheena yaqraoona alkitaba min qablika laqad jaaka alhaqqu min rabbika fala takoonanna mina almumtareen

# 1459

Wala takoonanna mina allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi fatakoona mina alkhasireen

# 1460

Inna allatheena haqqat 'alayhim kalimatu rabbika la yuminoon

# 1461

Walaw jaathum kullu ayatin hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleem

# 1462

Falawla kanat qaryatun amanat fanafa'aha eemanuha illa qawma yoonusa lamma amanoo kashafna 'anhum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati addunya wamatta'nahum ila heen

# 1463

Walaw shaa rabbuka laamana man fee alardi kulluhum jamee'an afaanta tukrihu annasa hatta yakoonoo mumineen

# 1464

Wama kana linafsin an tumina illa biithni Allahi wayaj'alu arrijsa 'ala allatheena la ya'qiloon

# 1465

Quli onthuroo matha fee assamawati walardi wama tughnee alayatu wannuthuru 'an qawmin la yuminoon

# 1466

Fahal yantathiroona illa mithla ayyami allatheena khalaw min qablihim qul fantathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireen

# 1467

Thumma nunajjee rusulana wallatheena amanoo kathalika haqqan 'alayna nunjee almumineen

# 1468

Qul ya ayyuha annasu in kuntum fee shakkin min deenee fala a'budu allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi walakin a'budu Allaha allathee yatawaffakum waomirtu an akoona mina almumineen

# 1469

Waan aqim wajhaka liddeeni haneefan wala takoonanna mina almushrikeen

# 1470

Wala tad'u min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'uka wala yadurruka fain fa'alta fainnaka ithan mina aththalimeen

# 1471

Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yuridka bikhayrin fala radda lifadlihi yuseebu bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi wahuwa alghafooru arraheem

# 1472

Qul ya ayyuha annasu qad jaakumu alhaqqu min rabbikum famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wama ana 'alaykum biwakeel

# 1473

Wattabi' ma yooha ilayka wasbir hatta yahkuma Allahu wahuwa khayru alhakimeen

# 1474

Aliflamra kitabun ohkimat ayatuhu thumma fussilat min ladun hakeemin khabeer

# 1475

Alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innanee lakum minhu natheerun wabasheer

# 1476

Waani istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yumatti'kum mata'an hasanan ila ajalin musamman wayuti kulla thee fadlin fadlahu wain tawallaw fainee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin kabeer

# 1477

Ila Allahi marji'ukum wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 1478

Ala innahum yathnoona sudoorahum liyastakhfoo minhu ala heena yastaghshoona thiyabahum ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 1479

Wama min dabbatin fee alardi illa 'ala Allahi rizquha waya'lamu mustaqarraha wamustawda'aha kullun fee kitabin mubeen

# 1480

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda fee sittati ayyamin wakana 'arshuhu 'ala almai liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amalan walain qulta innakum mab'oothoona min ba'di almawti layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeen

# 1481

Walain akhkharna 'anhumu al'athaba ila ommatin ma'doodatin layaqoolunna ma yahbisuhu ala yawma yateehim laysa masroofan 'anhum wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 1482

Walain athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan thumma naza'naha minhu innahu layaoosun kafoor

# 1483

Walain athaqnahu na'maa ba'da darraa massathu layaqoolanna thahaba assayyiatu 'annee innahu lafarihun fakhoor

# 1484

Illa allatheena sabaroo wa'amiloo assalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer

# 1485

Fala'allaka tarikun ba'da ma yooha ilayka wadaiqun bihi sadruka an yaqooloo lawla onzila 'alayhi kanzun aw jaa ma'ahu malakun innama anta natheerun wallahu 'ala kulli shayin wakeel

# 1486

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bi'ashri suwarin mithlihi muftarayatin wad'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeen

# 1487

Fai llam yastajeeboo lakum fa'lamoo annama onzila bi'ilmi Allahi waan la ilaha illa huwa fahal antum muslimoon

# 1488

Man kana yureedu alhayata addunya wazeenataha nuwaffi ilayhim a'malahum feeha wahum feeha la yubkhasoon

# 1489

Olaika allatheena laysa lahum fee alakhirati illa annaru wahabita ma sana'oo feeha wabatilun ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1490

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi wayatloohu shahidun minhu wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan olaika yuminoona bihi waman yakfur bihi mina alahzabi fannaru maw'iduhu fala taku fee miryatin minhu innahu alhaqqu min rabbika walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoon

# 1491

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban olaika yu'radoona 'ala rabbihim wayaqoolu alashhadu haolai allatheena kathaboo 'ala rabbihim ala la'natu Allahi 'ala aththalimeen

# 1492

Allatheena yasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan wahum bilakhirati hum kafiroon

# 1493

Olaika lam yakoonoo mu'jizeena fee alardi wama kana lahum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa yuda'afu lahumu al'athabu ma kanoo yastatee'oona assam'a wama kanoo yubsiroon

# 1494

Olaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 1495

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroon

# 1496

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo asalihati waakhbatoo ila rabbihim olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoon

# 1497

Mathalu alfareeqayni kala'ma walasammi walbaseeri wassamee'i hal yastawiyani mathalan afala tathakkaroon

# 1498

Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi innee lakum natheerun mubeen

# 1499

An la ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin aleem

# 1500

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma naraka illa basharan mithlana wama naraka ittaba'aka illa allatheena hum arathiluna badiya arrayi wama nara lakum 'alayna min fadlin bal nathunnukum kathibeen

# 1501

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee rahmatan min 'indihi fa'ummiyat 'alaykum anulzimukumooha waantum laha karihoon

# 1502

Waya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi malan in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wama ana bitaridi allatheena amanoo innahum mulaqoo rabbihim walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloon

# 1503

Waya qawmi man yansurunee mina Allahi in taradtuhum afala tathakkaroon

# 1504

Wala aqoolu lakum 'indee khazainu Allahi wala a'lamu alghayba wala aqoolu innee malakun wala aqoolu lillatheena tazdaree a'yunukum lan yutiyahumu Allahu khayran Allahu a'lamu bima fee anfusihim innee ithan lamina aththalimeen

# 1505

Qaloo ya noohu qad jadaltana faaktharta jidalana fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 1506

Qala innama yateekum bihi Allahu in shaa wama antum bimu'jizeen

# 1507

Wala yanfa'ukum nushee in aradtu an ansaha lakum in kana Allahu yureedu an yughwiyakum huwa rabbukum wailayhi turja'oon

# 1508

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fa'alayya ijramee waana bareeon mimma tujrimoon

# 1509

Waoohiya ila noohin annahu lan yumina min qawmika illa man qad amana fala tabtais bima kanoo yaf'aloon

# 1510

Wasna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoon

# 1511

Wayasna'u alfulka wakullama marra 'alayhi malaon min qawmihi sakhiroo minhu qala in taskharoo minna fainna naskharu minkum kama taskharoon

# 1512

Fasawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi wayahillu 'alayhi 'athabun muqeem

# 1513

Hatta itha jaa amruna wafara attannooru qulna ihmil feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu waman amana wama amana ma'ahu illa qaleel

# 1514

Waqala irkaboo feeha bismi Allahi majraha wamursaha inna rabbee laghafoorun raheem

# 1515

Wahiya tajree bihim fee mawjin kaljibali wanada noohunu ibnahu wakana fee ma'zilin ya bunayya irkab ma'ana wala takun ma'a alkafireen

# 1516

Qala saawee ila jabalin ya'simunee mina almai qala la 'asima alyawma min amri Allahi illa man rahima wahala baynahuma almawju fakana mina almughraqeen

# 1517

Waqeela ya ardu ibla'ee maaki waya samao aqli'ee wagheeda almao waqudiya alamru wastawat 'ala aljoodiyyi waqeela bu'dan lilqawmi aththalimeen

# 1518

Wanada noohun rabbahu faqala rabbi inna ibnee min ahlee wainna wa'daka alhaqqu waanta ahkamu alhakimeen

# 1519

Qala ya noohu innahu laysa min ahlika innahu 'amalun ghayru salihin fala tasalni ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun innee a'ithuka an takoona mina aljahileen

# 1520

Qala rabbi innee a'oothu bika an asalaka ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun wailla taghfir lee watarhamnee akun mina alkhasireen

# 1521

Qeela ya noohu ihbit bisalamin minna wabarakatin 'alayka wa'ala omamin mimman ma'aka waomamun sanumatti'uhum thumma yamassuhum minna 'athabun aleem

# 1522

Tilka min anbai alghaybi nooheeha ilayka ma kunta ta'lamuha anta wala qawmuka min qabli hatha fasbir inna al'aqibata lilmuttaqeen

# 1523

Waila 'adin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu in antum illa muftaroon

# 1524

Ya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi ajran in ajriya illa 'ala allathee fataranee afala ta'qiloon

# 1525

Waya qawmi istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yursili assamaa 'alaykum midraran wayazidkum quwwatan ila quwwatikum wala tatawallaw mujrimeen

# 1526

Qaloo ya hoodu ma jitana bibayyinatin wama nahnu bitarikee alihatina 'an qawlika wama nahnu laka bimumineen

# 1527

In naqoolu illa i'taraka ba'du alihatina bisooin qala innee oshhidu Allaha washhadoo annee bareeon mimma tushrikoon

# 1528

Min doonihi fakeedoonee jamee'an thumma la tunthiroon

# 1529

Innee tawakkaltu 'ala Allahi rabbee warabbikum ma min dabbatin illa huwa akhithun binasiyatiha inna rabbee 'ala siratin mustaqeem

# 1530

Fain tawallaw faqad ablaghtukum ma orsiltu bihi ilaykum wayastakhlifu rabbee qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroonahu shayan inna rabbee 'ala kulli shayin hafeeth

# 1531

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna hoodan wallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wanajjaynahum min 'athabin ghaleeth

# 1532

Watilka 'adun jahadoo biayati rabbihim wa'asaw rusulahu wattaba'oo amra kulli jabbarin 'aneed

# 1533

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi addunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati ala inna 'adan kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan li'adin qawmi hood

# 1534

Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu huwa anshaakum mina alardi wasta'marakum feeha fastaghfiroohu thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee qareebun mujeeb

# 1535

Qaloo ya salihu qad kunta feena marjuwwan qabla hatha atanhana an na'buda ma ya'budu abaona wainnana lafee shakkin mimma tad'oona ilayhi mureeb

# 1536

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee minhu rahmatan faman yansurunee mina Allahi in 'asaytuhu fama tazeedoonanee ghayra takhseer

# 1537

Waya qawmi hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum 'athabun qareeb

# 1538

Fa'aqarooha faqala tamatta'oo fee darikum thalathata ayyamin thalika wa'dun ghayru makthoob

# 1539

Falamma jaa amruna najjayna salihan wallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wamin khizyi yawmiithin inna rabbaka huwa alqawiyyu al'azeez

# 1540

Waakhatha allatheena thalamoo assayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeen

# 1541
