Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala inna thamooda kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan lithamood

# 1542

Walaqad jaat rusuluna ibraheema bilbushra qaloo salaman qala salamun fama labitha an jaa bi'ijlin haneeth

# 1543

Falamma raa aydiyahum la tasilu ilayhi nakirahum waawjasa minhum kheefatan qaloo la takhaf inna orsilna ila qawmi loot

# 1544

Wamraatuhu qaimatun fadahikat fabashsharnaha biishaqa wamin warai ishaqa ya'qoob

# 1545

Qalat ya waylata aalidu waana 'ajoozun wahatha ba'lee shaykhan inna hatha lashayon 'ajeeb

# 1546

Qaloo ata'jabeena min amri Allahi rahmatu Allahi wabarakatuhu 'alaykum ahla albayti innahu hameedun majeed

# 1547

Falamma thahaba 'an ibraheema arraw'u wajaathu albushra yujadiluna fee qawmi loot

# 1548

Inna ibraheema lahaleemun awwahun muneeb

# 1549

Ya ibraheemu a'rid 'an hatha innahu qad jaa amru rabbika wainnahum ateehim 'athabun ghayru mardood

# 1550

Walamma jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqala hatha yawmun 'aseeb

# 1551

Wajaahu qawmuhu yuhra'oona ilayhi wamin qablu kanoo ya'maloona assayyiati qala ya qawmi haolai banatee hunna atharu lakum fattaqoo Allaha wala tukhzooni fee dayfee alaysa minkum rajulun rasheed

# 1552

Qaloo laqad 'alimta ma lana fee banatika min haqqin wainnaka lata'lamu ma nureed

# 1553

Qala law anna lee bikum quwwatan aw awee ila ruknin shadeed

# 1554

Qaloo ya lootu inna rusulu rabbika lan yasiloo ilayka faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli wala yaltafit minkum ahadun illa imraataka innahu museebuha ma asabahum inna maw'idahumu assubhu alaysa assubhu biqareeb

# 1555

Falamma jaa amruna ja'alna 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayha hijaratan min sijjeelin mandood

# 1556

Musawwamatan 'inda rabbika wama hiya mina aththalimeena biba'eed

# 1557

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu wala tanqusoo almikyala walmeezana innee arakum bikhayrin wainnee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin muheet

# 1558

Waya qawmi awfoo almikyala walmeezana bilqisti wala tabkhasoo annasa ashyaahum wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideen

# 1559

Baqiyyatu Allahi khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena wama ana 'alaykum bihafeeth

# 1560

Qaloo ya shu'aybu asalatuka tamuruka an natruka ma ya'budu abaona aw an naf'ala fee amwalina ma nashao innaka laanta alhaleemu arrasheed

# 1561

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee warazaqanee minhu rizqan hasanan wama oreedu an okhalifakum ila ma anhakum 'anhu in oreedu illa alislaha ma istata'tu wama tawfeeqee illa billahi 'alayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi oneeb

# 1562

Waya qawmi la yajrimannakum shiqaqee an yuseebakum mithlu ma asaba qawma noohin aw qawma hoodin aw qawma salihin wama qawmu lootin minkum biba'eed

# 1563

Wastaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee raheemun wadood

# 1564

Qaloo ya shu'aybu ma nafqahu katheeran mimma taqoolu wainna lanaraka feena da'eefan walawla rahtuka larajamnaka wama anta 'alayna bi'azeez

# 1565

Qala ya qawmi arahtee a'azzu 'alaykum mina Allahi wattakhathtumoohu waraakum thihriyyan inna rabbee bima ta'maloona muheet

# 1566

Waya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun sawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi waman huwa kathibun wartaqiboo inne ma'akum raqeeb

# 1567

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna shu'ayban wallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna waakhathati allatheena thalamoo assayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeen

# 1568

Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala bu'dan limadyana kama ba'idat thamood

# 1569

Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeen

# 1570

Ila fir'awna wamalaihi fattaba'oo amra fir'awna wama amru fir'awna birasheed

# 1571

Yaqdumu qawmahu yawma alqiyamati faawradahumu annara wabisa alwirdu almawrood

# 1572

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi la'natan wayawma alqiyamati bisa arrifdu almarfood

# 1573

Thalika min anbai alqura naqussuhu 'alayka minha qaimun wahaseed

# 1574

Wama thalamnahum walakin thalamoo anfusahum fama aghnat 'anhum alihatuhumu allatee yad'oona min dooni Allahi min shayin lamma jaa amru rabbika wama zadoohum ghayra tatbeeb

# 1575

Wakathalika akhthu rabbika itha akhatha alqura wahiya thalimatun inna akhthahu aleemun shadeed

# 1576

Inna fee thalika laayatan liman khafa 'athaba alakhirati thalika yawmun majmoo'un lahu annasu wathalika yawmun mashhoodun

# 1577

Wama nuakhkhiruhu illa liajalin ma'dood

# 1578

Yawma yati la takallamu nafsun illa biithnihi faminhum shaqiyyun wasa'eed

# 1579

Faamma allatheena shaqoo fafee annari lahum feeha zafeerun washaheeq

# 1580

Khalideena feeha ma damati assamawatu walardu illa ma shaa rabbuka inna rabbaka fa''alun lima yureed

# 1581

Waamma allatheena su'idoo fafee aljannati khalideena feeha ma damati assamawatu walardu illa ma shaa rabbuka 'ataan ghayra majthooth

# 1582

Fala taku fee miryatin mimma ya'budu haolai ma ya'budoona illa kama ya'budu abaohum min qablu wainna lamuwaffoohum naseebahum ghayra manqoos

# 1583

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fakhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureeb

# 1584

Wainna kullan lamma layuwaffiyannahum rabbuka a'malahum innahu bima ya'maloona khabeer

# 1585

Fastaqim kama omirta waman taba ma'aka wala tatghaw innahu bima ta'maloona baseer

# 1586

Wala tarkanoo ila allatheena thalamoo fatamassakumu annaru wama lakum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa thumma la tunsaroon

# 1587

Waaqimi assalata tarafayi annahari wazulafan mina allayli inna alhasanati yuthhibna assayyiati thalika thikra liththakireen

# 1588

Wasbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineen

# 1589

Falawla kana mina alqurooni min qablikum oloo baqiyyatin yanhawna 'ani alfasadi fee alardi illa qaleelan mimman anjayna minhum wattaba'a allatheena thalamoo ma otrifoo feehi wakanoo mujrimeen

# 1590

Wama kana rabbuka liyuhlika alqura bithulmin waahluha muslihoon

# 1591

Walaw shaa rabbuka laja'ala annasa ommatan wahidatan wala yazaloona mukhtalifeen

# 1592

Illa man rahima rabbuka walithalika khalaqahum watammat kalimatu rabbika laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati wannasi ajma'een

# 1593

Wakullan naqussu 'alayka min anbai arrusuli ma nuthabbitu bihi fuadaka wajaaka fee hathihi alhaqqu wamaw'ithatun wathikra lilmumineen

# 1594

Waqul lillatheena la yuminoona i'maloo 'ala makanatikum inna 'amiloon

# 1595

Wantathiroo inna muntathiroon

# 1596

Walillahi ghaybu assamawati walardi wailayhi yurja'u alamru kulluhu fa'budhu watawakkal 'alayhi wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloon

# 1597

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeen

# 1598

Inna anzalnahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloon

# 1599

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka ahsana alqasasi bima awhayna ilayka hatha alqurana wain kunta min qablihi lamina alghafileen

# 1600

Ith qala yoosufu liabeehi ya abati innee raaytu ahada 'ashara kawkaban washshamsa walqamara raaytuhum lee sajideen

# 1601

Qala ya bunayya la taqsus ruyaka 'ala ikhwatika fayakeedoo laka kaydan inna ashshaytana lilinsani 'aduwwun mubeen

# 1602

Wakathalika yajtabeeka rabbuka wayu'allimuka min taweeli alahadeethi wayutimmu ni'matahu 'alayka wa'ala ali ya'qooba kama atammaha 'ala abawayka min qablu ibraheema waishaqa inna rabbaka 'aleemun hakeem

# 1603

Laqad kana fee yoosufa waikhwatihi ayatun lissaileen

# 1604

Ith qaloo layoosufu waakhoohu ahabbu ila abeena minna wanahnu 'usbatun inna abana lafee dalalin mubeen

# 1605

Oqtuloo yoosufa awi itrahoohu ardan yakhlu lakum wajhu abeekum watakoonoo min ba'dihi qawman saliheen

# 1606

Qala qailun minhum la taqtuloo yoosufa waalqoohu fee ghayabati aljubbi yaltaqithu ba'du assayyarati in kuntum fa'ileen

# 1607

Qaloo ya abana ma laka la tamanna 'ala yoosufa wainna lahu lanasihoon

# 1608

Arsilhu ma'ana ghadan yarta' wayal'ab wainna lahu lahafithoon

# 1609

Qala innee layahzununee an thathhaboo bihi waakhafu an yakulahu aththibu waantum 'anhu ghafiloon

# 1610

Qaloo lain akalahu aththibu wanahnu 'usbatun inna ithan lakhasiroon

# 1611

Falamma thahaboo bihi waajma'oo an yaj'aloohu fee ghayabati aljubbi waawhayna ilayhi latunabiannahum biamrihim hatha wahum la yash'uroon

# 1612

Wajaoo abahum 'ishaan yabkoon

# 1613

Qaloo ya abana inna thahabna nastabiqu watarakna yoosufa 'inda mata'ina faakalahu aththibu wama anta bimuminin lana walaw kunna sadiqeen

# 1614

Wajaoo 'ala qameesihi bidamin kathibin qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun wallahu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoon

# 1615

Wajaat sayyaratun faarsaloo waridahum faadla dalwahu qala ya bushra hatha ghulamun waasarroohu bida'atan wallahu 'aleemun bima ya'maloon

# 1616

Washarawhu bithamanin bakhsin darahima ma'doodatin wakanoo feehi mina azzahideen

# 1617

Waqala allathee ishtarahu min misra limraatihi akrimee mathwahu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wakathalika makkanna liyoosufa fee alardi walinu'allimahu min taweeli alahadeethi wallahu ghalibun 'ala amrihi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 1618

Walamma balagha ashuddahu ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineen

# 1619

Warawadathu allatee huwa fee baytiha 'an nafsihi waghallaqati alabwaba waqalat hayta laka qala ma'atha Allahi innahu rabbee ahsana mathwaya innahu la yuflihu aththalimoon

# 1620

Walaqad hammat bihi wahamma biha lawla an raa burhana rabbihi kathalika linasrifa 'anhu assooa walfahshaa innahu min 'ibadina almukhlaseen

# 1621

Wastabaqa albaba waqaddat qameesahu min duburin waalfaya sayyidaha lada albabi qalat ma jazao man arada biahlika sooan illa an yusjana aw 'athabun aleem

# 1622

Qala hiya rawadatnee 'an nafsee washahida shahidun min ahliha in kana qameesuhu qudda min qubulin fasadaqat wahuwa mina alkathibeen

# 1623

Wain kana qameesuhu qudda min duburin fakathabat wahuwa mina assadiqeen

# 1624

Falamma raa qameesahu qudda min duburin qala innahu min kaydikunna inna kaydakunna 'atheem

# 1625

Yoosufu a'rid 'an hatha wastaghfiree lithanbiki innaki kunti mina alkhatieen

# 1626

Waqala niswatun fee almadeenati imraatu al'azeezi turawidu fataha 'an nafsihi qad shaghafaha hubban inna lanaraha fee dalalin mubeen

# 1627

Falamma sami'at bimakrihinna arsalat ilayhinna waa'tadat lahunna muttakaan waatat kulla wahidatin minhunna sikkeenan waqalati okhruj 'alayhinna falamma raaynahu akbarnahu waqatta'na aydiyahunna waqulna hasha lillahi ma hatha basharan in hatha illa malakun kareem

# 1628

Qalat fathalikunna allathee lumtunnanee feehi walaqad rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi fast'sama walain lam yaf'al ma amuruhu layusjananna walayakoonan mina assaghireen

# 1629

Qala rabbi assijnu ahabbu ilayya mimma yad'oonanee ilayhi wailla tasrif 'annee kaydahunna asbu ilayhinna waakun mina aljahileen

# 1630

Fastajaba lahu rabbuhu fasarafa 'anhu kaydahunna innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 1631

Thumma bada lahum min ba'di ma raawoo alayati layasjununnahu hatta heen

# 1632

Wadakhala ma'ahu assijna fatayani qala ahaduhuma innee aranee a'siru khamran waqala alakharu innee aranee ahmilu fawqa rasee khubzan takulu attayru minhu nabbina bitaweelihi inna naraka mina almuhsineen

# 1633

Qala la yateekuma ta'amun turzaqanihi illa nabbatukuma bitaweelihi qabla an yatiyakuma thalikuma mimma 'allamanee rabbee innee taraktu millata qawmin la yuminoona billahi wahum bilakhirati hum kafiroon

# 1634

Wattaba'tu millata abaee ibraheema waishaqa waya'qooba ma kana lana an nushrika billahi min shayin thalika min fadli Allahi 'alayna wa'ala annasi walakinna akthara annasi la yashkuroon

# 1635

Ya sahibayi assijni aarbabun mutafarriqoona khayrun ami Allahu alwahidu alqahhar

# 1636

Ma ta'budoona min doonihi illa asmaan sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma anzala Allahu biha min sultanin ini alhukmu illa lillahi amara alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu thalika addeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 1637

Ya sahibayi assijni amma ahadukuma fayasqee rabbahu khamran waamma alakharu fayuslabu fatakulu attayru min rasihi qudiya alamru allathee feehi tastaftiyan

# 1638

Waqala lillathee thanna annahu najin minhuma othkurnee 'inda rabbika faansahu ashshaytanu thikra rabbihi falabitha fee assijni bid'a sineen

# 1639

Waqala almaliku innee ara sab'a baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'a sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee ruyaya in kuntum lirruya ta'buroon

# 1640

Qaloo adghathu ahlamin wama nahnu bitaweeli alahlami bi'alimeen

# 1641

Waqala allathee naja minhuma waddakara ba'da ommatin ana onabbiokum bitaweelihi faarsiloon

# 1642

Yoosufu ayyuha assiddeequ aftina fee sab'i baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'i sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin la'allee arji'u ila annasi la'allahum ya'lamoon

# 1643

Qala tazra'oona sab'a sineena daaban fama hasadtum fatharoohu fee sunbulihi illa qaleelan mimma takuloon

# 1644

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika sab'un shidadun yakulna ma qaddamtum lahunna illa qaleelan mimma tuhsinoon

# 1645

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika 'amun feehi yughathu annasu wafeehi ya'siroon

# 1646

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi falamma jaahu arrasoolu qala irji' ila rabbika fasalhu ma balu anniswati allatee qatta'na aydiyahunna inna rabbee bikaydihinna 'aleem

# 1647

Qala ma khatbukunna ith rawadtunna yoosufa 'an nafsihi qulna hasha lillahi ma 'alimna 'alayhi min sooin qalati imraatu al'azeezi alana hashasa alhaqqu ana rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi wainnahu lamina assadiqeen

# 1648

Thalika liya'lama annee lam akhunhu bilghaybi waanna Allaha la yahdee kayda alkhaineen

# 1649

Wama obarrio nafsee inna annafsa laammaratun bissooi illa ma rahima rabbee inna rabbee ghafoorun raheem

# 1650

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi astakhlishu linafsee falamma kallamahu qala innaka alyawma ladayna makeenun ameen

# 1651

Qala ij'alnee 'ala khazaini alardi innee hafeethun 'aleem

# 1652

Wakathalika makanna liyoosufa fee alardi yatabawwao minha haythu yashao nuseebu birahmatina man nashao wala nudee'u ajra almuhsineen

# 1653

Walaajru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon

# 1654

Wajaa ikhwatu yoosufa fadakhaloo 'alayhi fa'arafahum wahum lahu munkiroon

# 1655

Walamma jahhazahum bijahazihim qala itoonee biakhin lakum min abeekum ala tarawna annee oofee alkayla waana khayru almunzileen

# 1656

Fain lam tatoonee bihi fala kayla lakum 'indee wala taqraboon

# 1657

Qaloo sanurawidu 'anhu abahu wainna lafa'iloon

# 1658

Waqala lifityanihi ij'aloo bida'atahum fee rihalihim la'allahum ya'rifoonaha itha inqalaboo ila ahlihim la'allahum yarji'oon

# 1659

Falamma raja'oo ila abeehim qaloo ya abana muni'a minna alkaylu faarsil ma'ana akhana naktal wainna lahu lahafithoon

# 1660

Qala hal amanukum 'alayhi illa kama amintukum 'ala akheehi min qablu fallahu khayrun hafithan wahuwa arhamu arrahimeen

# 1661

Walamma fatahoo mata'ahum wajadoo bida'atahum ruddat ilayhim qaloo ya abana ma nabghee hathihi bida'atuna ruddat ilayna wanameeru ahlana wanahfathu akhana wanazdadu kayla ba'eerin thalika kaylun yaseer

# 1662

Qala lan orsilahu ma'akum hatta tutooni mawthiqan mina Allahi latatunnanee bihi illa an yuhata bikum falamma atawhu mawthiqahum qala Allahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeel

# 1663

Waqala ya baniyya la tadkhuloo min babin wahidin wadkhuloo min abwabin mutafarriqatin wama oghnee 'ankum mina Allahi min shayin ini alhukmu illa lillahi 'alayhi tawakkaltu wa'alayhi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloon

# 1664

Walamma dakhaloo min haythu amarahum aboohum ma kana yughnee 'anhum mina Allahi min shayin illa hajatan fee nafsi ya'qooba qadaha wainnahu lathoo 'ilmin lima 'allamnahu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 1665

Walamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi akhahu qala innee ana akhooka fala tabtais bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 1666

Falamma jahhazahum bijahazihim ja'ala assiqayata fee rahli akheehi thumma aththana muaththinun ayyatuha al'eeru innakum lasariqoon

# 1667

Qaloo waaqbaloo 'alayhim matha tafqidoon

# 1668

Qaloo nafqidu suwa'a almaliki waliman jaa bihi himlu ba'eerin waana bihi za'eem

# 1669

Qaloo tallahi laqad 'alimtum ma jina linufsida fee alardi wama kunna sariqeen

# 1670

Qaloo fama jazaohu in kuntum kathibeen

# 1671

Qaloo jazaohu man wujida fee rahlihi fahuwa jazaohu kathalika najzee aththalimeen

# 1672

Fabadaa biaw'iyatihim qabla wi'ai akheehi thumma istakhrajaha min wi'ai akheehi kathalika kidna liyoosufa ma kana liyakhutha akhahu fee deeni almaliki illa an yashaa Allahu narfa'u darajatin man nashao wafawqa kulli thee 'ilmin 'aleem

# 1673

Qaloo in yasriq faqad saraqa akhun lahu min qablu faasarraha yoosufu fee nafsihi walam yubdiha lahum qala antum sharrun makanan wallahu a'lamu bima tasifoon

# 1674

Qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu inna lahu aban shaykhan kabeeran fakhuth ahadana makanahu inna naraka mina almuhsineen

# 1675

Qala ma'atha Allahi an nakhutha illa man wajadna mata'ana 'indahu inna ithan lathalimoon

# 1676

Falamma istayasoo minhu khalasoo najiyyan qala kabeeruhum alam ta'lamoo anna abakum qad akhatha 'alaykum mawthiqan mina Allahi wamin qablu ma farrattum fee yoosufa falan abraha alarda hatta yathana lee abee aw yahkuma Allahu lee wahuwa khayru alhakimeen

# 1677

Irji'oo ila abeekum faqooloo ya abana inna ibnaka saraqa wama shahidna illa bima 'alimna wama kunna lilghaybi hafitheen

# 1678

Wasali alqaryata allatee kunna feeha wal'eera allatee aqbalna feeha wainna lasadiqoon

# 1679

Qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun 'asa Allahu an yatiyanee bihim jamee'an innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeem

# 1680

Watawalla 'anhum waqala ya asafa 'ala yoosufa wabyaddat 'aynahu mina alhuzni fahuwa katheem

# 1681

Qaloo tallahi taftao tathkuru yoosufa hatta takoona haradan aw takoona mina alhalikeen

# 1682

Qala innama ashkoo baththee wahuznee ila Allahi waa'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 1683

Ya baniyya ithhaboo fatahassasoo min yoosufa waakheehi wala tayasoo min rawhi Allahi innahu la yayasu min rawhi Allahi illa alqawmu alkafiroon

# 1684

Falamma dakhaloo 'alayhi qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu massana waahlana addurru wajina bibida'atin muzjatin faawfi lana alkayla watasaddaq 'alayna inna Allaha yajzee almutasaddiqeen

# 1685

Qala hal 'alimtum ma fa'altum biyoosufa waakheehi ith antum jahiloon

# 1686

Qaloo ainnaka laanta yoosufa qala ana yoosufu wahatha akhee qad manna Allahu 'alayna innahu man yattaqi wayasbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineen

# 1687

Qaloo tallahi laqad atharaka Allahu 'alayna wain kunna lakhatieen

# 1688

Qala la tathreeba 'alaykumu alyawma yaghfiru Allahu lakum wahuwa arhamu arrahimeen

# 1689

Ithhaboo biqameesee hatha faalqoohu 'ala wajhi abee yati baseeran watoonee biahlikum ajma'een

# 1690

Walamma fasalati al'eeru qala aboohum innee laajidu reeha yoosufa lawla an tufannidoon

# 1691

Qaloo tallahi innaka lafee dalalika alqadeem

# 1692

Falamma an jaa albasheeru alqahu 'ala wajhihi fartadda baseeran qala alam aqul lakum innee a'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoon

# 1693

Qaloo ya abana istaghfir lana thunoobana inna kunna khatieen

# 1694

Qala sawfa astaghfiru lakum rabbee innahu huwa alghafooru arraheem

# 1695

Falamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi abawayhi waqala odkhuloo misra in shaa Allahu amineen

# 1696

Warafa'a abawayhi 'ala al'arshi wakharroo lahu sujjadan waqala ya abati hatha taweelu ruyaya min qablu qad ja'alaha rabbee haqqan waqad ahsana bee ith akhrajanee mina assijni wajaa bikum mina albadwi min ba'di an nazagha ashshaytanu baynee wabayna ikhwatee inna rabbee lateefun lima yashao innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeem

# 1697

Rabbi qad ataytanee mina almulki wa'allamtanee min taweeli alahadeethi fatira assamawati walardi anta waliyyee fee addunya walakhirati tawaffanee musliman waalhiqnee bissaliheen

# 1698

Thalika min anbai alghaybi nooheehi ilayka wama kunta ladayhim ith ajma'oo amrahum wahum yamkuroon

# 1699

Wama aktharu annasi walaw harasta bimumineen

# 1700

Wama tasaluhum 'alayhi min ajrin in huwa illa thikrun lil'alameen

# 1701

Wakaayyin min ayatin fee assamawati walardi yamurroona 'alayha wahum 'anha mu'ridoon

# 1702

Wama yuminu aktharuhum billahi illa wahum mushrikoon

# 1703

Afaaminoo an tatiyahum ghashiyatun min 'athabi Allahi aw tatiyahumu assa'atu baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon

# 1704

Qul hathihi sabeelee ad'oo ila Allahi 'ala baseeratin ana wamani ittaba'anee wasubhana Allahi wama ana mina almushrikeen

# 1705

Wama arsalna min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim min ahli alqura afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim waladaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena ittaqaw afala ta'qiloon

# 1706

Hatta itha istayasa arrusulu wathannoo annahum qad kuthiboo jaahum nasruna fanujjiya man nashao wala yuraddu basuna 'ani alqawmi almujrimeen

# 1707

Laqad kana fee qasasihim 'ibratun liolee alalbabi ma kana hadeethan yuftara walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela kulli shayin wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoon

# 1708

Aliflammeemra tilka ayatu alkitabi wallathee onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoon

# 1709

Allahu allathee rafa'a assamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi wasakhkhara ashshamsa walqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman yudabbiru alamra yufassilu alayati la'allakum biliqai rabbikum tooqinoon

# 1710

Wahuwa allathee madda alarda waja'ala feeha rawasiya waanharan wamin kulli aththamarati ja'ala feeha zawjayni ithnayni yughshee allayla annahara inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 1711

Wafee alardi qita'un mutajawiratun wajannatun min a'nabin wazar'un wanakheelun sinwanun waghayru sinwanin yusqa bimain wahidin wanufaddilu ba'daha 'ala ba'din fee alokuli inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 1712

Wain ta'jab fa'ajabun qawluhum aitha kunna turaban ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin olaika allatheena kafaroo birabbihim waolaika alaghlalu fee a'naqihim waolaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoon

# 1713

Wayasta'jiloonaka bissayyiati qabla alhasanati waqad khalat min qablihimu almathulatu wainna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin linnasi 'ala thulmihim wainna rabbaka lashadeedu al'iqab

# 1714

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi innama anta munthirun walikulli qawmin had

# 1715

Allahu ya'lamu ma tahmilu kullu ontha wama tagheedu alarhamu wama tazdadu wakullu shayin 'indahu bimiqdar

# 1716

'alimu alghaybi washshahadati alkabeeru almuta'al

# 1717

Sawaon minkum man asarra alqawla waman jahara bihi waman huwa mustakhfin billayli wasaribun binnahar

# 1718

Lahu mu'aqqibatun min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi yahfathoonahu min amri Allahi inna Allaha la yughayyiru ma biqawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waitha arada Allahu biqawmin sooan fala maradda lahu wama lahum min doonihi min wal

# 1719

Huwa allathee yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunshio assahaba aththiqal

# 1720

Wayusabbihu arra'du bihamdihi walmalaikatu min kheefatihi wayursilu assawa'iqa fayuseebu biha man yashao wahum yujadiloona fee Allahi wahuwa shadeedu almihal

# 1721

Lahu da'watu alhaqqi wallatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yastajeeboona lahum bishayin illa kabasiti kaffayhi ila almai liyablugha fahu wama huwa bibalighihi wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalal

# 1722

Walillahi yasjudu man fee assamawati walardi taw'an wakarhan wathilaluhum bilghuduwwi walasal

# 1723

Qul man rabbu assamawati walardi quli Allahu qul afattakhathtum min doonihi awliyaa la yamlikoona lianfusihim naf'an wala darran qul hal yastawee ala'ma walbaseeru am hal tastawee aththulumatu wannooru am ja'aloo lillahi shurakaa khalaqoo kakhalqihi fatashabaha alkhalqu 'alayhim quli Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa alwahidu alqahhar

# 1724

Anzala mina assamai maan fasalat awdiyatun biqadariha fahtamala assaylu zabadan rabiyan wamimma yooqidoona 'alayhi fee annari ibtighaa hilyatin aw mata'in zabadun mithluhu kathalika yadribu Allahu alhaqqa walbatila faamma azzabadu fayathhabu jufaan waamma ma yanfa'u annasa fayamkuthu fee alardi kathalika yadribu Allahu alamthal

# 1725

Lillatheena istajaboo lirabbihimu alhusna wallatheena lam yastajeeboo lahu law anna lahum ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu laftadaw bihi olaika lahum sooo alhisabi wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almihad

# 1726

Afaman ya'lamu annama onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu kaman huwa a'ma innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbab

# 1727

Allatheena yoofoona bi'ahdi Allahi wala yanqudoona almeethaq

# 1728

Wallatheena yasiloona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayakhshawna rabbahum wayakhafoona sooa alhisab

# 1729

Wallatheena sabaroo ibtighaa wajhi rabbihim waaqamoo assalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan wayadraoona bilhasanati assayyiata olaika lahum 'uqba addar

# 1730

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim walmalaikatu yadkhuloona 'alayhim min kulli bab

# 1731

Salamun 'alaykum bima sabartum fani'ma 'uqba addar

# 1732

Wallatheena yanqudoona 'ahda Allahi min ba'di meethaqihi wayaqta'oona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayufsidoona fee alardi olaika lahumu alla'natu walahum sooo addar

# 1733

Allahu yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru wafarihoo bilhayati addunya wama alhayatu addunya fee alakhirati illa mata'

# 1734

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man anab

# 1735

Allatheena amanoo watatmainnu quloobuhum bithikri Allahi ala bithikri Allahi tatmainnu alquloob

# 1736

Allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati tooba lahum wahusnu maab

# 1737

Kathalika arsalnaka fee ommatin qad khalat min qabliha omamun litatluwa 'alayhimu allathee awhayna ilayka wahum yakfuroona birrahmani qul huwa rabbee la ilaha illa huwa 'alayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi matab

# 1738

Walaw anna quranan suyyirat bihi aljibalu aw qutti'at bihi alardu aw kullima bihi almawta bal lillahi alamru jamee'an afalam yayasi allatheena amanoo an law yashao Allahu lahada annasa jamee'an wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo tuseebuhum bima sana'oo qari'atun aw tahullu qareeban min darihim hatta yatiya wa'du Allahi inna Allaha la yukhlifu almee'ad

# 1739

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika faamlaytu lillatheena kafaroo thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqab

# 1740

Afaman huwa qaimun 'ala kulli nafsin bima kasabat waja'aloo lillahi shurakaa qul sammoohum am tunabbioonahu bima la ya'lamu fee alardi am bithahirin mina alqawli bal zuyyina lillatheena kafaroo makruhum wasuddoo 'ani assabeeli waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had

# 1741

Lahum 'athabun fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati ashaqqu wama lahum mina Allahi min waq

# 1742

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona tajree min tahtiha alanharu okuluha daimun wathilluha tilka 'uqba allatheena ittaqaw wa'uqba alkafireena annar

# 1743

Wallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yafrahoona bima onzila ilayka wamina alahzabi man yunkiru ba'dahu qul innama omirtu an a'buda Allaha wala oshrika bihi ilayhi ad'oo wailayhi maab

# 1744

Wakathalika anzalnahu hukman 'arabiyyan walaini ittaba'ta ahwaahum ba'da ma jaaka mina al'ilmi ma laka mina Allahi min waliyyin wala waq

# 1745

Walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika waja'alna lahum azwajan wathurriyyatan wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi likulli ajalin kitab

# 1746

Yamhoo Allahu ma yashao wayuthbitu wa'indahu ommu alkitab

# 1747

Wain ma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka fainnama 'alayka albalaghu wa'alayna alhisab

# 1748

Awalam yaraw anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha wallahu yahkumu la mu'aqqiba lihukmihi wahuwa saree'u alhisab

# 1749

Waqad makara allatheena min qablihim falillahi almakru jamee'an ya'lamu ma taksibu kullu nafsin wasaya'lamu alkuffaru liman 'uqba addar

# 1750

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lasta mursalan qul kafa billahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum waman 'indahu 'ilmu alkitab

# 1751

Aliflamra kitabun anzalnahu ilayka litukhrija annasa mina aththulumati ila annoori biithni rabbihim ila sirati al'azeezi alhameed

# 1752

Allahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wawaylun lilkafireena min 'athabin shadeed

# 1753

Allatheena yastahibboona alhayata addunya 'ala alakhirati wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan olaika fee dalalin ba'eed

# 1754

Wama arsalna min rasoolin illa bilisani qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayudillu Allahu man yashao wayahdee man yashao wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 1755

Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina an akhrij qawmaka mina aththulumati ila annoori wathakkirhum biayyami Allahi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor

# 1756

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith anjakum min ali fir'awna yasoomoonakum sooa al'athabi wayuthabbihoona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum 'atheem

# 1757

Waith taaththana rabbukum lain shakartum laazeedannakum walain kafartum inna 'athabee lashadeed

# 1758

Waqala moosa in takfuroo antum waman fee alardi jamee'an fainna Allaha laghaniyyun hameed

# 1759

Alam yatikum nabao allatheena min qablikum qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda wallatheena min ba'dihim la ya'lamuhum illa Allahu jaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati faraddoo aydiyahum fee afwahihim waqaloo inna kafarna bima orsiltum bihi wainna lafee shakkin mimma tad'oonana ilayhi mureeb

# 1760

Qalat rusuluhum afee Allahi shakkun fatiri assamawati walardi yad'ookum liyaghfira lakum min thunoobikum wayuakhkhirakum ila ajalin musamman qaloo in antum illa basharun mithluna tureedoona an tasuddoona 'amma kana ya'budu abaona fatoona bisultanin mubeen

# 1761

Qalat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa basharun mithlukum walakinna Allaha yamunnu 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi wama kana lana an natiyakum bisultanin illa biithni Allahi wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon

# 1762

Wama lana alla natawakkala 'ala Allahi waqad hadana subulana walanasbiranna 'ala ma athaytumoona wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloon

# 1763

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lirusulihim lanukhrijannakum min ardina aw lata'oodunna fee millatina faawha ilayhim rabbuhum lanuhlikanna aththalimeen

# 1764

Walanuskinannakumu alarda min ba'dihim thalika liman khafa maqamee wakhafa wa'eed

# 1765

Wastaftahoo wakhaba kullu jabbarin 'aneed

# 1766

Min waraihi jahannamu wayusqa min main sadeed

# 1767

Yatajarra'uhu wala yakadu yuseeghuhu wayateehi almawtu min kulli makanin wama huwa bimayyitin wamin waraihi 'athabun ghaleeth

# 1768

Mathalu allatheena kafaroo birabbihim a'maluhum karamadin ishtaddat bihi arreehu fee yawmin 'asifin la yaqdiroona mimma kasaboo 'ala shayin thalika huwa addalalu alba'eed

# 1769

Alam tara anna Allaha khalaqa assamawati walarda bilhaqqi in yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed

# 1770

Wama thalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeez

# 1771

Wabarazoo lillahi jamee'an faqala addu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna min 'athabi Allahi min shayin qaloo law hadana Allahu lahadaynakum sawaon 'alayna ajazi'na am sabarna ma lana min mahees

# 1772

Waqala ashshaytanu lamma qudiya alamru inna Allaha wa'adakum wa'da alhaqqi wawa'adtukum faakhlaftukum wama kana liya 'alaykum min sultanin illa an da'awtukum fastajabtum lee fala taloomoonee waloomoo anfusakum ma ana bimusrikhikum wama antum bimusrikhiyya innee kafartu bima ashraktumooni min qablu inna aththalimeena lahum 'athabun aleem

# 1773

Waodkhila allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha biithni rabbihim tahiyyatuhum feeha salam

# 1774

Alam tara kayfa daraba Allahu mathalan kalimatan tayyibatan kashajaratin tayyibatin asluha thabitun wafar'uha fee assama

# 1775

Tutee okulaha kulla heenin biithni rabbiha wayadribu Allahu alamthala linnasi la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 1776

Wamathalu kalimatin khabeethatin kashajaratin khabeethatin ijtuththat min fawqi alardi ma laha min qarar

# 1777

Yuthabbitu Allahu allatheena amanoo bilqawli aththabiti fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati wayudillu Allahu aththalimeena wayaf'alu Allahu ma yasha

# 1778

Alam tara ila allatheena baddaloo ni'mata Allahi kufran waahalloo qawmahum dara albawar

# 1779

Jahannama yaslawnaha wabisa alqarar

# 1780

Waja'aloo lillahi andadan liyudilloo 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta'oo fainna maseerakum ila annar

# 1781

Qul li'ibadiya allatheena amanoo yuqeemoo assalata wayunfiqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun la bay'un feehi wala khilal

# 1782

Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda waanzala mina assamai maan faakhraja bihi mina aththamarati rizqan lakum wasakhkhara lakumu alfulka litajriya fee albahri biamrihi wasakhkhara lakumu alanhar

# 1783

Wasakhkhara lakumu ashshamsa walqamara daibayni wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wannahar

# 1784

Waatakum min kulli ma saaltumoohu wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna alinsana lathaloomun kaffar

# 1785

Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi ij'al hatha albalada aminan wajnubnee wabaniyya an na'buda alasnam

# 1786

Rabbi innahunna adlalna katheeran mina annasi faman tabi'anee fainnahu minnee waman 'asanee fainnaka ghafoorun raheem

# 1787

Rabbana innee askantu min thurriyyatee biwadin ghayri thee zar'in 'inda baytika almuharrami rabbana liyuqeemoo assalata faj'al afidatan mina annasi tahwee ilayhim warzuqhum mina aththamarati la'allahum yashkuroon

# 1788

Rabbana innaka ta'lamu ma nukhfee wama nu'linu wama yakhfa 'ala Allahi min shayin fee alardi wala fee assama

# 1789

Alhamdu lillahi allathee wahaba lee 'ala alkibari isma'eela waishaqa inna rabbee lasamee'u addu'a

# 1790

Rabbi ij'alnee muqeema assalati wamin thurriyyatee rabbana wtaqabbal du'a

# 1791

Rabbana ighfir lee waliwalidayya walilmumineena yawma yaqoomu alhisab

# 1792

Wala tahsabanna Allaha ghafilan 'amma ya'malu aththalimoona innama yuakhkhiruhum liyawmin tashkhasu feehi alabsar

# 1793

Muhti'eena muqni'ee ruoosihim la yartaddu ilayhim tarfuhum waafidatuhum hawa

# 1794

Waanthiri annasa yawma yateehimu al'athabu fayaqoolu allatheena thalamoo rabbana akhkhirna ila ajalin qareebin nujib da'wataka wanattabi'i arrusula awalam takoonoo aqsamtum min qablu ma lakum min zawal

# 1795

Wasakantum fee masakini allatheena thalamoo anfusahum watabayyana lakum kayfa fa'alna bihim wadarabna lakumu alamthal

# 1796

Waqad makaroo makrahum wa'inda Allahi makruhum wain kana makruhum litazoola minhu aljibal

# 1797

Fala tahsabanna Allaha mukhlifa wa'dihi rusulahu inna Allaha 'azeezun thoo intiqam

# 1798

Yawma tubaddalu alardu ghayra alardi wassamawatu wabarazoo lillahi alwahidi alqahhar

# 1799

Watara almujrimeena yawmaithin muqarraneena fee alasfad

# 1800

Sarabeeluhum min qatranin wataghsha wujoohahumu annar

# 1801

Liyajziya Allahu kulla nafsin ma kasabat inna Allaha saree'u alhisab

# 1802

Hatha balaghun linnasi waliyuntharoo bihi waliya'lamoo annama huwa ilahun wahidun waliyaththakkara oloo alalbab

# 1803

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi waquranin mubeen

# 1804

Rubama yawaddu allatheena kafaroo law kanoo muslimeen

# 1805

Tharhum yakuloo wayatamatta'oo wayulhihimu alamalu fasawfa ya'lamoon

# 1806

Wama ahlakna min qaryatin illa walaha kitabun ma'loom

# 1807

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroon

# 1808

Waqaloo ya ayyuha allathee nuzzila 'alayhi aththikru innaka lamajnoon

# 1809

Law ma tateena bilmalaikati in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 1810

Ma nunazzilu almalaikata illa bilhaqqi wama kanoo ithan munthareen

# 1811

Inna nahnu nazzalna aththikra wainna lahu lahafithoon

# 1812

Walaqad arsalna min qablika fee shiya'i alawwaleen

# 1813

Wama yateehim min rasoolin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 1814

Kathalika naslukuhu fee quloobi almujrimeen

# 1815

La yuminoona bihi waqad khalat sunnatu alawwaleen

# 1816

Walaw fatahna 'alayhim baban mina assamai fathalloo feehi ya'rujoon

# 1817

Laqaloo innama sukkirat absaruna bal nahnu qawmun mashooroon

# 1818

Walaqad ja'alna fee assamai buroojan wazayyannaha linnathireen

# 1819

Wahafithnaha min kulli shaytanin rajeem

# 1820

Illa mani istaraqa assam'a faatba'ahu shihabun mubeen

# 1821

Walarda madadnaha waalqayna feeha rawasiya waanbatna feeha min kulli shayin mawzoon

# 1822

Waja'alna lakum feeha ma'ayisha waman lastum lahu biraziqeen

# 1823

Wain min shayin illa 'indana khazainuhu wama nunazziluhu illa biqadarin ma'loom

# 1824

Waarsalna arriyaha lawaqiha faanzalna mina assamai maan faasqaynakumoohu wama antum lahu bikhazineen

# 1825

Wainna lanahnu nuhyee wanumeetu wanahnu alwarithoon

# 1826

Walaqad 'alimna almustaqdimeena minkum walaqad 'alimna almustakhireen

# 1827

Wainna rabbaka huwa yahshuruhum innahu hakeemun 'aleem

# 1828

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min salsalin min hamain masnoon

# 1829

Waljanna khalaqnahu min qablu min nari assamoom

# 1830

Waith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee khaliqun basharan min salsalin min hamain masnoon

# 1831

Faitha sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roohee faqa'oo lahu sajideen

# 1832

Fasajada almalaikatu kulluhum ajma'oon

# 1833

Illa ibleesa aba an yakoona ma'a assajideen

# 1834

Qala ya ibleesu ma laka alla takoona ma'a assajideen

# 1835

Qala lam akun liasjuda libasharin khalaqtahu min salsalin min hamain masnoon

# 1836

Qala fakhruj minha fainnaka rajeem

# 1837

Wainna 'alayka alla'nata ila yawmi addeen

# 1838

Qala rabbi faanthirnee ila yawmi yub'athoon

# 1839

Qala fainnaka mina almunthareen

# 1840

Ila yawmi alwaqti alma'loom

# 1841

Qala rabbi bima aghwaytanee laozayyinanna lahum fee alardi walaoghwiyannahum ajma'een

# 1842

Illa 'ibadaka minhumu almukhlaseen

# 1843

Qala hatha siratun 'alayya mustaqeem

# 1844

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun illa mani ittaba'aka mina alghaween

# 1845

Wainna jahannama lamaw'iduhum ajma'een

# 1846

Laha sab'atu abwabin likulli babin minhum juzon maqsoom

# 1847

Inna almuttaqeena fee jannatin wa'uyoon

# 1848

Odkhulooha bisalamin amineen

# 1849

Wanaza'na ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin ikhwanan 'ala sururin mutaqabileen

# 1850

La yamassuhum feeha nasabun wama hum minha bimukhrajeen

# 1851

Nabbi 'ibadee annee ana alghafooru arraheem

# 1852

Wa anna 'athabee huwa al'athabu alaleem

# 1853

Wanabbihum 'an dayfi ibraheem

# 1854

Ith dakhaloo 'alayhi faqaloo salaman qala inna minkum wajiloon

# 1855

Qaloo la tawjal inna nubashshiruka bighulamin 'aleem

# 1856

Qala abashshartumoonee 'ala an massaniya alkibaru fabima tubashshiroon

# 1857

Qaloo bashsharnaka bilhaqqi fala takun mina alqaniteen

# 1858

Qala waman yaqnatu min rahmati rabbihi illa addalloon

# 1859

Qala fama khatbukum ayyuha almursaloon

# 1860

Qaloo inna orsilna ila qawmin mujrimeen

# 1861

Illa ala lootin inna lamunajjoohum ajma'een

# 1862

Illa imraatahu qaddarna innaha lamina alghabireen

# 1863

Falamma jaa ala lootin almursaloon

# 1864

Qala innakum qawmun munkaroon

# 1865

Qaloo bal jinaka bima kanoo feehi yamtaroon

# 1866

Waataynaka bilhaqqi wainna lasadiqoon

# 1867

Faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli wattabi' adbarahum wala yaltafit minkum ahadun wamdoo haythu tumaroon

# 1868

Waqadayna ilayhi thalika alamra anna dabira haolai maqtoo'un musbiheen

# 1869

Wajaa ahlu almadeenati yastabshiroon

# 1870

Qala inna haolai dayfee fala tafdahoon

# 1871

Wattaqoo Allaha wala tukhzoon

# 1872

Qaloo awalam nanhaka 'ani al'alameen

# 1873

Qala haolai banatee in kuntum fa'ileen

# 1874

La'amruka innahum lafee sakratihim ya'mahoona

# 1875

Faakhathathumu assayhatu mushriqeen

# 1876

Faja'alna 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayhim hijaratan min sijjeel

# 1877

Inna fee thalika laayatin lilmutawassimeen

# 1878

Wainnaha labisabeelin muqeem

# 1879

Inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineen

# 1880

Wain kana ashabu alaykati lathalimeen

# 1881

Fantaqamna minhum wainnahuma labiimamin mubeen

# 1882

Walaqad kaththaba ashabu alhijri almursaleen

# 1883

Waataynahum ayatina fakanoo 'anha mu'rideen

# 1884

Wakanoo yanhitoona mina aljibali buyootan amineen

# 1885

Faakhathathumu assayhatu musbiheen

# 1886

Fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboon

# 1887

Wama khalaqna assamawati walarda wama baynahuma illa bilhaqqi wainna assa'ata laatiyatun fasfahi assafha aljameel

# 1888

Inna rabbaka huwa alkhallaqu al'aleem

# 1889

Walaqad ataynaka sab'an mina almathanee walqurana al'atheem

# 1890

La tamuddanna 'aynayka ila ma matta'na bihi azwajan minhum wala tahzan 'alayhim wakhfid janahaka lilmumineen

# 1891

Waqul innee ana annatheeru almubeen

# 1892

Kama anzalna 'ala almuqtasimeen

# 1893

Allatheena ja'aloo alqurana 'ideen

# 1894

Fawarabbika lanasalannahum ajma'een

# 1895

'amma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1896

Fasda' bima tumaru waa'rid 'ani almushrikeen

# 1897

Inna kafaynaka almustahzieen

# 1898

Allatheena yaj'aloona ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fasawfa ya'lamoon

# 1899

Walaqad na'lamu annaka yadeequ sadruka bima yaqooloon

# 1900

Fasabbih bihamdi rabbika wakun mina assajideen

# 1901

Wa'bud rabbaka hatta yatiyaka alyaqeen

# 1902

Ata amru Allahi fala tasta'jiloohu subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 1903

Yunazzilu almalaikata birroohi min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi an anthiroo annahu la ilaha illa ana fattaqoon

# 1904

Khalaqa assamawati walarda bilhaqqi ta'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 1905

Khalaqa alinsana min nutfatin faitha huwa khaseemun mubeen

# 1906

Walan'ama khalaqaha lakum feeha difon wamanafi'u waminha takuloon

# 1907

Walakum feeha jamalun heena tureehoona waheena tasrahoon

# 1908

Watahmilu athqalakum ila baladin lam takoonoo baligheehi illa bishiqqi alanfusi inna rabbakum laraoofun raheem

# 1909

Walkhayla walbighala walhameera litarkabooha wazeenatan wayakhluqu ma la ta'lamoon

# 1910

Wa'ala Allahi qasdu assabeeli waminha jairun walaw shaa lahadakum ajma'een

# 1911

Huwa allathee anzala mina assamai maan lakum minhu sharabun waminhu shajarun feehi tuseemoon

# 1912

Yunbitu lakum bihi azzar'a wazzaytoona wannakheela wala'naba wamin kulli aththamarati inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 1913

Wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wannahara washshamsa walqamara wannujoomu musakhkharatun biamrihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 1914

Wama tharaa lakum fee alardi mukhtalifan alwanuhu inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yaththakkaroon

# 1915

Wahuwa allathee sakhkhara albahra litakuloo minhu lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoo minhu hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka mawakhira feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon

# 1916

Waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum waanharan wasubulan la'allakum tahtadoon

# 1917

Wa'alamatin wabinnajmi hum yahtadoon

# 1918

Afaman yakhluqu kaman la yakhluqu afala tathakkaroon

# 1919

Wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna Allaha laghafoorun raheem

# 1920

Wallahu ya'lamu ma tusirroona wama tu'linoon

# 1921

Wallatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoon

# 1922

Amwatun ghayru ahyain wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoon

# 1923

Ilahukum ilahun wahidun fallatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati quloobuhum munkiratun wahum mustakbiroon

# 1924

La jarama anna Allaha ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu la yuhibbu almustakbireen

# 1925

Waitha qeela lahum matha anzala rabbukum qaloo asateeru alawwaleen

# 1926

Liyahmiloo awzarahum kamilatan yawma alqiyamati wamin awzari allatheena yudilloonahum bighayri 'ilmin ala saa ma yaziroon

# 1927

Qad makara allatheena min qablihim faata Allahu bunyanahum mina alqawa'idi fakharra 'alayhimu assaqfu min fawqihim waatahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroon

# 1928

Thumma yawma alqiyamati yukhzeehim wayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tushaqqoona feehim qala allatheena ootoo al'ilma inna alkhizya alyawma wassooa 'ala alkafireen

# 1929

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu thalimee anfusihim faalqawoo assalama ma kunna na'malu min sooin bala inna Allaha 'aleemun bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 1930

Fadkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha falabisa mathwa almutakabbireen

# 1931

Waqeela lillatheena ittaqaw matha anzala rabbukum qaloo khayran lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi addunya hasanatun waladaru alakhirati khayrun walani'ma daru almuttaqeen

# 1932

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha tajree min tahtiha alanharu lahum feeha ma yashaoona kathalika yajzee Allahu almuttaqeen

# 1933

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu tayyibeena yaqooloona salamun 'alaykumu odkhuloo aljannata bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 1934

Hal yanthuroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim wama thalamahumu Allahu walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 1935

Faasabahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 1936

Waqala allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma 'abadna min doonihi min shayin nahnu wala abaona wala harramna min doonihi min shayin kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim fahal 'ala arrusuli illa albalaghu almubeen

# 1937

Walaqad ba'athna fee kulli ommatin rasoolan ani o'budoo Allaha wajtaniboo attaghoota faminhum man hada Allahu waminhum man haqqat 'alayhi addalalatu faseeroo fee alardi fanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeen

# 1938

In tahris 'ala hudahum fainna Allaha la yahdee man yudillu wama lahum min nasireen

# 1939

Waaqsamoo billahi jahda aymanihim la yab'athu Allahu man yamootu bala wa'dan 'alayhi haqqan walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 1940

Liyubayyina lahumu allathee yakhtalifoona feehi waliya'lama allatheena kafaroo annahum kanoo kathibeen

# 1941

Innama qawluna lishayin itha aradnahu an naqoola lahu kun fayakoon

# 1942

Wallatheena hajaroo fee Allahi min ba'di ma thulimoo lanubawwiannahum fee addunya hasanatan walaajru alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoon

# 1943

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon

# 1944

Wama arsalna min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim fasaloo ahla aththikri in kuntum la ta'lamoon

# 1945

Bilbayyinati wazzuburi waanzalna ilayka aththikra litubayyina linnasi ma nuzzila ilayhim wala'allahum yatafakkaroon

# 1946

Afaamina allatheena makaroo assayyiati an yakhsifa Allahu bihimu alarda aw yatiyahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroon

# 1947

Aw yakhuthahum fee taqallubihim fama hum bimu'jizeen

# 1948

Aw yakhuthahum 'ala takhawwufin fainna rabbakum laraoofun raheem

# 1949

Awa lam yaraw ila ma khalaqa Allahu min shayin yatafayyao thilaluhu 'ani alyameeni washshamaili sujjadan lillahi wahum dakhiroon

# 1950

Walillahi yasjudu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi min dabbatin walmalaikatu wahum la yastakbiroon

# 1951

Yakhafoona rabbahum min fawqihim wayaf'aloona ma yumaroon

# 1952

Waqala Allahu la tattakhithoo ilahayni ithnayni innama huwa ilahun wahidun faiyyaya farhaboon

# 1953

Walahu ma fee assamawati walardi walahu addeenu wasiban afaghayra Allahi tattaqoon

# 1954

Wama bikum min ni'matin famina Allahi thumma itha massakumu addurru failayhi tajaroon

# 1955

Thumma itha kashafa addurra 'ankum itha fareequn minkum birabbihim yushrikoon

# 1956

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoon

# 1957

Wayaj'aloona lima la ya'lamoona naseeban mimma razaqnahum tallahi latusalunna 'amma kuntum taftaroon

# 1958

Wayaj'aloona lillahi albanati subhanahu walahum ma yashtahoon

# 1959

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bilontha thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheem

# 1960

Yatawara mina alqawmi min sooi ma bushshira bihi ayumsikuhu 'ala hoonin am yadussuhu fee atturabi ala saa ma yahkumoon

# 1961

Lillatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati mathalu assawi walillahi almathalu ala'la wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 1962

Walaw yuakhithu Allahu annasa bithulmihim ma taraka 'alayha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoon

# 1963

Wayaj'aloona lillahi ma yakrahoona watasifu alsinatuhumu alkathiba anna lahumu alhusna la jarama anna lahumu annara waannahum mufratoon

# 1964

Tallahi laqad arsalna ila omamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu alyawma walahum 'athabun aleem

# 1965

Wama anzalna 'alayka alkitaba illa litubayyina lahumu allathee ikhtalafoo feehi wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoon

# 1966

Wallahu anzala mina assamai maan faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yasma'oon

# 1967

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butoonihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan khalisan saighan lishsharibeen

# 1968

Wamin thamarati annakheeli wala'nabi tattakhithoona minhu sakaran warizqan hasanan inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 1969

Waawha rabbuka ila annahli ani ittakhithee mina aljibali buyootan wamina ashshajari wamimma ya'rishoon

# 1970

Thumma kulee min kulli aththamarati faslukee subula rabbiki thululan yakhruju min butooniha sharabun mukhtalifun alwanuhu feehi shifaon linnasi inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 1971

Wallahu khalaqakum thumma yatawaffakum waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likay la ya'lama ba'da 'ilmin shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun qadeer

# 1972

Wallahu faddala ba'dakum 'ala ba'din fee arrizqi fama allatheena fuddiloo biraddee rizqihim 'ala ma malakat aymanuhum fahum feehi sawaon afabini'mati Allahi yajhadoon

# 1973

Wallahu ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan waja'ala lakum min azwajikum baneena wahafadatan warazaqakum mina attayyibati afabilbatili yuminoona wabini'mati Allahi hum yakfuroon

# 1974

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lahum rizqan mina assamawati walardi shayan wala yastatee'oon

# 1975

Fala tadriboo lillahi alamthala inna Allaha ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoon

# 1976

Daraba Allahu mathalan 'abdan mamlookan la yaqdiru 'ala shayin waman razaqnahu minna rizqan hasanan fahuwa yunfiqu minhu sirran wajahran hal yastawoona alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon

# 1977

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan rajulayni ahaduhuma abkamu la yaqdiru 'ala shayin wahuwa kallun 'ala mawlahu aynama yuwajjihhu la yati bikhayrin hal yastawee huwa waman yamuru bil'adli wahuwa 'ala siratin mustaqeem

# 1978

Walillahi ghaybu assamawati walardi wama amru assa'ati illa kalamhi albasari aw huwa aqrabu inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 1979

Wallahu akhrajakum min butooni ommahatikum la ta'lamoona shayan waja'ala lakumu assam'a walabsara walafidata la'allakum tashkuroon

# 1980

Alam yaraw ila attayri musakhkharatin fee jawwi assamai ma yumsikuhunna illa Allahu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 1981

Wallahu ja'ala lakum min buyootikum sakanan waja'ala lakum min juloodi alan'ami buyootan tastakhiffoonaha yawma tha'nikum wayawma iqamatikum wamin aswafiha waawbariha waash'ariha athathan wamata'an ila heen

# 1982

Wallahu ja'ala lakum mimma khalaqa thilalan waja'ala lakum mina aljibali aknanan waja'ala lakum sarabeela taqeekumu alharra wasarabeela taqeekum basakum kathalika yutimmu ni'matahu 'alaykum la'allakum tuslimoon

# 1983

Fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayka albalaghu almubeen

# 1984

Ya'rifoona ni'mata Allahi thumma yunkiroonaha waaktharuhumu alkafiroon

# 1985

Wayawma nab'athu min kulli ommatin shaheedan thumma la yuthanu lillatheena kafaroo wala hum yusta'taboon

# 1986

Waitha raa allatheena thalamoo al'athaba fala yukhaffafu 'anhum wala hum yuntharoon

# 1987

Waitha raa allatheena ashrakoo shurakaahum qaloo rabbana haolai shurakaona allatheena kunna nad'oo min doonika faalqaw ilayhimu alqawla innakum lakathiboon

# 1988

Waalqaw ila Allahi yawmaithin assalama wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 1989

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi zidnahum 'athaban fawqa al'athabi bima kanoo yufsidoon

# 1990

Wayawma nab'athu fee kulli ommatin shaheedan 'alayhim min anfusihim wajina bika shaheedan 'ala haolai wanazzalna 'alayka alkitaba tibyanan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan wabushra lilmuslimeen

# 1991

Inna Allaha yamuru bil'adli walihsani waeetai thee alqurba wayanha 'ani alfahshai walmunkari walbaghyi ya'ithukum la'allakum tathakkaroon

# 1992

Waawfoo bi'ahdi Allahi itha 'ahadtum wala tanqudoo alaymana ba'da tawkeediha waqad ja'altumu Allaha 'alaykum kafeelan inna Allaha ya'lamu ma taf'aloon

# 1993

Wala takoonoo kallatee naqadat ghazlaha min ba'di quwwatin ankathan tattakhithoona aymanakum dakhalan baynakum an takoona ommatun hiya arba min ommatin innama yablookumu Allahu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma alqiyamati ma kuntum feehi takhtalifoon

# 1994

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alakum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao walatusalunna 'amma kuntum ta'maloon

# 1995

Wala tattakhithoo aymanakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun ba'da thubootiha watathooqoo assooa bima sadadtum 'an sabeeli Allahi walakum 'athabun 'atheem

# 1996

Wala tashtaroo bi'ahdi Allahi thamanan qaleelan innama 'inda Allahi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 1997

Ma 'indakum yanfadu wama 'inda Allahi baqin walanajziyanna allatheena sabaroo ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1998

Man 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun falanuhyiyannahu hayatan tayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 1999

Faitha qarata alqurana fasta'ith billahi mina ashshaytani arrajeem

# 2000

Innahu laysa lahu sultanun 'ala allatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon

# 2001

Innama sultanuhu 'ala allatheena yatawallawnahu wallatheena hum bihi mushrikoon

# 2002

Waitha baddalna ayatan makana ayatin wallahu a'lamu bima yunazzilu qaloo innama anta muftarin bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon

# 2003

Qul nazzalahu roohu alqudusi min rabbika bilhaqqi liyuthabbita allatheena amanoo wahudan wabushra lilmuslimeen

# 2004

Walaqad na'lamu annahum yaqooloona innama yu'allimuhu basharun lisanu allathee yulhidoona ilayhi a'jamiyyun wahatha lisanun 'arabiyyun mubeen

# 2005

Inna allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi la yahdeehimu Allahu walahum 'athabun aleem

# 2006

Innama yaftaree alkathiba allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi waolaika humu alkathiboon

# 2007

Man kafara billahi min ba'di eemanihi illa man okriha waqalbuhu mutmainnun bileemani walakin man sharaha bilkufri sadran fa'alayhim ghadabun mina Allahi walahum 'athabun 'atheem

# 2008

Thalika biannahumu istahabboo alhayata addunya 'ala alakhirati waanna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireen

# 2009

Olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim wasam'ihim waabsarihim waolaika humu alghafiloon

# 2010

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alkhasiroon

# 2011

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena hajaroo min ba'di ma futinoo thumma jahadoo wasabaroo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheem

# 2012

Yawma tatee kullu nafsin tujadilu 'an nafsiha watuwaffa kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahum la yuthlamoon

# 2013

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan qaryatan kanat aminatan mutmainnatan yateeha rizquha raghadan min kulli makanin fakafarat bian'umi Allahi faathaqaha Allahu libasa aljoo'i walkhawfi bima kanoo yasna'oon

# 2014

Walaqad jaahum rasoolun minhum fakaththaboohu faakhathahumu al'athabu wahum thalimoon

# 2015

Fakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban washkuroo ni'mata Allahi in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoon

# 2016

Innama harrama 'alaykumu almaytata waddama walahma alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala 'adin fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 2017

Wala taqooloo lima tasifu alsinatukumu alkathiba hatha halalun wahatha haramun litaftaroo 'ala Allahi alkathiba inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoon

# 2018

Mata'un qaleelun walahum 'athabun aleem

# 2019

Wa'ala allatheena hadoo harramna ma qasasna 'alayka min qablu wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 2020

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena 'amiloo assooa bijahalatin thumma taboo min ba'di thalika waaslahoo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheem

# 2021

Inna ibraheema kana ommatan qanitan lillahi haneefan walam yaku mina almushrikeen

# 2022

Shakiran lian'umihi ijtabahu wahadahu ila siratin mustaqeem

# 2023

Waataynahu fee addunya hasanatan wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina assaliheen

# 2024

Thumma awhayna ilayka ani ittabi' millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeen

# 2025

Innama ju'ila assabtu 'ala allatheena ikhtalafoo feehi wainna rabbaka layahkumu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon

# 2026

Od'u ila sabeeli rabbika bilhikmati walmaw'ithati alhasanati wajadilhum billatee hiya ahsanu inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bilmuhtadeen

# 2027

Wain 'aqabtum fa'aqiboo bimithli ma 'ooqibtum bihi walain sabartum lahuwa khayrun lissabireen

# 2028

Wasbir wama sabruka illa billahi wala tahzan 'alayhim wala taku fee dayqin mimma yamkuroon

# 2029

Inna Allaha ma'a allatheena ittaqaw wallatheena hum muhsinoon

# 2030

Subhana allathee asra bi'abdihi laylan mina almasjidi alharami ila almasjidi alaqsa allathee barakna hawlahu linuriyahu min ayatina innahu huwa assamee'u albaseer

# 2031

Waatayna moosa alkitaba waja'alnahu hudan libanee israeela alla tattakhithoo min doonee wakeela

# 2032

Thurriyyata man hamalna ma'a noohin innahu kana 'abdan shakoora

# 2033

Waqadayna ila banee israeela fee alkitabi latufsidunna fee alardi marratayni walata'lunna 'uluwwan kabeera

# 2034

Faitha jaa wa'du oolahuma ba'athna 'alaykum 'ibadan lana olee basin shadeedin fajasoo khilala addiyari wakana wa'dan maf'oola

# 2035

Thumma radadna lakumu alkarrata 'alayhim waamdadnakum biamwalin wabaneena waja'alnakum akthara nafeera

# 2036

In ahsantum ahsantum lianfusikum wain asatum falaha faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati liyasoooo wujoohakum waliyadkhuloo almasjida kama dakhaloohu awwala marratin waliyutabbiroo ma 'alaw tatbeera

# 2037

'asa rabbukum an yarhamakum wain 'udtum 'udna waja'alna jahannama lilkafireena haseera

# 2038

Inna hatha alqurana yahdee lillatee hiya aqwamu wayubashshiru almumineena allatheena ya'maloona assalihati anna lahum ajran kabeera

# 2039

Waanna allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati a'tadna lahum 'athaban aleema

# 2040

Wayad'u alinsanu bishsharri du'aahu bilkhayri wakana alinsanu 'ajoola

# 2041

Waja'alna allayla wannahara ayatayni famahawna ayata allayli waja'alna ayata annahari mubsiratan litabtaghoo fadlan min rabbikum walita'lamoo 'adada assineena walhisaba wakulla shayin fassalnahu tafseela

# 2042

Wakulla insanin alzamnahu tairahu fee 'unuqihi wanukhriju lahu yawma alqiyamati kitaban yalqahu manshoora

# 2043

Iqra kitabaka kafa binafsika alyawma 'alayka haseeba

# 2044

Mani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wama kunna mu'aththibeena hatta nab'atha rasoola

# 2045

Waitha aradna an nuhlika qaryatan amarna mutrafeeha fafasaqoo feeha fahaqqa 'alayha alqawlu fadammarnaha tadmeera

# 2046

Wakam ahlakna mina alqurooni min ba'di noohin wakafa birabbika bithunoobi 'ibadihi khabeeran baseera

# 2047

Man kana yureedu al'ajilata 'ajjalna lahu feeha ma nashao liman nureedu thumma ja'alna lahu jahannama yaslaha mathmooman madhoora

# 2048

Waman arada alakhirata wasa'a laha sa'yaha wahuwa muminun faolaika kana sa'yuhum mashkoora

# 2049

Kullan numiddu haolai wahaolai min 'atai rabbika wama kana 'atao rabbika mahthoora

# 2050

Onthur kayfa faddalna ba'dahum 'ala ba'din walalakhiratu akbaru darajatin waakbaru tafdeela

# 2051

La taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fataq'uda mathmooman makhthoola

# 2052

Waqada rabbuka alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu wabilwalidayni ihsanan imma yablughanna 'indaka alkibara ahaduhuma aw kilahuma fala taqul lahuma offin wala tanharhuma waqul lahuma qawlan kareema

# 2053

Wakhfid lahuma janaha aththulli mina arrahmati waqul rabbi irhamhuma kama rabbayanee sagheera

# 2054

Rabbukum a'lamu bima fee nufoosikum in takoonoo saliheena fainnahu kana lilawwabeena ghafoora

# 2055

Waati tha alqurba haqqahu walmiskeena wabna assabeeli wala tubaththir tabtheera

# 2056

Inna almubaththireena kanoo ikhwana ashshayateeni wakana ashshaytanu lirabbihi kafoora

# 2057

Waimma tu'ridanna 'anhumu ibtighaa rahmatin min rabbika tarjooha faqul lahum qawlan maysoora

# 2058

Wala taj'al yadaka maghloolatan ila 'unuqika wala tabsutha kulla albasti fataq'uda malooman mahsoora

# 2059

Inna rabbaka yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseera

# 2060

Wala taqtuloo awladakum khashyata imlaqin nahnu narzuquhum waiyyakum inna qatlahum kana khitan kabeera

# 2061

Wala taqraboo azzina innahu kana fahishatan wasaa sabeela

# 2062

Wala taqtuloo annafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bilhaqqi waman qutila mathlooman faqad ja'alna liwaliyyihi sultanan fala yusrif fee alqatli innahu kana mansoora

# 2063

Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa billatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo bil'ahdi inna al'ahda kana masoola

# 2064

Waawfoo alkayla itha kiltum wazinoo bilqistasi almustaqeemi thalika khayrun waahsanu taweela

# 2065

Wala taqfu ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun inna assam'a walbasara walfuada kullu olaika kana 'anhu masoola

# 2066

Wala tamshi fee alardi marahan innaka lan takhriqa alarda walan tablugha aljibala toola

# 2067

Kullu thalika kana sayyiohu 'inda rabbika makrooha

# 2068

Thalika mimma awha ilayka rabbuka mina alhikmati wala taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fatulqa fee jahannama malooman madhoora

# 2069

Afaasfakum rabbukum bilbaneena wattakhatha mina almalaikati inathan innakum lataqooloona qawlan 'atheema

# 2070

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani liyaththakkaroo wama yazeeduhum illa nufoora

# 2071

Qul law kana ma'ahu alihatun kama yaqooloona ithan labtaghaw ila thee al'arshi sabeela

# 2072

Subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yaqooloona 'uluwwan kabeera

# 2073

Tusabbihu lahu assamawatu assab'u walardu waman feehinna wain min shayin illa yusabbihu bihamdihi walakin la tafqahoona tasbeehahum innahu kana haleeman ghafoora

# 2074

Waitha qarata alqurana ja'alna baynaka wabayna allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati hijaban mastoora

# 2075

Waja'alna 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran waitha thakarta rabbaka fee alqurani wahdahu wallaw 'ala adbarihim nufoora

# 2076

Nahnu a'lamu bima yastami'oona bihi ith yastami'oona ilayka waith hum najwa ith yaqoolu aththalimoona in tattabi'oona illa rajulan mashoora

# 2077

Onthur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastatee'oona sabeela

# 2078

Waqaloo aitha kunna 'ithaman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeeda

# 2079

Qul koonoo hijaratan aw hadeeda

# 2080

Aw khalqan mimma yakburu fee sudoorikum fasayaqooloona man yu'eeduna quli allathee fatarakum awwala marratin fasayunghidoona ilayka ruoosahum wayaqooloona mata huwa qul 'asa an yakoona qareeba

# 2081

Yawma yad'ookum fatastajeeboona bihamdihi watathunnoona in labithtum illa qaleela

# 2082

Waqul li'ibadee yaqooloo allatee hiya ahsanu inna ashshaytana yanzaghu baynahum inna ashshaytana kana lilinsani 'aduwwan mubeena

# 2083

Rabbukum a'lamu bikum in yasha yarhamkum aw in yasha yu'aththibkum wama arsalnaka 'alayhim wakeela

# 2084

Warabbuka a'lamu biman fee assamawati walardi walaqad faddalna ba'da annabiyyeena 'ala ba'din waatayna dawooda zaboora

# 2085

Quli od'u allatheena za'amtum min doonihi fala yamlikoona kashfa addurri 'ankum wala tahweela

# 2086

Olaika allatheena yad'oona yabtaghoona ila rabbihimu alwaseelata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjoona rahmatahu wayakhafoona 'athabahu inna 'athaba rabbika kana mahthoora

# 2087

Wain min qaryatin illa nahnu muhlikooha qabla yawmi alqiyamati aw mu'aththibooha 'athaban shadeedan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastoora

# 2088

Wama mana'ana an nursila bilayati illa an kaththaba biha alawwaloona waatayna thamooda annaqata mubsiratan fathalamoo biha wama nursilu bilayati illa takhweefa

# 2089

Waith qulna laka inna rabbaka ahata binnasi wama ja'alna arruya allatee araynaka illa fitnatan linnasi washshajarata almal'oonata fee alqurani wanukhawwifuhum fama yazeeduhum illa tughyanan kabeera

# 2090

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa qala aasjudu liman khalaqta teena

# 2091

Qala araaytaka hatha allathee karramta 'alayya lain akhkhartani ila yawmi alqiyamati laahtanikanna thurriyyatahu illa qaleela

# 2092

Qala ithhab faman tabi'aka minhum fainna jahannama jazaokum jazaan mawfoora

# 2093

Wastafziz mani istata'ta minhum bisawtika waajlib 'alayhim bikhaylika warajlika washarikhum fee alamwali walawladi wa'idhum wama ya'iduhumu ashshaytanu illa ghuroora

# 2094

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun wakafa birabbika wakeela

# 2095

Rabbukumu allathee yuzjee lakumu alfulka fee albahri litabtaghoo min fadlihi innahu kana bikum raheema

# 2096

Waitha massakumu addurru fee albahri dalla man tad'oona illa iyyahu falamma najjakum ila albarri a'radtum wakana alinsanu kafoora

# 2097

Afaamintum an yakhsifa bikum janiba albarri aw yursila 'alaykum hasiban thumma la tajidoo lakum wakeela

# 2098

Am amintum an yu'eedakum feehi taratan okhra fayursila 'alaykum qasifan mina arreehi fayughriqakum bima kafartum thumma la tajidoo lakum 'alayna bihi tabee'a

# 2099

Walaqad karramna banee adama wahamalnahum fee albarri walbahri warazaqnahum mina attayyibati wafaddalnahum 'ala katheerin mimman khalaqna tafdeela

# 2100

Yawma nad'oo kulla onasin biimamihim faman ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi faolaika yaqraoona kitabahum wala yuthlamoona fateela

# 2101

Waman kana fee hathihi a'ma fahuwa fee alakhirati a'ma waadallu sabeela

# 2102

Wain kadoo layaftinoonaka 'ani allathee awhayna ilayka litaftariya 'alayna ghayrahu waithan lattakhathooka khaleela

# 2103

Walawla an thabbatnaka laqad kidta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qaleela

# 2104

Ithan laathaqnaka di'fa alhayati wadi'fa almamati thumma la tajidu laka 'alayna naseera

# 2105

Wain kadoo layastafizzoonaka mina alardi liyukhrijooka minha waithan la yalbathoona khilafaka illa qaleela

# 2106

Sunnata man qad arsalna qablaka min rusulina wala tajidu lisunnatina tahweela

# 2107

Aqimi assalata lidulooki ashshamsi ila ghasaqi allayli waqurana alfajri inna qurana alfajri kana mashhooda

# 2108

Wamina allayli fatahajjad bihi nafilatan laka 'asa an yab'athaka rabbuka maqaman mahmooda

# 2109

Waqul rabbi adkhilnee mudkhala sidqin waakhrijnee mukhraja sidqin waj'al lee min ladunka sultanan naseera

# 2110

Waqul jaa alhaqqu wazahaqa albatilu inna albatila kana zahooqa

# 2111

Wanunazzilu mina alqurani ma huwa shifaon warahmatun lilmumineena wala yazeedu aththalimeena illa khasara

# 2112

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu ashsharru kana yaoosa

# 2113

Qul kullun ya'malu 'ala shakilatihi farabbukum a'lamu biman huwa ahda sabeela

# 2114

Wayasaloonaka 'ani arroohi quli arroohu min amri rabbee wama ooteetum mina al'ilmi illa qaleela

# 2115

Walain shina lanathhabanna billathee awhayna ilayka thumma la tajidu laka bihi 'alayna wakeela

# 2116

Illa rahmatan min rabbika inna fadlahu kana 'alayka kabeera

# 2117

Qul laini ijtama'ati alinsu waljinnu 'ala an yatoo bimithli hatha alqurani la yatoona bimithlihi walaw kana ba'duhum liba'din thaheera

# 2118

Walaqad sarrafna linnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin faaba aktharu annasi illa kufoora

# 2119

Waqaloo lan numina laka hatta tafjura lana mina alardi yanboo'a

# 2120

Aw takoona laka jannatun min nakheelin wa'inabin fatufajjira alanhara khilalaha tafjeera

# 2121

Aw tusqita assamaa kama za'amta 'alayna kisafan aw tatiya billahi walmalaikati qabeela

# 2122

Aw yakoona laka baytun min zukhrufin aw tarqa fee assamai walan numina liruqiyyika hatta tunazzila 'alayna kitaban naqraohu qul subhana rabbee hal kuntu illa basharan rasoola

# 2123

Wama mana'a annasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda illa an qaloo aba'atha Allahu basharan rasoola

# 2124

Qul law kana fee alardi malaikatun yamshoona mutmainneena lanazzalna 'alayhim mina assamai malakan rasoola

# 2125

Qul kafa billahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseera

# 2126

Waman yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahum awliyaa min doonihi wanahshuruhum yawma alqiyamati 'ala wujoohihim 'umyan wabukman wasumman mawahum jahannamu kullama khabat zidnahum sa'eera

# 2127

Thalika jazaohum biannahum kafaroo biayatina waqaloo aitha kunna 'ithaman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeeda

# 2128

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda qadirun 'ala an yakhluqa mithlahum waja'ala lahum ajalan la rayba feehi faaba aththalimoona illa kufoora

# 2129

Qul law antum tamlikoona khazaina rahmati rabbee ithan laamsaktum khashyata alinfaqi wakana alinsanu qatoora

# 2130

Walaqad atayna moosa tis'a ayatin bayyinatin fasal banee israeela ith jaahum faqala lahu fir'awnu innee laathunnuka ya moosa mashoora

# 2131

Qala laqad 'alimta ma anzala haolai illa rabbu assamawati walardi basaira wainnee laathunnuka ya fir'awnu mathboora

# 2132

Faarada an yastafizzahum mina alardi faaghraqnahu waman ma'ahu jamee'a

# 2133

Waqulna min ba'dihi libanee israeela oskunoo alarda faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati jina bikum lafeefa

# 2134

Wabilhaqqi anzalnahu wabilhaqqi nazala wama arsalnaka illa mubashshiran wanatheera

# 2135

Waquranan faraqnahu litaqraahu 'ala annasi 'ala mukthin wanazzalnahu tanzeela

# 2136

Qul aminoo bihi aw la tuminoo inna allatheena ootoo al'ilma min qablihi itha yutla 'alayhim yakhirroona lilathqani sujjada

# 2137

Wayaqooloona subhana rabbina in kana wa'du rabbina lamaf'oola

# 2138

Wayakhirroona lilathqani yabkoona wayazeeduhum khushoo'a

# 2139

Quli od'oo Allaha awi od'oo arrahmana ayyan ma tad'oo falahu alasmao alhusna wala tajhar bisalatika wala tukhafit biha wabtaghi bayna thalika sabeela

# 2140

Waquli alhamdu lillahi allathee lam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina aththulli wakabbirhu takbeera

# 2141

Alhamdu lillahi allathee anzala 'ala 'abdihi alkitaba walam yaj'al lahu 'iwaja

# 2142

Qayyiman liyunthira basan shadeedan min ladunhu wayubashshira almumineena allatheena ya'maloona assalihati anna lahum ajran hasana

# 2143

Makitheena feehi abada

# 2144

Wayunthira allatheena qaloo ittakhatha Allahu walada

# 2145

Ma lahum bihi min 'ilmin wala liabaihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwahihim in yaqooloona illa kathiba

# 2146

Fala'allaka bakhi'un nafsaka 'ala atharihim in lam yuminoo bihatha alhadeethi asafa

# 2147

Inna ja'alna ma 'ala alardi zeenatan laha linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu 'amala

# 2148

Wainna laja'iloona ma 'alayha sa'eedan juruza

# 2149

Am hasibta anna ashaba alkahfi warraqeemi kanoo min ayatina 'ajaba

# 2150

Ith awa alfityatu ila alkahfi faqaloo rabbana atina min ladunka rahmatan wahayyi lana min amrina rashada

# 2151

Fadarabna 'ala athanihim fee alkahfi sineena 'adada

# 2152

Thumma ba'athnahum lina'lama ayyu alhizbayni ahsa lima labithoo amada

# 2153

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka nabaahum bilhaqqi innahum fityatun amanoo birabbihim wazidnahum huda

# 2154

Warabatna 'ala quloobihim ith qamoo faqaloo rabbuna rabbu assamawati walardi lan nad'uwa min doonihi ilahan laqad qulna ithan shatata

# 2155

Haolai qawmuna ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan lawla yatoona 'alayhim bisultanin bayyinin faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiba

# 2156

Waithi i'tazaltumoohum wama ya'budoona illa Allaha fawoo ila alkahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min rahmatihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum mirfaqa

# 2157

Watara ashshamsa itha tala'at tazawaru 'an kahfihim thata alyameeni waitha gharabat taqriduhum thata ashshimali wahum fee fajwatin minhu thalika min ayati Allahi man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahu waliyyan murshida

# 2158

Watahsabuhum ayqathan wahum ruqoodun wanuqallibuhum thata alyameeni wathata ashshimali wakalbuhum basitun thira'ayhi bilwaseedi lawi ittala'ta 'alayhim lawallayta minhum firaran walamulita minhum ru'ba

# 2159

Wakathalika ba'athnahum liyatasaaloo baynahum qala qailun minhum kam labithtum qaloo labithna yawman aw ba'da yawmin qaloo rabbukum a'lamu bima labithtum fab'athoo ahadakum biwariqikum hathihi ila almadeenati falyanthur ayyuha azka ta'aman falyatikum birizqin minhu walyatalattaf wala yush'iranna bikum ahada

# 2160

Innahum in yathharoo 'alaykum yarjumookum aw yu'eedookum fee millatihim walan tuflihoo ithan abada

# 2161

Wakathalika a'tharna 'alayhim liya'lamoo anna wa'da Allahi haqqun waanna asa'ata la rayba feeha ith yatanaza'oona baynahum amrahum faqaloo ibnoo 'alayhim bunyanan rabbuhum a'lamu bihim qala allatheena ghalaboo 'ala amrihim lanattakhithanna 'alayhim masjida

# 2162

Sayaqooloona thalathatun rabi'uhum kalbuhum wayaqooloona khamsatun sadisuhum kalbuhum rajman bilghaybi wayaqooloona sab'atun wathaminuhum kalbuhum qul rabbee a'lamu bi'iddatihim ma ya'lamuhum illa qaleelun fala tumari feehim illa miraan thahiran wala tastafti feehim minhum ahada

# 2163

Wala taqoolanna lishayin innee fa'ilun thalika ghada

# 2164

Illa an yashaa Allahu wathkur rabbaka itha naseeta waqul 'asa an yahdiyani rabbee liaqraba min hatha rashada

# 2165

Walabithoo fee kahfihim thalatha miatin sineena wazdadoo tis'a

# 2166

Quli Allahu a'lamu bima labithoo lahu ghaybu assamawati walardi absir bihi waasmi' ma lahum min doonihi min waliyyin wala yushriku fee hukmihi ahada

# 2167

Watlu ma oohiya ilayka min kitabi rabbika la mubaddila likalimatihi walan tajida min doonihi multahada

# 2168

Wasbir nafsaka ma'a allatheena yad'oona rabbahum bilghadati wal'ashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu wala ta'du 'aynaka 'anhum tureedu zeenata alhayati addunya wala tuti' man aghfalna qalbahu 'an thikrina wattaba'a hawahu wakana amruhu furuta

# 2169

Waquli alhaqqu min rabbikum faman shaa falyumin waman shaa falyakfur inna a'tadna liththalimeena naran ahata bihim suradiquha wain yastagheethoo yughathoo bimain kalmuhli yashwee alwujooha bisa ashsharabu wasaat murtafaqa

# 2170

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati inna la nudee'u ajra man ahsana 'amala

# 2171

Olaika lahum jannatu 'adnin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waylbasoona thiyaban khudran min sundusin waistabraqin muttakieena feeha 'ala alaraiki ni'ma aththawabu wahasunat murtafaqa

# 2172

Wadrib lahum mathalan rajulayni ja'alna liahadihima jannatayni min a'nabin wahafafnahuma binakhlin waja'alna baynahuma zar'a

# 2173

Kilta aljannatayni atat okulaha walam tathlim minhu shayan wafajjarna khilalahuma nahara

# 2174

Wakana lahu thamarun faqala lisahibihi wahuwa yuhawiruhu ana aktharu minka malan waa'azzu nafara

# 2175

Wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa thalimun linafsihi qala ma athunnu an tabeeda hathihi abada

# 2176

Wama athunnu assa'ata qaimatan walain rudidtu ila rabbee laajidanna khayran minha munqalaba

# 2177

Qala lahu sahibuhu wahuwa yuhawiruhu akafarta billathee khalaqaka min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma sawwaka rajula

# 2178

Lakinna huwa Allahu rabbee wala oshriku birabbee ahada

# 2179

Walawla ith dakhalta jannataka qulta ma shaa Allahu la quwwata illa billahi in tarani ana aqalla minka malan wawalada

# 2180

Fa'asa rabbee an yutiyani khayran min jannatika wayursila 'alayha husbanan mina assamai fatusbiha sa'eedan zalaqa

# 2181

Aw yusbiha maoha ghawran falan tastatee'a lahu talaba

# 2182

Waoheeta bithamarihi faasbaha yuqallibu kaffayhi 'ala ma anfaqa feeha wahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wayaqoolu ya laytanee lam oshrik birabbee ahada

# 2183

Walam takun lahu fiatun yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana muntasira

# 2184

Hunalika alwalayatu lillahi alhaqqi huwa khayrun thawaban wakhayrun 'uqba

# 2185

Wadrib lahum mathala alhayati addunya kamain anzalnahu mina assamai fakhtalata bihi nabatu alardi faasbaha hasheeman tathroohu arriyahu wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin muqtadira

# 2186

Almalu walbanoona zeenatu alhayati addunya walbaqiyatu assalihatu khayrun 'inda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun amala

# 2187

Wayawma nusayyiru aljibala watara alarda barizatan wahasharnahum falam nughadir minhum ahada

# 2188

Wa'uridoo 'ala rabbika saffan laqad jitumoona kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin bal za'amtum allan naj'ala lakum maw'ida

# 2189

Wawudi'a alkitabu fatara almujrimeena mushfiqeena mimma feehi wayaqooloona ya waylatana ma lihatha alkitabi la yughadiru sagheeratan wala kabeeratan illa ahsaha wawajadoo ma 'amiloo hadiran wala yathlimu rabbuka ahada

# 2190

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa kana mina aljinni fafasaqa 'an amri rabbihi afatattakhithoonahu wathurriyyatahu awliyaa min doonee wahum lakum 'aduwwun bisa liththalimeena badala

# 2191

Ma ashhadtuhum khalqa assamawati walardi wala khalqa anfusihim wama kuntu muttakhitha almudilleena 'aduda

# 2192

Wayawma yaqoolu nadoo shurakaiya allatheena za'amtum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waja'alna baynahum mawbiqa

# 2193

Waraa almujrimoona annara fathannoo annahum muwaqi'ooha walam yajidoo 'anha masrifa

# 2194

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani linnasi min kulli mathalin wakana alinsanu akthara shayin jadala

# 2195

Wama mana'a annasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda wayastaghfiroo rabbahum illa an tatiyahum sunnatu alawwaleena aw yatiyahumu al'athabu qubula

# 2196

Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena wayujadilu allatheena kafaroo bilbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa wattakhathoo ayatee wama onthiroo huzuwa

# 2197

Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi faa'rada 'anha wanasiya ma qaddamat yadahu inna ja'alna 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain tad'uhum ila alhuda falan yahtadoo ithan abada

# 2198

Warabbuka alghafooru thoo arrahmati law yuakhithuhum bima kasaboo la'ajjala lahumu al'athaba bal lahum maw'idun lan yajidoo min doonihi mawila

# 2199

Watilka alqura ahlaknahum lamma thalamoo waja'alna limahlikihim maw'ida

# 2200

Waith qala moosa lifatahu la abrahu hatta ablugha majma'a albahrayni aw amdiya huquba

# 2201

Falamma balagha majma'a baynihima nasiya hootahuma fattakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri saraba

# 2202

Falamma jawaza qala lifatahu atina ghadaana laqad laqeena min safarina hatha nasaba

# 2203

Qala araayta ith awayna ila assakhrati fainnee naseetu alhoota wama ansaneehu illa ashshaytanu an athkurahu wattakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri 'ajaba

# 2204

Qala thalika ma kunna nabghi fartadda 'ala atharihima qasasa

# 2205

Fawajada 'abdan min 'ibadina ataynahu rahmatan min 'indina wa'allamnahu min ladunna 'ilma

# 2206

Qala lahu moosa hal attabi'uka 'ala an tu'allimani mimma 'ullimta rushda

# 2207

Qala innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra

# 2208

Wakayfa tasbiru 'ala ma lam tuhit bihi khubra

# 2209

Qala satajidunee in shaa Allahu sabiran wala a'see laka amra

# 2210

Qala faini ittaba'tanee fala tasalnee 'an shayin hatta ohditha laka minhu thikra

# 2211

Fantalaqa hatta itha rakiba fee assafeenati kharaqaha qala akharaqtaha litughriqa ahlaha laqad jita shayan imra

# 2212

Qala alam aqul innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra

# 2213

Qala la tuakhithnee bima naseetu wala turhiqnee min amree 'usra

# 2214

Fantalaqa hatta itha laqiya ghulaman faqatalahu qala aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad jita shayan nukra

# 2215

Qala alam aqul laka innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra

# 2216

Qala in saaltuka 'an shayin ba'daha fala tusahibnee qad balaghta min ladunnee 'uthra

# 2217

Fantalaqa hatta itha ataya ahla qaryatin istat'ama ahlaha faabaw an yudayyifoohuma fawajada feeha jidaran yureedu an yanqadda faaqamahu qala law shita lattakhathta 'alayhi ajra

# 2218

Qala hatha firaqu baynee wabaynika saonabbioka bitaweeli ma lam tastati' 'alayhi sabra

# 2219

Amma assafeenatu fakanat limasakeena ya'maloona fee albahri faaradtu an a'eebaha wakana waraahum malikun yakhuthu kulla safeenatin ghasba

# 2220

Waamma alghulamu fakana abawahu muminayni fakhasheena an yurhiqahuma tughyanan wakufra

# 2221

Faaradna an yubdilahuma rabbuhuma khayran minhu zakatan waaqraba ruhma

# 2222

Waamma aljidaru fakana lighulamayni yateemayni fee almadeenati wakana tahtahu kanzun lahuma wakana aboohuma salihan faarada rabbuka an yablugha ashuddahuma wayastakhrija kanzahuma rahmatan min rabbika wama fa'altuhu 'an amree thalika taweelu ma lam tasti' 'alayhi sabra

# 2223

Wayasaloonaka 'an thee alqarnayni qul saatloo 'alaykum minhu thikra

# 2224

Inna makkanna lahu fee alardi waataynahu min kulli shayin sababa

# 2225

Faatba'a sababa

# 2226

Hatta itha balagha maghriba ashshamsi wajadaha taghrubu fee 'aynin hamiatin wawajada 'indaha qawman qulna ya tha alqarnayni imma an tu'aththiba waimma an tattakhitha feehim husna

# 2227

Qala amma man thalama fasawfa nu'aththibuhu thumma yuraddu ila rabbihi fayu'aththibuhu 'athaban nukra

# 2228

Waamma man amana wa'amila salihan falahu jazaan alhusna wasanaqoolu lahu min amrina yusra

# 2229

Thumma atba'a sababa

# 2230
