Hatta itha balagha matli'a ashshamsi wajadaha tatlu'u 'ala qawmin lam naj'al lahum min dooniha sitra

# 2231

Kathalika waqad ahatna bima ladayhi khubra

# 2232

Thumma atba'a sababa

# 2233

Hatta itha balagha bayna assaddayni wajada min doonihima qawman la yakadoona yafqahoona qawla

# 2234

Qaloo ya tha alqarnayni inna yajooja wamajooja mufsidoona fee alardi fahal naj'alu laka kharjan 'ala an taj'ala baynana wabaynahum sadda

# 2235

Qala ma makkannee feehi rabbee khayrun faa'eenoonee biquwwatin aj'al baynakum wabaynahum radma

# 2236

Atoonee zubara alhadeedi hatta itha sawa bayna asadafayni qala onfukhoo hatta itha ja'alahu naran qala atoonee ofrigh 'alayhi qitra

# 2237

Fama ista'oo an yathharoohu wama istata'oo lahu naqba

# 2238

Qala hatha rahmatun min rabbee faitha jaa wa'du rabbee ja'alahu dakkaa wakana wa'du rabbee haqqa

# 2239

Watarakna ba'dahum yawmaithin yamooju fee ba'din wanufikha fee assoori fajama'nahum jam'a

# 2240

Wa'aradna jahannama yawmaithin lilkafireena 'arda

# 2241

Allatheena kanat a'yunuhum fee ghitain 'an thikree wakanoo la yastatee'oona sam'a

# 2242

Afahasiba allatheena kafaroo an yattakhithoo 'ibadee min doonee awliyaa inna a'tadna jahannama lilkafireena nuzula

# 2243

Qul hal nunabbiokum bilakhsareena a'mala

# 2244

Allatheena dalla sa'yuhum fee alhayati addunya wahum yahsaboona annahum yuhsinoona sun'a

# 2245

Olaika allatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim waliqaihi fahabitat a'maluhum fala nuqeemu lahum yawma alqiyamati wazna

# 2246

Thalika jazaohum jahannamu bima kafaroo wattakhathoo ayatee warusulee huzuwa

# 2247

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati kanat lahum jannatu alfirdawsi nuzula

# 2248

Khalideena feeha la yabghoona 'anha hiwala

# 2249

Qul law kana albahru midadan likalimati rabbee lanafida albahru qabla an tanfada kalimatu rabbee walaw jina bimithlihi madada

# 2250

Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun faman kana yarjoo liqaa rabbihi falya'mal 'amalan salihan wala yushrik bi'ibadati rabbihi ahada

# 2251

Kafhaya'aynsad

# 2252

Thikru rahmati rabbika 'abdahu zakariyya

# 2253

Ith nada rabbahu nidaan khafiyya

# 2254

Qala rabbi innee wahana al'athmu minnee washta'ala arrasu shayban walam akun bidu'aika rabbi shaqiyya

# 2255

Wainnee khiftu almawaliya min waraee wakanati imraatee 'aqiran fahab lee min ladunka waliyya

# 2256

Yarithunee wayarithu min ali ya'qooba waj'alhu rabbi radiyya

# 2257

Ya zakariyya inna nubashshiruka bighulamin ismuhu yahya lam naj'al lahu min qablu samiyya

# 2258

Qala rabbi anna yakoonu lee ghulamun wakanati imraatee 'aqiran waqad balaghtu mina alkibari 'itiyya

# 2259

Qala kathalika qala rabbuka huwa 'alayya hayyinun waqad khalaqtuka min qablu walam taku shaya

# 2260

Qala rabbi ij'al lee ayatan qala ayatuka alla tukallima annasa thalatha layalin sawiyya

# 2261

Fakharaja 'ala qawmihi mina almihrabi faawha ilayhim an sabbihoo bukratan wa'ashiyya

# 2262

Ya yahya khuthi alkitaba biquwwatin waataynahu alhukma sabiyya

# 2263

Wahananan min ladunna wazakatan wakana taqiyya

# 2264

Wabarran biwalidayhi walam yakun jabbaran 'asiyya

# 2265

Wasalamun 'alayhi yawma wulida wayawma yamootu wayawma yub'athu hayya

# 2266

Wathkur fee alkitabi maryama ithi intabathat min ahliha makanan sharqiyya

# 2267

Fattakhathat min doonihim hijaban faarsalna ilayha roohana fatamaththala laha basharan sawiyya

# 2268

Qalat innee a'oothu birrahmani minka in kunta taqiyya

# 2269

Qala innama ana rasoolu rabbiki liahaba laki ghulaman zakiyya

# 2270

Qalat anna yakoonu lee ghulamun walam yamsasnee basharun walam aku baghiyya

# 2271

Qala kathaliki qala rabbuki huwa 'alayya hayyinun walinaj'alahu ayatan linnasi warahmatan minna wakana amran maqdiyya

# 2272

Fahamalathu fantabathat bihi makanan qasiyya

# 2273

Faajaaha almakhadu ila jith'i annakhlati qalat ya laytanee mittu qabla hatha wakuntu nasyan mansiyya

# 2274

Fanadaha min tahtiha alla tahzanee qad ja'ala rabbuki tahtaki sariyya

# 2275

Wahuzzee ilayki bijith'i annakhlati tusaqit 'alayki rutaban janiyya

# 2276

Fakulee washrabee waqarree 'aynan faimma tarayinna mina albashari ahadan faqoolee innee nathartu lirrahmani sawman falan okallima alyawma insiyya

# 2277

Faatat bihi qawmaha tahmiluhu qaloo ya maryamu laqad jiti shayan fariyya

# 2278

Ya okhta haroona ma kana abooki imraa sawin wama kanat ommuki baghiyya

# 2279

Faasharat ilayhi qaloo kayfa nukallimu man kana fee almahdi sabiyya

# 2280

Qala innee 'abdu Allahi ataniya alkitaba waja'alanee nabiyya

# 2281

Waja'alanee mubarakan ayna ma kuntu waawsanee bissalati wazzakati ma dumtu hayya

# 2282

Wabarran biwalidatee walam yaj'alnee jabbaran shaqiyya

# 2283

Wassalamu 'alayya yawma wulidtu wayawma amootu wayawma ob'athu hayya

# 2284

Thalika 'eesa ibnu maryama qawla alhaqqi allathee feehi yamtaroon

# 2285

Ma kana lillahi an yattakhitha min waladin subhanahu itha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoon

# 2286

Wainna Allaha rabbee warabbukum fa'budoohu hatha siratun mustaqeem

# 2287

Fakhtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena kafaroo min mashhadi yawmin 'atheem

# 2288

Asmi' bihim waabsir yawma yatoonana lakini aththalimoona alyawma fee dalalin mubeen

# 2289

Waanthirhum yawma alhasrati ith qudiya alamru wahum fee ghaflatin wahum la yuminoon

# 2290

Inna nahnu narithu alarda waman 'alayha wailayna yurja'oon

# 2291

Wathkur fee alkitabi ibraheema innahu kana siddeeqan nabiyya

# 2292

Ith qala liabeehi ya abati lima ta'budu ma la yasma'u wala yubsiru wala yughnee 'anka shaya

# 2293

Ya abati innee qad jaanee mina al'ilmi ma lam yatika fattabi'nee ahdika siratan sawiyya

# 2294

Ya abati la ta'budi ashshaytana inna ashshaytana kana lirrahmani 'asiyya

# 2295

Ya abati innee akhafu an yamassaka 'athabun mina arrahmani fatakoona lishshyatani waliyya

# 2296

Qala araghibun anta 'an alihatee ya ibraheemu lain lam tantahi laarjumannaka wahjurnee maliyya

# 2297

Qala salamun 'alayka saastaghfiru laka rabbee innahu kana bee hafiyya

# 2298

Waa'tazilukum wama tad'oona min dooni Allahi waad'oo rabbee 'asa alla akoona bidu'ai rabbee shaqiyya

# 2299

Falamma i'tazalahum wama ya'budoona min dooni Allahi wahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba wakullan ja'alna nabiyya

# 2300

Wawahabna lahum min rahmatina waja'alna lahum lisana sidqin 'aliyya

# 2301

Wathkur fee alkitabi moosa innahu kana mukhlasan wakana rasoolan nabiyya

# 2306

# 2307

# 2308

Olaika allatheena an'ama Allahu 'alayhim mina annabiyyeena min thurriyyati adama wamimman hamalna ma'a noohin wamin thurriyyati ibraheema waisraeela wamimman hadayna wajtabayna itha tutla 'alayhim ayatu arrahmani kharroo sujjadan wabukiyya

# 2309

# 2310

# 2311

# 2313

# 2314

# 2315

# 2317

# 2418

# 2419

Qala amantum lahu qabla an athana lakum innahu lakabeerukumu allathee 'allamakumu assihra falaoqatti'anna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khilafin walaosallibannakum fee juthoo'i annakhli walata'lamunna ayyuna ashaddu 'athaban waabqa

# 2420

# 2484

# 2500

# 2504

# 2506

# 2507

# 2508

# 2510

# 2511

# 2512

# 2513

# 2514

# 2515

# 2516

# 2517

Wama ja'alna libasharin min qablika alkhulda afain mitta fahumu alkhalidoon

# 2518

# 2519

# 2520

# 2521

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen

# 2522

Law ya'lamu allatheena kafaroo heena la yakuffoona 'an wujoohihimu annara wala 'an thuhoorihim wala hum yunsaroon

# 2523

Bal tateehim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fala yastatee'oona raddaha wala hum yuntharoon

# 2524

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa billatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 2525

Qul man yaklaokum billayli wannahari mina arrahmani bal hum 'an thikri rabbihim mu'ridoon

# 2526

Am lahum alihatun tamna'uhum min doonina la yastatee'oona nasra anfusihim wala hum minna yushaboon

# 2527

Bal matta'na haolai waabaahum hatta tala 'alayhimu al'umuru afala yarawna anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha afahumu alghaliboon

# 2528

Qul innama onthirukum bilwahyi wala yasma'u assummu addu'aa itha ma yuntharoon

# 2529

Walain massathum nafhatun min 'athabi rabbika layaqoolunna ya waylana inna kunna thalimeen

# 2530

Wanada'u almawazeena alqista liyawmi alqiyamati fala tuthlamu nafsun shayan wain kana mithqala habbatin min khardalin atayna biha wakafa bina hasibeen

# 2531

Walaqad atayna moosa waharoona alfurqana wadiyaan wathikran lilmuttaqeen

# 2532

Allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bilghaybi wahum mina assa'ati mushfiqoon

# 2533

Wahatha thikrun mubarakun anzalnahu afaantum lahu munkiroon

# 2534

Walaqad atayna ibraheema rushdahu min qablu wakunna bihi 'alimeen

# 2535

Ith qala liabeehi waqawmihi ma hathihi attamatheelu allatee antum laha 'akifoon

# 2536

Qaloo wajadna abaana laha 'abideen

# 2537

Qala laqad kuntum antum waabaokum fee dalalin mubeen

# 2538

Qaloo ajitana bilhaqqi am anta mina alla'ibeen

# 2539

Qala bal rabbukum rabbu assamawati walardi allathee fatarahunna waana 'ala thalikum mina ashshahideen

# 2540

Watallahi laakeedanna asnamakum ba'da an tuwalloo mudbireen

# 2541

Faja'alahum juthathan illa kabeeran lahum la'allahum ilayhi yarji'oon

# 2542

Qaloo man fa'ala hatha bialihatina innahu lamina aththalimeen

# 2543

Qaloo sami'na fatan yathkuruhum yuqalu lahu ibraheem

# 2544

Qaloo fatoo bihi 'ala a'yuni annasi la'allahum yashhadoon

# 2545

Qaloo aanta fa'alta hatha bialihatina ya ibraheem

# 2546

Qala bal fa'alahu kabeeruhum hatha fasaloohum in kanoo yantiqoon

# 2547

Faraja'oo ila anfusihim faqaloo innakum antumu aththalimoon

# 2548

Thumma nukisoo 'ala ruoosihim laqad 'alimta ma haolai yantiqoon

# 2549

Qala afata'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'ukum shayan wala yadurrukum

# 2550

Offin lakum walima ta'budoona min dooni Allahi afala ta'qiloon

# 2551

Qaloo harriqoohu wansuroo alihatakum in kuntum fa'ileen

# 2552

Qulna ya naru koonee bardan wasalaman 'ala ibraheem

# 2553

Waaradoo bihi kaydan faja'alnahumu alakhsareen

# 2554

Wanajjaynahu walootan ila alardi allatee barakna feeha lil'alameen

# 2555

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba nafilatan wakullan ja'alna saliheen

# 2556

Waja'alnahum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina waawhayna ilayhim fi'la alkhayrati waiqama assalati waeetaa azzakati wakanoo lana 'abideen

# 2557

Walootan ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wanajjaynahu mina alqaryati allatee kanat ta'malu alkhabaitha innahum kanoo qawma sawin fasiqeen

# 2558

Waadkhalnahu fee rahmatina innahu mina assaliheen

# 2559

Wanoohan ith nada min qablu fastajabna lahu fanajjaynahu waahlahu mina alkarbi al'atheem

# 2560

Wanasarnahu mina alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawma sawin faaghraqnahum ajma'een

# 2561

Wadawooda wasulaymana ith yahkumani fee alharthi ith nafashat feehi ghanamu alqawmi wakunna lihukmihim shahideen

# 2562

Fafahhamnaha sulaymana wakullan atayna hukman wa'ilman wasakhkharna ma'a dawooda aljibala yusabbihna wattayra wakunna fa'ileen

# 2563

Wa'allamnahu san'ata laboosin lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum shakiroon

# 2564

Walisulaymana arreeha 'asifatan tajree biamrihi ila alardi allatee barakna feeha wakunna bikulli shayin 'alimeen

# 2565

Wamina ashshayateeni man yaghoosoona lahu waya'maloona 'amalan doona thalika wakunna lahum hafitheen

# 2566

Waayyooba ith nada rabbahu annee massaniya addurru waanta arhamu arrahimeen

# 2567

Fastajabna lahu fakashafna ma bihi min durrin waataynahu ahlahu wamithlahum ma'ahum rahmatan min 'indina wathikra lil'abideen

# 2568

Waisma'eela waidreesa watha alkifli kullun mina assabireen

# 2569

Waadkhalnahum fee rahmatina innahum mina assaliheen

# 2570

Watha annooni ith thahaba mughadiban fathanna an lan naqdira 'alayhi fanada fee aththulumati an la ilaha illa anta subhanaka innee kuntu mina aththalimeen

# 2571

Fastajabna lahu wanajjaynahu mina alghammi wakathalika nunjee almumineen

# 2572

Wazakariyya ith nada rabbahu rabbi la tatharnee fardan waanta khayru alwaritheen

# 2573

Fastajabna lahu wawahabna lahu yahya waaslahna lahu zawjahu innahum kanoo yusari'oona fee alkhayrati wayad'oonana raghaban warahaban wakanoo lana khashi'een

# 2574

Wallatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feeha min roohina waja'alnaha wabnaha ayatan lil'alameen

# 2575

Inna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum fao'budoon

# 2576

Wataqatta'oo amrahum baynahum kullun ilayna raji'oon

# 2577

Faman ya'mal mina assalihati wahuwa muminun fala kufrana lisa'yihi wainna lahu katiboon

# 2578

Waharamun 'ala qaryatin ahlaknaha annahum la yarji'oon

# 2579

Hatta itha futihat yajooju wamajooju wahum min kulli hadabin yansiloon

# 2580

Waqtaraba alwa'du alhaqqu faitha hiya shakhisatun absaru allatheena kafaroo ya waylana qad kunna fee ghaflatin min hatha bal kunna thalimeen

# 2581

Innakum wama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi hasabu jahannama antum laha waridoon

# 2582

Law kana haolai alihatan ma waradooha wakullun feeha khalidoon

# 2583

Lahum feeha zafeerun wahum feeha la yasma'oon

# 2584

Inna allatheena sabaqat lahum minna alhusna olaika 'anha mub'adoon

# 2585

La yasma'oona haseesaha wahum fee ma ishtahat anfusuhum khalidoon

# 2586

La yahzunuhumu alfaza'u alakbaru watatalaqqahumu almalaikatu hatha yawmukumu allathee kuntum too'adoon

# 2587

Yawma natwee assamaa katayyi assijlli lilkutubi kama badana awwala khalqin nu'eeduhu wa'dan 'alayna inna kunna fa'ileen

# 2588

Walaqad katabna fee azzaboori min ba'di aththikri anna alarda yarithuha 'ibadiya assalihoon

# 2589

Inna fee hatha labalaghan liqawmin 'abideen

# 2590

Wama arsalnaka illa rahmatan lil'alameen

# 2591

Qul innama yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fahal antum muslimoon

# 2592

Fain tawallaw faqul athantukum 'ala sawain wain adree aqareebun am ba'eedun ma too'adoon

# 2593

Innahu ya'lamu aljahra mina alqawli waya'lamu ma taktumoon

# 2594

Wain adree la'allahu fitnatun lakum wamata'un ila heen

# 2595

Qala rabbi ohkum bilhaqqi warabbuna arrahmanu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoon

# 2596

Ya ayyuha annasu ittaqoo rabbakum inna zalzalata assa'ati shayon 'atheem

# 2597

Yawma tarawnaha tathhalu kullu murdi'atin 'amma arda'at watada'u kullu thati hamlin hamlaha watara annasa sukara wama hum bisukara walakinna 'athaba Allahi shadeed

# 2598

Wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattabi'u kulla shaytanin mareed

# 2599

Kutiba 'alayhi annahu man tawallahu faannahu yudilluhu wayahdeehi ila 'athabi assa'eer

# 2600

Ya ayyuha annasu in kuntum fee raybin mina alba'thi fainna khalaqnakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma min mudghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fee alarhami ma nashao ila ajalin musamman thumma nukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaffa waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likayla ya'lama min ba'di 'ilmin shayan watara alarda hamidatan faitha anzalna 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat waanbatat min kulli zawjin baheej

# 2601

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waannahu yuhyee almawta waannahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 2602

Waanna assa'ata atiyatun la rayba feeha waanna Allaha yab'athu man fee alquboor

# 2603

Wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneer

# 2604

Thaniya 'itfihi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi lahu fee addunya khizyun wanutheequhu yawma alqiyamati 'athaba alhareeq

# 2605

Thalika bima qaddamat yadaka waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lil'abeed

# 2606

Wamina annasi man ya'budu Allaha 'ala harfin fain asabahu khayrun itmaanna bihi wain asabathu fitnatun inqalaba 'ala wajhihi khasira addunya walakhirata thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeen

# 2607

Yad'oo min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhu wama la yanfa'uhu thalika huwa addalalu alba'eed

# 2608

Yad'oo laman darruhu aqrabu min naf'ihi labisa almawla walabisa al'asheer

# 2609

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yureed

# 2610

Man kana yathunnu an lan yansurahu Allahu fee addunya walakhirati falyamdud bisababin ila assamai thumma liyaqta' falyanthur hal yuthhibanna kayduhu ma yagheeth

# 2611

Wakathalika anzalnahu ayatin bayyinatin waanna Allaha yahdee man yureed

# 2612

Inna allatheena amanoo wallatheena hadoo wassabieena wannasara walmajoosa wallatheena ashrakoo inna Allaha yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin shaheed

# 2613

Alam tara anna Allaha yasjudu lahu man fee assamawati waman fee alardi washshamsu walqamaru wannujoomu waljibalu washshajaru waddawabbu wakatheerun mina annasi wakatheerun haqqa 'alayhi al'athabu waman yuhini Allahu fama lahu min mukrimin inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yasha

# 2614

Hathani khasmani ikhtasamoo fee rabbihim fallatheena kafaroo qutti'at lahum thiyabun min narin yusabbu min fawqi ruoosihimu alhameem

# 2615

Yusharu bihi ma fee butoonihim waljulood

# 2616

Walahum maqami'u min hadeed

# 2617

Kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha min ghammin o'eedoo feeha wathooqoo 'athaba alhareeq

# 2618

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareer

# 2619

Wahudoo ila attayyibi mina alqawli wahudoo ila sirati alhameed

# 2620

Inna allatheena kafaroo wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi walmasjidi alharami allathee ja'alnahu linnasi sawaan al'akifu feehi walbadi waman yurid feehi biilhadin bithulmin nuthiqhu min 'athabin aleem

# 2621

Waith bawwana liibraheema makana albayti an la tushrik bee shayan watahhir baytiya littaifeena walqaimeena warrukka'i assujood

# 2622

Waaththin fee annasi bilhajji yatooka rijalan wa'ala kulli damirin yateena min kulli fajjin 'ameeq

# 2623

Liyashhadoo manafi'a lahum wayathkuroo isma Allahi fee ayyamin ma'loomatin 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami fakuloo minha waat'imoo albaisa alfaqeer

# 2624

Thumma lyaqdoo tafathahum walyoofoo nuthoorahum walyattawwafoo bilbayti al'ateeq

# 2625

Thalika waman yu'aththim hurumati Allahi fahuwa khayrun lahu 'inda rabbihi waohillat lakumu alan'amu illa ma yutla 'alaykum fajtaniboo arrijsa mina alawthani wajtaniboo qawla azzoor

# 2626

Hunafaa lillahi ghayra mushrikeena bihi waman yushrik billahi fakaannama kharra mina assamai fatakhtafuhu attayru aw tahwee bihi arreehu fee makanin saheeq

# 2627

Thalika waman yu'aththim sha'aira Allahi fainnaha min taqwa alquloob

# 2628

Lakum feeha manafi'u ila ajalin musamman thumma mahilluha ila albayti al'ateeq

# 2629

Walikulli ommatin ja'alna mansakan liyathkuroo isma Allahi 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami failahukum ilahun wahidun falahu aslimoo wabashshiri almukhbiteen

# 2630

Allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum wassabireena 'ala ma asabahum walmuqeemee assalati wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon

# 2631

Walbudna ja'alnaha lakum min sha'airi Allahi lakum feeha khayrun fathkuroo isma Allahi 'alayha sawaffa faitha wajabat junoobuha fakuloo minha waat'imoo alqani'a walmu'tarra kathalika sakhkharnaha lakum la'allakum tashkuroon

# 2632

Lan yanala Allaha luhoomuha wala dimaoha walakin yanaluhu attaqwa minkum kathalika sakhkharaha lakum litukabbiroo Allaha 'ala ma hadakum wabashshiri almuhsineen

# 2633

Inna Allaha yudafi'u 'ani allatheena amanoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla khawwanin kafoor

# 2634

Othina lillatheena yuqataloona biannahum thulimoo wainna Allaha 'ala nasrihim laqadeer

# 2635

Allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim bighayri haqqin illa an yaqooloo rabbuna Allahu walawla daf'u Allahi annasa ba'dahum biba'din lahuddimat sawami'u wabiya'un wasalawatun wamasajidu yuthkaru feeha ismu Allahi katheeran walayansuranna Allahu man yansuruhu inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeez

# 2636

Allatheena in makkannahum fee alardi aqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata waamaroo bilma'roofi wanahaw 'ani almunkari walillahi 'aqibatu alomoor

# 2637

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin wa'adun wathamood

# 2638

Waqawmu ibraheema waqawmu loot

# 2639

Waashabu madyana wakuththiba moosa faamlaytu lilkafireena thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana nakeer

# 2640

Fakaayyin min qaryatin ahlaknaha wahiya thalimatun fahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wabirin mu'attalatin waqasrin masheed

# 2641

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fatakoona lahum quloobun ya'qiloona biha aw athanun yasma'oona biha fainnaha la ta'ma alabsaru walakin ta'ma alquloobu allatee fee assudoor

# 2642

Wayasta'jiloonaka bil'athabi walan yukhlifa Allahu wa'dahu wainna yawman 'inda rabbika kaalfi sanatin mimma ta'uddoon

# 2643

Wakaayyin min qaryatin amlaytu laha wahiya thalimatun thumma akhathtuha wailayya almaseer

# 2644

Qul ya ayyuha annasu innama ana lakum natheerun mubeen

# 2645

Fallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem

# 2646

Wallatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika ashabu aljaheem

# 2647

Wama arsalna min qablika min rasoolin wala nabiyyin illa itha tamanna alqa ashshaytanu fee omniyyatihi fayansakhu Allahu ma yulqee ashshaytanu thumma yuhkimu Allahu ayatihi wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 2648

Liyaj'ala ma yulqee ashshaytanu fitnatan lillatheena fee quloobihim maradun walqasiyati quloobuhum wainna aththalimeena lafee shiqaqin ba'eed

# 2649

Waliya'lama allatheena ootoo al'ilma annahu alhaqqu min rabbika fayuminoo bihi fatukhbita lahu quloobuhum wainna Allaha lahadi allatheena amanoo ila siratin mustaqeem

# 2650

Wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo fee miryatin minhu hatta tatiyahumu assa'atu baghtatan aw yatiyahum 'athabu yawmin 'aqeem

# 2651

Almulku yawmaithin lillahi yahkumu baynahum fallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fee jannati anna'eem

# 2652

Wallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina faolaika lahum 'athabun muheen

# 2653

Wallatheena hajaroo fee sabeeli Allahi thumma qutiloo aw matoo layarzuqannahumu Allahu rizqan hasanan wainna Allaha lahuwa khayru arraziqeen

# 2654

Layudkhilannahum mudkhalan yardawnahu wainna Allaha la'aleemun haleem

# 2655

Thalika waman 'aqaba bimithli ma 'ooqiba bihi thumma bughiya 'alayhi layansurannahu Allahu inna Allaha la'afuwwun ghafoor

# 2656

Thalika bianna Allaha yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli waanna Allaha samee'un baseer

# 2657

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi huwa albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeer

# 2658

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan fatusbihu alardu mukhdarratan inna Allaha lateefun khabeer

# 2659

Lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wainna Allaha lahuwa alghaniyyu alhameed

# 2660

Alam tara anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee alardi walfulka tajree fee albahri biamrihi wayumsiku assamaa an taqa'a 'ala alardi illa biithnihi inna Allaha binnasi laraoofun raheem

# 2661

Wahuwa allathee ahyakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum inna alinsana lakafoor

# 2662

Likulli ommatin ja'alna mansakan hum nasikoohu fala yunazi'unnaka fee alamri wad'u ila rabbika innaka la'ala hudan mustaqeem

# 2663

Wain jadalooka faquli Allahu a'lamu bima ta'maloon

# 2664

Allahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati feema kuntum feehi takhtalifoon

# 2665

Alam ta'lam anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee assamai walardi inna thalika fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer

# 2666

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan wama laysa lahum bihi 'ilmun wama liththalimeena min naseer

# 2667

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ta'rifu fee wujoohi allatheena kafaroo almunkara yakadoona yastoona billatheena yatloona 'alayhim ayatina qul afaonabbiokum bisharrin min thalikum annaru wa'adaha Allahu allatheena kafaroo wabisa almaseer

# 2668

Ya ayyuha annasu duriba mathalun fastami'oo lahu inna allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lan yakhluqoo thubaban walawi ijtama'oo lahu wain yaslubuhumu aththubabu shayan la yastanqithoohu minhu da'ufa attalibu walmatloob

# 2669

Ma qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeez

# 2670

Allahu yastafee mina almalaikati rusulan wamina annasi inna Allaha samee'un baseer

# 2671

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum waila Allahi turja'u alomoor

# 2672

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo irka'oo wasjudoo wa'budoo rabbakum waf'aloo alkhayra la'allakum tuflihoon

# 2673

Wajahidoo fee Allahi haqqa jihadihi huwa ijtabakum wama ja'ala 'alaykum fee addeeni min harajin millata abeekum ibraheema huwa sammakumu almuslimeena min qablu wafee hatha liyakoona arrasoolu shaheedan 'alaykum watakoonoo shuhadaa 'ala annasi faaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata wa'tasimoo billahi huwa mawlakum fani'ma almawla wani'ma annaseer

# 2674

Qad aflaha almuminoon

# 2675

Allatheena hum fee salatihim khashi'oon

# 2676

Wallatheena hum 'ani allaghwi mu'ridoon

# 2677

Wallatheena hum lizzakati fa'iloon

# 2678

Wallatheena hum lifuroojihim hafithoon

# 2679

Illa 'ala azwajihim aw ma malakat aymanuhum fainnahum ghayru maloomeen

# 2680

Famani ibtagha waraa thalika faolaika humu al'adoon

# 2681

Wallatheena hum liamanatihim wa'ahdihim ra'oon

# 2682

Wallatheena hum 'ala salawatihim yuhafithoon

# 2683

Olaika humu alwarithoon

# 2684

Allatheena yarithoona alfirdawsa hum feeha khalidoon

# 2685

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min sulalatin min teen

# 2686

Thumma ja'alnahu nutfatan fee qararin makeen

# 2687

Thumma khalaqna annutfata 'alaqatan fakhalaqna al'alaqata mudghatan fakhalaqna almudghata 'ithaman fakasawna al'ithama lahman thumma anshanahu khalqan akhara fatabaraka Allahu ahsanu alkhaliqeen

# 2688

Thumma innakum ba'da thalika lamayyitoon

# 2689

Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati tub'athoon

# 2690

Walaqad khalaqna fawqakum sab'a taraiqa wama kunna 'ani alkhalqi ghafileen

# 2691

Waanzalna mina assamai maan biqadarin faaskannahu fee alardi wainna 'ala thahabin bihi laqadiroon

# 2692

Faanshana lakum bihi jannatin min nakheelin waa'nabin lakum feeha fawakihu katheeratun waminha takuloon

# 2693

Washajaratan takhruju min toori saynaa tanbutu bidduhni wasibghin lilakileen

# 2694

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butooniha walakum feeha manafi'u katheeratun waminha takuloon

# 2695

Wa'alayha wa'ala alfulki tuhmaloon

# 2696

Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoon

# 2697

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yureedu an yatafaddala 'alaykum walaw shaa Allahu laanzala malaikatan ma sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleen

# 2698

In huwa illa rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabbasoo bihi hatta heen

# 2699

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththaboon

# 2700

Faawhayna ilayhi ani isna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina faitha jaa amruna wafara attannooru fasluk feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu minhum wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoon

# 2701

Faitha istawayta anta waman ma'aka 'ala alfulki faquli alhamdu lillahi allathee najjana mina alqawmi aththalimeen

# 2702

Waqul rabbi anzilnee munzalan mubarakan waanta khayru almunzileen

# 2703

Inna fee thalika laayatin wain kunna lamubtaleen

# 2704

Thumma anshana min ba'dihim qarnan akhareen

# 2705

Faarsalna feehim rasoolan minhum ani o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoon

# 2706

Waqala almalao min qawmihi allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biliqai alakhirati waatrafnahum fee alhayati addunya ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yakulu mimma takuloona minhu wayashrabu mimma tashraboon

# 2707

Walain ata'tum basharan mithlakum innakum ithan lakhasiroon

# 2708

Aya'idukum annakum itha mittum wakuntum turaban wa'ithaman annakum mukhrajoon

# 2709

Hayhata hayhata lima too'adoon

# 2710

In hiya illa hayatuna addunya namootu wanahya wama nahnu bimab'ootheen

# 2711

In huwa illa rajulun iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban wama nahnu lahu bimumineen

# 2712

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththaboon

# 2713

Qala 'amma qaleelin layusbihunna nadimeen

# 2714

Faakhathathumu assayhatu bilhaqqi faja'alnahum ghuthaan fabu'dan lilqawmi aththalimeen

# 2715

Thumma anshana min ba'dihim quroonan akhareen

# 2716

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroon

# 2717

Thumma arsalna rusulana tatra kulla ma jaa ommatan rasooluha kaththaboohu faatba'na ba'dahum ba'dan waja'alnahum ahadeetha fabu'dan liqawmin la yuminoon

# 2718

Thumma arsalna moosa waakhahu haroona biayatina wasultanin mubeen

# 2719

Ila fir'awna wamalaihi fastakbaroo wakanoo qawman 'aleen

# 2720

Faqaloo anuminu libasharayni mithlina waqawmuhuma lana 'abidoon

# 2721

Fakaththaboohuma fakanoo mina almuhlakeen

# 2722

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba la'allahum yahtadoon

# 2723

Waja'alna ibna maryama waommahu ayatan waawaynahuma ila rabwatin thati qararin wama'een

# 2724

Ya ayyuha arrusulu kuloo mina attayyibati wa'maloo salihan innee bima ta'maloona 'aleem

# 2725

Wainna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum fattaqoon

# 2726

Fataqatta'oo amrahum baynahum zuburan kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoon

# 2727

Fatharhum fee ghamratihim hatta heen

# 2728

Ayahsaboona annama numidduhum bihi min malin wabaneen

# 2729

Nusari'u lahum fee alkhayrati bal la yash'uroon

# 2730

Inna allatheena hum min khashyati rabbihim mushfiqoon

# 2731

Wallatheena hum biayati rabbihim yuminoon

# 2732

Wallatheena hum birabbihim la yushrikoon

# 2733

Wallatheena yutoona ma ataw waquloobuhum wajilatun annahum ila rabbihim raji'oon

# 2734

Olaika yusari'oona fee alkhayrati wahum laha sabiqoon

# 2735

Wala nukallifu nafsan illa wus'aha waladayna kitabun yantiqu bilhaqqi wahum la yuthlamoon

# 2736

Bal quloobuhum fee ghamratin min hatha walahum a'malun min dooni thalika hum laha 'amiloon

# 2737

Hatta itha akhathna mutrafeehim bil'athabi itha hum yajaroon

# 2738

La tajaroo alyawma innakum minna la tunsaroon

# 2739

Qad kanat ayatee tutla 'alaykum fakuntum 'ala a'qabikum tankisoon

# 2740

Mustakbireena bihi samiran tahjuroon

# 2741

Afalam yaddabbaroo alqawla am jaahum ma lam yati abaahumu alawwaleen

# 2742

Am lam ya'rifoo rasoolahum fahum lahu munkiroon

# 2743

Am yaqooloona bihi jinnatun bal jaahum bilhaqqi waaktharuhum lilhaqqi karihoon

# 2744

Walawi ittaba'a alhaqqu ahwaahum lafasadati assamawatu walardu waman feehinna bal ataynahum bithikrihim fahum 'an thikrihim mu'ridoon

# 2745

Am tasaluhum kharjan fakharaju rabbika khayrun wahuwa khayru arraziqeen

# 2746

Wainnaka latad'oohum ila siratin mustaqeem

# 2747

Wainna allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati 'ani assirati lanakiboon

# 2748

Walaw rahimnahum wakashafna ma bihim min durrin lalajjoo fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon

# 2749

Walaqad akhathnahum bil'athabi fama istakanoo lirabbihim wama yatadarra'oon

# 2750

Hatta itha fatahna 'alayhim baban tha 'athabin shadeedin itha hum feehi mublisoon

# 2751

Wahuwa allathee anshaa lakumu assam'a walabsara walafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroon

# 2752

Wahuwa allathee tharaakum fee alardi wailayhi tuhsharoon

# 2753

Wahuwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu walahu ikhtilafu allayli wannahari afala ta'qiloon

# 2754

Bal qaloo mithla ma qala alawwaloon

# 2755

Qaloo aitha mitna wakunna turaban wa'ithaman ainna lamab'oothoon

# 2756

Laqad wu'idna nahnu waabaona hatha min qablu in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen

# 2757

Qul limani alardu waman feeha in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 2758

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tathakkaroon

# 2759

Qul man rabbu assamawati assab'i warabbu al'arshi al'atheem

# 2760

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tattaqoon

# 2761

Qul man biyadihi malakootu kulli shayin wahuwa yujeeru wala yujaru 'alayhi in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 2762

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul faanna tusharoon

# 2763

Bal ataynahum bilhaqqi wainnahum lakathiboon

# 2764

Ma ittakhatha Allahu min waladin wama kana ma'ahu min ilahin ithan lathahaba kullu ilahin bima khalaqa wala'ala ba'duhum 'ala ba'din subhana Allahi 'amma yasifoon

# 2765

'alimi alghaybi washshahadati fata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 2766

Qul rabbi imma turiyannee ma yoo'adoon

# 2767

Rabbi fala taj'alnee fee alqawmi aththalimeen

# 2768

Wainna 'ala an nuriyaka ma na'iduhum laqadiroon

# 2769

Idfa' billatee hiya ahsanu assayyiata nahnu a'lamu bima yasifoon

# 2770

Waqul rabbi a'oothu bika min hamazati ashshayateen

# 2771

Waa'oothu bika rabbi an yahduroon

# 2772

Hatta itha jaa ahadahumu almawtu qala rabbi irji'oon

# 2773

La'allee a'malu salihan feema taraktu kalla innaha kalimatun huwa qailuha wamin waraihim barzakhun ila yawmi yub'athoon

# 2774

Faitha nufikha fee assoori fala ansaba baynahum yawmaithin wala yatasaaloon

# 2775

Faman thaqulat mawazeenuhu faolaika humu almuflihoon

# 2776

Waman khaffat mawazeenuhu faolaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum fee jahannama khalidoon

# 2777

Talfahu wujoohahumu annaru wahum feeha kalihoon

# 2778

Alam takun ayatee tutla 'alaykum fakuntum biha tukaththiboon

# 2779

Qaloo rabbana ghalabat 'alayna shiqwatuna wakunna qawman dalleen

# 2780

Rabbana akhrijna minha fain 'udna fainna thalimoon

# 2781

Qala ikhsaoo feeha wala tukallimoon

# 2782

Innahu kana fareequn min 'ibadee yaqooloona rabbana amanna faghfir lana warhamna waanta khayru arrahimeen

# 2783

Fattakhathtumoohum sikhriyyan hatta ansawkum thikree wakuntum minhum tadhakoon

# 2784

Innee jazaytuhumu alyawma bima sabaroo annahum humu alfaizoon

# 2785

Qala kam labithtum fee alardi 'adada sineen

# 2786

Qaloo labithna yawman aw ba'da yawmin fasali al'addeen

# 2787

Qala in labithtum illa qaleelan law annakum kuntum ta'lamoon

# 2788

Afahasibtum annama khalaqnakum 'abathan waannakum ilayna la turja'oon

# 2789

Fata'ala Allahu almaliku alhaqqu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu al'arshi alkareem

# 2790

Waman yad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara la burhana lahu bihi fainnama hisabuhu 'inda rabbihi innahu la yuflihu alkafiroon

# 2791

Waqul rabbi ighfir warham waanta khayru arrahimeen

# 2792

Sooratun anzalnaha wafaradnaha waanzalna feeha ayatin bayyinatin la'allakum tathakkaroon

# 2793

Azzaniyatu wazzanee fajlidoo kulla wahidin minhuma miata jaldatin wala takhuthkum bihima rafatun fee deeni Allahi in kuntum tuminoona billahi walyawmi alakhiri walyashhad 'athabahuma taifatun mina almumineen

# 2794

Azzanee la yankihu illa zaniyatan aw mushrikatan wazzaniyatu la yankihuha illa zanin aw mushrikun wahurrima thalika 'ala almumineen

# 2795

Wallatheena yarmoona almuhsanati thumma lam yatoo biarba'ati shuhadaa fajlidoohum thamaneena jaldatan wala taqbaloo lahum shahadatan abadan waolaika humu alfasiqoon

# 2796

Illa allatheena taboo min ba'di thalika waaslahoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 2797

Wallatheena yarmoona azwajahum walam yakun lahum shuhadao illa anfusuhum fashahadatu ahadihim arba'u shahadatin billahi innahu lamina assadiqeen

# 2798

Walkhamisatu anna la'nata Allahi 'alayhi in kana mina alkathibeen

# 2799

Wayadrao 'anha al'athaba an tashhada arba'a shahadatin billahi innahu lamina alkathibeen

# 2800

Walkhamisata anna ghadaba Allahi 'alayha in kana mina assadiqeen

# 2801

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha tawwabun hakeem

# 2802

Inna allatheena jaoo bilifki 'usbatun minkum la tahsaboohu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli imriin minhum ma iktasaba mina alithmi wallathee tawalla kibrahu minhum lahu 'athabun 'atheem

# 2803

Lawla ith sami'tumoohu thanna almuminoona walmuminatu bianfusihim khayran waqaloo hatha ifkun mubeen

# 2804

Lawla jaoo 'alayhi biarba'ati shuhadaa faith lam yatoo bishshuhadai faolaika 'inda Allahi humu alkathiboon

# 2805

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu fee addunya walakhirati lamassakum fee ma afadtum feehi 'athabun 'atheem

# 2806

Ith talaqqawnahu bialsinatikum wataqooloona biafwahikum ma laysa lakum bihi 'ilmun watahsaboonahu hayyinan wahuwa 'inda Allahi 'atheem

# 2807

Walawla ith sami'tumoohu qultum ma yakoonu lana an natakallama bihatha subhanaka hatha buhtanun 'atheem

# 2808

Ya'ithukumu Allahu an ta'oodoo limithlihi abadan in kuntum mumineen

# 2809

Wayubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 2810

Inna allatheena yuhibboona an tashee'a alfahishatu fee allatheena amanoo lahum 'athabun aleemun fee addunya walakhirati wallahu ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoon

# 2811

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha raoofun raheem

# 2812

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattabi'oo khutuwati ashshaytani waman yattabi' khutuwati ashshaytani fainnahu yamuru bilfahshai walmunkari walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu ma zaka minkum min ahadin abadan walakinna Allaha yuzakkee man yashao wallahu samee'un 'aleem

# 2813

Wala yatali oloo alfadli minkum wassa'ati an yutoo olee alqurba walmasakeena walmuhajireena fee sabeeli Allahi walya'foo walyasfahoo ala tuhibboona an yaghfira Allahu lakum wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 2814

Inna allatheena yarmoona almuhsanati alghafilati almuminati lu'inoo fee addunya walakhirati walahum 'athabun 'atheem

# 2815

Yawma tashhadu 'alayhim alsinatuhum waaydeehim waarjuluhum bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 2816

Yawmaithin yuwaffeehimu Allahu deenahumu alhaqqa waya'lamoona anna Allaha huwa alhaqqu almubeen

# 2817

Alkhabeethatu lilkhabeetheena walkhabeethoona lilkhabeethati wattayyibatu littayyibeena wattayyiboona littayyibati olaika mubarraoona mimma yaqooloona lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem

# 2818

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra buyootikum hatta tastanisoo watusallimoo 'ala ahliha thalikum khayrun lakum la'allakum tathakkaroon

# 2819

Fain lam tajidoo feeha ahadan fala tadkhulooha hatta yuthana lakum wain qeela lakumu irji'oo farji'oo huwa azka lakum wallahu bima ta'maloona 'aleem

# 2820

Laysa 'alaykum junahun an tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra maskoonatin feeha mata'un lakum wallahu ya'lamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoon

# 2821

Qul lilmumineena yaghuddoo min absarihum wayahfathoo furoojahum thalika azka lahum inna Allaha khabeerun bima yasna'oon

# 2822

Waqul lilmuminati yaghdudna min absarihinna wayahfathna furoojahunna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa ma thahara minha walyadribna bikhumurihinna 'ala juyoobihinna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa libu'oolatihinna aw abaihinna aw abai bu'oolatihinna aw abnaihinna aw abnai bu'oolatihinna aw ikhwanihinna aw banee ikhwanihinna aw banee akhawatihinna aw nisaihinna aw ma malakat aymanuhunna awi attabi'eena ghayri olee alirbati mina arrijali awi attifli allatheena lam yathharoo 'ala 'awrati annisai wala yadribna biarjulihinna liyu'lama ma yukhfeena min zeenatihinna watooboo ila Allahi jamee'an ayyuha almuminoona la'allakum tuflihoon

# 2823

Waankihoo alayama minkum wassaliheena min 'ibadikum waimaikum in yakoonoo fuqaraa yughnihimu Allahu min fadlihi wallahu wasi'un 'aleem

# 2824

Walyasta'fifi allatheena la yajidoona nikahan hatta yughniyahumu Allahu min fadlihi wallatheena yabtaghoona alkitaba mimma malakat aymanukum fakatiboohum in 'alimtum feehim khayran waatoohum min mali Allahi allathee atakum wala tukrihoo fatayatikum 'ala albighai in aradna tahassunan litabtaghoo 'arada alhayati addunya waman yukrihhunna fainna Allaha min ba'di ikrahihinna ghafoorun raheem

# 2825

Walaqad anzalna ilaykum ayatin mubayyinatin wamathalan mina allatheena khalaw min qablikum wamaw'ithatan lilmuttaqeen

# 2826

Allahu nooru assamawati walardi mathalu noorihi kamishkatin feeha misbahun almisbahu fee zujajatin azzujajatu kaannaha kawkabun durriyyun yooqadu min shajaratin mubarakatin zaytoonatin la sharqiyyatin wala gharbiyyatin yakadu zaytuha yudeeo walaw lam tamsashu narun noorun 'ala noorin yahdee Allahu linoorihi man yashao wayadribu Allahu alamthala linnasi wallahu bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 2827

Fee buyootin athina Allahu an turfa'a wayuthkara feeha ismuhu yusabbihu lahu feeha bilghuduwwi walasal

# 2828

Rijalun la tulheehim tijaratun wala bay'un 'an thikri Allahi waiqami assalati waeetai azzakati yakhafoona yawman tataqallabu feehi alquloobu walabsar

# 2829

Liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma 'amiloo wayazeedahum min fadlihi wallahu yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisab

# 2830

Wallatheena kafaroo a'maluhum kasarabin biqee'atin yahsabuhu aththamanu maan hatta itha jaahu lam yajidhu shayan wawajada Allaha 'indahu fawaffahu hisabahu wallahu saree'u alhisab

# 2831

Aw kathulumatin fee bahrin lujjiyyin yaghshahu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sahabun thulumatun ba'duha fawqa ba'din itha akhraja yadahu lam yakad yaraha waman lam yaj'ali Allahu lahu nooran fama lahu min noor

# 2832

Alam tara anna Allaha yusabbihu lahu man fee assamawati walardi wattayru saffatin kullun qad 'alima salatahu watasbeehahu wallahu 'aleemun bima yaf'aloon

# 2833

Walillahi mulku assamawati walardi waila Allahi almaseer

# 2834

Alam tara anna Allaha yuzjee sahaban thumma yuallifu baynahu thumma yaj'aluhu rukaman fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi wayunazzilu mina assamai min jibalin feeha min baradin fayuseebu bihi man yashao wayasrifuhu 'an man yashao yakadu sana barqihi yathhabu bilabsar

# 2835

Yuqallibu Allahu allayla wannahara inna fee thalika la'ibratan liolee alabsar

# 2836

Wallahu khalaqa kulla dabbatin min main faminhum man yamshee 'ala batnihi waminhum man yamshee 'ala rijlayni waminhum man yamshee 'ala arba'in yakhluqu Allahu ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 2837

Laqad anzalna ayatin mubayyinatin wallahu yahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeem

# 2838

Wayaqooloona amanna billahi wabirrasooli waata'na thumma yatawalla fareequn minhum min ba'di thalika wama olaika bilmumineen

# 2839

Waitha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum itha fareequn minhum mu'ridoon

# 2840

Wain yakun lahumu alhaqqu yatoo ilayhi muth'ineen

# 2841

Afee quloobihim maradun ami irtaboo am yakhafoona an yaheefa Allahu 'alayhim warasooluhu bal olaika humu aththalimoon

# 2842

Innama kana qawla almumineena itha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum an yaqooloo sami'na waata'na waolaika humu almuflihoon

# 2843

Waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu wayakhsha Allaha wayattaqhi faolaika humu alfaizoon

# 2844

Waaqsamoo billahi jahda aymanihim lain amartahum layakhrujunna qul la tuqsimoo ta'atun ma'roofatun inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloon

# 2845

Qul atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayhi ma hummila wa'alaykum ma hummiltum wain tutee'oohu tahtadoo wama 'ala arrasooli illa albalaghu almubeen

# 2846

Wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum wa'amiloo assalihati layastakhlifannahum fee alardi kama istakhlafa allatheena min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum deenahumu allathee irtada lahum walayubaddilannahum min ba'di khawfihim amnan ya'budoonanee la yushrikoona bee shayan waman kafara ba'da thalika faolaika humu alfasiqoon

# 2847

Waaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata waatee'oo arrasoola la'allakum turhamoon

# 2848

La tahsabanna allatheena kafaroo mu'jizeena fee alardi wamawahumu annaru walabisa almaseer

# 2849

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo liyastathinkumu allatheena malakat aymanukum wallatheena lam yablughoo alhuluma minkum thalatha marratin min qabli salati alfajri waheena tada'oona thiyabakum mina aththaheerati wamin ba'di salati al'ishai thalathu 'awratin lakum laysa 'alaykum wala 'alayhim junahun ba'dahunna tawwafoona 'alaykum ba'dukum 'ala ba'din kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 2850

Waitha balagha alatfalu minkumu alhuluma falyastathinoo kama istathana allatheena min qablihim kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 2851

Walqawa'idu mina annisai allatee la yarjoona nikahan falaysa 'alayhinna junahun an yada'na thiyabahunna ghayra mutabarrijatin bizeenatin waan yasta'fifna khayrun lahunna wallahu samee'un 'aleem

# 2852

Laysa 'ala ala'ma harajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun wala 'ala anfusikum an takuloo min buyootikum aw buyooti abaikum aw buyooti ommahatikum aw buyooti ikhwanikum aw buyooti akhawatikum aw buyooti a'mamikum aw buyooti 'ammatikum aw buyooti akhwalikum aw buyooti khalatikum aw ma malaktum mafatihahu aw sadeeqikum laysa 'alaykum junahun an takuloo jamee'an aw ashtatan faitha dakhaltum buyootan fasallimoo 'ala anfusikum tahiyyatan min 'indi Allahi mubarakatan tayyibatan kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati la'allakum ta'qiloon

# 2853

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo billahi warasoolihi waitha kanoo ma'ahu 'ala amrin jami'in lam yathhaboo hatta yastathinoohu inna allatheena yastathinoonaka olaika allatheena yuminoona billahi warasoolihi faitha istathanooka liba'di shanihim fathan liman shita minhum wastaghfir lahumu Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 2854

La taj'aloo du'aa arrasooli baynakum kadu'ai ba'dikum ba'dan qad ya'lamu Allahu allatheena yatasallaloona minkum liwathan falyahthari allatheena yukhalifoona 'an amrihi an tuseebahum fitnatun aw yuseebahum 'athabun aleem

# 2855

Ala inna lillahi ma fee assamawati walardi qad ya'lamu ma antum 'alayhi wayawma yurja'oona ilayhi fayunabbiohum bima 'amiloo wallahu bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 2856

Tabaraka allathee nazzala alfurqana 'ala 'abdihi liyakoona lil'alameena natheera

# 2857

Allathee lahu mulku assamawati walardi walam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki wakhalaqa kulla shayin faqaddarahu taqdeera

# 2858

Wattakhathoo min doonihi alihatan la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona wala yamlikoona lianfusihim darran wala naf'an wala yamlikoona mawtan wala hayatan wala nushoora

# 2859

# 2860

Waqaloo asateeru alawwaleena iktatabaha fahiya tumla 'alayhi bukratan waaseela

# 2861

# 2862

# 2863

# 2864

# 2865

# 2866

# 2871

# 2872

# 2873

# 2874

# 2875

# 2876
