Walaw nazzalnahu 'ala ba'di ala'jameen

# 3131

Faqaraahu 'alayhim ma kanoo bihi mumineen

# 3132

Kathalika salaknahu fee quloobi almujrimeen

# 3133

La yuminoona bihi hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleem

# 3134

Fayatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon

# 3135

Fayaqooloo hal nahnu muntharoon

# 3136

Afabi'athabina yasta'jiloon

# 3137

Afaraayta in matta'nahum sineen

# 3138

Thumma jaahum ma kanoo yoo'adoon

# 3139

Ma aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yumatta'oon

# 3140

Wama ahlakna min qaryatin illa laha munthiroon

# 3141

Thikra wama kunna thalimeen

# 3142

Wama tanazzalat bihi ashshayateen

# 3143

Wama yanbaghee lahum wama yastatee'oon

# 3144

Innahum 'ani assam'i lama'zooloona

# 3145

Fala tad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fatakoona mina almu'aththabeen

# 3146

Waanthir 'asheerataka alaqrabeen

# 3147

Wakhfid janahaka limani ittaba'aka mina almumineen

# 3148

Fain 'asawka faqul innee bareeon mimma ta'maloon

# 3149

Watawakkal 'ala al'azeezi arraheem

# 3150

Allathee yaraka heena taqoom

# 3151

Wataqallubaka fee assajideen

# 3152

Innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 3153

Hal onabbiokum 'ala man tanazzalu ashshayateen

# 3154

Tanazzalu 'ala kulli affakin atheem

# 3155

Yulqoona assam'a waaktharuhum kathiboon

# 3156

Washshu'arao yattabi'uhumu alghawoon

# 3157

Alam tara annahum fee kulli wadin yaheemoon

# 3158

Waannahum yaqooloona ma la yaf'aloon

# 3159

Illa allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wathakaroo Allaha katheeran wantasaroo min ba'di ma thulimoo wasaya'lamu allatheena thalamoo ayya munqalabin yanqaliboon

# 3160

Taseen tilka ayatu alqurani wakitabin mubeen

# 3161

Hudan wabushra lilmumineen

# 3162

Allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wahum bilakhirati hum yooqinoon

# 3163

Inna allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati zayyanna lahum a'malahum fahum ya'mahoon

# 3164

Olaika allatheena lahum sooo al'athabi wahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroon

# 3165

Wainnaka latulaqqa alqurana min ladun hakeemin 'aleem

# 3166

Ith qala moosa liahlihi innee anastu naran saateekum minha bikhabarin aw ateekum bishihabin qabasin la'allakum tastaloon

# 3167

Falamma jaaha noodiya an boorika man fee annari waman hawlaha wasubhana Allahi rabbi al'alameen

# 3168

Ya moosa innahu ana Allahu al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3169

Waalqi 'asaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yu'aqqib ya moosa la takhaf innee la yakhafu ladayya almursaloon

# 3170

Illa man thalama thumma baddala husnan ba'da sooin fainnee ghafoorun raheem

# 3171

Waadkhil yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin fee tis'i ayatin ila fir'awna waqawmihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen

# 3172

Falamma jaathum ayatuna mubsiratan qaloo hatha sihrun mubeen

# 3173

Wajahadoo biha wastayqanatha anfusuhum thulman wa'uluwwan fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideen

# 3174

Walaqad atayna dawooda wasulaymana 'ilman waqala alhamdu lillahi allathee faddalana 'ala katheerin min 'ibadihi almumineen

# 3175

Wawaritha sulaymanu dawooda waqala ya ayyuha annasu 'ullimna mantiqa attayri waooteena min kulli shayin inna hatha lahuwa alfadlu almubeen

# 3176

Wahushira lisulaymana junooduhu mina aljinni walinsi wattayri fahum yooza'oon

# 3177

Hatta itha ataw 'ala wadi annamli qalat namlatun ya ayyuha annamlu odkhuloo masakinakum la yahtimannakum sulaymanu wajunooduhu wahum la yash'uroon

# 3178

Fatabassama dahikan min qawliha waqala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waadkhilnee birahmatika fee 'ibadika assaliheen

# 3179

Watafaqqada attayra faqala ma liya la ara alhudhuda am kana mina alghaibeen

# 3180

Lao'aththibannahu 'athaban shadeedan aw laathbahannahu aw layatiyannee bisultanin mubeen

# 3181

Famakatha ghayra ba'eedin faqala ahattu bima lam tuhit bihi wajituka min sabain binabain yaqeen

# 3182

Innee wajadtu imraatan tamlikuhum waootiyat min kulli shayin walaha 'arshun 'atheem

# 3183

Wajadtuha waqawmaha yasjudoona lishshamsi min dooni Allahi wazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum fasaddahum 'ani assabeeli fahum la yahtadoon

# 3184

Alla yasjudoo lillahi allathee yukhriju alkhabaa fee assamawati walardi waya'lamu ma tukhfoona wama tu'linoon

# 3185

Allahu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu al'arshi al'atheem

# 3186

Qala sananthuru asadaqta am kunta mina alkathibeen

# 3187

Ithhab bikitabee hatha faalqih ilayhim thumma tawalla 'anhum fanthur matha yarji'oon

# 3188

Qalat ya ayyuha almalao innee olqiya ilayya kitabun kareem

# 3189

Innahu min sulaymana wainnahu bismi Allahi arrahmani arraheem

# 3190

Alla ta'loo 'alayya watoonee muslimeen

# 3191

Qalat ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee amree ma kuntu qati'atan amran hatta tashhadoon

# 3192

Qaloo nahnu oloo quwwatin waoloo basin shadeedin walamru ilayki fanthuree matha tamureen

# 3193

Qalat inna almulooka itha dakhaloo qaryatan afsadooha waja'aloo a'izzata ahliha athillatan wakathalika yaf'aloon

# 3194

Wainnee mursilatun ilayhim bihadiyyatin fanathiratun bima yarji'u almursaloon

# 3195

Falamma jaa sulaymana qala atumiddoonani bimalin fama ataniya Allahu khayrun mimma atakum bal antum bihadiyyatikum tafrahoon

# 3196

Irji' ilayhim falanatiyannahum bijunoodin la qibala lahum biha walanukhrijannahum minha athillatan wahum saghiroon

# 3197

Qala ya ayyuha almalao ayyukum yateenee bi'arshiha qabla an yatoonee muslimeen

# 3198

Qala 'ifreetun mina aljinni ana ateeka bihi qabla an taqooma min maqamika wainne 'alayhi laqawiyyun ameen

# 3199

Qala allathee 'indahu 'ilmun mina alkitabi ana ateeka bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka tarfuka falamma raahu mustaqirran 'indahu qala hatha min fadli rabbee liyabluwanee aashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna rabbee ghaniyyun kareem

# 3200

Qala nakkiroo laha 'arshaha nanthur atahtadee am takoonu mina allatheena la yahtadoon

# 3201

Falamma jaat qeela ahakatha 'arshuki qalat kaannahu huwa waooteena al'ilma min qabliha wakunna muslimeen

# 3202

Wasaddaha ma kanat ta'budu min dooni Allahi innaha kanat min qawmin kafireen

# 3203

Qeela laha odkhulee assarha falamma raathu hasibathu lujjatan wakashafat 'an saqayha qala innahu sarhun mumarradun min qawareera qalat rabbi innee thalamtu nafsee waaslamtu ma'a sulaymana lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 3204

Walaqad arsalna ila thamooda akhahum salihan ani o'budoo Allaha faitha hum fareeqani yakhtasimoon

# 3205

Qala ya qawmi lima tasta'jiloona bissayyiati qabla alhasanati lawla tastaghfiroona Allaha la'allakum turhamoon

# 3206

Qaloo ittayyarna bika wabiman ma'aka qala tairukum 'inda Allahi bal antum qawmun tuftanoon

# 3207

Wakana fee almadeenati tis'atu rahtin yufsidoona fee alardi wala yuslihoon

# 3208

Qaloo taqasamoo billahi lanubayyitannahu waahlahu thumma lanaqoolanna liwaliyyihi ma shahidna mahlika ahlihi wainna lasadiqoon

# 3209

Wamakaroo makran wamakarna makran wahum la yash'uroon

# 3210

Fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu makrihim anna dammarnahum waqawmahum ajma'een

# 3211

Fatilka buyootuhum khawiyatan bima thalamoo inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 3212

Waanjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon

# 3213

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata waantum tubsiroon

# 3214

Ainnakum latatoona arrijala shahwatan min dooni annisai bal antum qawmun tajhaloon

# 3215

Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoo ala lootin min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoon

# 3216

Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu qaddarnaha mina alghabireen

# 3217

Waamtarna 'alayhim mataran fasaa mataru almunthareen

# 3218

Quli alhamdu lillahi wasalamun 'ala 'ibadihi allatheena istafa allahu khayrun amma yushrikoon

# 3219

Amman khalaqa assamawati walarda waanzala lakum mina assamai maan faanbatna bihi hadaiqa thata bahjatin ma kana lakum an tunbitoo shajaraha ailahun ma'a Allahi bal hum qawmun ya'diloon

# 3220

Amman ja'ala alarda qararan waja'ala khilalaha anharan waja'ala laha rawasiya waja'ala bayna albahrayni hajizan ailahun ma'a Allahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon

# 3221

Amman yujeebu almudtarra itha da'ahu wayakshifu assooa wayaj'alukum khulafaa alardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qaleelan ma tathakkaroon

# 3222

Amman yahdeekum fee thulumati albarri walbahri waman yursilu arriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi ailahun ma'a Allahi ta'ala Allahu 'amma yushrikoon

# 3223

Amman yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu waman yarzuqukum mina assamai walardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qul hatoo burhanakum in kuntum sadiqeen

# 3224

Qul la ya'lamu man fee assamawati walardi alghayba illa Allahu wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoon

# 3225

Bali iddaraka 'ilmuhum fee alakhirati bal hum fee shakkin minha bal hum minha 'amoon

# 3226

Waqala allatheena kafaroo aitha kunna turaban waabaona ainna lamukhrajoon

# 3227

Laqad wu'idna hatha nahnu waabaona min qablu in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen

# 3228

Qul seeroo fee alardi fanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almujrimeen

# 3229

Wala tahzan 'alayhim wala takun fee dayqin mimma yamkuroon

# 3230

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen

# 3231

Qul 'asa an yakoona radifa lakum ba'du allathee tasta'jiloon

# 3232

Wainna rabbaka lathoo fadlin 'ala annasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroon

# 3233

Wainna rabbaka laya'lamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yu'linoon

# 3234

Wama min ghaibatin fee assamai walardi illa fee kitabin mubeen

# 3235

Inna hatha alqurana yaqussu 'ala banee israeela akthara allathee hum feehi yakhtalifoon

# 3236

Wainnahu lahudan warahmatun lilmumineen

# 3237

Inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum bihukmihi wahuwa al'azeezu al'aleem

# 3238

Fatawakkal 'ala Allahi innaka 'ala alhaqqi almubeen

# 3239

Innaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u assumma addu'aa itha wallaw mudbireen

# 3240

Wama anta bihadee al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoon

# 3241

Waitha waqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim akhrajna lahum dabbatan mina alardi tukallimuhum anna annasa kanoo biayatina la yooqinoon

# 3242

Wayawma nahshuru min kulli ommatin fawjan mimman yukaththibu biayatina fahum yooza'oon

# 3243

Hatta itha jaoo qala akaththabtum biayatee walam tuheetoo biha 'ilman ammatha kuntum ta'maloon

# 3244

Wawaqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim bima thalamoo fahum la yantiqoon

# 3245

Alam yaraw anna ja'alna allayla liyaskunoo feehi wannahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 3246

Wayawma yunfakhu fee assoori fafazi'a man fee assamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu wakullun atawhu dakhireen

# 3247

Watara aljibala tahsabuha jamidatan wahiya tamurru marra assahabi sun'a Allahi allathee atqana kulla shayin innahu khabeerun bima taf'aloon

# 3248

Man jaa bilhasanati falahu khayrun minha wahum min faza'in yawmaithin aminoon

# 3249

Waman jaa bissayyiati fakubbat wujoohuhum fee annari hal tujzawna illa ma kuntum ta'maloon

# 3250

Innama omirtu an a'buda rabba hathihi albaldati allathee harramaha walahu kullu shayin waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeen

# 3251

Waan atluwa alqurana famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla faqul innama ana mina almunthireen

# 3252

Waquli alhamdu lillahi sayureekum ayatihi fata'rifoonaha wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloon

# 3253

Taseenmeem

# 3254

Tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeen

# 3255

Natloo 'alayka min nabai moosa wafir'awna bilhaqqi liqawmin yuminoon

# 3256

Inna fir'awna 'ala fee alardi waja'ala ahlaha shiya'an yastad'ifu taifatan minhum yuthabbihu abnaahum wayastahyee nisaahum innahu kana mina almufsideen

# 3257

Wanureedu an namunna 'ala allatheena istud'ifoo fee alardi wanaj'alahum aimmatan wanaj'alahumu alwaritheen

# 3258

Wanumakkina lahum fee alardi wanuriya fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma minhum ma kanoo yahtharoon

# 3259

Waawhayna ila ommi moosa an ardi'eehi faitha khifti 'alayhi faalqeehi fee alyammi wala takhafee wala tahzanee inna raddoohu ilayki waja'iloohu mina almursaleen

# 3260

Faltaqatahu alu fir'awna liyakoona lahum 'aduwwan wahazanan inna fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma kanoo khatieen

# 3261

Waqalati imraatu fir'awna qurratu 'aynin lee walaka la taqtuloohu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wahum la yash'uroon

# 3262

Waasbaha fuadu ommi moosa farighan in kadat latubdee bihi lawla an rabatna 'ala qalbiha litakoona mina almumineen

# 3263

Waqalat liokhtihi qusseehi fabasurat bihi 'an junubin wahum la yash'uroon

# 3264

Waharramna 'alayhi almaradi'a min qablu faqalat hal adullukum 'ala ahli baytin yakfuloonahu lakum wahum lahu nasihoon

# 3265

Faradadnahu ila ommihi kay taqarra 'aynuha wala tahzana walita'lama anna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 3266

Walamma balagha ashuddahu wastawa ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineen

# 3267

Wadakhala almadeenata 'ala heeni ghaflatin min ahliha fawajada feeha rajulayni yaqtatilani hatha min shee'atihi wahatha min 'aduwwihi fastaghathahu allathee min shee'atihi 'ala allathee min 'aduwwihi fawakazahu moosa faqada 'alayhi qala hatha min 'amali ashshaytani innahu 'aduwwun mudillun mubeen

# 3268

Qala rabbi innee thalamtu nafsee faghfir lee faghafara lahu innahu huwa alghafooru arraheem

# 3269

Qala rabbi bima an'amta 'alayya falan akoona thaheeran lilmujrimeen

# 3270

Faasbaha fee almadeenati khaifan yataraqqabu faitha allathee istansarahu bilamsi yastasrikhuhu qala lahu moosa innaka laghawiyyun mubeen

# 3271

Falamma an arada an yabtisha billathee huwa 'aduwwun lahuma qala ya moosa atureedu an taqtulanee kama qatalta nafsan bilamsi in tureedu illa an takoona jabbaran fee alardi wama tureedu an takoona mina almusliheen

# 3272

Wajaa rajulun min aqsa almadeenati yas'a qala ya moosa inna almalaa yatamiroona bika liyaqtulooka fakhruj innee laka mina annasiheen

# 3273

Fakharaja minha khaifan yataraqqabu qala rabbi najjinee mina alqawmi aththalimeen

# 3274

Walamma tawajjaha tilqaa madyana qala 'asa rabbee an yahdiyanee sawaa assabeel

# 3275

Walamma warada maa madyana wajada 'alayhi ommatan mina annasi yasqoona wawajada min doonihimu imraatayni tathoodani qala ma khatbukuma qalata la nasqee hatta yusdira arri'ao waaboona shaykhun kabeer

# 3276

Fasaqa lahuma thumma tawalla ila aththilli faqala rabbi innee lima anzalta ilayya min khayrin faqeer

# 3277

Fajaathu ihdahuma tamshee 'ala istihyain qalat inna abee yad'ooka liyajziyaka ajra ma saqayta lana falamma jaahu waqassa 'alayhi alqasasa qala la takhaf najawta mina alqawmi aththalimeen

# 3278

Qalat ihdahuma ya abati istajirhu inna khayra mani istajarta alqawiyyu alameen

# 3279

Qala innee oreedu an onkihaka ihda ibnatayya hatayni 'ala an tajuranee thamaniya hijajin fain atmamta 'ashran famin 'indika wama oreedu an ashuqqa 'alayka satajidunee in shaa Allahu mina assaliheen

# 3280

Qala thalika baynee wabaynaka ayyama alajalayni qadaytu fala 'udwana 'alayya wallahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeel

# 3281

Falamma qada moosaalajala wasara biahlihi anasa min janibi attoori naran qala liahlihi omkuthoo innee anastu naran la'allee ateekum minha bikhabarin aw jathwatin mina annari la'allakum tastaloon

# 3282

Falamma ataha noodiya min shatii alwadi alaymani fee albuq'ati almubarakati mina ashshajarati an ya moosa innee ana Allahu rabbu al'alameen

# 3283

Waan alqi 'asaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yu'aqqib ya moosa aqbil wala takhaf innaka mina alamineen

# 3284

Osluk yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin wadmum ilayka janahaka mina arrahbi fathanika burhanani min rabbika ila fir'awna wamalaihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen

# 3285

Qala rabbi innee qataltu minhum nafsan faakhafu an yaqtuloon

# 3286

Waakhee haroonu huwa afsahu minnee lisanan faarsilhu ma'iya ridan yusaddiqunee innee akhafu an yukaththiboon

# 3287

Qala sanashuddu 'adudaka biakheeka wanaj'alu lakuma sultanan fala yasiloona ilaykuma biayatina antuma wamani ittaba'akuma alghaliboon

# 3288

Falamma jaahum moosa biayatina bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa sihrun muftaran wama sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleen

# 3289

Waqala moosa rabbee a'lamu biman jaa bilhuda min 'indihi waman takoonu lahu 'aqibatu addari innahu la yuflihu aththalimoon

# 3290

Waqala fir'awnu ya ayyuha almalao ma 'alimtu lakum min ilahin ghayree faawqid lee ya hamanu 'ala atteeni faj'al lee sarhan la'allee attali'u ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu mina alkathibeen

# 3291

Wastakbara huwa wajunooduhu fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wathannoo annahum ilayna la yurja'oon

# 3292

Faakhathnahu wajunoodahu fanabathnahum fee alyammi fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu aththalimeen

# 3293

Waja'alnahum aimmatan yad'oona ila annari wayawma alqiyamati la yunsaroon

# 3294

Waatba'nahum fee hathihi addunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati hum mina almaqbooheen

# 3295

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba min ba'di ma ahlakna alquroona aloola basaira linnasi wahudan warahmatan la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 3296

Wama kunta bijanibi algharbiyyi ith qadayna ila moosa alamra wama kunta mina ashshahideen

# 3297

Walakinna anshana quroonan fatatawala 'alayhimu al'umuru wama kunta thawiyan fee ahli madyana tatloo 'alayhim ayatina walakinna kunna mursileen

# 3298

Wama kunta bijanibi attoori ith nadayna walakin rahmatan min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 3299

Walawla an tuseebahum museebatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fayaqooloo rabbana lawla arsalta ilayna rasoolan fanattabi'a ayatika wanakoona mina almumineen

# 3300

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo lawla ootiya mithla ma ootiya moosa awalam yakfuroo bima ootiya moosa min qablu qaloo sihrani tathahara waqaloo inna bikullin kafiroon

# 3301

Qul fatoo bikitabin min 'indi Allahi huwa ahda minhuma attabi'hu in kuntum sadiqeen

# 3302

Fain lam yastajeeboo laka fa'lam annama yattabi'oona ahwaahum waman adallu mimmani ittaba'a hawahu bighayri hudan mina Allahi inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 3303

Walaqad wassalna lahumu alqawla la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 3304

Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba min qablihi hum bihi yuminoon

# 3305

Waitha yutla 'alayhim qaloo amanna bihi innahu alhaqqu min rabbina inna kunna min qablihi muslimeen

# 3306

Olaika yutawna ajrahum marratayni bima sabaroo wayadraoona bilhasanati assayyiata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon

# 3307

Waitha sami'oo allaghwa a'radoo 'anhu waqaloo lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum salamun 'alaykum la nabtaghee aljahileen

# 3308

Innaka la tahdee man ahbabta walakinna Allaha yahdee man yashao wahuwa a'lamu bilmuhtadeen

# 3309

Waqaloo in nattabi'i alhuda ma'aka nutakhattaf min ardina awalam numakkin lahum haraman aminan yujba ilayhi thamaratu kulli shayin rizqan min ladunna walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 3310

Wakam ahlakna min qaryatin batirat ma'eeshataha fatilka masakinuhum lam tuskan min ba'dihim illa qaleelan wakunna nahnu alwaritheen

# 3311

Wama kana rabbuka muhlika alqura hatta yab'atha fee ommiha rasoolan yatloo 'alayhim ayatina wama kunna muhlikee alqura illa waahluha thalimoon

# 3312

Wama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati addunya wazeenatuha wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa afala ta'qiloon

# 3313

Afaman wa'adnahu wa'dan hasanan fahuwa laqeehi kaman matta'nahu mata'a alhayati addunya thumma huwa yawma alqiyamati mina almuhdareen

# 3314

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoon

# 3315

Qala allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu rabbana haolai allatheena aghwayna aghwaynahum kama ghawayna tabarrana ilayka ma kanoo iyyana ya'budoon

# 3316

Waqeela od'oo shurakaakum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waraawoo al'athaba law annahum kanoo yahtadoon

# 3317

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu matha ajabtumu almursaleen

# 3318

Fa'amiyat 'alayhimu alanbao yawmaithin fahum la yatasaaloon

# 3319

Faamma man taba waamana wa'amila salihan fa'asa an yakoona mina almufliheen

# 3320

Warabbuka yakhluqu ma yashao wayakhtaru ma kana lahumu alkhiyaratu subhana Allahi wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 3321

Warabbuka ya'lamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yu'linoon

# 3322

Wahuwa Allahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu alhamdu fee aloola walakhirati walahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oon

# 3323

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu allayla sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bidiyain afala tasma'oon

# 3324

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu annahara sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bilaylin taskunoona feehi afala tubsiroon

# 3325

Wamin rahmatihi ja'ala lakumu allayla wannahara litaskunoo feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon

# 3326

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoon

# 3327

Wanaza'na min kulli ommatin shaheedan faqulna hatoo burhanakum fa'alimoo anna alhaqqa lillahi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon

# 3328

Inna qaroona kana min qawmi moosa fabagha 'alayhim waataynahu mina alkunoozi ma inna mafatihahu latanooo bil'usbati olee alquwwati ith qala lahu qawmuhu la tafrah inna Allaha la yuhibbu alfariheen

# 3329

Wabtaghi feema ataka Allahu addara alakhirata wala tansa naseebaka mina addunya waahsin kama ahsana Allahu ilayka wala tabghi alfasada fee alardi inna Allaha la yuhibbu almufsideen

# 3330

Qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin 'indee awalam ya'lam anna Allaha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina alqurooni man huwa ashaddu minhu quwwatan waaktharu jam'an wala yusalu 'an thunoobihimu almujrimoon

# 3331

Fakharaja 'ala qawmihi fee zeenatihi qala allatheena yureedoona alhayata addunya ya layta lana mithla ma ootiya qaroonu innahu lathoo haththin 'atheem

# 3332

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma waylakum thawabu Allahi khayrun liman amana wa'amila salihan wala yulaqqaha illa assabiroon

# 3333

Fakhasafna bihi wabidarihi alarda fama kana lahu min fiatin yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana mina almuntasireen

# 3334

Waasbaha allatheena tamannaw makanahu bilamsi yaqooloona waykaanna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lawla an manna Allahu 'alayna lakhasafa bina waykaannahu la yuflihu alkafiroon

# 3335

Tilka addaru alakhiratu naj'aluha lillatheena la yureedoona 'uluwwan fee alardi wala fasadan wal'aqibatu lilmuttaqeen

# 3336

Man jaa bilhasanati falahu khayrun minha waman jaa bissayyiati fala yujza allatheena 'amiloo assayyiati illa ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 3337

Inna allathee farada 'alayka alqurana laradduka ila ma'adin qul rabbee a'lamu man jaa bilhuda waman huwa fee dalalin mubeen

# 3338

Wama kunta tarjoo an yulqa ilayka alkitabu illa rahmatan min rabbika fala takoonanna thaheeran lilkafireen

# 3339

Wala yasuddunnaka 'an ayati Allahi ba'da ith onzilat ilayka wad'u ila rabbika wala takoonanna mina almushrikeen

# 3340

Wala tad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara la ilaha illa huwa kullu shayin halikun illa wajhahu lahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oon

# 3341

Aliflammeem

# 3342

Ahasiba annasu an yutrakoo an yaqooloo amanna wahum la yuftanoon

# 3343

Walaqad fatanna allatheena min qablihim falaya'lamanna Allahu allatheena sadaqoo walaya'lamanna alkathibeen

# 3344

Am hasiba allatheena ya'maloona assayyiati an yasbiqoona saa ma yahkumoon

# 3345

Man kana yarjoo liqaa Allahi fainna ajala Allahi laatin wahuwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 3346

Waman jahada fainnama yujahidu linafsihi inna Allaha laghaniyyun 'ani al'alameen

# 3347

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanukaffiranna 'anhum sayyiatihim walanajziyannahum ahsana allathee kanoo ya'maloon

# 3348

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi husnan wain jahadaka litushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 3349

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanudkhilannahum fee assaliheen

# 3350

Wamina annasi man yaqoolu amanna billahi faitha oothiya fee Allahi ja'ala fitnata annasi ka'athabi Allahi walain jaa nasrun min rabbika layaqoolunna inna kunna ma'akum awalaysa Allahu bia'lama bima fee sudoori al'alameen

# 3351

Walaya'lamanna Allahu allatheena amanoo walaya'lamanna almunafiqeen

# 3352

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo ittabi'oo sabeelana walnahmil khatayakum wama hum bihamileena min khatayahum min shayin innahum lakathiboon

# 3353

Walayahmilunna athqalahum waathqalan ma'a athqalihim walayusalunna yawma alqiyamati 'amma kanoo yaftaroon

# 3354

Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi falabitha feehim alfa sanatin illa khamseena 'aman faakhathahumu attoofanu wahum thalimoon

# 3355

Faanjaynahu waashaba assafeenati waja'alnaha ayatan lil'alameen

# 3356

Waibraheema ith qala liqawmihi o'budoo Allaha wattaqoohu thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon

# 3357

Innama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi awthanan watakhluqoona ifkan inna allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona lakum rizqan fabtaghoo 'inda Allahi arrizqa wa'budoohu washkuroo lahu ilayhi turja'oon

# 3358

Wain tukaththiboo faqad kaththaba omamun min qablikum wama 'ala arrasooli illa albalaghu almubeen

# 3359

Awalam yaraw kayfa yubdio Allahu alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer

# 3360

Qul seeroo fee alardi fanthuroo kayfa badaa alkhalqa thumma Allahu yunshio annashata alakhirata inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 3361

Yu'aththibu man yashao wayarhamu man yashao wailayhi tuqlaboon

# 3362

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wala fee assamai wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseer

# 3363

Wallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi waliqaihi olaika yaisoo min rahmatee waolaika lahum 'athabun aleem

# 3364

Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo oqtuloohu aw harriqoohu faanjahu Allahu mina annari inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 3365

Waqala innama ittakhathtum min dooni Allahi awthanan mawaddata baynikum fee alhayati addunya thumma yawma alqiyamati yakfuru ba'dukum biba'din wayal'anu ba'dukum ba'dan wamawakumu annaru wama lakum min nasireen

# 3366

Faamana lahu lootun waqala innee muhajirun ila rabbee innahu huwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3367

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba waja'alna fee thurriyyatihi annubuwwata walkitaba waataynahu ajrahu fee addunya wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina assaliheen

# 3368

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi innakum latatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina al'alameen

# 3369

Ainnakum latatoona arrijala wataqta'oona assabeela watatoona fee nadeekumu almunkara fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo itina bi'athabi Allahi in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 3370

Qala rabbi onsurnee 'ala alqawmi almufsideen

# 3371

Walamma jaat rusuluna ibraheema bilbushra qaloo inna muhlikoo ahli hathihi alqaryati inna ahlaha kanoo thalimeen

# 3372

Qala inna feeha lootan qaloo nahnu a'lamu biman feeha lanunajjiyannahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireen

# 3373

Walamma an jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqaloo la takhaf wala tahzan inna munajjooka waahlaka illa imraataka kanat mina alghabireen

# 3374

Inna munziloona 'ala ahli hathihi alqaryati rijzan mina assamai bima kanoo yafsuqoon

# 3375

Walaqad tarakna minha ayatan bayyinatan liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 3376

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha warjoo alyawma alakhira wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideen

# 3377

Fakaththaboohu faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeen

# 3378

Wa'adan wathamooda waqad tabayyana lakum min masakinihim wazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum fasaddahum 'ani assabeeli wakanoo mustabsireen

# 3379

Waqaroona wafir'awna wahamana walaqad jaahum moosa bilbayyinati fastakbaroo fee alardi wama kanoo sabiqeen

# 3380

Fakullan akhathna bithanbihi faminhum man arsalna 'alayhi hasiban waminhum man akhathathu assayhatu waminhum man khasafna bihi alarda waminhum man aghraqna wama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 3381

Mathalu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa kamathali al'ankabooti ittakhathat baytan wainna awhana albuyooti labaytu al'ankabooti law kanoo ya'lamoon

# 3382

Inna Allaha ya'lamu ma yad'oona min doonihi min shayin wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3383

Watilka alamthalu nadribuha linnasi wama ya'qiluha illa al'alimoon

# 3384

Khalaqa Allahu assamawati walarda bilhaqqi inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineen

# 3385

Otlu ma oohiya ilayka mina alkitabi waaqimi assalata inna assalata tanha 'ani alfahshai walmunkari walathikru Allahi akbaru wallahu ya'lamu ma tasna'oon

# 3386

Wala tujadiloo ahla alkitabi illa billatee hiya ahsanu illa allatheena thalamoo minhum waqooloo amanna billathee onzila ilayna waonzila ilaykum wailahuna wailahukum wahidun wanahnu lahu muslimoon

# 3387

Wakathalika anzalna ilayka alkitaba fallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yuminoona bihi wamin haolai man yuminu bihi wama yajhadu biayatina illa alkafiroon

# 3388

Wama kunta tatloo min qablihi min kitabin wala takhuttuhu biyameenika ithan lartaba almubtiloon

# 3389

Bal huwa ayatun bayyinatun fee sudoori allatheena ootoo al'ilma wama yajhadu biayatina illa aththalimoon

# 3390

Waqaloo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul innama alayatu 'inda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeen

# 3391

Awalam yakfihim anna anzalna 'alayka alkitaba yutla 'alayhim inna fee thalika larahmatan wathikra liqawmin yuminoon

# 3392

Qul kafa billahi baynee wabaynakum shaheedan ya'lamu ma fee assamawati walardi wallatheena amanoo bilbatili wakafaroo billahi olaika humu alkhasiroon

# 3393

Wayasta'jiloonaka bil'athabi walawla ajalun musamman lajaahumu al'athabu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon

# 3394

Yasta'jiloonaka bil'athabi wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bilkafireen

# 3395

Yawma yaghshahumu al'athabu min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim wayaqoolu thooqoo ma kuntum ta'maloon

# 3396

Ya 'ibadiya allatheena amanoo inna ardee wasi'atun faiyyaya fa'budoon

# 3397

Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti thumma ilayna turja'oon

# 3398

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanubawwiannahum mina aljannati ghurafan tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha ni'ma ajru al'amileen

# 3399

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon

# 3400

Wakaayyin min dabbatin la tahmilu rizqaha Allahu yarzuquha waiyyakum wahuwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 3401

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa assamawati walarda wasakhkhara ashshamsa walqamara layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoon

# 3402

Allahu yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 3403

Walain saaltahum man nazzala mina assamai maan faahya bihi alarda min ba'di mawtiha layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'qiloon

# 3404

Wama hathihi alhayatu addunya illa lahwun wala'ibun wainna addara alakhirata lahiya alhayawanu law kanoo ya'lamoon

# 3405

Faitha rakiboo fee alfulki da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena falamma najjahum ila albarri itha hum yushrikoon

# 3406

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum waliyatamatta'oo fasawfa ya'lamoon

# 3407

Awalam yaraw anna ja'alna haraman aminan wayutakhattafu annasu min hawlihim afabilbatili yuminoona wabini'mati Allahi yakfuroon

# 3408

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba bilhaqqi lamma jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireen

# 3409

Wallatheena jahadoo feena lanahdiyannahum subulana wainna Allaha lama'a almuhsineen

# 3410

Aliflammeem

# 3411

Ghulibati arroom

# 3412

Fee adna alardi wahum min ba'di ghalabihim sayaghliboon

# 3413

Fee bid'i sineena lillahi alamru min qablu wamin ba'du wayawmaithin yafrahu almuminoon

# 3414

Binasri Allahi yansuru man yashao wahuwa al'azeezu arraheem

# 3415

Wa'da Allahi la yukhlifu Allahu wa'dahu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 3416

Ya'lamoona thahiran mina alhayati addunya wahum 'ani alakhirati hum ghafiloon

# 3417

Awalam yatafakkaroo fee anfusihim ma khalaqa Allahu assamawati walarda wama baynahuma illa bilhaqqi waajalin musamman wainna katheeran mina annasi biliqai rabbihim lakafiroon

# 3418

Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharoo alarda wa'amarooha akthara mimma 'amarooha wajaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoon

# 3419

Thumma kana 'aqibata allatheena asaoo assooa an kaththaboo biayati Allahi wakanoo biha yastahzioon

# 3420

Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu thumma ilayhi turja'oon

# 3421

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yublisu almujrimoon

# 3422

Walam yakun lahum min shurakaihim shufa'ao wakanoo bishurakaihim kafireen

# 3423

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yawmaithin yatafarraqoon

# 3424

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fahum fee rawdatin yuhbaroon

# 3425

Waamma allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati faolaika fee al'athabi muhdaroon

# 3426

Fasubhana Allahi heena tumsoona waheena tusbihoon

# 3427

Walahu alhamdu fee assamawati walardi wa'ashiyyan waheena tuthhiroon

# 3428

Yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi wayuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha wakathalika tukhrajoon

# 3429

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqakum min turabin thumma itha antum basharun tantashiroon

# 3430

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqa lakum min anfusikum azwajan litaskunoo ilayha waja'ala baynakum mawaddatan warahmatan inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 3431

Wamin ayatihi khalqu assamawati walardi wakhtilafu alsinatikum waalwanikum inna fee thalika laayatin lil'alimeen

# 3432

Wamin ayatihi manamukum billayli wannahari wabtighaokum min fadlihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oon

# 3433

Wamin ayatihi yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunazzilu mina assamai maan fayuhyee bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 3434

Wamin ayatihi an taqooma assamao walardu biamrihi thumma itha da'akum da'watan mina alardi itha antum takhrujoon

# 3435

Walahu man fee assamawati walardi kullun lahu qanitoon

# 3436

Wahuwa allathee yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu wahuwa ahwanu 'alayhi walahu almathalu ala'la fee assamawati walardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3437

Daraba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum mi mma malakat aymanukum min shurakaa fee ma razaqnakum faantum feehi sawaon takhafoonahum kakheefatikum anfusakum kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 3438

Bali ittaba'a allatheena thalamoo ahwaahum bighayri 'ilmin faman yahdee man adalla Allahu wama lahum min nasireen

# 3439

Faaqim wajhaka liddeeni haneefan fitrata Allahi allatee fatara annasa 'alayha la tabdeela likhalqi Allahi thalika addeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 3440

Muneebeena ilayhi wattaqoohu waaqeemoo assalata wala takoonoo mina almushrikeen

# 3441

Mina allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiya'an kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoon

# 3442

Waitha massa annasa durrun da'aw rabbahum muneebeena ilayhi thumma itha athaqahum minhu rahmatan itha fareequn minhum birabbihim yushrikoon

# 3443

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoon

# 3444

Am anzalna 'alayhim sultanan fahuwa yatakallamu bima kanoo bihi yushrikoon

# 3445

Watha athaqna annasa rahmatan farihoo biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim itha hum yaqnatoon

# 3446

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 3447

Faati tha alqurba haqqahu walmiskeena wabna assabeeli thalika khayrun lillatheena yureedoona wajha Allahi waolaika humu almuflihoon

# 3448

Wama ataytum min riban liyarbuwa fee amwali annasi fala yarboo 'inda Allahi wama ataytum min zakatin tureedoona wajha Allahi faolaika humu almud'ifoon

# 3449

Allahu allathee khalaqakum thumma razaqakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum hal min shurakaikum man yaf'alu min thalikum min shayin subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 3450

Thahara alfasadu fee albarri walbahri bima kasabat aydee annasi liyutheeqahum ba'da allathee 'amiloo la'allahum yarji'oon

# 3451

Qul seeroo fee alardi fanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablu kana aktharuhum mushrikeen

# 3452

Faaqim wajhaka liddeeni alqayyimi min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi yawmaithin yassadda'oon

# 3453

Man kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu waman 'amila salihan falianfusihim yamhadoon

# 3454

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati min fadlihi innahu la yuhibbu alkafireen

# 3455

Wamin ayatihi an yursila arriyaha mubashshiratin waliyutheeqakum min rahmatihi walitajriya alfulku biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon

# 3456

Walaqad arsalna min qablika rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bilbayyinati fantaqamna mina allatheena ajramoo wakana haqqan 'alayna nasru almumineen

# 3457

Allahu allathee yursilu arriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fayabsutuhu fee assamai kayfa yashao wayaj'aluhu kisafan fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi faitha asaba bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi itha hum yastabshiroon

# 3458

Wain kanoo min qabli an yunazzala 'alayhim min qablihi lamubliseen

# 3459

Fanthur ila athari rahmati Allahi kayfa yuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha inna thalika lamuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 3460

Walain arsalna reehan faraawhu musfarran lathalloo min ba'dihi yakfuroon

# 3461

Fainnaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u assumma addu'aa itha wallaw mudbireen

# 3462

Wama anta bihadi al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoon

# 3463

Allahu allathee khalaqakum min da'fin thumma ja'ala min ba'di da'fin quwwatan thumma ja'ala min ba'di quwwatin da'fan washaybatan yakhluqu ma yashao wahuwa al'aleemu alqadeer

# 3464

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yuqsimu almujrimoona ma labithoo ghayra sa'atin kathalika kanoo yufakoon

# 3465

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma waleemana laqad labithtum fee kitabi Allahi ila yawmi alba'thi fahatha yawmu alba'thi walakinnakum kuntum la ta'lamoon

# 3466

Fayawmaithin la yanfa'u allatheena thalamoo ma'thiratuhum wala hum yusta'taboon

# 3467

Walaqad darabna linnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin walain jitahum biayatin layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in antum illa mubtiloon

# 3468

Kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala quloobi allatheena la ya'lamoon

# 3469

Fasbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wala yastakhiffannaka allatheena la yooqinoon

# 3470

Aliflammeem

# 3471

Tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeem

# 3472

Hudan warahmatan lilmuhsineen

# 3473

Allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wahum bilakhirati hum yooqinoon

# 3474

Olaika 'ala hudan min rabbihim waolaika humu almuflihoon

# 3475

Wamina annasi man yashtaree lahwa alhadeethi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattakhithaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheen

# 3476

Waitha tutla 'alayhi ayatuna walla mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha kaanna fee othunayhi waqran fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleem

# 3477

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum jannatu anna'eem

# 3478

Khalideena feeha wa'da Allahi haqqan wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3479

Khalaqa assamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum wabaththa feeha min kulli dabbatin waanzalna mina assamai maan faanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin kareem

# 3480

Hatha khalqu Allahi faaroonee matha khalaqa allatheena min doonihi bali aththalimoona fee dalalin mubeen

# 3481

Walaqad atayna luqmana alhikmata ani oshkur lillahi waman yashkur fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna Allaha ghaniyyun hameed

# 3482

Waith qala luqmanu libnihi wahuwa ya'ithuhu ya bunayya la tushrik billahi inna ashshirka lathulmun 'atheem

# 3483

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi hamalathu ommuhu wahnan 'ala wahnin wafisaluhu fee 'amayni ani oshkur lee waliwalidayka ilayya almaseer

# 3484

Wain jahadaka 'ala an tushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma wasahibhuma fee addunya ma'roofan wattabi' sabeela man anaba ilayya thumma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 3485

Ya bunayya innaha in taku mithqala habbatin min khardalin fatakun fee sakhratin aw fee assamawati aw fee alardi yati biha Allahu inna Allaha lateefun khabeer

# 3486

Ya bunayya aqimi assalata wamur bilma'roofi wanha 'ani almunkari wasbir 'ala ma asabaka inna thalika min 'azmi alomoor

# 3487

Wala tusa''ir khaddaka linnasi wala tamshi fee alardi marahan inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoor

# 3488

Waqsid fee mashyika waghdud min sawtika inna ankara alaswati lasawtu alhameer

# 3489

Alam taraw anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi waasbagha 'alaykum ni'amahu thahiratan wabatinatan wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneer

# 3490

Waitha qeela lahumu ittabi'oo ma anzala Allahu qaloo bal nattabi'u ma wajadna 'alayhi abaana awalaw kana ashshaytanu yad'oohum ila 'athabi assa'eer

# 3491

Waman yuslim wajhahu ila Allahi wahuwa muhsinun faqadi istamsaka bil'urwati alwuthqa waila Allahi 'aqibatu alomoor

# 3492

Waman kafara fala yahzunka kufruhu ilayna marji'uhum fanunabbiohum bima 'amiloo inna Allaha 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 3493

Numatti'uhum qaleelan thumma nadtarruhum ila 'athabin ghaleeth

# 3494

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa assamawati walarda layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon

# 3495

Lillahi ma fee assamawati walardi inna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameed

# 3496

Walaw annama fee alardi min shajaratin aqlamun walbahru yamudduhu min ba'dihi sab'atu abhurin ma nafidat kalimatu Allahi inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeem

# 3497

Ma khalqukum wala ba'thukum illa kanafsin wahidatin inna Allaha samee'un baseer

# 3498

Alam tara anna Allaha yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli wasakhkhara ashshamsa walqamara kullun yajree ila ajalin musamman waanna Allaha bima ta'maloona khabeer

# 3499

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeer

# 3500

Alam tara anna alfulka tajree fee albahri bini'mati Allahi liyuriyakum min ayatihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor

# 3501

Waitha ghashiyahum mawjun kaththulali da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena falamma najjahum ila albarri faminhum muqtasidun wama yajhadu biayatina illa kullu khattarin kafoor

# 3502

Ya ayyuha annasu ittaqoo rabbakum wakhshaw yawman la yajzee walidun 'an waladihi wala mawloodun huwa jazin 'an walidihi shayan inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu addunya wala yaghurrannakum billahi algharoor

# 3503

Inna Allaha 'indahu 'ilmu assa'ati wayunazzilu alghaytha waya'lamu ma fee alarhami wama tadree nafsun matha taksibu ghadan wama tadree nafsun biayyi ardin tamootu inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeer

# 3504

Aliflammeem

# 3505

Tanzeelu alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameen

# 3506

Am yaqooloona iftarahu bal huwa alhaqqu min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yahtadoon

# 3507

Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi ma lakum min doonihi min waliyyin wala shafee'in afala tatathakkaroon

# 3508

Yudabbiru alamra mina assamai ila alardi thumma ya'ruju ilayhi fee yawmin kana miqdaruhu alfa sanatin mimma ta'uddoon

# 3509

Thalika 'alimu alghaybi washshahadati al'azeezu arraheem

# 3510

Allathee ahsana kulla shayin khalaqahu wabadaa khalqa alinsani min teen

# 3511

Thumma ja'ala naslahu min sulalatin min main maheen

# 3512

Thumma sawwahu wanafakha feehi min roohihi waja'ala lakumu assam'a walabsara walafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroon

# 3513

Waqaloo aitha dalalna fee alardi ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin bal hum biliqai rabbihim kafiroon

# 3514

Qul yatawaffakum malaku almawti allathee wukkila bikum thumma ila rabbikum turja'oon

# 3515

Walaw tara ithi almujrimoona nakisoo ruoosihim 'inda rabbihim rabbana absarna wasami'na faarji'na na'mal salihan inna mooqinoon

# 3516

Walaw shina laatayna kulla nafsin hudaha walakin haqqa alqawlu minnee laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati wannasi ajma'een

# 3517

Fathooqoo bima naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha inna naseenakum wathooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 3518

Innama yuminu biayatina allatheena itha thukkiroo biha kharroo sujjadan wasabbahoo bihamdi rabbihim wahum la yastakbiroon

# 3519

Tatajafa junoobuhum 'ani almadaji'i yad'oona rabbahum khawfan watama'an wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon

# 3520

Fala ta'lamu nafsun ma okhfiya lahum min qurrati a'yunin jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 3521

Afaman kana muminan kaman kana fasiqan la yastawoon

# 3522

Amma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati falahum jannatu almawa nuzulan bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 3523

Waamma allatheena fasaqoo famawahumu annaru kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha o'eedoo feeha waqeela lahum thooqoo 'athaba annari allathee kuntum bihi tukaththiboon

# 3524

Walanutheeqannahum mina al'athabi aladna doona al'athabi alakbari la'allahum yarji'oon

# 3525

Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi thumma a'rada 'anha inna mina almujrimeena muntaqimoon

# 3526

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fala takun fee miryatin min liqaihi waja'alnahu hudan libanee israeel

# 3527

Waja'alna minhum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina lamma sabaroo wakanoo biayatina yooqinoon

# 3528

Inna rabbaka huwa yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon

# 3529

Awalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna min qablihim mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin afala yasma'oon

# 3530

Awalam yaraw anna nasooqu almaa ila alardi aljuruzi fanukhriju bihi zar'an takulu minhu an'amuhum waanfusuhum afala yubsiroon

# 3531

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alfathu in kuntum sadiqeen

# 3532

Qul yawma alfathi la yanfa'u allatheena kafaroo eemanuhum wala hum yuntharoon

# 3533

Faa'rid 'anhum wantathir innahum muntathiroon

# 3534

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu ittaqi Allaha wala tuti'i alkafireena walmunafiqeena inna Allaha kana 'aleeman hakeema

# 3535

Wattabi' ma yooha ilayka min rabbika inna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeera

# 3536

Watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa billahi wakeela

# 3537

Ma ja'ala Allahu lirajulin min qalbayni fee jawfihi wama ja'ala azwajakumu allaee tuthahiroona minhunna ommahatikum wama ja'ala ad'iyaakum abnaakum thalikum qawlukum biafwahikum wallahu yaqoolu alhaqqa wahuwa yahdee assabeel

# 3538

Od'oohum liabaihim huwa aqsatu 'inda Allahi fain lam ta'lamoo abaahum faikhwanukum fee addeeni wamawaleekum walaysa 'alaykum junahun feema akhtatum bihi walakin ma ta'ammadat quloobukum wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 3539

Annabiyyu awla bilmumineena min anfusihim waazwajuhu ommahatuhum waoloo alarhami ba'duhum awla biba'din fee kitabi Allahi mina almumineena walmuhajireena illa an taf'aloo ila awliyaikum ma'roofan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastoora

# 3540

Waith akhathna mina annabiyyeena meethaqahum waminka wamin noohin waibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa ibni maryama waakhathna minhum meethaqan ghaleetha

# 3541

Liyasala assadiqeena 'an sidqihim waa'adda lilkafireena 'athaban aleema

# 3542

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith jaatkum junoodun faarsalna 'alayhim reehan wajunoodan lam tarawha wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseera

# 3543

Ith jaookum min fawqikum wamin asfala minkum waith zaghati alabsaru wabalaghati alquloobu alhanajira watathunnoona billahi aththunoona

# 3544

Hunalika ibtuliya almuminoona wazulziloo zilzalan shadeeda

# 3545

Waith yaqoolu almunafiqoona wallatheena fee quloobihim maradun ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu illa ghuroora

# 3546

Waith qalat taifatun minhum ya ahla yathriba la muqama lakum farji'oo wayastathinu fareequn minhumu annabiyya yaqooloona inna buyootana 'awratun wama hiya bi'awratin in yureedoona illa firara

# 3547

Walaw dukhilat 'alayhim min aqtariha thumma suiloo alfitnata laatawha wama talabbathoo biha illa yaseera

# 3548

Walaqad kanoo 'ahadoo Allaha min qablu la yuwalloona aladbara wakana 'ahdu Allahi masoola

# 3549

Qul lan yanfa'akumu alfiraru in farartum mina almawti awi alqatli waithan la tumatta'oona illa qaleela

# 3550

Qul man tha allathee ya'simukum mina Allahi in arada bikum sooan aw arada bikum rahmatan wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseera

# 3551

Qad ya'lamu Allahu almu'awwiqeena minkum walqaileena liikhwanihim halumma ilayna wala yatoona albasa illa qaleela

# 3552

Ashihhatan 'alaykum faitha jaa alkhawfu raaytahum yanthuroona ilayka tadooru a'yunuhum kallathee yughsha 'alayhi mina almawti faitha thahaba alkhawfu salaqookum bialsinatin hidadin ashihhatan 'ala alkhayri olaika lam yuminoo faahbata Allahu a'malahum wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera

# 3553

Yahsaboona alahzaba lam yathhaboo wain yati alahzabu yawaddoo law annahum badoona fee ala'rabi yasaloona 'an anbaikum walaw kanoo feekum ma qataloo illa qaleela

# 3554

Laqad kana lakum fee rasooli Allahi oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha walyawma alakhira wathakara Allaha katheera

# 3555

Walamma raa almuminoona alahzaba qaloo hatha ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu wasadaqa Allahu warasooluhu wama zadahum illa eemanan watasleema

# 3556

Mina almumineena rijalun sadaqoo ma 'ahadoo Allaha 'alayhi faminhum man qada nahbahu waminhum man yantathiru wama baddaloo tabdeela

# 3557

Liyajziya Allahu assadiqeena bisidqihim wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena in shaa aw yatooba 'alayhim inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheema

# 3558

Waradda Allahu allatheena kafaroo bighaythihim lam yanaloo khayran wakafa Allahu almumineena alqitala wakana Allahu qawiyyan 'azeeza

# 3559

Waanzala allatheena thaharoohum min ahli alkitabi min sayaseehim waqathafa fee quloobihimu arru'ba fareeqan taqtuloona watasiroona fareeqa

# 3560

Waawrathakum ardahum wadiyarahum waamwalahum waardan lam tataooha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeera

# 3561

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liazwajika in kuntunna turidna alhayata addunya wazeenataha fata'alayna omatti'kunna waosarrihkunna sarahan jameela

# 3562

Wain kuntunna turidna Allaha warasoolahu waddara alakhirata fainna Allaha a'adda lilmuhsinati minkunna ajran 'atheema

# 3563

Ya nisaa annabiyyi man yati minkunna bifahishatin mubayyinatin yuda'af laha al'athabu di'fayni wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera

# 3564

Waman yaqnut minkunna lillahi warasoolihi wata'mal salihan nutiha ajraha marratayni waa'tadna laha rizqan kareema

# 3565

Ya nisaa annabiyyi lastunna kaahadin mina annisai ini ittaqaytunna fala takhda'na bilqawli fayatma'a allathee fee qalbihi maradun waqulna qawlan ma'roofa

# 3566

Waqarna fee buyootikunna wala tabarrajna tabarruja aljahiliyyati aloola waaqimna assalata waateena azzakata waati'na Allaha warasoolahu innama yureedu Allahu liyuthhiba 'ankumu arrijsa ahla albayti wayutahhirakum tatheera

# 3567

Wathkurna ma yutla fee buyootikunna min ayati Allahi walhikmati inna Allaha kana lateefan khabeera

# 3568

Inna almuslimeena walmuslimati walmumineena walmuminati walqaniteena walqanitati wassadiqeena wassadiqati wassabireena wassabirati walkhashi'eena walkhashi'ati walmutasaddiqeena walmutasaddiqati wassaimeena wassaimati walhafitheena furoojahum walhafithati waththakireena Allaha katheeran waththakirati a'adda Allahu lahum maghfiratan waajran 'atheema

# 3569

Wama kana limuminin wala muminatin itha qada Allahu warasooluhu amran an yakoona lahumu alkhiyaratu min amrihim waman ya'si Allaha warasoolahu faqad dalla dalalan mubeena

# 3570

Waith taqoolu lillathee an'ama Allahu 'alayhi waan'amta 'alayhi amsik 'alayka zawjaka wattaqi Allaha watukhfee fee nafsika ma Allahu mubdeehi watakhsha annasa wallahu ahaqqu an takhshahu falamma qada zaydun minha wataran zawwajnakaha likay la yakoona 'ala almumineena harajun fee azwaji ad'iyaihim itha qadaw minhunna wataran wakana amru Allahi maf'oola

# 3571

Ma kana 'ala annabiyyi min harajin feema farada Allahu lahu sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu wakana amru Allahi qadaran maqdoora

# 3572

Allatheena yuballighoona risalati Allahi wayakhshawnahu wala yakhshawna ahadan illa Allaha wakafa billahi haseeba

# 3573

Ma kana muhammadun aba ahadin min rijalikum walakin rasoola Allahi wakhatama annabiyyeena wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleema

# 3574

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo Allaha thikran katheera

# 3575

Wasabbihoohu bukratan waaseela

# 3576

Huwa allathee yusallee 'alaykum wamalaikatuhu liyukhrijakum mina aththulumati ila annoori wakana bilmumineena raheema

# 3577

# 3578

# 3579

# 3581

# 3582

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha nakahtumu almuminati thumma tallaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna fama lakum 'alayhinna min 'iddatin ta'taddoonaha famatti'oohunna wasarrihoohunna sarahan jameela

# 3583

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu inna ahlalna laka azwajaka allatee atayta ojoorahunna wama malakat yameenuka mimma afaa Allahu 'alayka wabanati 'ammika wabanati 'ammatika wabanati khalika wabanati khalatika allatee hajarna ma'aka wamraatan muminatan in wahabat nafsaha linnabiyyi in arada annabiyyu an yastankihaha khalisatan laka min dooni almumineena qad 'alimna ma faradna 'alayhim fee azwajihim wama malakat aymanuhum likayla yakoona 'alayka harajun wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 3584

Turjee man tashao minhunna watuwee ilayka man tashao wamani ibtaghayta mimman 'azalta fala junaha 'alayka thalika adna an taqarra a'yunuhunna wala yahzanna wayardayna bima ataytahunna kulluhunna wallahu ya'lamu ma fee quloobikum wakana Allahu 'aleeman haleema

# 3585

La yahillu laka annisao min ba'du wala an tabaddala bihinna min azwajin walaw a'jabaka husnuhunna illa ma malakat yameenuka wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin raqeeba

# 3586

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyoota annabiyyi illa an yuthana lakum ila ta'amin ghayra nathireena inahu walakin itha du'eetum fadkhuloo faitha ta'imtum fantashiroo wala mustaniseena lihadeethin inna thalikum kana yuthee annabiyya fayastahyee minkum wallahu la yastahyee mina alhaqqi waitha saaltumoohunna mata'an fasaloohunna min warai hijabin thalikum atharu liquloobikum waquloobihinna wama kana lakum an tuthoo rasoola Allahi wala an tankihoo azwajahu min ba'dihi abadan inna thalikum kana 'inda Allahi 'atheema

# 3587

In tubdoo shayan aw tukhfoohu fainna Allaha kana bikulli shayin 'aleema

# 3588

La junaha 'alayhinna fee abaihinna wala abnaihinna wala ikhwanihinna wala abnai ikhwanihinna wala abnai akhawatihinna wala nisaihinna wala ma malakat aymanuhunna wattaqeena Allaha inna Allaha kana 'ala kulli shayin shaheeda

# 3589

Inna Allaha wamalaikatahu yusalloona 'ala annabiyyi ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo salloo 'alayhi wasallimoo tasleema

# 3590

Inna allatheena yuthoona Allaha warasoolahu la'anahumu Allahu fee addunya walakhirati waa'adda lahum 'athaban muheena

# 3591

Wallatheena yuthoona almumineena walmuminati bighayri ma iktasaboo faqadi ihtamaloo buhtanan waithman mubeena

# 3592

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liazwajika wabanatika wanisai almumineena yudneena 'alayhinna min jalabeebihinna thalika adna an yu'rafna fala yuthayna wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 3593

Lain lam yantahi almunafiqoona wallatheena fee quloobihim maradun walmurjifoona fee almadeenati lanughriyannaka bihim thumma la yujawiroonaka feeha illa qaleela

# 3594

Mal'ooneena aynama thuqifoo okhithoo waquttiloo taqteela

# 3595

Sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeela

# 3596

Yasaluka annasu 'ani assa'ati qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda Allahi wama yudreeka la'alla assa'ata takoonu qareeba

# 3597

Inna Allaha la'ana alkafireena waa'adda lahum sa'eera

# 3598

Khalideena feeha abadan la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseera

# 3599

Yawma tuqallabu wujoohuhum fee annari yaqooloona ya laytana ata'na Allaha waata'na arrasoola

# 3600

Waqaloo rabbana inna ata'na sadatana wakubaraana faadalloona assabeela

# 3601

Rabbana atihim di'fayni mina al'athabi wal'anhum la'nan kabeera

# 3602

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takoonoo kallatheena athaw moosa fabarraahu Allahu mimma qaloo wakana 'inda Allahi wajeeha

# 3603

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waqooloo qawlan sadeeda

# 3604

Yuslih lakum a'malakum wayaghfir lakum thunoobakum waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu faqad faza fawzan 'atheema

# 3605

Inna 'aradna alamanata 'ala assamawati walardi waljibali faabayna an yahmilnaha waashfaqna minha wahamalaha alinsanu innahu kana thalooman jahoola

# 3606

Liyu'aththiba Allahu almunafiqeena walmunafiqati walmushrikeena walmushrikati wayatooba Allahu 'ala almumineena walmuminati wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 3607

Alhamdu lillahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi walahu alhamdu fee alakhirati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeer

# 3608

Ya'lamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina assamai wama ya'ruju feeha wahuwa arraheemu alghafoor

# 3609

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tateena assa'atu qul bala warabbee latatiyannakum 'alimi alghaybi la ya'zubu 'anhu mithqalu tharratin fee assamawati wala fee alardi wala asgharu min thalika wala akbaru illa fee kitabin mubeen

# 3610

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem

# 3611

Wallatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleem

# 3612

Wayara allatheena ootoo al'ilma allathee onzila ilayka min rabbika huwa alhaqqa wayahdee ila sirati al'azeezi alhameed

# 3613

Waqala allatheena kafaroo hal nadullukum 'ala rajulin yunabbiokum itha muzziqtum kulla mumazzaqin innakum lafee khalqin jadeed

# 3614

Aftara 'ala Allahi kathiban am bihi jinnatun bali allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati fee al'athabi waddalali alba'eed

# 3615

Afalam yaraw ila ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum mina assamai walardi in nasha nakhsif bihimu alarda aw nusqit 'alayhim kisafan mina assamai inna fee thalika laayatan likulli 'abdin muneeb

# 3616

Walaqad atayna dawooda minna fadlan ya jibalu awwibee ma'ahu wattayra waalanna lahu alhadeed

# 3617

Ani i'mal sabighatin waqaddir fee assardi wa'maloo salihan innee bima ta'maloona baseer

# 3618

Walisulaymana arreeha ghuduwwuha shahrun warawahuha shahrun waasalna lahu 'ayna alqitri wamina aljinni man ya'malu bayna yadayhi biithni rabbihi waman yazigh minhum 'an amrina nuthiqhu min 'athabi assa'eer

# 3619

Ya'maloona lahu ma yashao min mahareeba watamatheela wajifanin kaljawabi waqudoorin rasiyatin i'maloo ala dawooda shukran waqaleelun min 'ibadiya ashshakoor

# 3620

Falamma qadayna 'alayhi almawta ma dallahum 'ala mawtihi illa dabbatu alardi takulu minsaatahu falamma kharra tabayyanati aljinnu an law kanoo ya'lamoona alghayba ma labithoo fee al'athabi almuheen

# 3621

Laqad kana lisabain fee maskanihim ayatun jannatani 'an yameenin washimalin kuloo min rizqi rabbikum washkuroo lahu baldatun tayyibatun warabbun ghafoor

# 3622

Faa'radoo faarsalna 'alayhim sayla al'arimi wabaddalnahum bijannatayhim jannatayni thawatay okulin khamtin waathlin washayin min sidrin qaleel

# 3623

Thalika jazaynahum bima kafaroo wahal nujazee illa alkafoor

# 3624

Waja'alna baynahum wabayna alqura allatee barakna feeha quran thahiratan waqaddarna feeha assayra seeroo feeha layaliya waayyaman amineen

# 3625

Faqaloo rabbana ba'id bayna asfarina wathalamoo anfusahum faja'alnahum ahadeetha wamazzaqnahum kulla mumazzaqin inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor

# 3626

Walaqad saddaqa 'alayhim ibleesu thannahu fattaba'oohu illa fareeqan mina almumineen

# 3627

Wama kana lahu 'alayhim min sultanin illa lina'lama man yuminu bilakhirati mimman huwa minha fee shakkin warabbuka 'ala kulli shayin hafeeth

# 3628

Quli od'oo allatheena za'amtum min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona mithqala tharratin fee assamawati wala fee alardi wama lahum feehima min shirkin wama lahu minhum min thaheer

# 3629

Wala tanfa'u ashshafa'atu 'indahu illa liman athina lahu hatta itha fuzzi'a 'an quloobihim qaloo matha qala rabbukum qaloo alhaqqa wahuwa al'aliyyu alkabeer

# 3630

Qul man yarzuqukum mina assamawati walardi quli Allahu wainna aw iyyakum la'ala hudan aw fee dalalin mubeen

# 3631

Qul la tusaloona 'amma ajramna wala nusalu 'amma ta'maloon

# 3632

Qul yajma'u baynana rabbuna thumma yaftahu baynana bilhaqqi wahuwa alfattahu al'aleem

# 3633

Qul arooniya allatheena alhaqtum bihi shurakaa kalla bal huwa Allahu al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3634

Wama arsalnaka illa kaffatan linnasi basheeran wanatheeran walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 3635

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen

# 3636

Qul lakum mee'adu yawmin la tastakhiroona 'anhu sa'atan wala tastaqdimoon

# 3637

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lan numina bihatha alqurani wala billathee bayna yadayhi walaw tara ithi aththalimoona mawqoofoona 'inda rabbihim yarji'u ba'duhum ila ba'din alqawla yaqoolu allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo lawla antum lakunna mumineen

# 3638

Qala allatheena istakbaroo lillatheena istud'ifoo anahnu sadadnakum 'ani alhuda ba'da ith jaakum bal kuntum mujrimeen

# 3639

Waqala allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo bal makru allayli wannahari ith tamuroonana an nakfura billahi wanaj'ala lahu andadan waasarroo annadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waja'alna alaghlala fee a'naqi allatheena kafaroo hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo ya'maloon

# 3640

Wama arsalna fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon

# 3641

Waqaloo nahnu aktharu amwalan waawladan wama nahnu bimu'aththabeen

# 3642

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 3643

Wama amwalukum wala awladukum billatee tuqarribukum 'indana zulfa illa man amana wa'amila salihan faolaika lahum jazao addi'fi bima 'amiloo wahum fee alghurufati aminoon

# 3644

Wallatheena yas'awna fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika fee al'athabi muhdaroon

# 3645

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu wama anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukhlifuhu wahuwa khayru arraziqeen

# 3646

Wayawma yahshuruhum jamee'an thumma yaqoolu lilmalaikati ahaolai iyyakum kanoo ya'budoon

# 3647

Qaloo subhanaka anta waliyyuna min doonihim bal kanoo ya'budoona aljinna aktharuhum bihim muminoon

# 3648

Falyawma la yamliku ba'dukum liba'din naf'an wala darran wanaqoolu lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo 'athaba annari allatee kuntum biha tukaththiboon

# 3649

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa rajulun yureedu an yasuddakum 'amma kana ya'budu abaokum waqaloo ma hatha illa ifkun muftaran waqala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum in hatha illa sihrun mubeen

# 3650

Wama ataynahum min kutubin yadrusoonaha wama arsalna ilayhim qablaka min natheer

# 3651

Wakaththaba allatheena min qablihim wama balaghoo mi'shara ma ataynahum fakaththaboo rusulee fakayfa kana nakeer

# 3652

Qul innama a'ithukum biwahidatin an taqoomoo lillahi mathna wafurada thumma tatafakkaroo ma bisahibikum min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun lakum bayna yaday 'athabin shadeed

# 3653

Qul ma saaltukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin shaheed

# 3654

Qul inna rabbee yaqthifu bilhaqqi 'allamu alghuyoob

# 3655

Qul jaa alhaqqu wama yubdio albatilu wama yu'eed

# 3656

Qul in dalaltu fainnama adillu 'ala nafsee waini ihtadaytu fabima yoohee ilayya rabbee innahu samee'un qareeb

# 3657

Walaw tara ith fazi'oo fala fawta waokhithoo min makanin qareeb

# 3658

Waqaloo amanna bihi waanna lahumu attanawushu min makanin ba'eed

# 3659

Waqad kafaroo bihi min qablu wayaqthifoona bilghaybi min makanin ba'eed

# 3660

Waheela baynahum wabayna ma yashtahoona kama fu'ila biashya'ihim min qablu innahum kanoo fee shakkin mureeb

# 3661

Alhamdu lillahi fatiri assamawati walardi ja'ili almalaikati rusulan olee ajnihatin mathna wathulatha waruba'a yazeedu fee alkhalqi ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 3662

Ma yaftahi Allahu linnasi min rahmatin fala mumsika laha wama yumsik fala mursila lahu min ba'dihi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 3663

Ya ayyuha annasu othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum hal min khaliqin ghayru Allahi yarzuqukum mina assamai walardi la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoon

# 3664

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika waila Allahi turja'u alomoor

# 3665

Ya ayyuha annasu inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu addunya wala yaghurrannakum billahi algharoor

# 3666

Inna ashshaytana lakum 'aduwwun fattakhithoohu 'aduwwan innama yad'oo hizbahu liyakoonoo min ashabi assa'eer

# 3667

Allatheena kafaroo lahum 'athabun shadeedun wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer

# 3668

Afaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi faraahu hasanan fainna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao fala tathhab nafsuka 'alayhim hasaratin inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yasna'oon

# 3669

Wallahu allathee arsala arriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fasuqnahu ila baladin mayyitin faahyayna bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha kathalika annushoor

# 3670

Man kana yureedu al'izzata falillahi al'izzatu jamee'an ilayhi yas'adu alkalimu attayyibu wal'amalu assalihu yarfa'uhu wallatheena yamkuroona assayyiati lahum 'athabun shadeedun wamakru olaika huwa yaboor

# 3671

Wallahu khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma ja'alakum azwajan wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wama yu'ammaru min mu'ammarin wala yunqasu min 'umurihi illa fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer

# 3672

Wama yastawee albahrani hatha 'athbun furatun saighun sharabuhu wahatha milhun ojajun wamin kullin takuloona lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoona hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka feehi mawakhira litabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon

# 3673

Yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli wasakhkhara ashshamsa walqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku wallatheena tad'oona min doonihi ma yamlikoona min qitmeer

# 3674

In tad'oohum la yasma'oo du'aakum walaw sami'oo ma istajaboo lakum wayawma alqiyamati yakfuroona bishirkikum wala yunabbioka mithlu khabeer

# 3675

Ya ayyuha annasu antumu alfuqarao ila Allahi wallahu huwa alghaniyyu alhameed

# 3676

In yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed

# 3677

Wama thalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeez

# 3678

Wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wain tad'u muthqalatun ila himliha la yuhmal minhu shayon walaw kana tha qurba innama tunthiru allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bilghaybi waaqamoo assalata waman tazakka fainnama yatazakka linafsihi waila Allahi almaseer

# 3679

Wama yastawee ala'ma walbaseer

# 3680

Wala aththulumatu wala annoor

# 3681

Wala aththillu wala alharoor

# 3682

Wama yastawee alahyao wala alamwatu inna Allaha yusmi'u man yashao wama anta bimusmi'in man fee alquboor

# 3683

In anta illa natheer

# 3684

Inna arsalnaka bilhaqqi basheeran wanatheeran wain min ommatin illa khala feeha natheer

# 3685

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim jaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati wabizzuburi wabilkitabi almuneer

# 3686

Thumma akhathtu allatheena kafaroo fakayfa kana nakeer

# 3687

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan faakhrajna bihi thamaratin mukhtalifan alwanuha wamina aljibali judadun beedun wahumrun mukhtalifun alwanuha wagharabeebu sood

# 3688

Wamina annasi waddawabbi walan'ami mukhtalifun alwanuhu kathalika innama yakhsha Allaha min 'ibadihi al'ulamao inna Allaha 'azeezun ghafoor

# 3689

Inna allatheena yatloona kitaba Allahi waaqamoo assalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan yarjoona tijaratan lan taboor

# 3690

Liyuwaffiyahum ojoorahum wayazeedahum min fadlihi innahu ghafoorun shakoor

# 3691

Wallathee awhayna ilayka mina alkitabi huwa alhaqqu musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi inna Allaha bi'ibadihi lakhabeerun baseer

# 3692

Thumma awrathna alkitaba allatheena istafayna min 'ibadina faminhum thalimun linafsihi waminhum muqtasidun waminhum sabiqun bilkhayrati biithni Allahi thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeer

# 3693

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareer

# 3694

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee athhaba 'anna alhazana inna rabbana laghafoorun shakoor

# 3695

Allathee ahallana dara almuqamati min fadlihi la yamassuna feeha nasabun wala yamassuna feeha lughoob

# 3696

Wallatheena kafaroo lahum naru jahannama la yuqda 'alayhim fayamootoo wala yukhaffafu 'anhum min 'athabiha kathalika najzee kulla kafoor

# 3697

Wahum yastarikhoona feeha rabbana akhrijna na'mal salihan ghayra allathee kunna na'malu awalam nu'ammirkum ma yatathakkaru feehi man tathakkara wajaakumu annatheeru fathooqoo fama liththalimeena min naseer

# 3698

Inna Allaha 'alimu ghaybi assamawati walardi innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 3699

Huwa allathee ja'alakum khalaifa fee alardi faman kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum 'inda rabbihim illa maqtan wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum illa khasara

# 3700

Qul araaytum shurakaakumu allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee assamawati am ataynahum kitaban fahum 'ala bayyinatin minhu bal in ya'idu aththalimoona ba'duhum ba'dan illa ghuroora

# 3701

Inna Allaha yumsiku assamawati walarda an tazoola walain zalata in amsakahuma min ahadin min ba'dihi innahu kana haleeman ghafoora

# 3702

Waaqsamoo billahi jahda aymanihim lain jaahum natheerun layakoonunna ahda min ihda alomami falamma jaahum natheerun ma zadahum illa nufoora

# 3703

Istikbaran fee alardi wamakra assayyii wala yaheequ almakru assayyio illa biahlihi fahal yanthuroona illa sunnata alawwaleena falan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tahweela

# 3704

Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim wakanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan wama kana Allahu liyu'jizahu min shayin fee assamawati wala fee alardi innahu kana 'aleeman qadeera

# 3705

Walaw yuakhithu Allahu annasa bima kasaboo ma taraka 'ala thahriha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa ajaluhum fainna Allaha kana bi'ibadihi baseera

# 3706

Yaseen

# 3707

Walqurani alhakeem

Innaka lamina almursaleen

'ala siratin mustaqeem

Tanzeela al'azeezi arraheem

# 3711

# 3712

Laqad haqqa alqawlu 'ala aktharihim fahum la yuminoon

# 3713

Inna ja'alna fee a'naqihim aghlalan fahiya ila alathqani fahum muqmahoon

# 3714

Waja'alna min bayni aydeehim saddan wamin khalfihim saddan faaghshaynahum fahum la yubsiroon

# 3715

Wasawaon 'alayhim aanthartahum am lam tunthirhum la yuminoon

# 3716

Innama tunthiru mani ittaba'a aththikra wakhashiya arrahmana bilghaybi fabashshirhu bimaghfiratin waajrin kareem

# 3717

Inna nahnu nuhyee almawta wanaktubu ma qaddamoo waatharahum wakulla shayin ahsaynahu fee imamin mubeen

# 3718

Wadrib lahum mathalan ashaba alqaryati ith jaaha almursaloon

# 3719

Ith arsalna ilayhimu ithnayni fakaththaboohuma fa'azzazna bithalithin faqaloo inna ilaykum mursaloon

# 3720

Qaloo ma antum illa basharun mithluna wama anzala arrahmanu min shayin in antum illa takthiboon

# 3721

Qaloo rabbuna ya'lamu inna ilaykum lamursaloon

# 3722

Wama 'alayna illa albalaghu almubeen

# 3723

Qaloo inna tatayyarna bikum lain lam tantahoo lanarjumannakum walayamassannakum minna 'athabun aleem

# 3724

Qaloo tairukum ma'akum ain thukkirtum bal antum qawmun musrifoon

# 3725

Wajaa min aqsa almadeenati rajulun yas'a qala ya qawmi ittabi'oo almursaleen

# 3726

Ittabi'oo man la yasalukum ajran wahum muhtadoon

# 3727

Wama liya la a'budu allathee fataranee wailayhi turja'oon

# 3728

Aattakhithu min doonihi alihatan in yuridni arrahmanu bidurrin la tughni 'annee shafa'atuhum shayan wala yunqithoon

# 3729

Innee ithan lafee dalalin mubeen

# 3730

Innee amantu birabbikum fasma'oon

# 3731

Qeela odkhuli aljannata qala ya layta qawmee ya'lamoon

# 3732

Bima ghafara lee rabbee waja'alanee mina almukrameen

# 3733

Wama anzalna 'ala qawmihi min ba'dihi min jundin mina assamai wama kunna munzileen

# 3734

In kanat illa sayhatan wahidatan faitha hum khamidoon

# 3735

Ya hasratan 'ala al'ibadi ma yateehim min rasoolin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 3736

Alam yaraw kam ahlakna qablahum mina alqurooni annahum ilayhim la yarji'oon

# 3737

Wain kullun lamma jamee'un ladayna muhdaroon

# 3738

Waayatun lahumu alardu almaytatu ahyaynaha waakhrajna minha habban faminhu yakuloon

# 3739

Waja'alna feeha jannatin min nakheelin waa'nabin wafajjarna feeha mina al'uyoon

# 3740

Liyakuloo min thamarihi wama 'amilathu aydeehim afala yashkuroon

# 3741

Subhana allathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha mimma tunbitu alardu wamin anfusihim wamimma la ya'lamoon

# 3742

# 3743

Washshamsu tajree limustaqarrin laha thalika taqdeeru al'azeezi al'aleem

# 3744

Walqamara qaddarnahu manazila hatta 'ada kal'urjooni alqadeem

# 3745

# 3746

# 3747

# 3748

# 3751

# 3752

# 3753

# 3754

# 3755

# 3756

# 3757

Qaloo ya waylana man ba'athana min marqadina hatha ma wa'ada arrahmanu wasadaqa almursaloon

# 3758

# 3759

# 3760

# 3762

# 3763

# 3764

Wamtazoo alyawma ayyuha almujrimoon

# 3765

# 3770

# 3771

# 4061

Ala lillahi addeenu alkhalisu wallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa ma na'buduhum illa liyuqarriboona ila Allahi zulfa inna Allaha yahkumu baynahum fee ma hum feehi yakhtalifoona inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa kathibun kaffar

# 4062

# 4063

# 4064

Khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin thumma ja'ala minha zawjaha waanzala lakum mina alan'ami thamaniyata azwajin yakhluqukum fee butooni ommahatikum khalqan min ba'di khalqin fee thulumatin thalathin thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku la ilaha illa huwa faanna tusrafoon

# 4065

In takfuroo fainna Allaha ghaniyyun 'ankum wala yarda li'ibadihi alkufra wain tashkuroo yardahu lakum wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra thumma ila rabbikum marji'ukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 4066

Waitha massa alinsana durrun da'a rabbahu muneeban ilayhi thumma itha khawwalahu ni'matan minhu nasiya ma kana yad'oo ilayhi min qablu waja'ala lillahi andadan liyudilla 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta' bikufrika qaleelan innaka min ashabi annar

# 4067

Amman huwa qanitun anaa allayli sajidan waqaiman yahtharu alakhirata wayarjoo rahmata rabbihi qul hal yastawee allatheena ya'lamoona wallatheena la ya'lamoona innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbab

# 4068

Qul ya 'ibadi allatheena amanoo ittaqoo rabbakum lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi addunya hasanatun waardu Allahi wasi'atun innama yuwaffa assabiroona ajrahum bighayri hisab

# 4069

# 4070

# 4071

# 4072

# 4073

Fa'budoo ma shitum min doonihi qul inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeen

# 4074

Lahum min fawqihim thulalun mina annari wamin tahtihim thulalun thalika yukhawwifu Allahu bihi 'ibadahu ya 'ibadi fattaqoon

# 4075

# 4076
