# 4077

Afaman haqqa 'alayhi kalimatu al'athabi afaanta tunqithu man fee annar

# 4078

Lakini allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum lahum ghurafun min fawqiha ghurafun mabniyyatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu wa'da Allahi la yukhlifu Allahu almee'ad

# 4079

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan fasalakahu yanabee'a fee alardi thumma yukhriju bihi zar'an mukhtalifan alwanuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yaj'aluhu hutaman inna fee thalika lathikra liolee alalbab

# 4080

Afaman sharaha Allahu sadrahu lilislami fahuwa 'ala noorin min rabbihi fawaylun lilqasiyati quloobuhum min thikri Allahi olaika fee dalalin mubeen

# 4081

Allahu nazzala ahsana alhadeethi kitaban mutashabihan mathaniya taqsha'irru minhu juloodu allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum thumma taleenu julooduhum waquloobuhum ila thikri Allahi thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had

# 4082

Afaman yattaqee biwajhihi sooa al'athabi yawma alqiyamati waqeela liththalimeena thooqoo ma kuntum taksiboon

# 4083

Kaththaba allatheena min qablihim faatahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroon

# 4084

Faathaqahumu Allahu alkhizya fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoon

# 4085

Walaqad darabna linnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 4086

Quranan 'arabiyyan ghayra thee 'iwajin la'allahum yattaqoon

# 4087

Daraba Allahu mathalan rajulan feehi shurakao mutashakisoona warajulan salaman lirajulin hal yastawiyani mathalan alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon

# 4088

Innaka mayyitun wainnahum mayyitoon

# 4089

Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati 'inda rabbikum takhtasimoon

# 4090

Faman athlamu mimman kathaba 'ala Allahi wakaththaba bissidqi ith jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireen

# 4091

Wallathee jaa bissidqi wasaddaqa bihi olaika humu almuttaqoon

# 4092

Lahum ma yashaoona 'inda rabbihim thalika jazao almuhsineen

# 4093

Liyukaffira Allahu 'anhum aswaa allathee 'amiloo wayajziyahum ajrahum biahsani allathee kanoo ya'maloon

# 4094

Alaysa Allahu bikafin 'abdahu wayukhawwifoonaka billatheena min doonihi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had

# 4095

Waman yahdi Allahu fama lahu min mudillin alaysa Allahu bi'azeezin thee intiqam

# 4096

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa assamawati walarda layaqoolunna Allahu qul afaraaytum ma tad'oona min dooni Allahi in aradaniya Allahu bidurrin hal hunna kashifatu durrihi aw aradanee birahmatin hal hunna mumsikatu rahmatihi qul hasbiya Allahu 'alayhi yatawakkalu almutawakkiloon

# 4097

Qul ya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun fasawfa ta'lamoon

# 4098

Man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi wayahillu 'alayhi 'athabun muqeem

# 4099

Inna anzalna 'alayka alkitaba linnasi bilhaqqi famani ihtada falinafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wama anta 'alayhim biwakeel

# 4100

Allahu yatawaffa alanfusa heena mawtiha wallatee lam tamut fee manamiha fayumsiku allatee qada 'alayha almawta wayursilu alokhra ila ajalin musamman inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 4101

Ami ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi shufa'aa qul awalaw kanoo la yamlikoona shayan wala ya'qiloon

# 4102

Qul lillahi ashshafa'atu jamee'an lahu mulku assamawati walardi thumma ilayhi turja'oon

# 4103

Waitha thukira Allahu wahdahu ishmaazzat quloobu allatheena la yuminoona bilakhirati waitha thukira allatheena min doonihi itha hum yastabshiroon

# 4104

Quli allahumma fatira assamawati walardi 'alima alghaybi washshahadati anta tahkumu bayna 'ibadika fee ma kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon

# 4105

Walaw anna lillatheena thalamoo ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu laftadaw bihi min sooi al'athabi yawma alqiyamati wabada lahum mina Allahi ma lam yakoonoo yahtasiboon

# 4106

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 4107

Faitha massa alinsana durrun da'ana thumma itha khawwalnahu ni'matan minna qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin bal hiya fitnatun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 4108

Qad qalaha allatheena min qablihim fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboon

# 4109

Faasabahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wallatheena thalamoo min haolai sayuseebuhum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wama hum bimu'jizeen

# 4110

Awalam ya'lamoo anna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon

# 4111

Qul ya 'ibadiya allatheena asrafoo 'ala anfusihim la taqnatoo min rahmati Allahi inna Allaha yaghfiru aththunooba jamee'an innahu huwa alghafooru arraheem

# 4112

Waaneeboo ila rabbikum waaslimoo lahu min qabli an yatiyakumu al'athabu thumma la tunsaroon

# 4113

Wattabi'oo ahsana ma onzila ilaykum min rabbikum min qabli an yatiyakumu al'athabu baghtatan waantum la tash'uroon

# 4114

An taqoola nafsun ya hasrata 'ala ma farrattu fee janbi Allahi wain kuntu lamina assakhireen

# 4115

Aw taqoola law anna Allaha hadanee lakuntu mina almuttaqeen

# 4116

Aw taqoola heena tara al'athaba law anna lee karratan faakoona mina almuhsineen

# 4117

Bala qad jaatka ayatee fakaththabta biha wastakbarta wakunta mina alkafireen

# 4118

Wayawma alqiyamati tara allatheena kathaboo 'ala Allahi wujoohuhum muswaddatun alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilmutakabbireen

# 4119

Wayunajjee Allahu allatheena ittaqaw bimafazatihim la yamassuhumu assooo wala hum yahzanoon

# 4120

Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin wakeel

# 4121

Lahu maqaleedu assamawati walardi wallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi olaika humu alkhasiroon

# 4122

Qul afaghayra Allahi tamuroonnee a'budu ayyuha aljahiloon

# 4123

Walaqad oohiya ilayka waila allatheena min qablika lain ashrakta layahbatanna 'amaluka walatakoonanna mina alkhasireen

# 4124

Bali Allaha fa'bud wakun mina ashshakireen

# 4125

Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi walardu jamee'an qabdatuhu yawma alqiyamati wassamawatu matwiyyatun biyameenihi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon

# 4126

Wanufikha fee assoori fasa'iqa man fee assamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu thumma nufikha feehi okhra faitha hum qiyamun yanthuroon

# 4127

Waashraqati alardu binoori rabbiha wawudi'a alkitabu wajeea binnabiyyeena washshuhadai waqudiya baynahum bilhaqqi wahum la yuthlamoon

# 4128

Wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahuwa a'lamu bima yaf'aloon

# 4129

Waseeqa allatheena kafaroo ila jahannama zumaran hatta itha jaooha futihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatloona 'alaykum ayati rabbikum wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo bala walakin haqqat kalimatu al'athabi 'ala alkafireen

# 4130

Qeela odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireen

# 4131

Waseeqa allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum ila aljannati zumaran hatta itha jaooha wafutihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha salamun 'alaykum tibtum fadkhulooha khalideen

# 4132

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee sadaqana wa'dahu waawrathana alarda natabawwao mina aljannati haythu nashao fani'ma ajru al'amileen

# 4133

Watara almalaikata haffeena min hawli al'arshi yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim waqudiya baynahum bilhaqqi waqeela alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 4134

Hameem

# 4135

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi al'aleem

# 4136

Ghafiri aththanbi waqabili attawbi shadeedi al'iqabi thee attawli la ilaha illa huwa ilayhi almaseer

# 4137

Ma yujadilu fee ayati Allahi illa allatheena kafaroo fala yaghrurka taqallubuhum fee albilad

# 4138

Kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin walahzabu min ba'dihim wahammat kullu ommatin birasoolihim liyakhuthoohu wajadaloo bilbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa faakhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqab

# 4139

Wakathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena kafaroo annahum ashabu annar

# 4140

Allatheena yahmiloona al'arsha waman hawlahu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayuminoona bihi wayastaghfiroona lillatheena amanoo rabbana wasi'ta kulla shayin rahmatan wa'ilman faghfir lillatheena taboo wattaba'oo sabeelaka waqihim 'athaba aljaheem

# 4141

Rabbana waadkhilhum jannati 'adnin allatee wa'adtahum waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim innaka anta al'azeezu alhakeem

# 4142

Waqihimu assayyiati waman taqi assayyiati yawmaithin faqad rahimtahu wathalika huwa alfawzu al'atheem

# 4143

Inna allatheena kafaroo yunadawna lamaqtu Allahi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum ith tud'awna ila aleemani fatakfuroon

# 4144

Qaloo rabbana amattana ithnatayni waahyaytana ithnatayni fa'tarafna bithunoobina fahal ila khuroojin min sabeel

# 4145

Thalikum biannahu itha du'iya Allahu wahdahu kafartum wain yushrak bihi tuminoo falhukmu lillahi al'aliyyi alkabeer

# 4146

Huwa allathee yureekum ayatihi wayunazzilu lakum mina assamai rizqan wama yatathakkaru illa man yuneeb

# 4147

Fad'oo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena walaw kariha alkafiroon

# 4148

Rafee'u addarajati thoo al'arshi yulqee arrooha min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi liyunthira yawma attalaq

# 4149

Yawma hum barizoona la yakhfa 'ala Allahi minhum shayon limani almulku alyawma lillahi alwahidi alqahhar

# 4150

Alyawma tujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat la thulma alyawma inna Allaha saree'u alhisab

# 4151

Waanthirhum yawma alazifati ithi alquloobu lada alhanajiri kathimeena ma liththalimeena min hameemin wala shafee'in yuta'

# 4152

Ya'lamu khainata ala'yuni wama tukhfee assudoor

# 4153

Wallahu yaqdee bilhaqqi wallatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yaqdoona bishayin inna Allaha huwa assamee'u albaseer

# 4154

Awa lam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena kanoo min qablihim kanoo hum ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharan fee alardi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim wama kana lahum mina Allahi min waq

# 4155

Thalika biannahum kanat tateehim rusuluhum bilbayyinati fakafaroo faakhathahumu Allahu innahu qawiyyun shadeedu al'iqab

# 4156

Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeen

# 4157

Ila fir'awna wahamana waqaroona faqaloo sahirun kaththab

# 4158

Falamma jaahum bilhaqqi min 'indina qaloo oqtuloo abnaa allatheena amanoo ma'ahu wastahyoo nisaahum wama kaydu alkafireena illa fee dalal

# 4159

Waqala fir'awnu tharoonee aqtul moosa walyad'u rabbahu innee akhafu an yubaddila deenakum aw an yuthhira fee alardi alfasad

# 4160

Waqala moosa innee 'uthtu birabbee warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin la yuminu biyawmi alhisab

# 4161

Waqala rajulun muminun min ali fir'awna yaktumu eemanahu ataqtuloona rajulan an yaqoola rabbiyya Allahu waqad jaakum bilbayyinati min rabbikum wain yaku kathiban fa'alayhi kathibuhu wain yaku sadiqan yusibkum ba'du allathee ya'idukum inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa musrifun kaththab

# 4162

Ya qawmi lakumu almulku alyawma thahireena fee alardi faman yansuruna min basi Allahi in jaana qala fir'awnu ma oreekum illa ma ara wama ahdeekum illa sabeela arrashad

# 4163

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum mithla yawmi alahzab

# 4164

Mithla dabi qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda wallatheena min ba'dihim wama Allahu yureedu thulman lil'ibad

# 4165

Waya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum yawma attanad

# 4166

Yawma tuwalloona mudbireena ma lakum mina Allahi min 'asimin waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had

# 4167

Walaqad jaakum yoosufu min qablu bilbayyinati fama ziltum fee shakkin mimma jaakum bihi hatta itha halaka qultum lan yab'atha Allahu min ba'dihi rasoolan kathalika yudillu Allahu man huwa musrifun murtab

# 4168

Allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum kabura maqtan 'inda Allahi wa'inda allatheena amanoo kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabbar

# 4169

Waqala fir'awnu ya hamanu ibni lee sarhan la'allee ablughu alasbab

# 4170

Asbaba assamawati faattali'a ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu kathiban wakathalika zuyyina lifir'awna sooo 'amalihi wasudda 'ani assabeeli wama kaydu fir'awna illa fee tabab

# 4171

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi ittabi'ooni ahdikum sabeela arrashad

# 4172

Ya qawmi innama hathihi alhayatu addunya mata'un wainna alakhirata hiya daru alqarar

# 4173

Man 'amila sayyiatan fala yujza illa mithlaha waman 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata yurzaqoona feeha bighayri hisab

# 4174

Waya qawmi ma lee ad'ookum ila annajati watad'oonanee ila annar

# 4175

Tad'oonanee liakfura billahi waoshrika bihi ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun waana ad'ookum ila al'azeezi alghaffar

# 4176

La jarama annama tad'oonanee ilayhi laysa lahu da'watun fee addunya wala fee alakhirati waanna maraddana ila Allahi waanna almusrifeena hum ashabu annar

# 4177

Fasatathkuroona ma aqoolu lakum waofawwidu amree ila Allahi inna Allaha baseerun bil'ibad

# 4178

Fawaqahu Allahu sayyiati ma makaroo wahaqa biali fir'awna sooo al'athab

# 4179

Annaru yu'radoona 'alayha ghuduwwan wa'ashiyyan wayawma taqoomu assa'atu adkhiloo ala fir'awna ashadda al'athab

# 4180

Waith yatahajjoona fee annari fayaqoolu addu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna naseeban mina annar

# 4181

Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna kullun feeha inna Allaha qad hakama bayna al'ibad

# 4182

Waqala allatheena fee annari likhazanati jahannama od'oo rabbakum yukhaffif 'anna yawman mina al'athab

# 4183

Qaloo awalam taku tateekum rusulukum bilbayyinati qaloo bala qaloo fad'oo wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalal

# 4184

Inna lanansuru rusulana wallatheena amanoo fee alhayati addunya wayawma yaqoomu alashhad

# 4185

Yawma la yanfa'u aththalimeena ma'thiratuhum walahumu alla'natu walahum sooo addar

# 4186

Walaqad atayna moosa alhuda waawrathna banee israeela alkitab

# 4187

Hudan wathikra liolee alalbab

# 4188

Fasbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wastaghfir lithanbika wasabbih bihamdi rabbika bil'ashiyyi walibkar

# 4189

Inna allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum in fee sudoorihim illa kibrun ma hum bibaligheehi fasta'ith billahi innahu huwa assamee'u albaseer

# 4190

Lakhalqu assamawati walardi akbaru min khalqi annasi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 4191

Wama yastawee ala'ma walbaseeru wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wala almuseeo qaleelan ma tatathakkaroon

# 4192

Inna assa'ata laatiyatun la rayba feeha walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoon

# 4193

Waqala rabbukumu od'oonee astajib lakum inna allatheena yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatee sayadkhuloona jahannama dakhireen

# 4194

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi wannahara mubsiran inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala annasi walakinna akthara annasi la yashkuroon

# 4195

Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum khaliqu kulli shayin la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoon

# 4196

Kathalika yufaku allatheena kanoo biayati Allahi yajhadoon

# 4197

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda qararan wassamaa binaan wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum warazaqakum mina attayyibati thalikumu Allahu rabbukum fatabaraka Allahu rabbu al'alameen

# 4198

Huwa alhayyu la ilaha illa huwa fad'oohu mukhliseena lahu addeena alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen

# 4199

Qul innee nuheetu an a'buda allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lamma jaaniya albayyinatu min rabbee waomirtu an oslima lirabbi al'alameen

# 4200

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma yukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum thumma litakoonoo shuyookhan waminkum man yutawaffa min qablu walitablughoo ajalan musamman wala'allakum ta'qiloon

# 4201

Huwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu faitha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoon

# 4202

Alam tara ila allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi anna yusrafoon

# 4203

Allatheena kaththaboo bilkitabi wabima arsalna bihi rusulana fasawfa ya'lamoon

# 4204

Ithi alaghlalu fee a'naqihim wassalasilu yushaboon

# 4205

Fee alhameemi thumma fee annari yusjaroon

# 4206

Thumma qeela lahum ayna ma kuntum tushrikoon

# 4207

Min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo 'anna bal lam nakun nad'oo min qablu shayan kathalika yudillu Allahu alkafireen

# 4208

Thalikum bima kuntum tafrahoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tamrahoon

# 4209

Odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireen

# 4210

Fasbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun faimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna yurja'oon

# 4211

Walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika minhum man qasasna 'alayka waminhum man lam naqsus 'alayka wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi faitha jaa amru Allahi qudiya bilhaqqi wakhasira hunalika almubtiloon

# 4212

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alan'ama litarkaboo minha waminha takuloon

# 4213

Walakum feeha manafi'u walitablughoo 'alayha hajatan fee sudoorikum wa'alayha wa'ala alfulki tuhmaloon

# 4214

Wayureekum ayatihi faayya ayati Allahi tunkiroon

# 4215

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo akthara minhum waashadda quwwatan waatharan fee alardi fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboon

# 4216

Falamma jaathum rusuluhum bilbayyinati farihoo bima 'indahum mina al'ilmi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 4217

Falamma raaw basana qaloo amanna billahi wahdahu wakafarna bima kunna bihi mushrikeen

# 4218

Falam yaku yanfa'uhum eemanuhum lamma raaw basana sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat fee 'ibadihi wakhasira hunalika alkafiroon

# 4219

Hameem

# 4220

Tanzeelun mina arrahmani arraheem

# 4221

Kitabun fussilat ayatuhu quranan 'arabiyyan liqawmin ya'lamoon

# 4222

Basheeran wanatheeran faa'rada aktharuhum fahum la yasma'oon

# 4223

Waqaloo quloobuna fee akinnatin mimma tad'oona ilayhi wafee athanina waqrun wamin baynina wabaynika hijabun fa'mal innana 'amiloon

# 4224

Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fastaqeemoo ilayhi wastaghfiroohu wawaylun lilmushrikeen

# 4225

Allatheena la yutoona azzakata wahum bilakhirati hum kafiroon

# 4226

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum ajrun ghayru mamnoon

# 4227

Qul ainnakum latakfuroona billathee khalaqa alarda fee yawmayni wataj'aloona lahu andadan thalika rabbu al'alameen

# 4228

Waja'ala feeha rawasiya min fawqiha wabaraka feeha waqaddara feeha aqwataha fee arba'ati ayyamin sawaan lissaileen

# 4229

Thumma istawa ila assamai wahiya dukhanun faqala laha walilardi itiya taw'an aw karhan qalata atayna tai'een

# 4230

Faqadahunna sab'a samawatin fee yawmayni waawha fee kulli samain amraha wazayyanna assamaa addunya bimasabeeha wahifthan thalika taqdeeru al'azeezi al'aleem

# 4231

Fain a'radoo fuqul anthartukum sa'iqatan mithla sa'iqati 'adin wathamood

# 4232

Ith jaathumu arrusulu min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim alla ta'budoo illa Allaha qaloo law shaa rabbuna laanzala malaikatan fainna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon

# 4233

Faamma 'adun fastakbaroo fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi waqaloo man ashaddu minna quwwatan awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqahum huwa ashaddu minhum quwwatan wakanoo biayatina yajhadoon

# 4234

Faarsalna 'alayhim reehan sarsaran fee ayyamin nahisatin linutheeqahum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati akhza wahum la yunsaroon

# 4235

Waamma thamoodu fahadaynahum fastahabboo al'ama 'ala alhuda faakhathathum sa'iqatu al'athabi alhooni bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 4236

Wanajjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon

# 4237

Wayawma yuhsharu a'dao Allahi ila annari fahum yooza'oon

# 4238

Hatta itha ma jaooha shahida 'alayhim sam'uhum waabsaruhum wajulooduhum bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 4239

Waqaloo lijuloodihim lima shahidtum 'alayna qaloo antaqana Allahu allathee antaqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin wailayhi turja'oon

# 4240

Wama kuntum tastatiroona an yashhada 'alaykum sam'ukum wala absarukum wala juloodukum walakin thanantum anna Allaha la ya'lamu katheeran mimma ta'maloon

# 4241

Wathalikum thannukumu allathee thanantum birabbikum ardakum faasbahtum mina alkhasireen

# 4242

Fain yasbiroo fannaru mathwan lahum wain yasta'tiboo fama hum mina almu'tabeen

# 4243

Waqayyadna lahum quranaa fazayyanoo lahum ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wahaqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee omamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni walinsi innahum kanoo khasireen

# 4244

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tasma'oo lihatha alqurani walghaw feehi la'allakum taghliboon

# 4245

Falanutheeqanna allatheena kafaroo 'athaban shadeedan walanajziyannahum aswaa allathee kanoo ya'maloon

# 4246

Thalika jazao a'dai Allahi annaru lahum feeha daru alkhuldi jazaan bima kanoo biayatina yajhadoon

# 4247

Waqala allatheena kafaroo rabbana arina allathayni adallana mina aljinni walinsi naj'alhuma tahta aqdamina liyakoona mina alasfaleen

# 4248

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo tatanazzalu 'alayhimu almalaikatu alla takhafoo wala tahzanoo waabshiroo biljannati allatee kuntum too'adoon

# 4249

Nahnu awliyaokum fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati walakum feeha ma tashtahee anfusukum walakum feeha ma tadda'oon

# 4250

Nuzulan min ghafoorin raheem

# 4251

Waman ahsanu qawlan mimman da'a ila Allahi wa'amila salihan waqala innanee mina almuslimeen

# 4252

Wala tastawee alhasanatu wala assayyiatu idfa' billatee hiya ahsanu faitha allathee baynaka wabaynahu 'adawatun kaannahu waliyyun hameem

# 4253

Wama yulaqqaha illa allatheena sabaroo wama yulaqqaha illa thoo haththin 'atheem

# 4254

Waimma yanzaghannaka mina ashshaytani nazghun fasta'ith billahi innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 4255

Wamin ayatihi allaylu wannaharu washshamsu walqamaru la tasjudoo lishshamsi wala lilqamari wasjudoo lillahi alathee khalaqahunna in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoon

# 4256

Faini istakbaroo fallatheena 'inda rabbika yusabbihoona lahu billayli wannahari wahum la yasamoon

# 4257

Wamin ayatihi annaka tara alarda khashi'atan faitha anzalna 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat inna allathee ahyaha lamuhyee almawta innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 4258

Inna allatheena yulhidoona fee ayatina la yakhfawna 'alayna afaman yulqa fee annari khayrun am man yatee aminan yawma alqiyamati i'maloo ma shitum innahu bima ta'maloona baseer

# 4259

Inna allatheena kafaroo biththikri lamma jaahum wainnahu lakitabun 'azeez

# 4260

La yateehi albatilu min bayni yadayhi wala min khalfihi tanzeelun min hakeemin hameed

# 4261

Ma yuqalu laka illa ma qad qeela lirrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin wathoo 'iqabin aleem

# 4262

Walaw ja'alnahu quranan a'jamiyyan laqaloo lawla fussilat ayatuhu aa'jamiyyun wa'arabiyyun qul huwa lillatheena amanoo hudan washifaon wallatheena la yuminoona fee athanihim waqrun wahuwa 'alayhim 'aman olaika yunadawna min makanin ba'eed

# 4263

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fakhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureeb

# 4264

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha wama rabbuka bithallamin lil'abeed

# 4265

Ilayhi yuraddu 'ilmu assa'ati wama takhruju min thamaratin min akmamiha wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wayawma yunadeehim ayna shurakaee qaloo athannaka ma minna min shaheed

# 4266

Wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yad'oona min qablu wathannoo ma lahum min mahees

# 4267

La yasamu alinsanu min du'ai alkhayri wain massahu ashsharru fayaoosun qanoot

# 4268

Walain athaqnahu rahmatan minna min ba'di darraa massathu layaqoolanna hatha lee wama athunnu assa'ata qaimatan walain ruji'tu ila rabbee inna lee 'indahu lalhusna falanunabbianna allatheena kafaroo bima 'amiloo walanutheeqannahum min 'athabin ghaleeth

# 4269

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu ashsharru fathoo du'ain 'areed

# 4270

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi thumma kafartum bihi man adallu mimman huwa fee shiqaqin ba'eed

# 4271

Sanureehim ayatina fee alafaqi wafee anfusihim hatta yatabayyana lahum annahu alhaqqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu 'ala kulli shayin shaheed

# 4272

Ala innahum fee miryatin min liqai rabbihim ala innahu bikulli shayin muheet

# 4273

Hameem

# 4274

'aynseenqaf

# 4275

Kathalika yoohee ilayka waila allatheena min qablika Allahu al'azeezu alhakeem

# 4276

Lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'aliyyu al'atheem

# 4277

Takadu assamawatu yatafattarna min fawqihinna walmalaikatu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayastaghfiroona liman fee alardi ala inna Allaha huwa alghafooru arraheem

# 4278

Wallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa Allahu hafeethun 'alayhim wama anta 'alayhim biwakeel

# 4279

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka quranan 'arabiyyan litunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha watunthira yawma aljam'i la rayba feehi fareequn fee aljannati wafareequn fee assa'eer

# 4280

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alahum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudkhilu man yashao fee rahmatihi waththalimoona ma lahum min waliyyin wala naseer

# 4281

Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa fallahu huwa alwaliyyu wahuwa yuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 4282

Wama ikhtalaftum feehi min shayin fahukmuhu ila Allahi thalikumu Allahu rabbee 'alayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi oneeb

# 4283

Fatiru assamawati walardi ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wamina alan'ami azwajan yathraokum feehi laysa kamithlihi shayon wahuwa assamee'u albaseer

# 4284

Lahu maqaleedu assamawati walardi yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin 'aleem

# 4285

Shara'a lakum mina addeeni ma wassa bihi noohan wallathee awhayna ilayka wama wassayna bihi ibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa an aqeemoo addeena wala tatafarraqoo feehi kabura 'ala almushrikeena ma tad'oohum ilayhi Allahu yajtabee ilayhi man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man yuneeb

# 4286

Wama tafarraqoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika ila ajalin musamman laqudiya baynahum wainna allatheena oorithoo alkitaba min ba'dihim lafee shakkin minhu mureeb

# 4287

Falithalika fad'u wastaqim kama omirta wala tattabi' ahwaahum waqul amantu bima anzala Allahu min kitabin waomirtu lia'dila baynakum Allahu rabbuna warabbukum lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum la hujjata baynana wabaynakumu Allahu yajma'u baynana wailayhi almaseer

# 4288

Wallatheena yuhajjoona fee Allahi min ba'di ma istujeeba lahu hujjatuhum dahidatun 'inda rabbihim wa'alayhim ghadabun walahum 'athabun shadeed

# 4289

Allahu allathee anzala alkitaba bilhaqqi walmeezani wama yudreeka la'alla assa'ata qareeb

# 4290

Yasta'jilu biha allatheena la yuminoona biha wallatheena amanoo mushfiqoona minha waya'lamoona annaha alhaqqu ala inna allatheena yumaroona fee assa'ati lafee dalalin ba'eed

# 4291

Allahu lateefun bi'ibadihi yarzuqu man yashao wahuwa alqawiyyu al'azeez

# 4292

Man kana yureedu hartha alakhirati nazid lahu fee harthihi waman kana yureedu hartha addunya nutihi minha wama lahu fee alakhirati min naseeb

# 4293

Am lahum shurakao shara'oo lahum mina addeeni ma lam yathan bihi Allahu walawla kalimatu alfasli laqudiya baynahum wainna aththalimeena lahum 'athabun aleem

# 4294

Tara aththalimeena mushfiqeena mimma kasaboo wahuwa waqi'un bihim wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fee rawdati aljannati lahum ma yashaoona 'inda rabbihim thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeer

# 4295

Thalika allathee yubashshiru Allahu 'ibadahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati qul la asalukum 'alayhi ajran illa almawaddata fee alqurba waman yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu feeha husnan inna Allaha ghafoorun shakoor

# 4296

Am yaqooloona iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban fain yashai Allahu yakhtim 'ala qalbika wayamhu Allahu albatila wayuhiqqu alhaqqa bikalimatihi innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoor

# 4297

Wahuwa allathee yaqbalu attawbata 'an 'ibadihi waya'foo 'ani assayyiati waya'lamu ma taf'aloon

# 4298

Wayastajeebu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wayazeeduhum min fadlihi walkafiroona lahum 'athabun shadeed

# 4299

Walaw basata Allahu arrizqa li'ibadihi labaghaw fee alardi walakin yunazzilu biqadarin ma yashao innahu bi'ibadihi khabeerun baseer

# 4300

Wahuwa allathee yunazzilu alghaytha min ba'di ma qanatoo wayanshuru rahmatahu wahuwa alwaliyyu alhameed

# 4301

Wamin ayatihi khalqu assamawati walardi wama baththa feehima min dabbatin wahuwa 'ala jam'ihim itha yashao qadeer

# 4302

Wama asabakum min museebatin fabima kasabat aydeekum waya'foo 'an katheer

# 4303

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseer

# 4304

Wamin ayatihi aljawari fee albahri kala'lam

# 4305

In yasha yuskini arreeha fayathlalna rawakida 'ala thahrihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor

# 4306

Aw yoobiqhunna bima kasaboo waya'fu 'an katheer

# 4307

Waya'lama allatheena yujadiloona fee ayatina ma lahum min mahees

# 4308

Fama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati addunya wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa lillatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon

# 4309

Wallatheena yajtaniboona kabaira alithmi walfawahisha waitha ma ghadiboo hum yaghfiroon

# 4310

Wallatheena istajaboo lirabbihim waaqamoo assalata waamruhum shoora baynahum wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon

# 4311

Wallatheena itha asabahumu albaghyu hum yantasiroon

# 4312

Wajazao sayyiatin sayyiatun mithluha faman 'afa waaslaha faajruhu 'ala Allahi innahu la yuhibbu aththalimeen

# 4313

Walamani intasara ba'da thulmihi faolaika ma 'alayhim min sabeel

# 4314

Innama assabeelu 'ala allatheena yathlimoona annasa wayabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi olaika lahum 'athabun aleem

# 4315

Walaman sabara waghafara inna thalika lamin 'azmi alomoor

# 4316

Waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min waliyyin min ba'dihi watara aththalimeena lamma raawoo al'athaba yaqooloona hal ila maraddin min sabeel

# 4317

Watarahum yu'radoona 'alayha khashi'eena mina aththulli yanthuroona min tarfin khafiyyin waqala allatheena amanoo inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala inna aththalimeena fee 'athabin muqeem

# 4318

Wama kana lahum min awliyaa yansuroonahum min dooni Allahi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min sabeel

# 4319

Istajeeboo lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi ma lakum min maljain yawmaithin wama lakum min nakeer

# 4320

Fain a'radoo fama arsalnaka 'alayhim hafeethan in 'alayka illa albalaghu wainna itha athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan fariha biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fainna alinsana kafoor

# 4321

Lillahi mulku assamawati walardi yakhluqu ma yashao yahabu liman yashao inathan wayahabu liman yashao aththukoor

# 4322

Aw yuzawwijuhum thukranan wainathan wayaj'alu man yashao 'aqeeman innahu 'aleemun qadeer

# 4323

Wama kana libasharin an yukallimahu Allahu illa wahyan aw min warai hijabin aw yursila rasoolan fayoohiya biithnihi ma yashao innahu 'aliyyun hakeem

# 4324

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka roohan min amrina ma kunta tadree ma alkitabu wala aleemanu walakin ja'alnahu nooran nahdee bihi man nashao min 'ibadina wainnaka latahdee ila siratin mustaqeem

# 4325

Sirati Allahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi ala ila Allahi taseeru alomoor

# 4326

Hameem

# 4327

Walkitabi almubeen

# 4328

Inna ja'alnahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 4329

Wainnahu fee ommi alkitabi ladayna la'aliyyun hakeem

# 4330

Afanadribu 'ankumu aththikra safhan an kuntum qawman musrifeen

# 4331

Wakam arsalna min nabiyyin fee alawwaleen

# 4332

Wama yateehim min nabiyyin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 4333

Faahlakna ashadda minhum batshan wamada mathalu alawwaleen

# 4334

Walain saaltahum man khalaqa assamawati walarda layaqoolunna khalaqahunna al'azeezu al'aleem

# 4335

Allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda mahdan waja'ala lakum feeha subulan la'allakum tahtadoon

# 4336

Wallathee nazzala mina assamai maan biqadarin faansharna bihi baldatan maytan kathalika tukhrajoon

# 4337

Wallathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha waja'ala lakum mina alfulki walan'ami ma tarkaboon

# 4338

Litastawoo 'ala thuhoorihi thumma tathkuroo ni'mata rabbikum itha istawaytum 'alayhi wataqooloo subhana allathee sakhkhara lana hatha wama kunna lahu muqrineen

# 4339

Wainna ila rabbina lamunqaliboon

# 4340

Waja'aloo lahu min 'ibadihi juzan inna alinsana lakafoorun mubeen

# 4341

Ami ittakhatha mimma yakhluqu banatin waasfakum bilbaneen

# 4342

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bima daraba lirrahmani mathalan thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheem

# 4343

Awaman yunashshao fee alhilyati wahuwa fee alkhisami ghayru mubeen

# 4344

Waja'aloo almalaikata allatheena hum 'ibadu arrahmani inathan ashahidoo khalqahum satuktabu shahadatuhum wayusaloon

# 4345

Waqaloo law shaa arrahmanu ma 'abadnahum ma lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa yakhrusoon

# 4346

Am ataynahum kitaban min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsikoon

# 4347

Bal qaloo inna wajadna abaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'ala atharihim muhtadoon

# 4348

Wakathalika ma arsalna min qablika fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna wajadna abaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'ala atharihim muqtadoon

# 4349

Qala awalaw jitukum biahda mimma wajadtum 'alayhi abaakum qaloo inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon

# 4350

Fantaqamna minhum fanthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeen

# 4351

Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi waqawmihi innanee baraon mimma ta'budoon

# 4352

Illa allathee fataranee fainnahu sayahdeen

# 4353

Waja'alaha kalimatan baqiyatan fee 'aqibihi la'allahum yarji'oon

# 4354

Bal matta'tu haolai waabaahum hatta jaahumu alhaqqu warasoolun mubeen

# 4355

Walamma jaahumu alhaqqu qaloo hatha sihrun wainna bihi kafiroon

# 4356

Waqaloo lawla nuzzila hatha alquranu 'ala rajulin mina alqaryatayni 'atheem

# 4357

Ahum yaqsimoona rahmata rabbika nahnu qasamna baynahum ma'eeshatahum fee alhayati addunya warafa'na ba'dahum fawqa ba'din darajatin liyattakhitha ba'duhum ba'dan sukhriyyan warahmatu rabbika khayrun mimma yajma'oon

# 4358

Walawla an yakoona annasu ommatan wahidatan laja'alna liman yakfuru birrahmani libuyootihim suqufan min fiddatin wama'arija 'alayha yathharoon

# 4359

Walibuyootihim abwaban wasururan 'alayha yattakioon

# 4360

Wazukhrufan wain kullu thalika lamma mata'u alhayati addunya walakhiratu 'inda rabbika lilmuttaqeen

# 4361

Waman ya'shu 'an thikri arrahmani nuqayyid lahu shaytanan fahuwa lahu qareen

# 4362

Wainnahum layasuddoonahum 'ani assabeeli wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoon

# 4363

Hatta itha jaana qala ya layta baynee wabaynaka bu'da almashriqayni fabisa alqareen

# 4364

Walan yanfa'akumu alyawma ith thalamtum annakum fee al'athabi mushtarikoon

# 4365

Afaanta tusmi'u assumma aw tahdee al'umya waman kana fee dalalin mubeen

# 4366

Faimma nathhabanna bika fainna minhum muntaqimoon

# 4367

Aw nuriyannaka allathee wa'adnahum fainna 'alayhim muqtadiroon

# 4368

Fastamsik billathee oohiya ilayka innaka 'ala siratin mustaqeem

# 4369

Wainnahu lathikrun laka waliqawmika wasawfa tusaloon

# 4370

Wasal man arsalna min qablika min rusulina aja'alna min dooni arrahmani alihatan yu'badoon

# 4371

Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina ila fir'awna wamalaihi faqala innee rasoolu rabbi al'alameen

# 4372

Falamma jaahum biayatina itha hum minha yadhakoon

# 4373

Wama nureehim min ayatin illa hiya akbaru min okhtiha waakhathnahum bil'athabi la'allahum yarji'oon

# 4374

Waqaloo ya ayyuha asahiru od'u lana rabbaka bima 'ahida 'indaka innana lamuhtadoon

# 4375

Falamma kashafna 'anhumu al'athaba itha hum yankuthoon

# 4376

Wanada fir'awnu fee qawmihi qala ya qawmi alaysa lee mulku misra wahathihi alanharu tajree min tahtee afala tubsiroon

# 4377

Am ana khayrun min hatha allathee huwa maheenun wala yakadu yubeen

# 4378

Falawla olqiya 'alayhi aswiratun min thahabin aw jaa ma'ahu almalaikatu muqtarineen

# 4379

Fastakhaffa qawmahu faata'oohu innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen

# 4380

Falamma asafoona intaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum ajma'een

# 4381

Faja'alnahum salafan wamathalan lilakhireen

# 4382

Walamma duriba ibnu maryama mathalan itha qawmuka minhu yasiddoon

# 4383

Waqaloo aalihatuna khayrun am huwa ma daraboohu laka illa jadalan bal hum qawmun khasimoon

# 4384

In huwa illa 'abdun an'amna 'alayhi waja'alnahu mathalan libanee israeel

# 4385

Walaw nashao laja'alna minkum malaikatan fee alardi yakhlufoon

# 4386

Wainnahu la'ilmun lissa'ati fala tamtarunna biha wattabi'ooni hatha siratun mustaqeem

# 4387

Wala yasuddannakumu ashshaytanu innahu lakum 'aduwwun mubeen

# 4388

Walamma jaa 'eesa bilbayyinati qala qad jitukum bilhikmati waliobayyina lakum ba'da allathee takhtalifoona feehi fattaqoo Allaha waatee'oon

# 4389

Inna Allaha huwa rabbee warabbukum fa'budoohu hatha siratun mustaqeem

# 4390

Fakhtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena thalamoo min 'athabi yawmin aleem

# 4391

Hal yanthuroona illa assa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon

# 4392

Alakhillao yawmaithin ba'duhum liba'din 'aduwwun illa almuttaqeen

# 4393

Ya 'ibadi la khawfun 'alaykumu alyawma wala antum tahzanoon

# 4394

Allatheena amanoo biayatina wakanoo muslimeen

# 4395

Odkhuloo aljannata antum waazwajukum tuhbaroon

# 4396

Yutafu 'alayhim bisihafin min thahabin waakwabin wafeeha ma tashtaheehi alanfusu watalaththu ala'yunu waantum feeha khalidoon

# 4397

Watilka aljannatu allatee oorithtumooha bima kuntum ta'maloon

# 4398

Lakum feeha fakihatun katheeratun minha takuloon

# 4399

Inna almujrimeena fee 'athabi jahannama khalidoon

# 4400

La yufattaru 'anhum wahum feehi mublisoon

# 4401

Wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo humu aththalimeen

# 4402

Wanadaw ya maliku liyaqdi 'alayna rabbuka qala innakum makithoon

# 4403

Laqad jinakum bilhaqqi walakinna aktharakum lilhaqqi karihoon

# 4404

Am abramoo amran fainna mubrimoon

# 4405

Am yahsaboona anna la nasma'u sirrahum wanajwahum bala warusuluna ladayhim yaktuboon

# 4406

Qul in kana lirrahmani waladun faana awwalu al'abideen

# 4407

Subhana rabbi assamawati walardi rabbi al'arshi 'amma yasifoon

# 4408

Fatharhum yakhoodoo wayal'aboo hatta yulaqoo yawmahumu allathee yoo'adoon

# 4409

Wahuwa allathee fee assamai ilahun wafee alardi ilahun wahuwa alhakeemu al'aleem

# 4410

Watabaraka allathee lahu mulku assamawati walardi wama baynahuma wa'indahu 'ilmu assa'ati wailayhi turja'oon

# 4411

Wala yamliku allatheena yad'oona min doonihi ashshafa'ata illa man shahida bilhaqqi wahum ya'lamoon

# 4412

Walain saaltahum man khalaqahum layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoon

# 4413

Waqeelihi yarabbi inna haolai qawmun la yuminoon

# 4414

Fasfah 'anhum waqul salamun fasawfa ya'lamoon

# 4415

Hameem

# 4416

Walkitabi almubeen

# 4417

Inna anzalnahu fee laylatin mubarakatin inna kunna munthireen

# 4418

Feeha yufraqu kullu amrin hakeem

# 4419

Amran min 'indina inna kunna mursileen

# 4420

Rahmatan min rabbika innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleem

# 4421

Rabbi assamawati walardi wama baynahuma in kuntum mooqineen

# 4422

La ilaha illa huwa yuhyee wayumeetu rabbukum warabbu abaikumu alawwaleen

# 4423

Bal hum fee shakkin yal'aboon

# 4424

Fartaqib yawma tatee assamao bidukhanin mubeen

# 4425

Yaghsha annasa hatha 'athabun aleem

# 4426

Rabbana ikshif 'anna al'athaba inna muminoon

# 4427

Anna lahumu aththikra waqad jaahum rasoolun mubeen

# 4428

Thumma tawallaw 'anhu waqaloo mu'allamun majnoon

# 4429

Inna kashifoo al'athabi qaleelan innakum 'aidoon

# 4430

Yawma nabtishu albatshata alkubra inna muntaqimoon

# 4431

Walaqad fatanna qablahum qawma fir'awna wajaahum rasoolun kareem

# 4432

An addoo ilayya 'ibada Allahi innee lakum rasoolun ameen

# 4433

Waan la ta'loo 'ala Allahi innee ateekum bisultanin mubeen

# 4434

Wainnee 'uthtu birabbee warabbikum an tarjumoon

# 4435

Wain lam tuminoo lee fa'taziloon

# 4436

Fada'a rabbahu anna haolai qawmun mujrimoon

# 4437

Faasri bi'ibadee laylan innakum muttaba'oon

# 4438

Watruki albahra rahwan innahum jundun mughraqoon

# 4439

Kam tarakoo min jannatin wa'uyoon

# 4440

Wazuroo'in wamaqamin kareem

# 4441

Wana'matin kanoo feeha fakiheen

# 4442

Kathalika waawrathnaha qawman akhareen

# 4443

Fama bakat 'alayhimu assamao walardu wama kanoo munthareen

# 4444

Walaqad najjayna banee israeela mina al'athabi almuheen

# 4445

Min fir'awna innahu kana 'aliyan mina almusrifeen

# 4446

Walaqadi ikhtarnahum 'ala 'ilmin 'ala al'alameen

# 4447

Waataynahum mina alayati ma feehi balaon mubeen

# 4448

Inna haolai layaqooloon

# 4449

In hiya illa mawtatuna aloola wama nahnu bimunshareen

# 4450

Fatoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeen

# 4451

Ahum khayrun am qawmu tubba'in wallatheena min qablihim ahlaknahum innahum kanoo mujrimeen

# 4452

Wama khalaqna assamawati walarda wama baynahuma la'ibeen

# 4453

Ma khalaqnahuma illa bilhaqqi walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon

# 4454

Inna yawma alfasli meeqatuhum ajma'een

# 4455

Yawma la yughnee mawlan 'an mawlan shayan wala hum yunsaroon

# 4456

Illa man rahima Allahu innahu huwa al'azeezu arraheem

# 4457

Inna shajarata azzaqqoom

# 4458

Ta'amu alatheem

# 4459

Kalmuhli yaghlee fee albutoon

# 4460

Kaghalyi alhameem

# 4461

Khuthoohu fa'tiloohu ila sawai aljaheem

# 4462

Thumma subboo fawqa rasihi min 'athabi alhameem

# 4463

Thuq innaka anta al'azeezu alkareem

# 4464

Inna hatha ma kuntum bihi tamtaroon

# 4465

Inna almuttaqeena fee maqamin ameen

# 4466

Fee jannatin wa'uyoon

# 4467

Yalbasoona min sundusin waistabraqin mutaqabileen

# 4468

Kathalika wazawwajnahum bihoorin 'een

# 4469

Yad'oona feeha bikulli fakihatin amineen

# 4470

La yathooqoona feeha almawta illa almawtata aloola wawaqahum 'athaba aljaheem

# 4471

Fadlan min rabbika thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheem

# 4472

Fainnama yassarnahu bilisanika la'allahum yatathakkaroon

# 4473

Fartaqib innahum murtaqiboon

# 4474

Hameem

# 4475

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeem

# 4476

Inna fee assamawati walardi laayatin lilmumineen

# 4477

Wafee khalqikum wama yabuththu min dabbatin ayatun liqawmin yooqinoon

# 4478

Wakhtilafi allayli wannahari wama anzala Allahu mina assamai min rizqin faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha watasreefi arriyahi ayatun liqawmin ya'qiloon

# 4479

Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha 'alayka bilhaqqi fabiayyi hadeethin ba'da Allahi waayatihi yuminoon

# 4480

Waylun likulli affakin atheem

# 4481

Yasma'u ayati Allahi tutla 'alayhi thumma yusirru mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleem

# 4482

Waitha 'alima min ayatina shayan ittakhathaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheen

# 4483

Min waraihim jahannamu wala yughnee 'anhum ma kasaboo shayan wala ma ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa walahum 'athabun 'atheem

# 4484

Hatha hudan wallatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleem

# 4485

Allahu allathee sakhkhara lakumu albahra litajriya alfulku feehi biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon

# 4486

Wasakhkhara lakum ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi jamee'an minhu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon

# 4487

Qul lillatheena amanoo yaghfiroo lillatheena la yarjoona ayyama Allahi liyajziya qawman bima kanoo yaksiboon

# 4488

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha thumma ila rabbikum turja'oon

# 4489

Walaqad atayna banee israeela alkitaba walhukma wannubuwwata warazaqnahum mina attayyibati wafaddalnahum 'ala al'alameen

# 4490

Waataynahum bayyinatin mina alamri fama ikhtalafoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon

# 4491

Thumma ja'alnaka 'ala sharee'atin mina alamri fattabi'ha wala tattabi' ahwaa allatheena la ya'lamoon

# 4492

Innahum lan yughnoo 'anka mina Allahi shayan wainna aththalimeena ba'duhum awliyao ba'din wallahu waliyyu almuttaqeen

# 4493

Hatha basairu linnasi wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yooqinoon

# 4494

Am hasiba allatheena ijtarahoo assayyiati an naj'alahum kallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati sawaan mahyahum wamamatuhum saa ma yahkumoon

# 4495

Wakhalaqa Allahu assamawati walarda bilhaqqi walitujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat wahum la yuthlamoon

# 4496

Afaraayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu waadallahu Allahu 'ala 'ilmin wakhatama 'ala sam'ihi waqalbihi waja'ala 'ala basarihi ghishawatan faman yahdeehi min ba'di Allahi afala tathakkaroon

# 4497

Waqaloo ma hiya illa hayatuna addunya namootu wanahya wama yuhlikuna illa addahru wama lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa yathunnoon

# 4498

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ma kana hujjatahum illa an qaloo itoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeen

# 4499

Quli Allahu yuhyeekum thumma yumeetukum thumma yajma'ukum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoon

# 4500

Walillahi mulku assamawati walardi wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yawmaithin yakhsaru almubtiloon

# 4501

Watara kulla ommatin jathiyatan kullu ommatin tud'a ila kitabiha alyawma tujzawna ma kuntum ta'maloon

# 4502

Hatha kitabuna yantiqu 'alaykum bilhaqqi inna kunna nastansikhu ma kuntum ta'maloon

# 4503

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fayudkhiluhum rabbuhum fee rahmatihi thalika huwa alfawzu almubeen

# 4504

Waamma allatheena kafaroo afalam takun ayatee tutla 'alaykum fastakbartum wakuntum qawman mujrimeen

# 4505

Waitha qeela inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wassa'atu la rayba feeha qultum ma nadree ma assa'atu in nathunnu illa thannan wama nahnu bimustayqineen

# 4506

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 4507

Waqeela alyawma nansakum kama naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha wamawakumu annaru wama lakum min nasireen

# 4508

Thalikum biannakumu ittakhathtum ayati Allahi huzuwan wagharratkumu alhayatu addunya falyawma la yukhrajoona minha wala hum yusta'taboon

# 4509

Falillahi alhamdu rabbi assamawati warabbi alardi rabbi al'alameen

# 4510

Walahu alkibriyao fee assamawati walardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem

# 4511

Hameem

# 4512

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeem

# 4513

Ma khalaqna assamawati walarda wama baynahuma illa bilhaqqi waajalin musamman wallatheena kafaroo 'amma onthiroo mu'ridoon

# 4514

Qul araaytum ma tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee assamawati eetoonee bikitabin min qabli hatha aw atharatin min 'ilmin in kuntum sadiqeen

# 4515

Waman adallu mimman yad'oo min dooni Allahi man la yastajeebu lahu ila yawmi alqiyamati wahum 'an du'aihim ghafiloon

# 4516

Waitha hushira annasu kanoo lahum a'daan wakanoo bi'ibadatihim kafireen

# 4517

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum hatha sihrun mubeen

# 4518

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fala tamlikoona lee mina Allahi shayan huwa a'lamu bima tufeedoona feehi kafa bihi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum wahuwa alghafooru arraheem

# 4519

Qul ma kuntu bid'an mina arrusuli wama adree ma yuf'alu bee wala bikum in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya wama ana illa natheerun mubeen

# 4520

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi wakafartum bihi washahida shahidun min banee israeela 'ala mithlihi faamana wastakbartum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeen

# 4521

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo law kana khayran ma sabaqoona ilayhi waith lam yahtadoo bihi fasayaqooloona hatha ifkun qadeem

# 4522

Wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan wahatha kitabun musaddiqun lisanan 'arabiyyan liyunthira allatheena thalamoo wabushra lilmuhsineen

# 4523

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon

# 4524

Olaika ashabu aljannati khalideena feeha jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloon

# 4525

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi ihsanan hamalathu ommuhu kurhan wawada'athu kurhan wahamluhu wafisaluhu thalathoona shahran hatta itha balagha ashuddahu wabalagha arba'eena sanatan qala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waaslih lee fee thurriyyatee innee tubtu ilayka wainnee mina almuslimeen

# 4526

Olaika allatheena nataqabbalu 'anhum ahsana ma 'amiloo wanatajawazu 'an sayyiatihim fee ashabi aljannati wa'da assidqi allathee kanoo yoo'adoon

# 4527

Wallathee qala liwalidayhi offin lakuma ata'idaninee an okhraja waqad khalati alquroonu min qablee wahuma yastagheethani Allaha waylaka amin inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fayaqoolu ma hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen

# 4528

Olaika allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni walinsi innahum kanoo khasireen

# 4529

Walikullin darajatun mimma 'amiloo waliyuwaffiyahum a'malahum wahum la yuthlamoon

# 4530

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala annari athhabtum tayyibatikum fee hayatikumu addunya wastamta'tum biha falyawma tujzawna 'athaba alhooni bima kuntum tastakbiroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tafsuqoon

# 4531

Wathkur akha 'adin ith anthara qawmahu bilahqafi waqad khalati annuthuru min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin 'atheem

# 4532

Qaloo ajitana litafikana 'an alihatina fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeen

# 4533

Qala innama al'ilmu 'inda Allahi waoballighukum ma orsiltu bihi walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloon

# 4534

Falamma raawhu 'aridan mustaqbila awdiyatihim qaloo hatha 'aridun mumtiruna bal huwa ma ista'jaltum bihi reehun feeha 'athabun aleem

# 4535

Tudammiru kulla shayin biamri rabbiha faasbahoo la yura illa masakinuhum kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeen

# 4536

Walaqad makkannahum feema in makkannakum feehi waja'alna lahum sam'an waabsaran waafidatan fama aghna 'anhum sam'uhum wala absaruhum wala afidatuhum min shayin ith kanoo yajhadoona biayati Allahi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon

# 4537

Walaqad ahlakna ma hawlakum mina alqura wasarrafna alayati la'allahum yarji'oon

# 4538

Falawla nasarahumu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi qurbanan alihatan bal dalloo 'anhum wathalika ifkuhum wama kanoo yaftaroon

# 4539

Waith sarafna ilayka nafaran mina aljinni yastami'oona alqurana falamma hadaroohu qaloo ansitoo falamma qudiya wallaw ila qawmihim munthireen

# 4540

Qaloo ya qawmana inna sami'na kitaban onzila min ba'di moosa musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi yahdee ila alhaqqi waila tareeqin mustaqeem

# 4541

Ya qawmana ajeeboo da'iya Allahi waaminoo bihi yaghfir lakum min thunoobikum wayujirkum min 'athabin aleem

# 4542

Waman la yujib da'iya Allahi falaysa bimu'jizin fee alardi walaysa lahu min doonihi awliyaa olaika fee dalalin mubeen

# 4543

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa assamawati walarda walam ya'ya bikhalqihinna biqadirin 'ala an yuhyiya almawta bala innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer

# 4544

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala annari alaysa hatha bilhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroon

# 4545

Fasbir kama sabara oloo al'azmi mina arrusuli wala tasta'jil lahum kaannahum yawma yarawna ma yoo'adoona lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan min naharin balaghun fahal yuhlaku illa alqawmu alfasiqoon

# 4546

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi adalla a'malahum

# 4547

Wallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati waamanoo bima nuzzila 'ala muhammadin wahuwa alhaqqu min rabbihim kaffara 'anhum sayyiatihim waaslaha balahum

# 4548

Thalika bianna allatheena kafaroo ittaba'oo albatila waanna allatheena amanoo ittaba'oo alhaqqa min rabbihim kathalika yadribu Allahu linnasi amthalahum

# 4549

Faitha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo fadarba arriqabi hatta itha athkhantumoohum fashuddoo alwathaqa faimma mannan ba'du waimma fidaan hatta tada'a alharbu awzaraha thalika walaw yashao Allahu lantasara minhum walakin liyabluwa ba'dakum biba'din wallatheena qutiloo fee sabeeli Allahi falan yudilla a'malahum

# 4550

Sayahdeehim wayuslihu balahum

# 4551

Wayudkhiluhumu aljannata 'arrafaha lahum

# 4552

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tansuroo Allaha yansurkum wayuthabbit aqdamakum

# 4553

Wallatheena kafaroo fata'san lahum waadalla a'malahum

# 4554

Thalika biannahum karihoo ma anzala Allahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4555

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim dammara Allahu 'alayhim walilkafireena amthaluha

# 4556

Thalika bianna Allaha mawla allatheena amanoo waanna alkafireena la mawla lahum

# 4557

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wallatheena kafaroo yatamatta'oona wayakuloona kama takulu alan'amu wannaru mathwan lahum

# 4558

Wakaayyin min qaryatin hiya ashaddu quwwatan min qaryatika allatee akhrajatka ahlaknahum fala nasira lahum

# 4559

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi kaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi wattaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4560

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona feeha anharun min main ghayri asinin waanharun min labanin lam yataghayyar ta'muhu waanharun min khamrin laththatin lishsharibeena waanharun min 'asalin musaffan walahum feeha min kulli aththamarati wamaghfiratun min rabbihim kaman huwa khalidun fee annari wasuqoo maan hameeman faqatta'a am'aahum

# 4561

Waminhum man yastami'u ilayka hatta itha kharajoo min 'indika qaloo lillatheena ootoo al'ilma matha qala anifan olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim wattaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4562

Wallatheena ihtadaw zadahum hudan waatahum taqwahum

# 4563

Fahal yanthuroona illa assa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan faqad jaa ashratuha faanna lahum itha jaathum thikrahum

# 4564

Fa'lam annahu la ilaha illa Allahu wastaghfir lithanbika walilmumineena walmuminati wallahu ya'lamu mutaqallabakum wamathwakum

# 4565

Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo lawla nuzzilat sooratun faitha onzilat sooratun muhkamatun wathukira feeha alqitalu raayta allatheena fee quloobihim maradun yanthuroona ilayka nathara almaghshiyyi 'alayhi mina almawti faawla lahum

# 4566

Ta'atun waqawlun ma'roofun faitha 'azama alamru falaw sadaqoo Allaha lakana khayran lahum

# 4567

Fahal 'asaytum in tawallaytum an tufsidoo fee alardi watuqatti'oo arhamakum

# 4568

Olaika allatheena la'anahumu Allahu faasammahum waa'ma absarahum

# 4569

Afala yatadabbaroona alqurana am 'ala quloobin aqfaluha

# 4570

Inna allatheena irtaddoo 'ala adbarihim min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda ashshaytanu sawwala lahum waamla lahum

# 4571

Thalika biannahum qaloo lillatheena karihoo ma nazzala Allahu sanutee'ukum fee ba'di alamri wallahu ya'lamu israrahum

# 4572

Fakayfa itha tawaffathumu almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum

# 4573

Thalika biannahumu ittaba'oo ma askhata Allaha wakarihoo ridwanahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4574

Am hasiba allatheena fee quloobihim maradun an lan yukhrija Allahu adghanahum

# 4575

Walaw nashao laaraynakahum fala'araftahum biseemahum walata'rifannahum fee lahni alqawli wallahu ya'lamu a'malakum

# 4576

Walanabluwannakum hatta na'lama almujahideena minkum wassabireena wanabluwa akhbarakum

# 4577

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi washaqqoo arrasoola min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda lan yaduroo Allaha shayan wasayuhbitu a'malahum

# 4578

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola wala tubtiloo a'malakum

# 4579

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi thumma matoo wahum kuffarun falan yaghfira Allahu lahum

# 4580

Fala tahinoo watad'oo ila assalmi waantumu ala'lawna wallahu ma'akum walan yatirakum a'malakum

# 4581

Innama alhayatu addunya la'ibun walahwun wain tuminoo watattaqoo yutikum ojoorakum wala yasalkum amwalakum

# 4582

In yasalkumooha fayuhfikum tabkhaloo wayukhrij adghanakum

# 4583

Haantum haolai tud'awna litunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi faminkum man yabkhalu waman yabkhal fainnama yabkhalu 'an nafsihi wallahu alghaniyyu waantumu alfuqarao wain tatawallaw yastabdil qawman ghayrakum thumma la yakoonoo amthalakum

# 4584

Inna fatahna laka fathan mubeena

# 4585

Liyaghfira laka Allahu ma taqaddama min thanbika wama taakhkhara wayutimma ni'matahu 'alayka wayahdiyaka siratan mustaqeema

# 4586

Wayansuraka Allahu nasran 'azeeza

# 4587

Huwa allathee anzala assakeenata fee quloobi almumineena liyazdadoo eemanan ma'a eemanihim walillahi junoodu assamawati walardi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema

# 4588

Liyudkhila almumineena walmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wayukaffira 'anhum sayyiatihim wakana thalika 'inda Allahi fawzan 'atheema

# 4589

Wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena walmunafiqati walmushrikeena walmushrikati aththanneena billahi thanna assawi 'alayhim dairatu assawi waghadiba Allahu 'alayhim wala'anahum waa'adda lahum jahannama wasaat maseera

# 4590

Walillahi junoodu assamawati walardi wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema

# 4591

Inna arsalnaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheera

# 4592

Lituminoo billahi warasoolihi watu'azziroohu watuwaqqiroohu watusabbihoohu bukratan waaseela

# 4593

Inna allatheena yubayi'oonaka innama yubayi'oona Allaha yadu Allahi fawqa aydeehim faman nakatha fainnama yankuthu 'ala nafsihi waman awfa bima 'ahada 'alayhu Allaha fasayuteehi ajran 'atheema

# 4594

Sayaqoolu laka almukhallafoona mina ala'rabi shaghalatna amwaluna waahloona fastaghfir lana yaqooloona bialsinatihim ma laysa fee quloobihim qul faman yamliku lakum mina Allahi shayan in arada bikum darran aw arada bikum naf'an bal kana Allahu bima ta'maloona khabeera

# 4595

Bal thanantum an lan yanqaliba arrasoolu walmuminoona ila ahleehim abadan wazuyyina thalika fee quloobikum wathanantum thanna assawi wakuntum qawman boora

# 4596

Waman lam yumin billahi warasoolihi fainna a'tadna lilkafireena sa'eera

# 4597

Walillahi mulku assamawati walardi yaghfiru liman yashao wayu'aththibu man yashao wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema

# 4598

Sayaqoolu almukhallafoona itha intalaqtum ila maghanima litakhuthooha tharoona nattabi'kum yureedoona an yubaddiloo kalama Allahi qul lan tattabi'oona kathalikum qala Allahu min qablu fasayaqooloona bal tahsudoonana bal kanoo la yafqahoona illa qaleela

# 4599

Qul lilmukhallafeena mina ala'rabi satud'awna ila qawmin olee basin shadeedin tuqatiloonahum aw yuslimoona fain tutee'oo yutikumu Allahu ajran hasanan wain tatawallaw kama tawallaytum min qablu yu'aththibkum 'athaban aleema

# 4600

Laysa 'ala ala'ma harajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu waman yatawalla yu'aththibhu 'athaban aleema

# 4601

Laqad radiya Allahu 'ani almumineena ith yubayi'oonaka tahta ashshajarati fa'alima ma fee quloobihim faanzala asakeenata 'alayhim waathabahum fathan qareeba

# 4602

Wamaghanima katheeratan yakhuthoonaha wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema

# 4603

Wa'adakumu Allahu maghanima katheeratan takhuthoonaha fa'ajjala lakum hathihi wakaffa aydiya annasi 'ankum walitakoona ayatan lilmumineena wayahdiyakum siratan mustaqeema

# 4604

Waokhra lam taqdiroo 'alayha qad ahata Allahu biha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeera

# 4605

Walaw qatalakumu allatheena kafaroo lawallawoo aladbara thumma la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseera

# 4606

Sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeela

# 4607

Wahuwa allathee kaffa aydiyahum 'ankum waaydiyakum 'anhum bibatni makkata min ba'di an athfarakum 'alayhim wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseera

# 4608

Humu allatheena kafaroo wasaddookum 'ani almasjidi alharami walhadya ma'koofan an yablugha mahillahu walawla rijalun muminoona wanisaon muminatun lam ta'lamoohum an tataoohum fatuseebakum minhum ma'arratun bighayri 'ilmin liyudkhila Allahu fee rahmatihi man yashao law tazayyaloo la'aththabna allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athaban aleema

# 4609

Ith ja'ala allatheena kafaroo fee quloobihimu alhamiyyata hamiyyata aljahiliyyati faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'ala rasoolihi wa'ala almumineena waalzamahum kalimata attaqwa wakanoo ahaqqa biha waahlaha wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleema

# 4610

Laqad sadaqa Allahu rasoolahu arruya bilhaqqi latadkhulunna almasjida alharama in shaa Allahu amineena muhalliqeena ruoosakum wamuqassireena la takhafoona fa'alima ma lam ta'lamoo faja'ala min dooni thalika fathan qareeba

# 4611

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bilhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu 'ala addeeni kullihi wakafa billahi shaheeda

# 4612

Muhammadun rasoolu Allahi wallatheena ma'ahu ashiddao 'ala alkuffari ruhamao baynahum tarahum rukka'an sujjadan yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan seemahum fee wujoohihim min athari assujoodi thalika mathaluhum fee attawrati wamathaluhum fee alinjeeli kazar'in akhraja shatahu faazarahu fastaghlatha fastawa 'ala sooqihi yu'jibu azzurra'a liyagheetha bihimu alkuffara wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati minhum maghfiratan waajran 'atheema

# 4613

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuqaddimoo bayna yadayi Allahi warasoolihi wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha samee'un 'aleem

# 4614

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tarfa'oo aswatakum fawqa sawti annabiyyi wala tajharoo lahu bilqawli kajahri ba'dikum liba'din an tahbata a'malukum waantum la tash'uroon

# 4615

Inna allatheena yaghuddoona aswatahum 'inda rasooli Allahi olaika allatheena imtahana Allahu quloobahum littaqwa lahum maghfiratun waajrun 'atheem

# 4616

Inna allatheena yunadoonaka min warai alhujurati aktharuhum la ya'qiloon

# 4617

Walaw annahum sabaroo hatta takhruja ilayhim lakana khayran lahum wallahu ghafoorun raheem

# 4618

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in jaakum fasiqun binabain fatabayyanoo an tuseeboo qawman bijahalatin fatusbihoo 'ala ma fa'altum nadimeen

# 4619

Wa'lamoo anna feekum rasoola Allahi law yutee'ukum fee katheerin mina alamri la'anittum walakinna Allaha habbaba ilaykumu aleemana wazayyanahu fee quloobikum wakarraha ilaykumu alkufra walfusooqa wal'isyana olaika humu arrashidoon

# 4620

Fadlan mina Allahi wani'matan wallahu 'aleemun hakeem

# 4621

Wain taifatani mina almumineena iqtataloo faaslihoo baynahuma fain baghat ihdahuma 'ala alokhra faqatiloo allatee tabghee hatta tafeea ila amri Allahi fain faat faaslihoo baynahuma bil'adli waaqsitoo inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteen

# 4622

Innama almuminoona ikhwatun faaslihoo bayna akhawaykum wattaqoo Allaha la'allakum turhamoon

# 4623

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yaskhar qawmun min qawmin 'asa an yakoonoo khayran minhum wala nisaon min nisain 'asa an yakunna khayran minhunna wala talmizoo anfusakum wala tanabazoo bilalqabi bisa alismu alfusooqu ba'da aleemani waman lam yatub faolaika humu aththalimoon

# 4624

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ijtaniboo katheeran mina aththanni inna ba'da aththanni ithmun wala tajassasoo wala yaghtab ba'dukum ba'dan ayuhibbu ahadukum an yakula lahma akheehi maytan fakarihtumoohu wattaqoo Allaha inna Allaha tawwabun raheem

# 4625

Ya ayyuha annasu inna khalaqnakum min thakarin waontha waja'alnakum shu'ooban waqabaila lita'arafoo inna akramakum 'inda Allahi atqakum inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeer

# 4626

Qalati ala'rabu amanna qul lam tuminoo walakin qooloo aslamna walamma yadkhuli aleemanu fee quloobikum wain tutee'oo Allaha warasoolahu la yalitkum min a'malikum shayan inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem

# 4627

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo billahi warasoolihi thumma lam yartaboo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi olaika humu assadiqoon

# 4628

# 4629
